# 金锁流珠引

**The *Taixuan* *Jinsuo* *Liuzhu* Introduction**
Title: *Taixuan Jinsuo Liuzhu* Introduction.
Attributed to Li Chunfeng’s annotation.
Likely composed between the Tang and Song dynasties.
Detailed exposition of Daoist *fuxu* (ritual incantations and talismans) for averting disasters (*lingzai*), including practices of the **Zhengyi** and **Shangqing** schools.
Twenty-nine fascicles.
Source of the base text: *Zhengtong Daozang* (Canon of the Orthodox Daoist Treasury), *Taixuan* section.

**Contents**
1. Preface to the *Taixuan Jinsuo Liuzhu* Introduction
2. The *Sanwu* *Bugu* (Three-Five Step Halter) Introduction
3. Diagram of the *Sanbu Jiuji* (Three Steps, Nine Traces)
4. Initial Reception of the *Sanwu* Method
5. Incantations for the Five-Ranked Ritual Masters
6. The *Taixuan Yuanqi* (Primordial *Qi*/Vitality) Generation of the *San Yuan* (Three Primordials) Introduction
7. Diagram of the *Zhenshi Zhou Jiangjun* (Retained General Zhou) Method, Diagram of the *Zhenshi Ge Jiangjun* (Retained General Ge) Method, Diagram of the *Zhenshi Tang Jiangjun* (Retained General Tang) Method, Diagram of the *Zhenshi Qidou* (Seven-Fight Retained) Method
8. Explanation of the Middle Section (Upper Part) Turning the Body for Retained Use
9. Explanation of the *Shangyuan* (Upper Primordial) Three Divisions: Generals, *San Gongcao* (Three Functionaries), etc.
   - Diagram of the *Shangyuan Shangbu Jiangjun Bugu* (Upper Primordial Upper Division General Step Halter)
   - Diagram of the *Shangyuan Zhongbu Jiangjun Bugu* (Upper Primordial Middle Division General Step Halter)
   - Diagram of the *Shangyuan Xiabu Jiangjun Bugu* (Upper Primordial Lower Division General Step Halter)
10. Diagram of the *Zhen Song Zhongdou Qixing* (Retained Recitation of the Middle Dipper Seven Stars) Method
    - Explanation of the *Zhenshi Sidou* (Retained Four-Fight) Method
    - Explanation of the *Yipei Yitian Yincai* (Leaning and Wearing the Retained Talisman) Method
    - Explanation of the *Lipei Yitian Zhenxing* (Standing and Wearing the Retained Talisman) Method
    - Explanation of the *Mianpei Yitian Zhenfa* (Sleeping and Wearing the Retained Talisman) Method
    - The *Wudou* (Lying Dipper) Method
    - Explanation of the *Zuopei Yitian Zhenfa* (Sitting and Wearing the Retained Talisman) Method
    - Explanation of the *Shitiantian Lishijishi Ji Di* (Invoking the *Zhutiantian* [Polar Void Heaven] *Lishi* [Celestial Force] to Strike Enemies and Banish Evil) Method
11. Explanation of the *Pei Zhutian Yinhu* (Wearing the Celestial Names of the *Zhutiantian* [Polar Void Heaven]) Method

**The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl Method** (*Jinsuo Liuzhu*)
　　The *Three-Five Step Framework* (*Sanwu Bugang*) Introduction
　　The *Step Framework* (*Bugang*) is a method to strengthen the body, invigorate the spirit, and fortify the **qi** (*pò*).

　　First, one begins with the *Earthly Poles* (*Diji*), laboring the body and fortifying the spirit so that the **qi** (*shénqì*) naturally settles and is stored. Then, one harmonizes with Heaven and Earth, summoning the divine spirits.

　　Annotation: This method serves two purposes: first, to heal oneself; second, to retain surplus **virtue/power** (*dé*) for healing others.

　　Its application is swift against calamities of water and fire.

　　The *Celestial Lord* (*Lǎojūn*) instructed the *Supreme Void High Spirit Flying Morning Central Daoist Sovereign* (*Tàixū Shànglíng Fēichén Zhōngyāng Dàojūn*), who shaped the *Earthly Poles* as the *Seven-Star Dipper* (*Qīxīng Dǒu*). Annotation: The form of the *Seven-Star Dipper* (*Dǒu*).

　　Annotation: *Long Life* (*Chángshēng*) emerges from the *Five Sufferings* (*Wǔkǔ*), the starting point of one’s life span. Annotation: The *Five Sufferings* (*Wǔkǔ*) are the calculations of the *Five Phases* (*Wǔyùn*).

　　For instance, if one’s life is governed by the *Metal Phase* (*Jīn*), their vitality lies in *Peri* (*Sì*), for *Peri* is *Long Life*. Their death occurs in *Zi* (*Child*), and their burial in *Chǒu* (*Buffalo*). *Zi* and *Chǒu* are the *Five Sufferings*, and one steps out from them into *Long Life*—thus, it is called *Exiting Death and Entering Life* (*Chūsǐ Rùshēng*).

　　For those governed by the *Wood Phase* (*Mù*), vitality lies in *Hài* (*Boar*), for *Hài* is *Long Life*. Their death occurs in *Wǔ* (*Horse*), and their burial in *Wèi* (*Sheep*). *Wǔ* and *Wèi* are the *Five Sufferings*.

　　For those governed by the *Water Phase* (*Shuǐ*), vitality lies in *Shēn* (*Monkey*), for *Shēn* is *Long Life*. Their death occurs in *Mǎo* (*Rabbit*), and their burial in *Chén* (*Dragon*). *Mǎo* and *Chén* are the *Five Sufferings*.

　　For those governed by the *Fire Phase* (*Huǒ*), vitality lies in *Yín* (*Tiger*), for *Yín* is *Long Life*. Their death occurs in *Yǒu* (*Rooster*), and their burial in *Xū* (*Dog*). *Yǒu* and *Xū* are the *Five Sufferings*.

　　For those governed by the *Earth Phase* (*Tǔ*), the calculations are the same as those for the *Water Phase*. One takes the *Five Sufferings* as the starting points for vitality, death, and burial, and the *Eight Hardships* and *Nine Calamities* as the *Nine Difficulties* (*Jiǔ È*).

　　The ancient true immortals all taught this method. It is called *Transcending the Five Sufferings and Eight Hardships*, *Dispelling the Nine Calamities*, and *Healing a Hundred Illnesses*—the master leads the disciple to ascend the framework.

　　The later *Celestial Lord* (*Shàngjūn*) introduced the *Great Youth Lord* (*Dàtóngjūn*) and the *Lesser Youth Lord* (*Xiǎotóngjūn*), allowing one to exit the *Five Sufferings* and enter *Long Life*.

　　Next, one proceeds from *Long Life* into the *King* and *Minister* phases. Annotation: For the *Metal Phase* (*Jīn*), vitality lies in *Peri* (*Sì*), and the *King* phase is in *Yǒu* (*Rooster*). For the *Wood Phase* (*Mù*), vitality lies in *Hài* (*Boar*), and the *King* phase is in *Mǎo* (*Rabbit*). For the *Water Phase* (*Shuǐ*), vitality lies in *Shēn* (*Monkey*), and the *King* phase is in *Zi* (*Child*). For the *Fire Phase* (*Huǒ*), vitality lies in *Yín* (*Tiger*), and the *King* phase is in *Wǔ* (*Horse*). For the *Earth Phase* (*Tǔ*), the calculations are the same as those for the *Water Phase*. The *Five Lineages* (*Wǔxìng*) cannot harm one another, thereby dispelling the calamities of the *Five Phases* (*Wǔxíng*).

　　The *Celestial Lord* (*Zhàng*) further instructed: Annotation: *Zhàng* refers to the *Grand Supreme* (*Zǒngzhēn*), and *Zhang* refers to the *Celestial Master* (*Tiānshī*).

　　*"The human body begins its life from the Five Phases and also perishes through them. I have known this for a long time. Even if one does not understand it early, they will still be harmed by these calamities. All must first practice the *Yú Bù* (Tortoise Steps), tread upon the *Earthly Poles*, and follow the reverse and inverted order of the three ranks. Then, recite the Five-Phase incantations to dispel them, and within one year, the calamities will be dispelled. Annotation: The Five-Phase incantations are found in the first volume of the *Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (*Jinsuo Liuzhu*), containing five verses.*

　　First, one performs the *Bundle Facing* (*Shùxiàng*) ritual, drums the *Heavenly Drum* (*Tiāngǔ*) thirty-six times, and invigorates the body as prescribed. Then, one ignites the furnace, raises the *Official* (*Guān*), and sits in reflection upon the *Supreme One’s Hall* (*Tàiyī Fǔ*). Upon completion, one stands and reflects upon the *Officials of the Six Star Lords* (*Liuxingjun*) and their *Soldiers* (*Bīng*), as depicted in the diagram to the left and right. One then dons the *Seven-Star Dipper* (*Qīxīng Dǒu*) robes in a full circle, weeping while donning the robes, and raises the *Official* (*Guān*). After completing the ritual, one ascends the *Step Framework*.

　　Upon finishing the *Step Framework*, one recites the five incantations to break the mutual opposition of the Five Phases. Then, one ascends the *Step Framework* five times again, circling it. After completion, one recites the twelve incantations to subdue the twelve *Branches* (*Zhīgān*) and *Heavenly Stems* (*Tiāngān*), securing *Long Life* and dispelling the Five-Phase calamities. Within one year, one avoids evil; within two years, one avoids harm from weapons; within three years, one avoids harm from spirits. By the fourth year, one becomes an *Earthly Immortal* (*Dìxiān*), and all harm and calamity dare not approach.

　　From this point onward, blessings and joy are boundless. One commands the divine spirits, tames the flying dragon, the *Supreme Ultimate* (*Tàijí*) bestows the *Numinous Herb* (*Shízhī*), and the *Jade Emperor* (*Yùdì*) grants the *Youthful Immortal* (*Tóng*). If practiced for twenty-seven years, one becomes a *High Clarity True Person* (*Shàngqīng Zhēnrén*). Annotation: This explanation states that the *Golden Lock* (*Jinsuo*) method must be practiced first, followed by the *Heavenly Framework* (*Tiāngāng*) and *Flying Steps* (*Fēibù*) method, to achieve the effects as described earlier by the *Celestial Lord* (*Shàngjūn*). If one only practices the *Heavenly Framework*, it may not necessarily dispel evil.

　　This method requires first practicing the *Earthly Poles*, then ascending the *Heavenly Framework*—only then will one have the effects of dispelling evil. If one practices the *Heavenly Framework* without first establishing the *Earthly Poles*, there will be no response from the divine spirits.

　　In the past, the ancient *Broad Achievement Lord* (*Guǎngchéngjūn*) taught the *Yellow Emperor* (*Huángdì*) the *Flying Steps of Heavenly Steel* (*Tiāngāng Fēibù*). The *Yellow Emperor* practiced it for thirty years without divine response. Later, he sought the method again, and the *Celestial Lord* then gave him the first volume of the *Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (*Jinsuo Liuzhu*) and explained the *Earthly Poles* method. Within one year, he could summon and subdue spirits to his will. In the second year, he annihilated *Chīyóu* (a mythical tyrant). In the third year, his strength was sufficient to wrestle tigers and leopards. By the twenty-seventh year, he could transform his form and manifest countless wonders. At the twenty-eighth year, he ascended to Heaven.

　　Though the human body is born of Heaven and nurtured by Earth, its foundation is rooted in Earth. If one seeks the *Heavenly Framework* without first establishing the *Earthly Poles* as the root and foundation, it is like building a pavilion without a base—how can it stand firmly in the air? The *Ancient Lords* (*Qiánshèng Hòushèng*) all descended personally to instruct their disciples in practice.

　　Annotation: The master leads the disciple to ascend the framework, transcending the *Five Sufferings* and *Eight Hardships*."

Upon completion, the master unites with the disciple, donning the **Seven Stars** like a garment, which is called the **Conjoined Garment**. The master and disciple wear the **Conjoined Garment** on their left and right sides.

　　Annotation: The male first begins from the left, the female from the right.

The first **Star of Vitality** (*Chīyóu*’s constellation).
　　Annotation: The left hand is **□**, the left elbow (above the head) is **□**, the left shoulder is **□**, the heart is **□**, the right shoulder is **□**, the right elbow is **□**, and the right hand is **□**. When the first **Star of Vitality** is formed, the **Child of the Central Lord** (*Zǐshēng Rénzhǔ*) is born. The practitioner stands upright, raises their hands, and covers their head. Annotation: This wards off malevolent humans and evil spirits; the right hand points at them, and the practitioner twists the **incantation formula** (*niǎnjué*) as needed, with the formula found in the **Palm Incantations** (*Zhǎngjué*).

Initially, when the **Conjoined Garment** is worn, the **incantation formula** is not yet applied. Annotation: *Idle* means not yet applied; in urgent moments, it can be instantly bound to water and fire.

The second **Star of Yin Precision** (*Yīnjīng* constellation).
　　Annotation: The right hand is **□**, the right elbow is **□**, the right shoulder is **□**, the heart is **□**, the left shoulder is **□**, the left elbow is **□**, and the left hand is **□**. When the second **Star of Yin Precision** is formed, the **Child of the Central Lord** born under the hours of *Chǒu* and *Hài* (*Hòushèng*) is summoned. The practitioner stands upright, raises their right hand, and covers their head. Annotation: This wards off serpents, tigers and leopards, spirits and beasts, venom, silence, and malevolent ghosts and deities. The **□** is used, and the practitioner grasps the **□ Star**, pointing at each one sequentially. If facing an enemy, the practitioner turns their hand around their body as needed. The **Stars of Vitality** are worn on the left and right sides of the **Star of Yin Precision**, which is then applied.

If used urgently, it will instantly take effect. If not yet applied, it is still superior; superior, it reaches the **Seven Stars**, and further verification is made.

The third **Star of the True Immortal** (*Zhēnrén Dàxīng*).
　　Annotation: The left hand is **□**, the left elbow is **□**, the left shoulder is **□**, the heart is **□**, the right elbow is **□**, the right knee is **□**, and the right foot is **□**. When the third **Star of the True Immortal** is formed, the **Child of the Central Lord** born under the hours of *Yín* and *Xū* (*Rénzhǔ*) is summoned. Annotation: The **Child of the Central Lord** may be summoned for matters related to the hour of *Yín*, or for seeking longevity when born under *Yín* and *Xū*, or to counter those who plot against them. It can also repel malevolent humans and ghosts, tigers and wolves, ferocious beasts, mountain spirits, poisonous deities, and demonic figures—all coming from the eastern *Yín* or western *Xū* directions. When they arrive, the practitioner twists the **Grand Marshal Formula** (*Dūjiàn Jué*), causing the **Third True Immortal Star** (**□**) to strike them down, and they will all submit and die.

If an enemy comes, the practitioner forms the left hand as **Arcuate Cover** (*Kuìgài*), covers their head, and points with the right hand as **□**, causing the enemy to submit. If they do not submit, the **Northern Dipper** (*Běidǒu*) will drink their blood, and they will die within ten days from heartache. Practitioners of the **Dao** must be cautious not to invoke this.

The application of the first two stars is also the same as this third star.

Bend your right hand forward, covering your head with your left hand, then apply the three or five fingers [as prescribed].

**Note:** *"Fingers"* here refers to the act of exorcising with a shout.

For seeking longevity, calculating fortune and rank, or ensuring military advantage, face the sun and perform this at noon when hidden—it will cause them to self-destruct.

True persons do not suffer from stalking. If one wears the **Configurative Robe** (*Pèiyī*) on their body, its efficacy is profound. However, it should only be used by those cultivating longevity while sleeping at night, keeping the breath (*hū*) stored on the left shoulder.

**Note:** For women, it is on the right shoulder.

This ensures the practitioner’s spirit remains tranquil, fearing no malevolent spirits or ghosts. Within a year, such disturbances will cease.

**Note:** If a husband performs this monthly, three times a day, after a year, its power will manifest like a deity’s emergence and disappearance.

**Fourth Star of Mysterious Obscurity** (*Xuánmíng Xīng*)
**Note:** Form the right hand as **□**, the right elbow as **□**, the right shoulder as **□**, the heart as **□**, the left chest as **□**, the left knee as **□**, the left foot as **□**, and **□** to complete the gesture.

When all four limbs are aligned, those born in the *Mao-Yǒu* directions govern it.

**Note:** Its applications are twofold:
1. For self-cultivation—seeking blessings of longevity, fortune, and rank, or healing bodily misfortunes, diseases, and calamities.
2. For others—when practicing prohibitive *qi*-binding methods, all seven stars must be used in conjunction with the *Bǎi Jìn* (Hundred Prohibitions).

Bend your left foot forward, covering your head with your right hand, then apply the three or five methods [as prescribed].

**Note:** This method is particularly effective against military conflicts and official misfortunes. Other uses align with the seven stars.

**Fifth Star of the Elixir Origin** (*Dānyuán Xīng*)
**Note:** Form the left foot as **□**, the left knee as **□**, the left elbow as **□**, the heart as **□**, the right shoulder as **□**, the right elbow as **□**, and the right hand as **□**, then **□** to exorcise demons and malevolent spirits.

When all five limbs are aligned, those born in the *Chén-Shēn* directions govern it.

**Note:** Its applications are the same as the fourth star.

Bend your left foot forward, covering your head with your right hand, and apply it as before.

**Sixth Star of the Northern Pole** (*Běijí Xīng*)
**Note:** Form the right foot as **□**, the right knee as **□**, the right elbow as **□**, the heart as **□**, the left shoulder as **□**, the left elbow as **□**, and the left hand as **□**, then **□** for prohibitive control.

When all six limbs are aligned, those born in the *Wèi-Wèi* directions govern it.

**Note:** Its applications are the same as before.

Bend your right foot forward, covering your head with your left hand, and apply it as before.

**Seventh Star of the Heavenly Pass** (*Tiānguān Xīng*)
**Note:** Form the left hand as **□**, the left elbow as **□**, the left shoulder as **□**, the heart as **□**, the right shoulder as **□**, the right elbow as **□**, and the right hand as **□**, then **□** to apply it.

When all seven limbs are aligned, those born in the *Wǔ* direction govern it.

**Note:** This star uniquely subdues all malevolent humans, demons, and spirits—ten thousand spirits and myriad evils that cause disturbances. It is the sole star capable of swiftly controlling them, surpassing even water and fire in speed.

Though the stars are used sequentially, the *Step-Star* method retains its prohibitive power. Only the **Heavenly Pass Star** can dominantly subdue ghosts, malevolent figures, military conflicts, official misfortunes, and countless diseases. Its execution is as swift as water and fire.

The seven stars have various ritual offerings (*jiào*). Know this: offerings must follow the prescribed rites and timing.

In the spring months of the first and second lunar months, or in autumn during the seventh and eighth lunar months, perform sacrifices according to one’s natal star on clear days.

Do not perform sacrifices at other times, lest misfortune be invited—do not presume to seek blessings recklessly.

Additionally, for those practicing the *Step-Halo* (*Bùgāng*), sacrifices must be conducted twice yearly in spring and autumn.

**Note:** If one practices the *Step-Halo* or *Memory-Tracing* methods, monthly cultivation is required, with sacrifices performed twice a year. Offerings should include money, wine, fresh rice cakes, fruits, and other ritual foods as specified in the *Líu Zhū Jīng* (Lower Grade).

This is the later sage-emperor’s revelation to the Celestial Master: the **Northern Dipper** is the **Central Dipper**. The Central Dipper’s nine stars transform into the nine spirits, forming the **Star-Halo** (*Xīnggāng*) through their steps.

Yu saw a spirit bird stepping on the Star-Halo, turning stones and wood, and consuming serpents. After three years of learning, his art perfected, he could invert the nine stars, aligning them with his feet—touching objects with his toes made them move, unaware his hands were the true agents.

Later, ascending the peaks of the Shèkè Mountains, a divine person instructed him: *"Why do you step with your feet when your hands can do it?"* Yu was then taught to use his toes instead. The king saw the spirit bird stepping with its beak-like toes and bowed in acceptance.

Afterward, he attained the Dao, commanding ghosts, dragons, tigers, and leopards. He dredged rivers, regulated floods, and delineated the Nine Regions.

Upon ascending to imperial rule, he mastered the Dao, interpreted the *Yì*, transformed his form, and ascended to the **Supreme Pole** (*Tàijí*).

**Note:** Though he did not attain the **Upper Clarity True Person**, he governed the lower realm’s water and drought from the **Left Great One’s Domain** (*Zuǒ Tài Yī Fǔ*).

Yu received divine instruction:

**Note:** This is the **Mandate of the Celestial Official** passed to Yu.

The words were: *"Observe the Northern Dipper—this is the Central Dipper’s **Heavenly Pass Star**."*

**Note:** Daoist scriptures state that the **Central Dipper’s Great Arc** oversees all spirits, thus this is the Central Dipper.

The *Dà Jīn Suǒ Liú Zhū Pǐn* states: *"Now observe the Northern Dipper—this is the Central Dipper."*

For those facing sudden official persecution, military threats, or illnesses, this method is as swift as water and fire. Its power lies in the heart and hands, resonating with the palm, while the body and spirit also hold governing formulas—these are found in the **Palm Diagram**.

The **Most High Laozi** declared: *"The Central Dipper governs the four limbs and the twenty-eight lunar mansions. In one day and night, it completes a celestial circuit. The Northern Dipper is revered, paying homage to the two Great True Stars."*

Its third star is named the **True Person Star**, overseeing those in this world who seek true immortality. Thus, those cultivating the Dao must align their steps accordingly, daring not to offend the True Person Star, lest their fate and lifespan be diminished.

「Moreover, there are **Nine Stars**, which must also be invoked in accordance with the **Stepwise Daoist Circuit** (*bùgāng*) while in cultivation. One must practice the **formulas of the True Person Star** and the **Emperor-Worthy Stars** (*Dìzūn*).

*Note: The formulas are found in the *Gold Lock Flowing Pearl Palm Diagram Formulas* (*Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Zhǎngzhōng Jué*).*

Additionally, within the mind, one must constantly visualize the **Three True** (*Sān Zhēn*). In the course of a month, one must practice the **Stepwise Daoist Circuit** five times.

*Note: The Circuit also comprises **Seven Stars**—specifically, excluding the **Assisting Minister Stars** (*Fǔbì*).*

If the position of the **True Person Star** is unfavorable, one must avoid stepping upon it; instead, one must tread the **Stepwise Daoist Circuit** accordingly. This is known in the world as the **"Treading the Earth Circuit"** (*Nièdì Jì*).

This method requires one to follow the **Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper** (*Běidǒu Qīxīng*), excluding calamities and misfortunes, ascending to transcendence and emerging from mortality. It subjugates malevolent spirits, deities, and demons—such as **Dragon, Tiger, Leopard, and Manticore** (*lónghǔ páo jīng*), **noxious spirits and poisonous serpents** (*yāosuì dúshé*), and the **Great Demons of Heaven and Earth** (*Tiāndì Dàmó*). All must be invoked using the **Northern Dipper**, aligning with the **Five Dipper Lords** (*Wǔ Dǒu Jūn*) by sealing their names.

*Note: The Five Dipper Lords are the seven stars of the Northern Dipper, excluding the **Assisting Minister Stars** (*Fǔbì*).*

The **Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper** are properly named **Dipper, Ox, Girl, Void, Peril, Hall, and Wall** (*Dǒu, Niú, Nǚ, Xū, Wēi, Shì, Bì*). However, in practice, they are called the **Five Dipper Lords** (*Wǔ Dǒu Jūn*)—that is, the **Luminous Yang** (*Yángmíng*) and **Yin Essence** (*Yīnjīng*), though this is incorrect.

*Note: Because people do not know the true names of the Northern Dipper, they mistakenly call them Luminous Yang and Yin Essence.*

This is the **Central Dipper** (*Zhōng Dǒu*), which augments one’s lifespan and fulfills merit in the mortal realm, harmonizing with **Daoist Immortals** (*xiān pǐn*) and aligning with the **Northern Dipper**. One must first cultivate the **Northern Dipper**, then proceed to the **Central Dipper**.

If there are merits or misfortunes, one seeks salvation for others with the same swiftness as water and fire—this is verified.

The **Later Sage Emperor** (*Hòushèng Jūn*) instructed **Grandmaster of the True** (*Zǒng Zhēn*):

*"You must convey the **Supreme Daoist Teachings** (*Zhìrén Shàngjiào*) to those who are **Daoist Aspirants** (*zhìrén*).*
*Note: It is not given to ordinary people.*

*Daoist Aspirants* must cultivate with their hearts and minds, transmitting and practicing the teachings as instructed. Those who do so are then taught this method, entrusted to attain the **True Person** (*Zhēn Rén*) stage of cultivation. Do not let *Daoist Aspirants* lose their merit or diminish their lifespan, for then you would fail in your duty as the **Grandmaster of the True** (*Zǒng Zhēn Rén*).

I command you to pass this on to all, and you must teach it to all *Daoist Aspirants*. Cultivation cannot surpass this.

*Note: After transmitting the *Gold Lock Flowing Pearl Canon* (*Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Zhèngjīng*), one concludes with a **ritual exorcism** (*jiào*). Then, this method is practiced.*

Every night, after completing the ritual exorcism, one must
*Note: The invocation of fate is without urgency, aligning the names of the Seven Stars with the Five Dipper Lords.*

seal the name of the Dipper Lord when the **Northern Dipper** (*Běidǒu*) is upright. The **Five Dipper Lords** (*Wǔ Dǒu Jūn*)—such as **□, □, □, □, □, □, □**—rotate in celestial vigilance, protecting mortals and allowing them to attain their own **True Essence** (*Zhēn*).

Cultivation must always be like the **"Embodied Stars Diagram"** (*Hán Yǐng Tú*). Those who seal the positions are entrusted to command the *Daoist Aspirants*.

*Note: Daoist Aspirants do not use the Seven Stars to cover their bodies like clothing; rather, they visualize them within the mind without causing harm to the vital essence or diminishing one’s lifespan. By day, they remain in a tranquil state, practicing the Seven Stars Diagram to ensure their souls and spirits ascend with their bodies. Their bodily essence remains steadfast and undispersed, with the Seven Stars radiating brilliance. Ghosts and spirits fear this, and the cultivation resembles the "Embodied Stars" and the "Embodied Grand Dao" (Hán Hóng). Their Dao is inherently true, revered and guarded by Heaven and Earth, with spirits and demons submitting to their command. The Heavenly Demons welcome them, and the Three Officials (of Heaven, Earth, and Man) report their merit. When their merit is complete, they ascend to transcendence by day, becoming True Persons (Zhēn Rén). In all actions—standing, sitting, resting, or sleeping—they must not depart from their bodies.*

*Note: Daoist Aspirants who constantly visualize the Seven Stars, day and night, without pause, will have their bodily essence shine like stars after a year. Their forms will embody the True Essence.*

*Note: After a year of uninterrupted practice—standing, sitting, resting, or sleeping—while constantly visualizing the sealed Seven Stars, the stars’ essence enters deeply into the body, circulating in a perpetual Daoist Circuit, akin to the rotation of Heaven. Thus, it is named the "Embodied Stars Daoist Essence Circuit" (Hánxīng Zhēn Qīwéi Xīng Zhēn), also known as the "Ascension to the Upper Clarity" (Rù Shàngqīng), enabling one to repel armies.*

After two years, they attain the **"Embodied True Essence"** (*Hán Zhēn*).

*Note: For a year, in all actions—standing, sitting, resting, or sleeping—one must constantly strike the teeth and practice the formulas, which are found in the Palm Diagram. These are named the **Three Supreme Formulas** (Dōujīān, Dōushī, Dàdào). By constantly visualizing the Seven Stars, the Three Officials (of Heaven, Earth, and Man) fear the Seven Stars and dare not linger. They also do not allow the **Three Inches of Vital Essence** (*Sān Cùn*) to determine the Daoist Aspirants’ merits or demerits, virtues or faults. Instead, they report these directly to the Heavenly Emperor. Thus, the Nine Assemblies (of the underworld) have no records, and one’s fate is determined by their merits and demerits, either ascending to Daoist Immortality or being removed from the register of death. There is no killing or injury, no resentment or opposition. Their bodies tread the Daoist Circuit of Heaven and the Earthly Memorial, free from disease and death, firm and unyielding. Their spirits are controlled, their souls are stabilized, and their True Essence is not lost, so it is called the "Stabilized True Essence" (Dìng Zhēn).*

After three years, they attain the **"Earthly True Essence"** (*Dì Zhēn*).

*Note: Daoist Aspirants cultivate the Earthly Memorial (Dì Jì) while also practicing the Heavenly Circuit (Tiān Gāng), never ceasing in their standing, sitting, resting, or sleeping. They combine this with the service of the **Sacred Talismans** (*Líng Fú*), **Six Celestial Stems** (*Liù Jiǎ*), and **Three Sovereigns** (*Sān Huáng*). Such practitioners attain the True Essence within humanity, hence the name "Earthly True Essence" (Dì Xiān Zhēn).*

*Note: As the scriptures describe the Earthly Immortals (Dì Xiān), they only practice the Heavenly Circuit (Tiān Gāng) or solely tread the Earthly Memorial (Dì Jì) to attain the rank of Earthly Immortals. Ghosts, spirits, and malevolent demons cannot harm their bodies. Even their families, plagued by evil spirits and demons, are protected. How much more so can they safeguard others with their talismanic power! In lands of calamity and evil, they become beacons of fortune and virtue. In homes of disaster and misfortune, they transform them into abodes of joy and prosperity. Once their divine power is attained, they must not act recklessly. They should emulate the loyalty and virtue of the **Supreme Sage** (Tàishàng), the **Later Sage Emperor** (Hòushèng Jūn), and the **Second Later Sage Emperor** (Èr Hòushèng Jūn).*」

「Above all, do not lightly divulge this—be cautious.

After five years, one gradually attains divine communion.

At **one-seven years**—
*Note: In the first seven years, one follows the seven stars of the Northern Dipper (Beidou); in the next seven years, one follows the seven stars of the Central Dipper (Zhongdou).*

These two sets of seven stars were, by decree of the **Supreme Dao/Way Emperor of the Later Sage of Taiping Golden Gate (Taiping Jinque Housheng Xuanyuan Yuhuang Shangdaojun)**, sealed and appointed to guard and assist the human body, bearing titles such as [vacant]★, [vacant]★, [vacant]★, [vacant]★, [vacant]★, [vacant]★, [vacant]★—each a rank of Immortal. Those who earnestly receive this will immediately attain the True Immortal.

If a person of superior wisdom discerns these two sets of stars as identical in practice, then in **fourteen years**, they may attain the rank of *Tianzhen* (Heavenly True) and ascend in broad daylight. If an entire household practices together, even the house and its fowl will ascend with them—how much more so the people within.

**Five Dippers should stand guard**—
*Note: The five Dippers refer to one Dipper each in the east, west, south, and north, plus one central Dipper.*

Each of the seven stars, along with the central ten, makes **fifteen Dippers**. Each Dipper has a sovereign, and each of the seven stars has its own name, as recorded in *The Golden Lock* (Jinsuo), Volume Two.

The Later Sage Emperor decreed and sealed the Earthly Memorial (Dì Jì) and Heavenly Gate (Tianque), naming these seven stars [vacant]★, [vacant]★, etc., all as appointed by the Dipper Sovereigns, according to their designated ranks and duties.

For instance, in spring, the Eastern Dipper Sovereign assigns the stars *Jiāo* (角), *Kàng* (亢), *Shì* (氏), *Fáng* (房), *Xīn* (心), *Wěi* (尾), and *Jī* (箕) to stand guard in the Central Dipper, bearing titles [vacant]★, [vacant]★, etc., for the purpose of prohibiting and directing.

In summer, it is the Southern Dipper; in autumn, the Western Dipper; in winter, the Northern Dipper. The four seasonal Dipper Sovereigns oversee the Central Dipper’s appointed stars.

The seven Dippers correspond to the *clothing of the Dipper* (Dòuyī), used to complete the ritual.

Seated in tranquility, with the *Kui* (魁) star facing the Heavenly Circuit (Tiān Gāng), drumming **fifteen beats**.

*Note: The initial seven Dippers’ clothing also contains methods for official ascension, detailed in the previous section. One must first complete the official ascension rites before donning the seven Dippers’ clothing, and the subsequent process follows similarly.*

Only then may one proceed with the incantations and dispel the Five Phases’ great calamities.

Respectfully submitted by the humble servant—
*Note: Then Xuán.*」

「Notes: This pertains only to disciples’ wives, children, and successive descendants—others are ineligible.

Within the body, the **Sanwu Officials** (三五功曹) are established.

As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (《金锁流珠》), Upper Volume, these were originally present but were later expanded in full by the Sage Emperor, hence the red script.

Upon completing the **official ascension (出官)**, one stands immediately. First, hold the **Jingxing Star** (景星) in hand, then raise the left foot and recite:

*"Sanwu raises the foot—action complete!"*

*"Ten Thousand Spirits assent, Sanwu is established, Ten Thousand Spirits unite, Sanwu proceeds, concealing form and shadow, ascending to the Azure Clouds."*

Proceed with the ritual: grip firmly, close the **qi**, and perform the **Tianzhu** (天柱) posture once.

If dispelling calamities and misfortunes, urgently use the left-hand sword grip, perform the **Yubu Steps** (禹步), and recite the **Sanwu Incantations** three times.
*Note: Three recitations of five verses each—swift against water and fire, and the calamity shall dissolve.*

**First Incantation:**
*"I receive the qi of Heaven and Earth, destined to be their envoy."*
*(As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*, Upper Volume, originally taught by the Old Lord.)*

**Second Incantation:**
*Note: Further instructed by the Sage Emperor to the Heavenly Master.*
*"I was born of father and mother."*
*(As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*, Upper Volume.)*

**Third Incantation:**
*Note: The Dao Lord taught the Old Lord, who passed it to Emperor Yu of Xia, who reversed it to form the *Qiankun Incantation* (乾坤祝).*
*"I was born of father and mother."*
*(As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*, Upper Volume.)*

**Fourth Incantation:**»

**Note:** Emperor Yu reversed the third incantation of the Dao Lord, thereby obtaining the four characters *Qian Zun Yao Ling* (乾尊耀灵). Heaven bestowed the *Chengcheng* (成成) blessing to dispel calamity and grant longevity—this method was bestowed upon Yu, who recited and practiced it to attain the Dao.

**Qian Zun Yao Ling.**
*Note:* These four characters were spoken by Yu.

**Reported Note:** The character *Kun* (坤) was derived from the mouth of Heaven.

**Harmonizing the inner cultivation,** the two principles unite in harmony, the six directions bring auspiciousness.
**Aligned with Heaven, enjoying Earth,** eternal peace and purity prevail.
**Responding to the Mysterious Yellow,** the upper garment and lower robe are complete.
**Zhen ascends, Gen thrives,** the unformed achieves clarity, Xun’s ruler brings vitality, the tiger strides and the dragon soars.
**Heaven’s Gate and Earth’s Portal,** where people walk and ghosts move—**those who guard my body are the august and boundless Heaven.**
Today’s Yu Step aligns with Heaven’s decree.
Ghosts and spirits submit as guests; below, all inauspiciousness is repelled.
All requests are fulfilled; ten thousand spirits dare not resist.
**Chìduó!**
*Note:* This is *Xuan* (玄).
One version reads: *"This is I."*

Within my body, the five sufferings, eight hardships, nine calamities, a hundred illnesses, myriad disasters, malevolent men and evil spirits, scheming tongues and slanderous plots, Heaven’s nets and Earth’s cords—all are subdued beneath the *Kui Gang* (魁纲), motionless and inactive.
**Swiftly, as per the newly issued edicts of the Old Lord.**

**Fifth Incantation:**
*Note:* The Yu Step incantation for averting calamity and seeking wishes, to be constantly practiced for longevity.

**Qian Yuan Chong Fu,** Kun Da Hou Zai.
*As recorded in The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl, Upper Volume.*

The Later Sage instructed the Celestial Master:

*"The Five-Headed Incantation—if used merely to dispel calamity, only the third and second incantations need be recited. Then, with the Step of the Halter, you may gather and subdue the calamities. Spirits and humans alike will submit and rest.
*Note:* This includes the first eight incantations in the Step of the Halter.

The Halter is the Northern Dipper’s Female Void, the Central Dipper—reversed three times, and the Yu Step three times, then cease.
*Note:* Also, the *Supporting* technique must be employed.
*Note:* The *Supporting* key.

After three days, the calamity will disperse, and matters will settle—then do not employ the key.

If seeking longevity, then all nine later incantations may be fully used.
*Note:* As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl, Upper Volume.*

Before and after, [the incantations] are uttered in the Hall of Officials. The Celestial Master is invoked.

It is customary to dispel calamities on *jiǎzǐ* days. It is also said: If there is calamity or illness, use it immediately—it is not restricted to *jiǎzǐ*, *huìshuò*, or *gēngshēn* days. Within a month, one day per *xún* is practiced.
*Note:* The Celestial Master practices two days per *xún* for longevity, aligning with the practice of the Central Dipper.

Additionally, on *gēngshēn* days, one’s natal days, and *liùjiǎ* days.
*Note:* *Jiǎzǐ*, *jiǎxū*, *jiǎshēn*, *jiǎwǔ*, *jiǎchén*, and *jiǎyín* days.

Before practice, the Northern Dipper is cultivated, then the Central Dipper. There are separate scriptures for this, found in *The Flowing Pearl, Middle Volume*.
*Note:* *The Golden Lock Scripture, Upper Volume* is in four volumes, while *The Flowing Pearl, Middle Volume* is in five.

This is the *Tàiwéi Heavenly Emperor*, the *Flying Step of the Halter*.
*Note:* The sound of *gāngjì* is used, not the sound of *gāng* (rigid). The original Step of the *Gāng* is this very character.

Yu, in regulating the waters and ascending the mountains, established the rigid Step. Yu did not use it squarely but employed the *Stepping on the Earthly Gāng* technique—this is the character.

The scripture was transmitted by the Later Sage Lord, hence its name, *The Great Elixir Hidden Book*.
Anciently, it was called *Yù Zhù*; the Later Sage Lord renamed it *Liúzhū*, and *Jīnzhù* became *Jīnsuǒ*.
Another name is *The Tàishàng Hidden Book*.
*Note:* Some today do not recognize it."*

The Sixth Diagram of the Northern Dipper *Gāng* depicts seven stars, without auxiliary ministers. Beginning from the first star of the Dipper, the male steps forward with the left foot, reaching the Ox Star with the right foot.
*Note:* This is the name of the Northern Dipper star, one of the Twenty-Eight Constellations.

Next is the Female Star.
*Note:* All movements follow the Dao of Heaven, with the left foot always stepping forward first. The Female Star requires the right foot to step forward first.

Next is the Void, then Danger, then Room, and finally the Wall Star. The seven stars complete a full circuit with a leftward turn of the body.

**Obsequy Ritual:** *"Come to life, depart from death"*—or *"calamity departs, fortune arises."*
*Note:* This is the forward progression.

Again, reverse the steps in a full circuit—beginning from the seventh star toward the first.

**Return Step.**
*Note:* From the first star toward the seventh.

This is then divided into **Yu’s Step to Seek the True**.

Next is **Yu’s Step**—Yu performed the *Heavenly Gāng* and *Earthly Ji*, manifesting it as Yu’s Step to seek the True and restrain all things. Humans, gods, dragons, spirits, ghosts, insects, beasts, venomous serpents, and all monstrous things—all submit and are not slain. Those that resist are destroyed.

Its principle involves combining five Dipper steps into three steps of nine traces, or thirty-five traces. The Great Yu’s Step consists of fifteen traces. These two grades of Yu’s Step are the inner secrets for averting disasters, escaping calamities, and entering the Dao of immortality.
*Note:* Daoists know only of the *Flying Heavenly Gāng* technique but are unaware of the *Earthly Ji* and Yu’s Step. Using only the *Two-Sevens* method for two years without attaining divinity, they criticize it as unspiritual and unholy—a false claim against the scriptures of immortality.

Moreover, the Later Sage Lord clearly revised and demonstrated the *Three-Five Golden Lock Flowing Pearl* text. The three—*One* (元), *Three Steps*, and *Gāng*—contain the secrets. At the moment of stepping, the Five-Colored Silk binds the secrets, held within the palm.

If seeking longevity, pinch the *Sìmìng* (司命) and *Three Officials* targets. For prohibitions, pinch the *certain object* targets. Against enemy armies, pinch the *Heavenly Soldiers* and *Great General* targets, etc.

---
**Golden Lock Flowing Pearl Preface (卷之一)**
*Original Title:* Attributed to the Great True Master of China, Wang Fangping, Zhang Daoling, Zhao Sheng, Wang Chang, Sìmìng Li Zhongfu, Mao Ying, Xu Yufu, etc.—these are fabricated claims and unreliable.

Yet this book’s content is referenced in *The Sacred Traces of the Mixed Primordium*, suggesting it predates the Northern Song. Many annotations are self-attributed as *"Wind-Read"* (风读) and *"Wind-Seen"* (风见), likely linked to Li Chunfeng. The entire work consists of seventy-eight scrolls, detailing step-alignment, Dipper-treading, talisman-holding, incantations, summoning gods and ghosts, fasting and ritual rites, executing calamities, and dispelling illnesses. It synthesizes the techniques of the Celestial Master and Upper Clarity schools into one system, serving as a crucial document for studying pre-Northern Song Daoist practices.

---
**Preface to the *Tàishàng Sānwǔ Tàixuān Jīnzhù Liúzhū* (太玄金箓金锁流珠引序)**
**Sequence by the Daoist Immortal Li Chunfeng**

The *Tàishàng Sānwǔ Tàixuān Jīnzhù* is the transmission from the **Primordial Beginning Heavenly Venerable** to the **Tàishàng Dàdào Jun** (太上大道君), also called the **Highest Holy Tàishàng Yùchén Xuánhuáng Dàdào Jun** (玉晨玄皇大道君).
*Note:* A manifestation of the Primordial Beginning, or said to be a disciple of the Heavenly Venerable, ruling over all Dao.

The **Dàdào Jun** transmitted to the **Zǐqīng Tàisù Gāoxū Dòngyào Sānyuān Shàngdào Jun** (紫清太素高虚洞曜三元上道君), who transmitted to the **Zǐchén Tàiwéi Tiāndì Dàodào Jun** (紫晨太微天帝道君).
*Note:* Also called the *Upper Clarity Most True Dao Venerable*, ruling over the Thirty-Six Heavens.

The **Dàodào Jun** transmitted to the **Zǐmíng Tàiwéi Jiǔdào Gāoyuán Yùchén Dàodào Jun** (紫明太微九道高元玉晨道君), who then transmitted to the **Tàishàng Lǎojūn**.
*Note:* Some say Tàishàng Lǎojūn was a disciple of Tàishàng Dàodào Jun, not a teacher of Tiāndì. It should be the transmission to the *Tàipíng Jīnquè Dìchén Hòushèng Xuányuān Shàngdào Jun* (太平金阙帝晨后圣玄元上道君). This is also a manifestation of Tàishàng Lǎojūn, hence the name *Laozi* (老子) as a reincarnation, teaching the *Flowing Pearl Layered Years* method.

Under **Tiāndì Jun**, the **Yùchén Dàodào Jun** transmitted to the **Zǐyuán Tàiwéi Bāsù Sānyuān Xuánchén Yuánjūn** (紫元太微八素三元玄晨元君), who transmitted to the **Zǐwēi Yuánlíng Guītái Jiǔlíng Tàizhēn Yuánjūn** (紫微元灵龟台九灵太真元君).
*Note:* This ruler instructs those in the world who study the True Dao.

The **Yuánjūn** transmitted to the **Dàlíng Shàngxiāo Féichén Zhōngyáng Huánglǎo Jun** (大灵上霄飞晨中央黄老君), who transmitted to the **Tàiyuán Dōngxiá Bósāng Dānlín Dàdì Shàngdào Jun** (太元东霞搏桑丹林大帝上道君). This Jun resided in Bósāng and transmitted to the Twenty-Four True Ones. The transmission was lost in Central Plains.

The **Zǐchén Tàiwéi Tiāndì Dàodào Jun** transmitted to the **Shàngqīng Tàipíng Jīnquè Dìchén Hòushèng Xuányuān Yùhuáng Shàngdào Jun** (上清太平金阙帝晨后圣玄元玉皇上道君).
*Note:* Also called the *Great Dao Venerable of the Jade Emperor*.

This Jun governs the lower Ten Heavens, oversees the fate of all beings, and communicates with the Upper Clarity. As the Later Sage Lord, the **Forefather Tàishàng Dàodào Jun** was called the *Empty Sovereign* (虚皇), ruling all Dao. The **Later Sage Tàishàng Lǎojūn** was called the *Jade Sovereign* (玉皇), ruling all Dao.

Since the establishment of the **Jīnquè Emperor**, officials and ministers were fully appointed, mirroring the hierarchical duties of mortal rulers. Each has its domain, encompassing the Nine Wilds and all Heavens.

The Jun’s surname is **Li**, given name **Dān**, and courtesy name **Bóyáng**. He renamed the *Golden Lock* as the *Tàixuān Sānwǔ Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Jīngzhù*, formally expounding the essentials of the Dipper Step and Gāng alignment.

The *Jīngzhù* consists of eighty-six chapters and forty-three volumes. Presented to the **Tàishàng Lǎojūn**, also called the **Highest Holy Tàishàng Yùchén Xuánhuáng Dàdào Jun**, who then transmitted it to mortals as the true sovereign and true ministers, wishing to save the Ten Heavens.
*Note:* The Nine Wilds, including the lower celestial realms, are called the Ten Heavens. The world is the Upper Heavenly Daoist Capital, the *Jade Emperor’s Divine Sovereign*.

He compiled a concise fifteen-volume core scripture, along with manuals and diagrams on palm-secrets, discussing the alignment of steps and the treading of *Ji*. Collectively, these are titled the *Golden Lock Great Name*, followed by *Flowing Pearl*, *Flying Step Heavenly Gāng*, and finally *Yu’s Step Earthly Ji*.

The *Jīngzhù* passed twenty volumes to **Emperor Yīn**, who was titled the **Posterior Sage Great Master Left Supreme Minister**.

The **Minister** transmitted them to the **Great True Persons of the Schools**, all of whom assisted the **Posterior Sage**. The **Sage** then transmitted them to the **Posterior Sage Master**—*Note:* this is the **Celestial Master**—the **Left True Guardian of Tàiwēi**, the **Imperial Preserver of the Dao**, who was the **Lord of the Nine Heavens Above the Three Heavens**.

The **Posterior Sage** further transmitted them to the **Nine-Mysteries Supreme True Lord**, the **Jade Gate Supreme Attendant**, the **Grand Marshal of the High Command**, the **Morning Sage Master of the Eastern Sea**, the **Lord of Jade Clarity and Azure Splendor**, the **Young Daoist of the Little Palace**.

*Note:* This title belongs to those who teach and attain the **True Persons**.

For those with the resolve to cultivate it, they may receive the **True Transmission of the Dao** and become ministers of the **Jade Gate Golden Palace**, the **Posterior Sage Jade Emperor**, who eternally descends among the immortals.

The **Posterior Sage Master** then transmitted them to the **Supreme Protector of the Limbs**—*Note:* the **Master** conferred this rank—**Lord of the South Pole Great Cinnabar**, **Purple Primordial Lady**, and her **Purple-Mysteries Consort**, surnamed **Lǐ**, the **Posterior Sage Master’s** third daughter, who once served **Emperor Qīnghé**—*Note:* this is **Fāngpíng**—as a **Young Attendant**.

「For those who are **True Daoists** and attain **True Persons**, the **Posterior Sage Master** appointed the son as the **Prime Minister of the Zhou Mù King**—*Note:* his name was **Zhòngchūn**—serving for only one hundred years. Yet his nature did not align with **Dao/Way** in attaining **virtue/power**, and the **Purple-Mysteries Consort** urged him to practice the **Law of the Treaded Dipper**—*Note:* this refers to the **Flying Steps Technique**—but he did not follow.

The **Posterior Sage Master** then transmitted the **Supreme True Lord of White Mountain**—*Note:* to instruct the same teachings as the **King of the Yellow Emperor**—and further conferred the **Supreme Prime Minister**—*Note:* the **Prime Minister of the Dao** is a rank where the disciple attains the **True Persons** position, akin to the worldly **Chancellor and Prime Minister**.—**True Lord of the South Pole and South Mountain**, surnamed **Zuò**, the **Supreme True Lord of Azure Mystery**.

*Note:* For those who teach and guide disciples to become **True Persons**, they are first petitioned to the **Golden Dipper** and then granted **Dao/Way**, rank, and titles.

The **Supreme True Lord of the South Pole and South Mountain** further transmitted the **Right Minister of the Five Peaks**, surnamed **Tóngbì**, the **True Lord of the Five Peaks**, who assisted the **Posterior Sage Jade Emperor**. The **Posterior Sage Jade Emperor** then bestowed upon **Mystic Territory**—*Note:* also written as **Mystic State**—the **Twenty-Nine True Persons**.

*Note:* These **True Persons** are responsible for petitioning the names of **Daoists** to the heavens. If one’s merit does not meet the standards after three trials, they are first petitioned to the **Posterior Sage Jade Emperor**, who may then grant **Daoist** titles and ranks based on their merit. These **True Persons** oversee the nine realms and myriad lands of the lower world, commanding mountains and waters, and are known by the names of mortals. The **Little Attendant** governs **Qín, Chǔ, and the Southern Seas**; the **Great Attendant** governs **Yān and Qí**; the **Western Spirit Attendant** governs **Sòng, Wèi, Zhèng, and Liáng**. The **Great Attendant** also oversees the **Eastern Seas Administration**.

For those who have attained **virtue/power** in the **Dao/Way** and become **Daoists** or **True Persons** in the various regions, upon being heard by the **Supreme Protector of the Golden Dipper**, the **Posterior Sage Master**, they are commanded to teach and test others. Those who pass are granted **Dao/Way** according to their merit, and those who attain **Daoist** status are granted **True Persons** rank.

Among these three categories, the first rank are those who cultivate their bodies with restraint, act prudently, speak truthfully without deceit, refine their **True Heart**, delight in **Daoist** classics, and recite them to fulfill **virtue/power**. They maintain incense and lamps continuously, healing others’ afflictions. If they encounter the **Six Auspicious Talismans** and practice them over many years, they may even attain **immortality**, becoming **Daoists** among mortals. Further cultivation may lead them to meet a **Daoist Master**, who then grants them this **Scripture and Diagram**, allowing them to practice the **Flying Steps Technique** and thus become **True Persons** and **Daoist Immortals**.

The second rank are those who refine **gold and stone elixirs**, using them as medicines of ultimate **Daoist** attainment to heal others’ illnesses, strengthen their bodies, and regulate their **organs and meridians**—*Note:* **藏** here refers to **organs and meridians**.—They take these elixirs in secluded mountain forests and thus live far beyond the **Ten Thousand Years**, dying not before a hundred years. Even after death, they do not become lower ghosts but are reborn, receiving their original blessings.

The third rank are those who sincerely aspire to the **Dao/Way**, following a **Clear Master** without hesitation, even traveling ten thousand miles. They offer their **heart** and exert their **virtue/power** without sparing effort or labor. Over long years and months, the **Master** will naturally record their **virtue/power** and merit, then teach them this **Scripture**, transmitting it afterward. Those who sincerely cultivate will reap **virtue/power** from their **Master** first and be petitioned to the **Posterior Sage**. Many are then granted **Daoist** titles and ranks, becoming **True Persons**.

These three categories were taught by the **Posterior Sage Master**—*Note:* **Zhang the Daoist Master**—and the **Supreme True Lord of the Golden Dipper**. The **Posterior Sage Master** also instructed the **Purple-Mysteries Left Consort**—*Note:* For those who teach and guide disciples to become **True Persons**, after three successful trials, they are first petitioned to the **Golden Dipper**, granted **Daoist** titles, and conferred as **True Persons**.

The **Posterior Sage Master** further descended to instruct the **Twenty-Four True Persons**, who ascended to the heavens as **Twenty-Four Supreme True Lords of the Left and Right Golden Dippers**. *Note:* These **True Persons** oversee the affairs of all the heavens and earth, the living populace, and determine the merit of those who attain **True Persons** rank, as well as the depth of their cultivation over years and months, petitioning their degrees and commendations.

The **Posterior Sage Master** also appointed the **Supreme True Lord** to oversee trials and conferred upon **Máo Yíng** and **Lǐ Zhòngfǔ**—*Note:* **Máo** and **Lǐ** are **Daoist Masters**—and others as **Lords of Fate**. *Note:* They lead and instruct those who follow the **Dao/Way** to become **True Persons**, testing them. Those who pass are taught accordingly.

**Máo Yíng** instructed his two brothers, **Máo Zǐfǔ** and **Lǐ Zhòngfǔ**, as well as **Yáng Zuǒ**’s six disciples, all of whom were granted the **Scripture** and taught to practice it. Later, all **Daoists** and **True Persons** from the various regions attained their ranks through this **Scripture**.

Some were transmitted by the **Supreme Daoist Lord of the Highest Venerable**, others by the **Supreme Daoist Lord of the Great Prime Minister of the Anterior Sage**, or by the **Posterior Sage Mystic Jade Emperor** through a **divided body transmission**. Some were conferred by the **Supreme Daoist Master of the Posterior Sage**, who served as the **Supreme True Lord**, granting them **ascension to celestial abodes** and elevating their families to immortality as well.

The multitude of **True Persons** and **Daoists** thus attained became countless—some numbering in the hundreds of millions, others seen ascending in broad daylight. Their numbers were so vast that they cannot be recorded one by one.

Now, I shall briefly enumerate them in sequence, using them as introductory titles for those who follow, detailing the transmissions from the **Anterior Sage’s Golden Mouth** and the **Posterior Sage’s Golden Mouth** in the *Golden Talisman, Jade Diagram, Flowing Pearl, and Induction*.

Next, I employ the combined methods of the Anterior and Posterior Sages, arranging the titles according to their prescribed order, dividing each into diagrams, and extracting their essential secrets and inner precepts to guide practitioners into the **Great Dao’s** gate. Those who cultivate and attain it shall, in turn, transmit it to future generations of worthy disciples—those whose hearts and spirits align with **Daoist transcendence**. None may recklessly transmit this to the unworthy.

This **Black Script** was granted by **Laozi**, while the **Red Script** was reaffirmed by the **Posterior Sage Emperor**. The **Celestial Master** received this instruction, and **King Wáng** recorded it, with each detail annotated in the subsequent chapters and paired with the respective scrolls.

**Preface to the *Great Dao’s Three Pure Ones, Golden Lock, and Flowing Pearl Genealogy***

The terms *Golden Lock* originated when **Yǐn Jun** transmitted them to **Wáng Jun**, who then passed on the term *Flowing Pearl*.

**Wáng Jun** asked: *"What is the meaning of *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl*?"*

**Yǐn Jun** replied: *"The **Supreme Venerable Laozi**, upon returning to his **True Emperor** rank, was titled **Highest Pure Emperor of the Golden Threshold, Celestial Master**. When **Wáng Jun** instructed his disciple **Wáng Èr Jūn**—
*(Note: The first Wáng is **Wáng Cháng**, the second is **Wáng Zǐdēng**.)*
—he said: The **Anterior Sage’s Void Emperor, Great Dao Lord** is none other than the **Primordial Supreme Dao Lord**. The **Posterior Sage’s Jade Emperor, Mysterious Origin Supreme Dao Lord**—
*(Note: Also called the **Supreme Great Dao Lord**, corresponding to the Anterior rank.)*
—was renamed from *Golden Talisman* to *Golden Lock*.

Its original intent was to teach the method of **locking the soul and refining the spirit**, seeking life and avoiding death. It spoke of **fortifying the body like gold** and **retaining the spirit like a lock**.
*(Note: Another version says, "Retaining the spirit as a lock, hence *Golden Lock*." This was from the old *Golden Talisman* teachings.)*

When reciting aloud the *Golden Lock*,
*(Note: The name *Golden Lock* signifies the inherent principle of the self, aiding the realm to save others.)*
and when walking in *Golden Halter steps*,
*(Note: Stepping the Heavenly Halter, treading the Earthly Measures.)*
these two terms were bestowed upon later worthies, clarifying their names so that practitioners might attain the **Dao** in their time.

**Wáng Jun** asked again: *"Why is it called *Flowing Pearl*?"*

**Yǐn Jun** replied: *"The *Flowing Pearl* refers to the **Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper**.*
*(Note: Though seven stars are visible, two are unseen, totaling nine.)*
Practitioners, through their cultivation and stepping the Halter, are said to *flow and turn like pearls*.*
*(Note: The nightly rotation of the Dipper encircles the heavens endlessly, like unceasing flowing water, and the stars resemble pearls, hence *Flowing Pearl*.)*
Originally, this was called the *Golden Talisman’s Method*.
*(Note: The old *Golden Talisman* text states, "The Method locks the spirit." These four characters were its opening.)*
The **Posterior Sage Emperor** renamed the *Method* as *Flowing Pearl*, which is now the *Seven-Star Flying Step*, paired with the *Nine-Dipper Robe*, used to subdue evil and rectify inversions.

The **Supreme Venerable Yǐn True Person** transmitted the four characters *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* to the **Posterior Sage Emperor**, pointing to the **Three Pure Ones**—
*(Note: The **Jade Pure, Highest Pure, and Supreme Pure**.)*
—the **Celestial Master** composed the *Three Pure Ones’ Sequence*, **Yǐn True Person** wrote the *Three Pure Ones’ Words*, and **Wáng Jun** sang the *Three Pure Ones’ Song*.
*(Note: All speak of deriving *One* to attain *Three*, *Three* to attain *Five*, *Five* to attain *Seven*, and *Seven* to attain *Nine*—this refers to the three celestial yang numbers, culminating at *Nine*.)*

The **Supreme One** above is **Taiyi**,
*(Note: The One Heaven.)*
while the **Two Principles** below encompass **Earth**.
*(Note: Earth.)*
The **Two Principles** generate the **Four Symbols**, the **Four** generate the **Six**, the **Six** generate the **Eight**, and the **Eight** generate the **Ten**.
*(Note: All originate from the **Dao** and represent the extreme yin numbers.)*

The **Emperor of Jade Pure** is the **Void Emperor, Great Dao Lord**.
*(Note: The title of **Primordial**.)*
The **Middle Emperor of Jade Pure** is the **High Emperor, Supreme Dao Lord**.
*(Note: The title of **Supreme Dao Lord**.)*
The **High Emperor** above is the **Supreme Dao Lord**.
*(Note: The **Supreme Dao Lord**.)*
The **Highest Pure** above and the **Jade Pure** below is the **Jade Emperor**.
*(Note: **Supreme Venerable Laozi**.)*
It is also said: The **Posterior Sage’s Peaceful Emperor**.
The **Supreme Pure** above and the **Highest Pure** below is the **Heavenly Emperor, Taiyi Venerable Sovereign**.
*(Note: The **Taiyi Dao Lord**.)*
It is also said: **Taiyi, the Master of Heaven**, the **Supreme Extremity’s Venerable Sovereign**, called **Heaven**, the **Dao’s Son**.

Those who study the **Dao** must know the **Three Pure Ones’ true sovereigns** to learn from the **Posterior Sage Emperor**, the current **Highest Pure’s sovereign**. The **Supreme Pure’s Taiyi Lord**—
*(Note: The **Heavenly Sovereign**.)*
—is the sovereign.

All petitions must first pass through the **Supreme Pure**, enter the **Highest Pure**, and then be registered with the **Daoist name**.
*(Note: Also, first register in the **Supreme Pure**, then proceed to the **Highest Pure**, submitting the **Golden Seal**.)*

The **Posterior Sage Emperor** instructed the **True Persons**: *"To seek the **True Dao**, one must first practice the **Yǔ Step**, which is the **Heavenly Halter**.*
*(Note: *Yǔ* means *garment*. Originally the character for *feather*. This is the correct pronunciation. Because **Yǔ** of the Xia Dynasty mastered water control, he encountered this **Heavenly Halter Step Method**. After four years of cultivation, he attained the **Dao**, commanding dragons, tigers, and spirits to dredge rivers and regulate the waters, earning merit. Later, he became a **Sage and True Person**, and his name was changed to *Yǔ*. After fulfilling his earthly merit, thirty years later, he ascended in flesh. **Yǔ** is now the **Supreme Extremity True Person**, whom the ministers occasionally see. His sister also departed. His robes and cap were buried at **Kuàijī Mountain**, where a temple remains in his honor. His name may be inscribed among the **Three Pure Ones**.)*

If one walks the **Heavenly Halter in emptiness** but does not know the **Yǔ Step’s Method**, they cannot ascend to the **Three Pure Ones**, nor will their names be recorded there. The **Underworld** will not register them, and the **Celestial Bureaus** will have no record of them.
*(Note: Though humans are born of Heaven, they are nurtured by Earth. Life and death are decreed by Heaven, but merit and vice depend on Earth. The enlightened of Earth must first be subdued.)*

「Thus, the **Heavenly Halter** is mastered by subduing the **Earthly Halter**, and the **Yǔ Step** is achieved by following the **Heavenly Halter’s Method**. The spirit and vitality are thereby tamed.

Those who do not know this Dao cannot pay homage to the **Three Pure Ones**. The original *Sutra of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*—which originates from **Great Dao Lord of Jade Purity**—was initially named *The Inner Canon of Golden Talisman and Jade Talisman*.
*(Note: The Celestial Sovereign named it *The Golden Talisman and Jade Talisman*.)*

Later sages renamed it *The Golden Lock Sutra* and *The Flowing Pearl Sutra*, thus passing it down. This is the second scroll of *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*.

The **Great Sovereign of Total Perfection, Zhāng Dàolíng, Zhào Shēng, Wáng Cháng, Lǐ Zhòngfǔ, Máo Yíng, Xǔ Yùfǔ**, and others are successive authors who compiled it. **Li Chūnfēng**, the Daoist sage, annotated it.

**The Diagram of Three Steps and Nine Traces**
This diagram was taught by **Laozi** to **Yǔ**; it depicts the **Yǔ Step** of three steps and nine traces.
*(Note: **Yǔ** first tamed the **Earthly Halter**, completing the three matters of **advancing, retreating, and reversing**, then proceeded with the two feet.)*

Whether the **Yǔ Step** is large or small, the two matters (advancing and retreating) are unnecessary if one wishes to **ascend to the Pole Star**. Simply follow the diagram’s prescribed method.

The **Yǔ Step** (right and left) is used to seek longevity and avert calamities. Later sages instructed the **Celestial Master**, initially teaching the **Heavenly Halter’s Method**, then refining it into the **Nine Traces**. This also aligns with **Pole Star numerology**.

The three matters of **advancing, retreating, and reversing** are completed in three rounds.
*(Note: Three rounds of the **Heavenly Halter** are inferior to the **Three Halters and Three Degrees**—the **Yǔ Step** must be performed right and left in three rounds.)*

If one desires swift results and effective practice, they should perform three steps of the **Heavenly Halter’s Method**, advancing and retreating once each. Boys advance left, girls advance right.
*(Note: After completing right and left, one more round must be done—totaling three.)*

This is the successive **advancing, retreating, and reversing** in three rounds.

If one wishes to **subdue malevolence and deploy martial methods**, or fears calamities, they should practice the **Yǔ Step of the Twenty-Eight Constellations**.

After completing the **Heavenly Halter** in one hundred steps, within thirty-five days, its efficacy may be tested by **water and fire**.
*(Note: According to **Laozi’s** initial instruction to **Yǔ**, the **Pole Star Method** was perfected later, and only the **Yǔ Step** remains. The **Twenty-Eight Constellations** were later taught to **Wáng Jūn**.)

Begin with the **Northern Pole**, then proceed to the **Eastern Pole**, the **Southern Pole**, and the **Western Pole**, finally ascending to the **Central Pole** without stepping on the **True Person Star**.

Treading the **Northern Pole** seeks the **Law of the Pole**, reciting the **Deciphering of Jiazi**. The **Eastern Pole** recites the **Deciphering of Jia-yin**, the **Southern Pole** the **Deciphering of Jia-wu**, the **Western Pole** the **Deciphering of Jia-shēn**, and the **Central Pole** the **Decipherings of Jia-xū and Jia-chén**. These are the **Pole Star Decipherings** corresponding to their directions.

For longevity practice, mark the **Deciphering of the Life Officer** with red ink, or bind it with five-colored silk threads, then perform the **Heavenly Halter**. After three years, one attains **Earthly True Personhood**, reaching the point where the **Life Officer** descends to remove one’s name from the **Register of the Dead**.
*(Note: Those born under Jiazi and similar **Metal** signs use **Ding-sì (丙午、丁巳)** as the **Life Officer**. Wood-born individuals use **Gēng-shēn and Xīn-xǔ (庚申、辛酉)**; water-born use **Wù-chén and Jǐ-wèi (戊辰、己未)**; fire-born use **Rén-zǐ and Guǐ-hài (壬子、癸亥)**; earth-born use **Jiā-yín and Yǐ-mǎo (甲寅、乙卯)**. These are used in practice.)*

In all three grades of this **Heavenly Halter** practice, one must recite the **Nine Post-Step Invocations** afterward.
*(Note: After the invocation, retain the **Twenty-Eight Constellations** in the body as per the diagram. The diagram is found in *The Third Central Element Diagram of the Golden Lock*.)*

The **Twelve Post-Step Invocations** are incorporated into the three pre-existing ones, and their names must also be recited.

First, after one step and one round, invoke:
*"In days of old, I received instruction from the **Mysterious Sage**,
who taught me the **Heavenly Halter’s Method**—
all my requests are fulfilled.
Thus it is spoken."*

After one round of the **Heavenly Halter**, *(Note: Invoke while stepping on the **Pole Star**.)*
invoke:
*"The **Five Phases** mutually generate.
Thus it is spoken."*

After two rounds of the **Heavenly Halter**, *(Note: Invoke after two rounds of the **Pole Star**.)*
invoke:
*"The **Five Phases** mutually generate.
Thus it is spoken."*

Then recite the **Heavenly Key Deciphering**, briefly.

Fourth, three steps toward **Kui**, one round of the **Earthly Halter**. *(Note: Three rounds of stepping, performed in reverse.)*
Invoke:
*"In days of old, I received instruction from the **Mysterious Sage**,
who taught me to tread the **Earthly Halter** and master the **Heavenly Halter**.
Thus it is spoken."*

Recite the **Decipherings of the Grand Prohibition and Grand Sage**.

Fifth, three steps toward **Kui**, one round of the **Earthly Halter**. *(Note: In the third round of stepping, advance from the **seventh star** toward **Kui Star**.)*
Invoke:
*"The **Three Five** form the **Weft**,
within which the **Thread** is named **Qi**.
Thus it is spoken."*

*(Note: **Disaster points**—for **Metal-born**, disaster lies in **Fire**.)*

Sixth, one round toward **Kui**, piercing and subduing malevolence, **souls and ghosts**. The calamities of the **Five Phases** will return to strike the one who summoned them.
*(Note: **Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth**—**Metal** always fears **Fire** as **ghost**, hence the **Heavenly Halter** subdues **Fire** and seeks **Earth** as the remedy, turning misfortune into fortune.)*

Invoke using the **Five Phases Invocation**:
*"The **Five Phases** mutually generate;
the **Heavenly Halter** holds supreme authority.
Thus it is spoken."*

Recite the **Ghost Deciphering**.
*(Note: After the invocation, add *"Today, I tread **Kui**—all matters are auspicious."* The piercing follows the diagram: **soul above, ghost below**.)*

*(Note: This is the **subduing of malevolence**; do not practice recklessly. If practicing for longevity, perform it as **Three Elements**.)*
*(Note: **Heaven, Earth, Water**. The **Five Phases** below are **Wood, Metal, Water, Fire, Earth**—those that harm my body must be countered through the **Heavenly Halter** and **Earthly Halter**.)*

*(Note: Even if calamities manifest in sound alone without physical form, one can endure them and attain eternal longevity.)*

The remaining invocations and piercings are all explained similarly.

For the **left foot**, step on the **□ Star** to pierce **ghosts**; the **left foot** again advances in **Ding** sequence, retaining the posture as if seated toward the **□ Star**, advancing to the **□** to pierce malevolence.
*(Note: Recite the **Ghost and Malevolence Deciphering** and the **Force Support Deciphering**. Below, strike with the **left fist** as if weighing fifteen *jīn*. Above, use the **right hand**.)*
*(Note: Follow the upper method.)*

**Seventh [Step]:**
When passing through **Wuqi**, pierce, step, and invoke—beginning from the **first star** and the **second star** of the **Gang**.
*(Note: With the **left hand’s sword**, pierce the malevolent influences of the Five Phases clashing against you to dispel calamity. Then ascend to the **fourth star**, seize the malevolence, and strike with **seven fists**.)
*(Note: Each fist weighs **fifteen *jīn***.)*
Recite the invocation:
*"The Five Phases push the Gang,
Holding supreme authority over the Six *Ji*."*
*(And so forth.)*
Twist the **Five Phases’ palace** to nurture my body, along with the **Two Decipherings of the Marshal of Destiny**—this brings auspiciousness.
Use the **Entry of the Army** only to aid others and the state; store the remaining strikes, and do not act recklessly. Even minor malevolence or evil spirits must not be trodden upon with **Heavenly Mechanics**.

**Eighth [Step]:**
Pass through **Gang** once, step on **Ji**, and pierce—retracing from the **seventh star** to the **□ third star**, seizing the **Heavenly Killer** and malevolent ghosts that are incompatible with my body.
With the **left fist** and **right stomp**, each stomp weighs **twenty-five *jīn***. Nine fists, ten stomps.
Stomp with the foot and recite:
*"The Five Phases push the Gang,
Holding supreme authority over the Six *Ji*."*
*(And so forth.)*
Twist the **third fingernail of the left hand** to subdue the **Three Officials’ Heavenly Killer ghosts**.

**Ninth [Step]:**
Pass through **Gang** once, step on **Ji**, and pierce—with the **left hand holding the sword** and the **right hand grasping the head**, pierce the **three corpses** of malevolent ghosts plotting to kill me.
The **Yǔ Step** may be retained to seize and pierce them. After **nine passes**, strike with the **left knee** seven times, then behead them.
Recite:
*"The Five Phases follow in sequence,
The rigid first in wrath."*
*(And so forth.)*

Twist the **Heavenly Ghost’s Eye**:
With the **left hand’s fourth finger**, at the **second joint’s right side** (the irregular node—only the right side counts).
If subduing a **malevolent soul**, proceed likewise.
Then **pierce three times**, strike **three times**, and cease.
*Note: If resistance is met, act as you will.*

**Tenth [Step]:**
With the **left foot**, step upon **Gang** to its head, then step **Ji** left and right.
*Note: Both the Ninth and Tenth Steps must step upon Ji.*
In the Ninth, the **right foot** steps upon **Ji** (the second star).
In the Tenth, the **left foot** steps upon the **fourth star**.
To dispel **heavenly and earthly disasters**, and **malevolent ghosts**, step with the **left foot** upon the **first star**, reaching **Gang’s head** and sitting upon the **sixth star**.
If the ghost lies within **Gang**, pierce it within the **first star**.
**Nine left thrusts**, **ten right thrusts**.
Recite:
*"The Five Phases push in sequence."*
*(And so forth.)*
Twist the **ghost’s eye** at its **true center**—
the **left hand’s fourth finger, second joint**.

This method first **dispels slander**, faster than water or fire.

**Eleventh [Step]:**
With the **right foot**, step upon **Gang** to its head, then **pierce left and right**.
Step **Ji** and return, turn to face **west**, and tread upon **Kui Star** to **Gang’s head**.
With the **left hand**, grasp the **head of malevolent, evil essence**, and strike **ten times** with the **right fist**.
*Note: Each strike weighs **fifteen *jīn***.*
Recite:
*"Five times entrusted within the Three-Five."*
*(And so forth.)*
**Secret Technique:** Bind the **first joint of the left hand’s fourth finger**.

If practicing the **Yǔ Step** upon this **Gang** for **three years**, then using **talismans** to treat **malevolent diseases** across the land, the **evil ghosts** will be bound by the talisman officers, executed, and the afflicted will recover instantly.
*Note: If pursuing them, point remotely in their direction, or point and affix a talisman to a shrine to compel their arrival.*

**Twelfth [Step]:**

---

**Note:** Walk from **Kui’s** wrapped form to **Gang’s head**, with the **left foot** ascending **Tian Guan** upon the **Red Elixir** (Dan Yuan), then turn **right** toward **Gang**, and **left** upon **Ji**, returning to **Kui’s left** **Yangming**. Strike back and forth.
This step is used to **collect misfortune** from the **Five Phases** that are not favorable to my fate, and to **subdue** the **malevolent, evil essence** of the **Three Officials** of Heaven, Earth, and Water.

With the **right hand** held inverted and suspended, the **left hand** formed into a fist, strike **fifteen times**.
*Note: Each strike weighs **fifteen *jīn***.*
After striking, **bury the ghost** beneath the **Heaven Bridge**.
*Note: The **Heaven Bridge Star** is located to the **northwest**.*
Recite:
*"The Five Phases repel one another—Metal subdues Wood, Water extinguishes Fire."*
*(And so forth.)*

The **Secret Technique** for **subduing ghosts** and **supporting the Ghost-Slaying Palm Diagram** is found in the *Liu Zhu (Flowing Pearl) Palm Diagram*.
This **incantation** and the **previous eleven incantations** are highly effective in eliminating **household and national Daoist calamities** (家国祆祟), as well as **diseases, misfortunes, and afflictions** that must be dispelled.
Begin with the **initial sacrifice**, announcing to all directions, first reciting the **Five Incantations**, then the **Twelfth Incantation**, and declare:
*"(Now) self-destruction and removal of misfortune shall be accomplished."*
*Note: It is essential to **tread upon the Three Platforms and Five Stars**, each **three times** (遍), to ensure no harm can befall any matter—then proclaim success.*

**Initial Declaration:** Having finished the **Kui’s head** striking and incantation, proclaim success, facing **east**, and beat the drum **twelve times**.
*Note: The text may also be read aloud; it is not necessary to recite it verbally.*
I, **Zhu Xuanjin**, humbly request the **Celestial Master** and **Female Celestial Master**.

*(And so forth.)*
The text is recorded in the *Liu Zhu (Flowing Pearl)* **upper scroll**, **second section**.

This method was later passed down by **sagely teachings** to the **Celestial Master**, who transmitted it through the **Han dynasty** lineage.
When practiced:
- **One year** subdues **ten thousand demons**,
- **Two years** instills fear in **ten thousand soldiers**,
- **Three years** grants **longevity**,
And **ten thousand ghosts and spirits** of the land will all **submit as guests** and be **bound in servitude**.
*Note: Some practice it in tandem, reaching as far as **fourteen years**.*
*Note: Others perform this method for **three to four years**, and after **verifying spiritual communion**, cease it, only continuing the **Heavenly Gang** (飞天纲).*
To **eliminate calamities**, **command the spirits**, and **urgently dispatch them** like water or fire:
In ancient times, **Master Wang Junchang** practiced it in tandem for **ten years**, then ascended to **Heavenly Truth** (天真).
If one **misses the Heavenly Gang** or **treads upon the Earthly Ji**, the method will **never succeed**.
One must first receive the **Earthly Ji**, then follow the method **until the Heavenly Gang**.
**Nine sessions** of **three days and three nights** must be performed before **completing the cycle**.
*Note: This method is not transmitted to mortals.*
If this text is to be transmitted, the **master** must first **test** the disciple, subjecting them to **anger, foul *qi*, and insults** (嗔炁色恶言骂辱).
Only if the disciple remains **unmoved in spirit and demeanor** may the **master** pass it on and allow the text to be **copied and written**.

---
**Gold Lock Flowing Pearl (Jin Suo Liu Zhu) Introduction, Second Section**
**Gold Lock Flowing Pearl (Jin Suo Liu Zhu) Introduction, Third Section**

The **Great Perfected Master of the Central Realm**, **Zai Wang Fangping**, **Zhang Daoling**, **Zhao Sheng**, **Wang Chang**, **Sisheng**, **Li Zhongfu**, **Mao Ying**, **Xu Yufu**, and others of successive generations compiled this text.
The **Daoist Immortal Li Chunfeng** annotated it.

**The Initial Reception of the Three-Five Methods**
When a **vow-holder** receives the **Dao-scriptures**, they first receive the **Three-Five methods**.
Not yet comprehending their principles, they distinguish the **Three Elements**—**Upper, Middle, and Lower**.

*Note: The Three Elements refer to the Upper, Middle, and Lower Trigrams.*
The **Ancient Sage Laozi** called it **Taiyi**—
*Note: Derived from the *Tai Xuan*, hence "Taiyi."*
The **True Receivers of the Taiji** received it from **Laozi, the Most High**. They divided the **symbols** and **broken seals**, swearing an oath to the **Two Heavens**.

The **master and disciple** awaited each other within the **altar hall**. One by one, they invoked the **generals’ names** and transmitted the **Dao-scriptures** to the disciple, who received them in response. After receiving, they must not act recklessly.

The **Elemental Command** required piercing the hand to draw blood, which was mixed with water. The **master and disciple** drank it as an oath.
They bound their hair into **knots**, tied **girdles** as vows, and swore not to betray the **Way of the master and friends**, nor to betray the **Three Officials**.
If they violated this, their **bodies would be examined**, and the **Record-Keepers and Soldiers** would first sit in judgment of their crimes—how could one not be cautious?
Thus, they took oaths to **preserve their bodies**.

This is the **method of the Dao-scriptures**.

This text originally had **1,790 volumes**, named **Taiyi** (Great Unity), called the **Heavenly Teachings**. The threefold method is called the **Three Officials' Dao-scriptures**, and the fivefold method is called the **Five Phases Dao-scriptures**. Their three-and-fivefold methods are divided into **upper, middle, and lower** grades of practice.

The **Dao/Way of Cultivation** section is the **upper grade**. The **Heavenly and Human Beings** practice the **middle grade**, while the **Immortal Ones of the World** cultivate the **lower grade**. Thus, through the **Three Officials' Dao-scriptures**, one ascends from **lower-grade True Immortals** to **middle-grade Daoists**, then to **upper-grade Heavenly Immortals**.
