The common folk dwell in the **lower realm**, so they first receive the **lower-grade Dao-scriptures** of True Immortals, and their cultivation progresses toward the middle and upper grades. This book completes the **upper extreme** of the upper grade, the **middle extreme** of the middle grade, and the **lower extreme** of the lower grade, and is titled *The Inner Canon of Taiyi’s Three-Five Golden Dao-scriptures and Jade Dao-scriptures*.

**Note:** Later sages revised this to the **Zhengyi Dao-scriptures**, naming it *The Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl*.

Later sages, when transmitting the **Zhengyi True Person**, **Note:** This refers to **Zhang the Dao-Master**, titled **Zhengyi True Person**. Then, based on the name of the **Three-Five**, established the **Zhengyi** title. The threefold refers to the **Three Officials**, and the fivefold refers to the **Five Phases**.

The **essence of Heaven and Earth**, also the **Five Spirits** of humankind.
**Note:** The Five Phases manifest in Heaven as the **Five Stars**, on Earth as the **Five Sacred Peaks**, and in humans as the **Five Zang Organs**. If one can **calm the mind and stabilize** the **Five Zang Organs**, the **Five Phases’ divine essences** will always be present, and the **Sacred Furnace** will never fail or decay. This is the **True Person’s eternal life and deathlessness**, called the **Five Spirits**.

Those who master the **Three-Five Dao-scriptures** attain **eternal life**. This is the **Zhengyi Dao-scripture**, originally **1,790 volumes** with **3,624 stages**, later classified by the sages as the **Three Officials' section**. The **upper grade** is named **Upper Official**, overseeing Heaven.
**Note:** This should be the **upper-grade Great Truth, Great Spirit, Great Immortal** multitudes, all with Dao-scriptures and officials overseeing them. Three **Great Generals’ Dao-scriptures** are placed, leading **1,360 stages** of Dao-scriptures.
**Note:** **224 stages** are transmitted to the **lower Earthly Caverns**, with **120 stages** manifesting in the world. Those in the world who attain these will all hold **heavenly and immortal official ranks**, becoming **eternally living True Persons**. If they lack or fall short, they will not attain eternal life.

The **Middle Official** oversees humanity, also with three **Great Generals**, leading **1,000 stages** of Dao-scriptures.
**Note:** **560 stages** are transmitted to the **lower Earthly Caverns**, with **248 stages** manifesting among humanity. Those in the world who attain these will all hold **True Official ranks**. If they lack or fall short for long, they will not be **transmitted into the world**.

The **Lower Official** oversees Earth and Water, also with three **Great Generals**, leading **1,152 stages** of Dao-scriptures.
**Note:** **872 stages**. Transmitted to the **lower Earthly Caverns**, with **550 stages** manifesting among humanity. Those in the world who attain these will all hold **Earthly Immortal ranks**. If they lack or fall short, they will not attain **prolonged lifespan** or **transformation into noble families**.

These are divided into the **Three Officials’ section**, with the **Three Officials’ Generals** guarding internally, **nurturing the body and saving lives**. The **Three Officials** oversee externally, **expelling demons and commanding spirits**, **restraining and guiding people**. All are under the authority of the **Three Officials and Five Stars**, all kept secret in the **upper heavens**.

The **Zhengyi Dao-scriptures** total **3,624 stages**. Those in the lower realm who know of their existence may also enter the ranks of **eternally living persons**. How much more so for those who receive transmission and retain or manifest the stages in the world, who become **Daoists**. Beyond ten years of practice, they ascend in broad daylight to the **True Heaven**.

Later sages again declare: Those in the world who practice and attain the **upper-grade stages** hold **Heavenly Immortal ranks**, those who attain the **middle-grade stages** hold **Immortal ranks among humanity**, and those who attain the **lower-grade stages** hold **Earthly Immortal ranks**. Those who attain all three grades will hold **Heavenly Immortal official ranks**, the **True Person’s station**, and upon fulfilling their merit, ascend in broad daylight.

If one encounters a **non-Daoist**, whatever is seen or heard must be answered with **falsehoods**—but one must **not speak**, only respond with other words. This is called the **Golden Lock**. Thus, the **original Dao of Heavenly and Human Immortals** was revised, naming it *The Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl*.

The **Three-Five Dao-scriptures** are the **foundational teachings** for initial reception.
**Note:** The **Taiyi** refers to the original **Upper Clarity Taiuan Dao-scriptures**.

The **Dao/Laozi** took the name **Taiyi Dao-scriptures**, establishing three grades. The **Zhengyi Later Sage** again declares: **Zheng** means **rectifying the heart**.

The **One** refers to the **unification of the Dao**. **Note:** Master Lu’s interpretation: *Rectify the heart, take the Dao from its Oneness*—the Dao’s nature is free from bias, surpassing even rectitude of heart.

If one can **embrace uprightness in resolve and conduct**, without generating **two or three** (i.e., duality or deviation), then the Dao will never leave the **rectified heart-nature**. Hence the scripture states: *"The Dao generates the One."*

The name **Zhengyi** encompasses the **Three-Five** divisions. **Note:** The **Upper Division** is the **Upper Clarity** (Taiqing); the **Middle Division** is the **Middle Clarity** (Zhongyuan); the **Lower Division** is the **Lower Clarity** (Xianyuan), following the **Five Adaptations**. The **Upper Division** speaks of **Upper Clarity**, the **Middle Division** of **Zhengyi**, **Note:** *Zhengyi* addresses matters of the **human body**, hence it is placed in the **Middle Clarity** of the **Middle Division**. The *Lingbao Wufu* and *Wuyue Zhenxing Tu* discuss the **laws of the Earthly realm**, thus they belong to the **Lower Clarity** of the **Lower Division**.

The **Lower Division** speaks of the **Five Laws**. At the time when the **Later Sage** transmitted his teachings, there were **three divisions** entrusted to **Grandmaster Fang Ping**, numbered **256**, called the **Three Clarities** (*Sanyuan*), and the **Three Clarities Ritual** (*Sanyuan zhai*) was established. **Note:** *This transmission occurred on the fifteenth day of the first month of the fourth year of King Zhao of Qin’s reign.*

The **Master of the Reed** (Maojun) rejoiced at this time, and together with **70 volumes**, ascended as an **Immortal**—the **Grandmaster** became a **True Person** (*Zhenren*) alone. The teachings were divided into the **Three Clarities Dao-scriptures**, **Note:** *The 'laws' (*fa*) refer to scriptures, without the historical records of Generals Shishi and Bingjun or the names of gods and Immortals. The 'Dao-scriptures' (*lu*) are the Heavenly Talismans, inscribed with Heaven’s writings, commanding Heaven’s spirits; the talismans are written in bold, crimson script, their forms vivid and striking. Above, they rectify Heaven; in the middle, they rectify humans and subdue spirits; below, they constrain and govern the *qi* of earthly waters, dragons, ghosts, and rebellious demons, compelling them to return to the **True Dao**.*—thus named **Heaven, Earth, and Human**.

The **Upper Clarity** constrains Heaven, transmitting **Upper Clarity Dao-scriptures**. **Note:** *The Upper Clarity scriptures, laws, and Dao-scriptures all belong to the Upper Clarity division, with 360 stages of form and shadow.*

The **Middle Clarity** subdues spirits and aids humans, extending to **healing diseases and assisting the nation**.

The **Lower Clarity** governs the **Earthly Waters Dao-scriptures**, commanding the *qi* of earthly waters, gods, ghosts, and rebellious demons, using them to **protect people and repel calamities**—this is the application of the **Lower Clarity laws**.

The **Later Sage** declared: The **Upper Clarity laws** are overseen by the **Heavenly Officials**, the **Middle Clarity laws** by the **Human Body Middle Immortal Spirit Officials**, and the **Lower Clarity laws** by the **Earthly Waters Middle Immortal Spirit Officials**. Each has its **commanding generals and soldiers**, to constrain the spirits and gods of the **Three Clarities**, ensuring they do not harm **humans and Heaven**. Thus, the **Supreme Sage** established the **Three-Five Dao-scriptures and diagrams** of **Zhengyi**.

**Note:** *Zhengyi means rectifying the heart and taking the Dao, without any duality or deviation, hence the name Zhengyi.*

The **Later Sage**, seeing that the **great Dao’s gateways** were becoming numerous, feared that later disciples might be confused in their **initial resolve**, and lose their **true nature**. Thus, he petitioned the **Supreme Dao/Way Lord** before him, requesting a change of the names of the **Golden Dao-scriptures** and **Jade Dao-scriptures**, to instruct the **lower realms’ people**—those who **unified their hearts in reverence and faith**, entering a **single gateway** for **precise cultivation**, would then **attain the Dao** and be named **Zhengyi**.

This law is **one-way in rectifying the heart**, seeking **cultivation of the utmost truth**, not through **deviant perceptions** that confuse the resolve, but by **meritorious deeds** to attain the Dao. It is **not about abandoning wives and children**, nor **refraining from grains and dwelling in mountains**, nor **abandoning office and secluding oneself**—only later does one **ascend the Dao**.

The **Later Sage** served as **Prime Minister three times**, and for **750 years** under the **Yin and Zhou dynasties**, attending to **64 Heavenly Sovereigns**, before ascending as the **Supreme Clarity Emperor of the Golden Gate** and **Later Sage Lord of Jade Sovereignty**, **Upper Dao Lord** (*Xuan Yuan Yu Huang Shang Dao Jun*). Could he have attained this through **mountain forests**, abandoning wives and children, refraining from grains, or secluding himself from the world?

The **gateways for initial reception and cultivation** are detailed in the previous notes.

The **Initial Reception of the Upper Clarity Dao** proceeds thus:

The **Venerable Lord Lao** speaks:
*"The Upper Clarity Dao is the supreme, most exalted, most true, and most sacred Dao of the **Great Dao Lord of Inner Jade Talismans and Golden Talismans** within the **Uppermost Clarity**. It governs the **Uppermost Clarity’s Supreme Lords, Ancestral Masters of the Dao, Celestial Emperors, Great Gods, True Officials of the Upper Immortals, High Spirit Generals, Soldiers, and Clerks**—countless billions of hosts—all as **commanders under the Upper Clarity’s scriptures, laws, and talismans**.*

At the time of **initial reception**, one must **fast and purify oneself for seven days**, solemnly pledging allegiance to **Heaven, Earth, the Sun, Moon, and Starry Hosts**. Upon completion, one must **seek another Daoist** to **report to one’s sponsoring master**, requesting that they **guard one’s body and mind**, **preserve one’s upright resolve**, and **devoutly emulate the Great Dao**, even if it means **traveling ten thousand *li* to seek a teacher**—
*Note: If the teacher is nearby, one may simply say, ‘I carry my satchel to seek a teacher.’*

One humbly beseeches the **Venerable Teacher** to **mercifully accept and guide** this disciple, stating:
‘I now enter beneath the **door of the Venerable Teacher**, to receive the **Upper Clarity Jade Talismans**—thus and so.’

Through **twenty-four stages** or **thirty-six stages**, one may receive the **favor of transmission**. Should one **betray this oath**, the **Seven Ancestors** will bear witness.

Should one **disrespect the teacher or betray the Dao**, one’s life will be forfeit to the **Three Officials**, with no regret in death.

This is my **solemn declaration**; I dare not presume further. I bow twice.
*Note: If permitted, one must then, in the **Transmission Rites**, formally submit these words and follow the teacher’s instructions as broken down. If unable to discern something, one must **bow and request clarification**, stating, ‘This matter is beyond my understanding.’ If the teacher grants it, one must **establish an altar for three days and nights**, declaring to the **Ten Directions**, petitioning the **Supreme Dao Lord, Supreme Venerable Lord Lao, the Emperor of Golden Gate Supreme Peace, the Later Sage Lord of Jade Sovereignty, and the Three Sacred Celestial Sovereigns**—all with **yellow tablets bearing red script**. Only after this **report is received** may one **begin the transmission**, following the prescribed rites.

**Initial Reception** consists of **three**—
*Note: The Three Elements (Upper, Middle, Lower).*
**and five**—
*Note: The Five Stars, Five Spirits, Five Phases, Five Tones, Five Forms, Five Viscera, Five Fingers, Five Heads, Five *qi*s.*
As the *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Scripture* states:
‘In Heaven, they are the **Five Stars**; in the Dao, they are the **Five Spirits**; in the numinous, they are the **Five Phases**; in music, they are the **Five Tones**; on Earth, they are the **Five Peaks**; in humans, they are the **Five Viscera**; in the hand, they are the **Five Fingers**; in the law, they are the **Five Heads**; in prohibitive arts, they are the **Five *qi*s**—thus, they are **three times five, fifteen in total**.’
Human **life and destiny** belong to these **Five Phases**.

The **Later Sage Lord** instructed **Emperor Yin’s True Person** on the **oral transmission**:
‘Those who know to receive the **three and five** each have their **merits**; follow the teacher’s guidance in reception.’

If the **aspirant depends on the teacher** and the teacher **does not violate the rites**, and if the **transmission of the law and talismans is properly conferred**, then such resolve **will surely attain the Dao**.
The Scripture says:
‘The **Supreme Dao is the teacher**; the **aspirant seeks the Dao**. Having received the **three elements to their utmost**, one endures for **a hundred *kalpas** and lives eternally.’

Upon completion, the **Five Stars reappear**, granting **longevity, immortality, world-transcendence, and ascension**—this is the **Upper Clarity Law**.

If the **Law resides in another land**, one must **go to that land**.
*Note: The Scripture says: ‘A **clear teacher and supreme law** may be in distant lands. If one seeks to receive it, one must not **beg the teacher to come**, for even if they do, it is **not the true law**. If there is a **royal command** that one cannot refuse, then one may **properly invite them**. The invitation must not violate the **ritual statutes**.’*

If the **Law is on the **Sacred Mountain**, one must **go to the Sacred Mountain**.
*Note: The **Later Sage Lord** told the **Later Sage Grand Marshal**:
‘Your **rank is noble yet humble**; you cannot attain the Dao. I have prepared your **body** for this. If the Dao is in the **mountains**, you must **depend on the mountain** to receive it. If the Dao is in the **city**, you must **depend on the city** to receive it. If the Dao is with a **lowly, vulgar person**, you must still **follow their instruction** in reception. **Do not disrespect the teacher or belittle the Dao**. Even if your words seem slight, you will **lose your human form** and become a **lower ghost**, never regaining humanity. Even if you are the wife of a **frivolous, lowly man**, yet you possess **virtue and power**, and you **kneel before him as a disciple**, how could you suddenly **mock him with words**, blame yourself, and call him a **foolish youth**, ignorant of a **common, vulgar woman**, yet receive the **three and five** and the **Upper Clarity Law**? Your regret would be profound. Do you not recall these words?’

The **Grand Marshal** replied:
‘I **inquired of a foolish, vulgar person** and **laughed at the teacher**, acting with **frivolous disrespect**. Now that I have attained the **position of Upper True Person** and am called **Heaven’s Noble Lady**, I **mocked the utterly foolish and vulgar**, with **no wisdom or recognition**—a **deadly sin**. I humbly pray that the **Celestial Sovereign and Great Dao’s power** take pity, and I **beg to know what rites or offerings** I may make to **atonement**.’

The **Later Sage Lord** spoke again:
‘You need only **wear the three-and-five talismans**, **repent on your natal day**, and **apologize for your words**. You must also **repent on *jiazi* days** and within **two years**, you shall **attain the Dao**.’
The Grand Marshal **followed these instructions**, and two years later, the **Later Sage Lord** summoned him as the **Grand Marshal of the Southern Palace**, overseeing the **ten heavens’ union for ascension**. **Do not belittle the Dao of the teacher!**

The **Later Sage Lord** again instructed **Emperor Yin’s True Person**:
‘Even a **common teacher** has their **principles**; one must **not speak ill of them**. How much more so if the teacher **has Daoic resolve**—one must **never speak ill**, lest one **fail the test**. The **Supreme Lord sees from afar** and will **certainly impose punishment**. The **crime of disrespecting the teacher** causes **disciples to lose their immortality**, demoting them **two ranks**, and the teacher is also **demoted a rank**. **Beware! Beware!**’

The **Venerable Lord Lao** says:
‘To **transmit the Great Dao’s law** as a teacher—if one has **not fathomed the Dao’s source**, has **not communicated with spirits or harmonized with Heaven and Earth**, and lacks **meritorious deeds in saving the world**—then one **should not be a teacher**. To **recklessly transmit the Supreme Dao** will cause **future generations to lose the Dao’s lineage**, and the **offense is not light**. Such **heavenly tribunals judge as crimes of leaking secrets**.’

In the **Yellow Emperor’s era**, there was **South Mountain Lord**—
*Note: Surname **South**, given name **Mountain Lord**; he hid in the mountains and studied deeply, mastering the **Confucian rites and music**.*

The **Supreme Daoist Lord** [太上大道君] decreed, *"You claim to have accumulated virtue and accumulated benevolence, to delve deeply into the Great Dao’s teachings. You dwelled in the mountains for four lifetimes and over ten years, never venturing into the world, yet you claim to have taught a thousand disciples—renowned for their multitude. Suddenly, you are heard to have proclaimed the **Celestial Lord’s** [上帝] command that you instruct the **Venerable Spirit-Person** [仙真人], and you descend to examine **South Mountain Lord** [南山君]. You reproach him: ‘How did you learn the Dao? Who was your teacher? Now you recklessly transmit the Dao’s law to the masses.’

**South Mountain Lord** replied: ‘My teacher was **West Mountain Lord** [西山君].’
*Note: Surname **West**, given name **Mountain Lord**; now his surname is changed to **White** [白], taking the meaning of "White West" [白西], and his name is **West Mountain White** [西山大白].*

Then the **Venerable Spirit-Person** summoned **West Mountain Lord** [西山子] and asked: ‘You presumptuously claim to be **one with the Dao** [有道]. What virtue do you possess toward Heaven? What virtue do you possess toward Earth? What merit have you earned for humanity? Yet you secretly transmit the **Supreme Dao’s** [至道] teachings to **South Mountain Lord** [南山子], and he, in turn, spreads them among the common folk. Many accuse you of leaking celestial secrets, corrupting the **pure and sacred** [真圣], and defiling the **Heavenly Patterns** [天文] with impure *qi* [炁].

Moreover, you yourself have not yet **communicated with spirits** [通灵] or **saved your own life** [济身], nor have you **mastered the Dao’s arts** [炁术] to the point of **transcending sickness and death** [老病垂死]. Yet you suddenly **transmit the Dao to others** [度人].

The **Supreme Daoist Lord** [太上大道君] commands me to summon you and inquire into your reckless transmission of the Dao. You must swiftly and fully explain its cause. I will report it above, and I will also **open the path of rectification** [开正方便] for you, **reducing your offense and mitigating your guilt** [减罪].

**West Mountain Lord** [西山子] replied to the **Lord**: ‘With sincere resolve, I studied the Dao. For a long time, I hid in the mountains, **cultivating myself** [修行]. Later, I intended to **save the people** [济民]. But **South Mountain Lord** [南山子] relentlessly pressed me with **knee-walking** [膝行], begging to receive the **Dao’s arts** [炁术] and the **Spirit-Symbols of the Five Emperors** [五帝灵符].
*Note: The **true script** [真文] is the Dao’s arts. The **five symbols** [五符] are the Spirit-Symbols of the Five Emperors.*

The *Three Sovereigns’ Inner Golden Scriptures* [《三皇内箓金经》],
*Note: This is the* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl [《金锁流珠》].

The Jade Scriptures,
*Note: These are the Twenty-Four Dao Lords’ Jade Scriptures [二十四道君玉箓].*
Thirty-six volumes in total. Moreover, I formerly received them at the Brink of the Wu Heavenly Clan [吴天氏边], with the mandate to pass them down in succession, forbidding reckless transmission.

I humbly pray that the Celestial Pure [天真] take pity and save Lord West Mountain for his offense of leaking the Heavenly Texts [泄露天书]. I do not dare to presumptuously refuse instruction, nor do I dare to transmit without succession. I humbly accept the crime of receiving stolen transmissions.

The True Person [真人] said: *"Unrighteous! You presumptuously transmitted as if receiving the Law [妄传为受法]. You yourself have not yet attained spiritual penetration [通灵], nor have you fulfilled your allotted years. How much have you violated the precepts? There is no name for ‘theft’ here—according to this, you should be demoted from the Dao."*

"Only if you have nurtured the Recommended One, Broad-Chest Lord [广成君], and he guarantees no leakage, will you yourself be free of offense."

Lord West Mountain bowed twice, acknowledging his death-guilt and offering repeated thanks.

The True Person ascended to the Heavenly Palace and reported Lord West Mountain’s transgression to the Most High [太上].
*Note: If this is followed, one must not transmit recklessly—transmission must align with its principles and precepts.*

Later, the Holy Sovereign [圣君] told the Heavenly Master [天师]:
"You inherit and transmit the Three-Five True Laws [三五正法], the Upper Clarity True Scriptures [上清真经], and the Inner Scriptures [内箓], encompassing the Three Primordials [三元] and the Five Spirits [五灵].
*Note: The Five Spirits’ Laws [五灵法] are complete within the Three Primordials, hence called the Five Spirits.*

Upon completion, one receives True *qi*.
*Note: *Qi* has three grades.
The highest grade is the Three Primordials, which refine *qi* into Heavenly Dao Scriptures and Laws [大道文法].
The middle grade is the Five Phases [五行], which refine True *qi* into Heavenly Martial Laws [武法].
The lowest grade is the Six Jia [六甲], called Spirit-*qi*, which operates between Heaven and Earth and among humans—this is the One Dao, One Martial [一文一武], the power to inhibit and communicate with spirits.
Thus, the initial stage of Daoist practice is the first rank of immortality and divinity.

Command the later disciples: none should receive the Scriptures and Laws without first following this sequence. Those who complete the cycle receive these three grades of True *qi*, knowing the gates of cultivation and achieving daily spiritual merit.

The superior adept, upon fulfilling three thousand merits, ascends in broad daylight. This encompasses the Three Primordials, the Five Phases, the Six Jia, and the Seven Stars.
*Note: The Star-Stepping Method [蹑步] follows the Heavenly and Earthly Laws [天纲地纪法].*

The Six Laws,
*Note: The Six Laws are: One Orthodoxy [正一], the Three Primordials [三元], the Five Phases [五行], the Six Jia [六甲], the Seven Stars [七星], and the Eight Trigrams and Nine Palaces [八卦九宫]. Together, they govern Heaven, Earth, and spirits, encompassing all without exception, driving and commanding them.*

Upon completion, they are divided into banners [旌], nodes [节], and inscribed with the Sword Edict [授剑]. When finished, the Master divides the banners, nodes, and name tablets at the Earthly Portal of the Nine Immortal Palace [洞府地户九仙宫之门].
*Note: The Earthly Portal Nine Immortal Palace is the Bracketed Azure Grotto Heaven [括苍洞天]. Within Bracketed Azure Mountain, the Eastern Orthodoxy is Mount Le-Cheng [东正乐成], the Western connection is Bracketed Prefecture [西连括州], the Southern Orthodoxy is Yongjia [南正永嘉], and the Northern border is Mount Le-An [北接乐安].*

After the Master completes the transmission at the gate, he writes out the human-world Scriptures, Laws, and Sacred Texts sufficient for practice. Then, through the Six Jia Laws and the Star-Stepping Method, one cultivates and achieves spiritual merit, fulfilling the merit to ascend in broad daylight.

If one wishes to descend to the mortal world, or if the Master petitions, one is granted an official position among the True Officials of the World. You must inherit and record this, sealing it into the immortal lineage and registers, reporting it one by one to the Heavenly Bureau [天曹籍].

Thus, the Heavenly Master, following the Most High’s words, established twenty-four administrative districts in the West Sichuan Mountains as governance, appointing officials to embody the Earthly Portal Nine Immortal Palace’s intent.
*Note: The Heavenly Master said: ‘The Eastern and Southern Earthly Portals are distant, so I established the Sichuan Mountains as twenty-four districts.’ Each district was petitioned to register ten thousand ascended immortals to replace the Nine Immortals of the Earthly Portal Palace.*

While the Heavenly Master lived, the Earthly Portal Palace’s affairs were managed in Sichuan. After the Heavenly Master ascended, they were moved to the Eastern Orthodoxy Grotto Heaven within Bracketed Azure Mountain.

All earthly matters are reported to the Heavenly Bureau here, and responses are given. Heavenly Edicts descend accordingly.

The Venerable Lord [老君] told the Eastern Sea Water-and-Land Immortal Mother:
*Note: The Water-and-Land Immortal Mother is Peng’s Wife [彭夫人], the eldest daughter of Pengzu.*
Initially, she married into the Wang clan, but her husband died after ten years. She then married into the Meng clan, but he also died. Thus, she withdrew into seclusion, devoting herself to the Dao.

Initially, she saw an earth snake moving along a winding path. She began practicing its three-step serpentine gait, often imitating it, and took delight in it. After seven years of this, she suddenly saw a woman who said: *"You are learning the Step of the Halter [步纲]."* She replied: *"I was merely playing with irregular movements—this is not the Step of the Halter."*

Because she daily practiced the serpent’s gait, her footsteps gradually became familiar, pleasing to others, though she had no intention of seeking the Dao. Such reckless movement—how could I, with sincere resolve, engage in such deceit? What benefit would it bring to those cultivating the heart?

The woman said: *"The serpent’s step is the Dragon’s Halter—it wards off inauspiciousness. I am the middle daughter of the Western Queen Mother [西王母仲女]. Seeing my mother practice the Step of the Halter, I gave you the Earthly Measure Method [蹑地纪之法]."*

After practicing for fourteen years, she ascended to the Eastern Sea, where the Most High sealed her at Fangzhang Mountain, where she resides as the Water-and-Land Immortal Mother. She was ordered to oversee the women of Fangzhang and the seas and lands who seek immortality, teaching them as the Heavenly Messenger of the Dao. She said:

*"You are of mortal birth, receiving instruction from the Immortal Teacher. Your ascension will be swift. You must teach others, transmitting your resolve to humanity."*

The man said: *"You are also to perfect the Three Five Dao/Way [三五之法], directly pointing to its essence [元], so that you may attain ascension swiftly [得仙在速]. Do not transmit it to mortals [非人], nor violate it [勿犯之]. Otherwise, you should withdraw yourself [退汝身]. Now, in this age, seven women have all received the Dao/Way [得道] after practicing it."*

The **Most High Sovereign of the Total Perfection [后圣统仙总真王君]** said: *"From this scroll onward, it is the Dao/Way of the Upper Primordial [上元之法]."*

**Gold Lock Flowing Pearl Scroll, Section Three [金锁流珠引卷之三]**
**Gold Lock Flowing Pearl Scroll, Section Four [金锁流珠引卷之四]**

The **Total Perfection Great Immortal Sovereign of China [中华总真大仙宰王]**, Zhang Daoling [张道陵], Zhao Sheng [赵升], Wang Chang [王长], Li Zhongfu [李仲甫], Mao Ying [茅盈], Xu Yu Fu [许玉斧], and others, were later generations who compiled this text.

**Li Chunfeng [李淳风]**, the Daoist Sage of China, annotated it.

**Five Ranks Ritual Master [五等礼师] Instructions:**

1. **First, the Ritual Master of Petitions and Offerings [奏章拜表礼师]**
   The *Record of the Heavenly Master’s Former Rituals and Petitions [天师旧仪关奏典录]* states:
   *"The Heavenly Master’s primary duty is to receive the **Orthodox One [正一]** Teacher and perfect all functions. The **Rectification of Qi [治炁]** must be clear and distinct."*

   **Annotation:** What is meant by *clear and distinct* [分明]?
   The Heavenly Master has **twenty-four stages of rectification [二十四治]**, each corresponding to a **Rectified Official of Qi [正治官]** and **Rectified Qi [正炁]**. The total of these twenty-four rectifications [二十四生炁] is sufficient for one to be called a **First Rank Rectification Master [正一度师]**.

   *"After three bows [三拜], I pray that the Teacher may descend the twenty-four **Qi Rectifications [生炁]** into my body. Then, I shall emerge as an Official [出官], as requested in the petition. The Officials shall all emerge, and the one who emerges shall be solemnly arrayed, fully guarding my gate. This is to open and allow the petition to reach the Most High [达上言]."*

   This is called the **First Rank Rectification Master [正一度师]**.

   *"I pray to lead the twenty-four Qi Rectifications [二十四治], and the twenty-four **Qi Rectifications within Rectification [治中二十四生炁]**, descending and entering into my body."*

   *"I also pray to lead the **Officials of Rectification [治中吏兵功曹使者]**, all descending into my body. Three bows [礼三拜]."*

   **Annotation:** If the Rectification Master [治师] is also granted the **Orthodox One Scripture [正一箓]**, then only this one Teacher need be invoked [存], without the need for separate invocation.

   *"After the invocation, follow the petition’s ritual instructions [拜章表诀], and then offer incense. This is the complete method [具足法]."*

   The **Later Sage Sovereign [后圣君]** told the Heavenly Master:
   *"If you wish to petition and offer obeisance, first declare: ‘The **Upper Primordial Rectification of the Orthodox One [太玄都正一平炁]**, is the **Primordial Rectification of the Most High [上阳平治]**, the **Left Rectification of the Primordial [左平炁]**.’*
   *"The Dao/Way you transmit to me and my disciples, when a disciple petitions, shall be declared as: ‘The Heavenly Master’s **Primordial Rectification of the Most High [天师阳平治]**, the **Left Rectification of the Primordial [左平炁]**.’"*

   Then, invoke the **Rectification Master [治师]** as the **Supreme Teacher [尊师]**, wearing the **crimson robe [紫衣]**, the **peony flower crown [芙蓉花冠]**, and following the ritual scriptures [如法简刺]. Lead the troops from the **western-northwestern direction [西北]**, and perform three bows [礼三拜]. The **Scripture Master [箓师]** shall then lead the **three generals [三将军]**, the **Officials of Rectification [功曹使者]**, descending as seen. The **Supreme Teacher [尊师]** shall wear the **crimson robe [紫衣]**, the **lotus flower crown [莲花冠]**.

   *"I pray that the Teacher may lead the **Officials of Rectification [功曹使者吏兵]**, descending into my body. Three bows [礼三拜]."*

   **Annotation:** If it is the **Rectification Master [治师]**, and he is also granted the **Orthodox One Scripture [正一箓]**, then only this one Teacher need be invoked, without further separate invocation.

   *"After the invocation, follow the petition’s ritual instructions [拜章表诀], then offer incense. This is the complete method [具足法]."*

   The **Later Sage Sovereign [后圣君]** told the Heavenly Master:
   *"When petitioning and offering obeisance, first declare: ‘The **Upper Primordial Rectification of the Orthodox One [太玄都正一平炁]**, is the **Primordial Rectification of the Most High [上阳平治]**, the **Left Rectification of the Primordial [左平炁]**.’*
   *"The Dao/Way you transmit to me and my disciples, when a disciple petitions, shall be declared as: ‘The Heavenly Master’s **Primordial Rectification of the Most High [天师阳平治]**, the **Left Rectification of the Primordial [左平炁]**.’"*

   Then, invoke the **Supreme Teacher [尊师]** as before, and perform the rituals [行法事]. This is effective in this age [系代灵验].

2. **Second, the Ritual Master of the Dragon’s Halter and Earthly Measure [步纲蹑纪礼师]**
   The *Secret Scripture of the Jade Capital’s Flying Step [玉京飞步秘箓]* states:
   *"If one desires to practice the **Earthly Measure [蹑地纪]**, the **Dragon’s Halter [飞天纲]**, and the **various Dao/Way methods of the Halter and Measure [纲禁之法]**, such as the **Yugaitan Step [禹步]**, first invoke the **Great Halter Master [纲头大度师]**.*

   **Annotation:** **Fangzhu’s Treatise on the Halter and Measure [樊夫人作《纲纪论》]** states:
   *"The **Iron Head Master [钢头师]** is named the **Great Halter Master [大禁师]**. If one receives this **Flying Step Dao/Way [飞步之法]**, it must be from a Teacher who is **penetrating in spirit [通灵]**, **moving in power [威动]**, and can **inspire awe in heaven and earth, ghosts and gods [感天地鬼神畏敬]**, whose **virtue/power is profound [德行重]**, and whose **practice is unyielding [行用不泄]**. Only such a Teacher may be invoked as the **Great Halter Master [纲头大禁师]**.*

   *"This Teacher shall receive the Dao/Way, and the disciple shall later practice and invoke this Teacher in meditation [修行思存此师]. Within a year, the disciple shall often dream of receiving instruction in the Dao/Way. Within two years, the disciple shall be **penetrating in spirit [通神灵]**, **moving in power [威动]**, and able to **command heaven and earth, and drive the spirits of the ancestral halls and temples [驱使社庙]**, all as desired. The words shall flow smoothly and naturally [依口顺言]."*

Mistress’ Teacher, **Lu Wénqiáng**, received the *Golden Lock Flowing Pearl Sutra* in fifteen volumes, the **orthodox talismans of the Pure and Precious Three Hundred and Sixty Stages**, and the diagrams of **Earth’s Measure and Heaven’s Halter**.

Later, through practice not exceeding two years, she felt the response of spirits and the movement of heaven and earth, knowing that all her wishes were granted and her requests fulfilled abundantly.

**Li Huìjǔ’s Note:** Now, simply call upon the Teacher’s name softly.

When the Teacher arrives, riding upon **nine-colored flying clouds**, clad in **purple robes and crown**, bearing a sword, descending from heaven, she shall be greeted with **three bows**. *(Note: Either in heart or in truth.)*

Afterward, may the Teacher attain immortality, ascending to the **Supreme Pure and True Person**.

The disciple—*(Note: Zé Xuán)*—shall also attain immortality, succeeding generation after generation without end, free from calamity, forever banished from sickness and misfortune, entering **Eternal Life**, with household stability and no external harm. Dare I betray the Teacher’s grace? I humbly beseech divine protection.

Then, **twirl the Three Teachers’ Incantation**. *(Note: On the left hand’s fourth finger, first joint, facing left.)*

After performing the rites on the **five-colored silk**, having completed the incantation—*(Note: The scripture says: After binding with the five-colored silk, one must then twirl the silk again before reciting the spell.)*—then proceed with the ritual.

This spell is the **Secret of the Later Sage Emperor**, not to be passed to the world. **One character is worth ten thousand gold**—do not transmit it.

Recite the **Later Sage Emperor’s Incantation Given to Chi Sōngzi**. *(Note: Command that not a single character be carelessly transmitted; keep it secret.)*

The **Taiping** title now emerges in this age, as heaven and earth transmit it through the **Great Teacher**. **Yuánshǐ** first obtained it, heaven and earth forming it together. **Yuánshǐ** transmitted it, the **Dao Lord** knowing it first, hence the title **Supreme Venerable Lord**.

Preserved across generations, **Pángǔ the Heavenly Emperor** received it. The **Human Emperor** and **Earth Emperor** successively taught one another, giving rise to the **Five Emperors**, the **Six Jia** and **Ten Heavenly Stems**, the **Twelve Earthly Branches**, the sun, moon, and stars, the **Rotating Sphere and Seven Governors**, all harmoniously transmitted. **Xī** and **Shénnóng**, the **Yellow Emperor**, and their descendants all inherited it properly. *(Note: Wùyóu’s son hid it; it was not transmitted for five thousand years.)*

In the **Yáo** dynasty, it was passed to the **Western Barbarians**, who became kings and teachers, flourishing for **one thousand five hundred years**. After one thousand five hundred years, the **Dao** again prospered.

Its influence spread westward. *(Note: The Western influence transformed the Barbarian King into the Buddha.)* After **one thousand five hundred years**, *(Note: When the time was fulfilled, it returned to China.)* it properly reunited.

The **Golden Gate Later Sage Emperors** succeeded as Teachers, instructing their ministers to chant the incantation and recite it silently. *(Note: Thereafter, the Later Sage Emperor instructed Yín Zhēnren as the Teacher, passing it down.)*

The **True Incantation** is as follows: *(Note: This incantation was structured by the Yuánshǐ Heavenly Venerable to gather the qi of all heavens as a true spoken spell, transmitted by Teachers generation after generation before performing the Halter. There is verification for this.)*

**Three Heavens Departed, Azure Heaven Divine, Crimson Heaven Radiant, Seven Heavens Net, Wú Heaven Bright, Azure Heaven Named, Eight Heavens Resplendent, Imperial Heaven Pearl, Yǔyú Heaven Devouring, Nine Heavens Pressed, Dragon Heaven Revived, King Heaven Mysterious.**

Above are **fifteen phrases**, declaring my **eighty-one gates**. The **Red Mother Water Gate** is acceptable. *(Note: The above is the Later Sage Emperor’s transmission to the Twenty-Eight True Persons of Xuánzhōu, who chanted together and stored the Teacher in thought. Within seven years, the twenty-eight ascended together to Xuánzhōu as True Persons. This is the inner taboo of yin-yang and the Five Phases, and also the hidden name of the True Consort within the Northern Dipper. The Later Sage Emperor treasured this as an extraordinary secret—do not dare to casually transmit it.)*

The **eleven characters** are recorded at the end of the second volume of the *Golden Lock Flowing Pearl*.

If people see it but do not know how to apply it, one must use this passage to explain it before understanding.

There are also **two characters of the True Person’s name within the Northern Dipper**. Call upon it, and the Teacher will appear before you. In **three steps**, speak softly, invoking the Teacher’s compassionate step of the Halter, requesting instruction. May the Teacher teach me to **walk the Earth’s Measure**, **fly into Heaven’s Halter**, seeking life and attaining it, seeking nobility and attaining it, seeking healing and recovering, all wishes fulfilled, all desires granted. Through Dao practice, I attain immortality, my household receiving blessings, both inner and outer touched by grace. The disciple dares not betray the Teacher’s kindness. **Two bows**, then **close the qi for three breaths**, chanting the **True Person’s name within the Dipper**, and proceed with the rites.

The **True Person’s name within the Dipper** is **Gē**. The **Lord’s name** is **Jiān**. Call upon them **three times**, twirl the **Northern Dipper Incantation**, and then step the Halter.

**Thirdly, the Examination and Summoning Ritual for the Platform and Teacher’s Rites**, as in the *Pure and Precious Examination and Summoning Rites*:

The **Examination and Summoning Ritual** is to examine ghosts and summon gods. The matter is great, not small—**purity and clarity** are required. Establish the platform, set up the registers, build the prison, and open the gate. Tie the rope around the platform and prison; the platform has **four gates**, with **forbidden steps and boundary seals**. Place the **green incense case and clear lamp**; at night, during the **first watch’s third hour**, it is acceptable.

Seal the boundary, restrain the water, and prohibit the platform. **Reside in the heart with Yǔ’s Step**, encircle the outside in a **Ding-character formation**, and sprinkle water within the platform.

Then, stand facing west, invoking the **Three Pure Ones’ Examination and Summoning Pure and Precious Master, Lord Li**, clad in **floating purple robes**, crowned with sword, riding **flying purple clouds**, all arriving from the **west-north**, circling the platform **three times**.

Then, the Teacher shall **seal the platform with me**, leading the **Yang Soldiers** to the **Heavenly Tribunals and Human Intervals**, together with the **talisman soldiers within my body**, united in heart and strength, for the sake of **this household’s**—whether to **capture malevolent ghosts** or **fulfill a certain matter**.

Again, **Lord Zhōu** leads the **Yin Soldiers**, assisting within **this body**, entering the **underworld and waters**, or the **tomb of this household**, seizing the **ghost bandits harming this household**, bringing them to the platform for interrogation. The cause shall be examined, and the case reported. *(Note: Alternatively, use this text to report the case.)*

「Pursue and capture. The disciple shall perform the rites according to the **Heavenly Tribulations** (*Tiānkēo*), following the **Orthodox Dao/Way of the One** (*Zhēngyī Zhīfǎ*), and pray for the **Yang Master** and **Yin Master** to be granted.

*Note: If the Yang Master is unavailable, the disciple shall instead visualize the Master’s presence within oneself, substituting for the Master’s own body.*

Upon completion, the disciple shall **twirl the Heavenly Master’s incantation** (*tiàomù*), **concentrate the Heavenly Master’s descending true qi** (*jiàng zhēn qì*), and **infuse it into one’s own body**. Then, the disciple shall **assist the body’s talisman soldiers** (*fǔ qì*) in deploying **water, fire, and lion forces** (*fàng shuǐ fàng huǒ fàng shīzi*), dispatching the **Three Elements and Nine Heavenly Generals** (*Sānyuán Jiǔtiān Jiāngjūn*), uniting in heart and strength to **shatter the malevolent ghosts** (*zhēngyāo*) encamped in **certain mountains, temples, or bandit strongholds**, as well as **the household’s rogue spirits** (*fǒuhuài yǐn*). All shall be **reduced to dust and rubble** (*shā bēng wà suì*), **consumed by flames** (*huǒ shāo*), or **swept away by water** (*shuǐ dàng*). The **vital spirits** (*jīngyāo*) shall be **beheaded at the waist**, and the household’s afflictions—whether **disease or misfortune**—shall be **alleviated and resolved**.

*Note: The following words may be added as needed, and the invocation may be adjusted accordingly.*

**Proceed to the summoning ritual.**
*Note: The summoning ritual requires contemplating the Master’s presence before one’s body.*

The **Three Elements and Nine Heavenly Generals** shall be led, along with the **Five Virtue/Power Generals** (*Wǔdé Jiāngjūn*)—five in number—and **a hundred thousand soldiers**, arrayed to encircle the target’s dwelling. If the disciple performs this alone, they shall **fortify their own household’s gates and doors**, stationing **sixteen guards at each door** (*chāi yī shíliù rén bǎ yī mén bā rén liè mén yībiān*), with blades facing downward, and **one guard per door** (*yīyī lìzhù dāo*), as if in military formation, deploying **soldiers and officers** (*fǔ liè xíngzhèn*) to **seize the encampment’s gates**, resembling the **austerity of a tribunal**.

Upon completion, the Master shall appear, riding upon **nine-colored clouds** (*jiǔsè yún*) or a **lion**, arriving from the **east**. The disciple shall lead the soldiers to **patrol the target’s doors and gates above and below**, **establishing protective barriers** (*jiéjiè*), **sealing with prohibitions** (*jìnzhòu*), and **pursuing with talismans and writs** (*zhuīdié*), ensuring all rites are properly observed.

The Master shall **emanate radiant light from the void** (*fàng chū guāngmíng*), **summoning soldiers** (*yǒng chū bīngshì*) to **encircle the seas and block the earth**, **inspecting the Heavenly Prisons of the Nine Heavens** (*rào tiān jiǎn yù*), and **extract the three souls and seven spirits** (*sān hún qī pò*) of **certain relatives or individuals** (*mǒu qīn biǎo mǒu rén*). If the target is a woman, it is **fourteen spirits** (*shísì pò*). The **three souls** (*sān hún*) shall be **separated from the ghost** (*dé lí yāo*), and within the courtyard, they shall **attach to the disciple’s own body**, thereby **curing the disease instantly**.

**Twirl the Three Masters’ incantations** (*niǎn sān shī tiàomù*).
*Note: The incantations are located on the left hand’s fifth finger—first is the Master’s incantation, second is the Orthodox Dao/Way Master’s incantation, and third is the Heavenly Master’s incantation. The Orthodox Dao/Way Master’s incantation for summoning the Heavenly Master’s disciples to assist is as follows:*
The **Later Sage** (*Hòushèngjūn*) instructs the Heavenly Master: *"If one visualizes the Master’s presence as a substitute, and the Master understands this method, it shall be effective. If the Master does not understand this method but only knows the transmitted rituals of succession and talisman-writing, then visualization shall not be used. Otherwise, the rites shall fail, the prohibitions shall not subdue, and retribution shall ensue. Do not presume to act—beware, beware!"*

**Visualize the Master’s soldiers emerging**, each as prescribed by the method. **Refer to previous annotations.**

Next, **contemplate the Twenty-Eight Constellations** (*Érshíbā Xiù*), arraying them upon one’s body. Then, **invoke the Nine Heavenly Generals and their officers and soldiers** (*Jiǔ Jiāngjūn Lì bīngshì*), ensuring the **Three Elements are fully prepared** (*Sānyuán bèijù*), as detailed in the **Comprehensive Diagram** (*Hán tú*).
*Note: The diagram contains the full complement of the Three Elements’ soldiers and generals.*

**Twirl the Three Elements’ Generals’ incantations** (*niǎn Sānyuán Jiāngjūn tiàomù*).
*Note: The incantations are located on the left hand’s thumb—first is the heart of the first node.*

Upon completion, the disciple shall **face the ritual seat** (*xiàng àn biān zuòyí*), recite the scripture, and **summon the spirits and ghosts** (*chào shén yāo guǐ shàng*). The disciple shall **interrogate the perpetrators of the affliction**, recording their names and **sentencing them to imprisonment**. Later, the disciple shall submit a **red petition** (*chì zhāng*), requesting the **Heavenly Soldiers** (*Tiān bīng*) to **execute and behead the malevolent spirits**, so that the **disease may swiftly heal** or **certain matters may swiftly resolve**.

**Offer gratitude and conclude the rites.**
*Note: There are invocations within the soldier-deployment rites; these are not repeated here.*

The **Later Sage** further instructs the Heavenly Master: *"These six methods of summoning and interrogation are universal among mortals. The first is to **cure demonic afflictions** (*yízhòu*) and **diseases**, **seize and subdue malevolent spirits and ghosts** (*zhūdié zhēngyāo*), and **execute them**. The second is to **investigate the Heavenly Tribulations and Underworld** (*kān Tiānkēo Dìfǔ*), determining **one’s lifespan, fortune, and social standing** (*niánmìng chángduǎn, pínfù guìjiàn*). The third is to **prohibit and sever public and private grievances and mutual harm** (*gōngsī yuān duì xiāng hài*). The fourth is to **resolve conflicts between spouses or lovers** (*nánnǚ shēngmìng xiāng kè*), ensuring they **do not harm each other**, and **permanently harmonize**, escaping **metal and wood calamities** (*jīn mù zhī zāi*), **water and fire disasters** (*shuǐ huǒ zhī hài*), and **obstacles of disobedience**. The fifth is to **dispel public and private curses and hexes** (*zāi zhòu*), **vengeful ghosts**, and **harm from spirits**, whether from the living or the dead, as well as **plotted slander and verbal assaults** (*túmóu kǒushé zhī hài*), all of which shall be **consumed**, leaving no trace of harm between parties. The sixth is to **mitigate celestial and terrestrial disasters** (*Tiāndì zāihài*), such as **untimely winds and rains** (*fēngyǔ bùshí*), **imbalanced Four Qi** (*sì qì bùzhèng*), **venomous dragons and malevolent ghosts** (*dúlóng zhēngyāo*), **excessive floods or droughts** (*yínshuǐ yínhàn*), and **epidemic and toxic spirits** (*wēndú guǐ qì*). If not performed by a **Properly Orthodox Dao/Way Practitioner** (*Zhèngtiān xíngzhě*), this method shall **remove them as well**.*

The **Later Sage** further declares to the Heavenly Master: *"These six categories of summoning and interrogation are the **Supreme Dao/Way Lord** (*Tàishàng Dàdào Jūn*), who **refined and cultivated the true and authentic qi of Heaven and Earth** (*jié xí Tiāndì zhēnzhèng qì*), establishing the **talisman, writ, and scripture rites** (*fújié jīngfǎ*). There are **three thousand eight hundred and one stages** (*yī qiān sānbǎi bāshí yī jiē*) within the **Three Elements’ Orthodox Talismans** (*Sānyuán Zhèngjié*), sufficient to **qualify as a Grand Summoning Master** (*Kǎochāo Dàfǎshī*). This shall **open the Martial and Civil Divisions** (*kāi Wǔnǚ Bù*), appointing **left and right inspecting officers** (*tuīxún guān*), **judicial officers** (*pàn guān*), and **assistant summoning masters** (*fù Kǎochāo Fǎshī*). Such is the **Great Dao/Way**, the **wondrous method of salvation for humankind and benefit for all things** (*miào shàng jiùrén jì wù zhī dàfǎ*). Those who **receive and practice it faithfully** (*néng shòu néng xíng, bù qī bù wàng*) shall **ascend to the Highest Truth** (*lì qǔ shàngzhēn*).

This method’s merit is **three thousandfold** (*gōng mǎn sāniàn*), enabling **daytime ascension from the household** (*báizhōu shàngshēng*), where **all family members and livestock** shall **together attain Heaven**.

*Note: The merit of three thousand is divided into two categories—this reflects the distinction between the Martial and Civil Divisions. The first category, the **Civil Rites** (*Wénfǎ*), involves studying the **Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl** (*Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū*), **walking the Earth’s Measure** (*Niè dì jì*), **soaring the Heavenly Ropes** (*Fēi Tiān gāng*), **dispersing the Steps of Yu** (*Sàn yǔ bù*), **twirling the True Incantations** (*niǎn zhēn tiàomù*), and **performing these rites year-round without cessation**. One shall **cultivate hidden virtue** (*yīn dé*), **renounce sensory pleasures** (*chú shēngsè*), **avoid idle speech** (*kǒu bù wàng xuān*), and **refrain from spreading falsehoods** (*xīn bù wàng chuán*). Internally, one shall **refine hidden virtue** (*nèi xiū yīn dé*).

One shall **wear the Six Hexagram Talismans and Scriptures** (*Fú liù jiǎ fúwén*), **don the Five Talismans** (*dài wǔ fú*), and **walk the Five Phases’ Steps** (*bù wǔ xíng*), whether **authentic or counterfeit** (*zhēn wěi*). One shall **remain silent, concealed, and speak little**, **not be misled by others**, and **ensure that grand earthen structures and resounding bells and drums** (*guǎng zào tǔmù gōngdiàn, shēng zá zhōnggǔ*) are constructed—thus, **this method shall eliminate such disturbances**. One shall **solely guard the heart and refine inner cultivation**, **follow the scriptures’ steps and measures**, **wear the talismans**, and **visualize the true and wondrous rites** (*cún zhèng zhēn miào fǎ*). After **twenty-seven years**, the **Supreme Dao/Way Lord**, the **Former Sage, the Hollow Emperor** (*Qūhuáng*), and the **Golden Threshold Emperor of the Great Peace** (*Tàipíng Jīn què Dì*), along with the **Later Sage, the Jade Emperor** (*Xuānyuán Yùhuáng Shàngdàojūn*), shall **dispatch emissaries to welcome** the disciple, enabling **daytime ascension to Heaven**. The **Martial Immortals** (*Wénxiān Zhēn guān*) shall recognize them as **Civil Rites Masters** (*Wénlǐ Fǎshī).*」

「The First Rank of Martial Dao/Way, first taught by the Venerable Lord Lao, involves summoning the Six Grades to examine and rescue sentient beings from illness. When one’s merit reaches three thousand, and the lives saved number three hundred thousand, those who attain enlightenment through healing and those who benefit from their deeds shall be granted joy and nourishment for three thousand souls—this is called *Function of the Multitude*. When the total reaches three thousand, one ascends to Heaven in broad daylight.

This First Rank of Civil Dao/Way allows only solitary ascension, without transporting one’s residence to Heaven.

If one practices both Civil and Martial Dao/Way, their entire household—including fowl and dogs—shall ascend together, attaining the rank of Heavenly Sage-King.

**Fourth:** Practice the *Restraint of Qi* for all things between Heaven and Earth. Master Hu Gong’s *Restraint of Qi* scripture states:
The *Restraint of Heaven Master* is Li Bo Yang—*note: also the appellation of the Venerable Lord*.
The *Restraint of Earth Master* is Luo Wenqiang.
The *Restraint of the Halter Master* is Hu Xuanzang—these three are the primary leaders of the *Restraint Halter* traditions.
Those learning *Restraint* must first visualize these three descending from the void, their cloud-canopied radiance converging at the nape, clad in purple robes amid nine clouds.
With the left hand, pinch the *Supreme Restraint*—visualizing them within three steps—then bow three times in reverence.
If the *qi* enters, perform nine bows to each of the three masters, three bows per figure.
When complete, follow the original formula to restrain a specific matter or thing—this is highly efficacious.
*Note: Each formula is pinched according to its respective restraint.*
The *Restraint of Qi Three Masters’ Formula* is located on the left hand’s fourth finger at the first joint, and also on the fifth finger’s first joint.
After pinching the formula, take three *Yu Steps*, then chant the restraint incantation.
*Note: The incantation varies according to the specific restraint.*
The Later Sage-King told the Heavenly Master:
*"To restrain all things between Heaven and Earth, the master’s name must differ accordingly."*
*Note: This implies succession.*
The *Restraint of Heaven Master* is Zhao Boqin.
The *Restraint of Earth Master* is Yin Fuzhi.
The *Restraint of Ghost Master* is Huang Tiansheng.
The *Restraint of Human Master* is Zhang Tuling.
These are newly supplemented, yet must be visualized alongside the previous masters, bowing in reverence before performing any of the hundred restraints—all shall succeed divinely.
The Heavenly Master’s lineage must be succeeded; why limit reverence to only the previous masters? Three bows suffice.

**Fifth:** Entering armies, mountains, or waters, or traveling to foreign lands where fear of harm or loss of life is imminent—urgent methods to invoke the master’s salvation.
*Note: This protects oneself and one’s household; do not transmit recklessly, lest it harm the master.*
The Yellow Emperor obtained the *Play of the Mysterious Woman’s Urgent Military Strategies* (*Xuánnǚ Bīngjī Jíyào Lù*), saying:
*"Those who follow the army without injury—my maiden has the Nine-Heaven Concealment Method. You may pass it to your successors for urgent use. When needed, visualize me as your master, leading soldiers to guard above the Nine Heavens, departing the Nine Calamities, and vanishing unseen, with ten thousand cavalry unable to pursue."*
*Note: From this martial method’s formation, there are formations of the Nine Heavens Above, the Nine Calamities Within, the Nine Earths Below, the Void and Space Within, the Eight Arrays Inside and Outside, the Five Phases Within and the Five Weapons Without—sufficient to calculate the Nine Heavens Above.*
Visualize the *Original Two-Formation Master*, the *Twelve-Formation Master*, and the *Thirty-Six-Formation Master* within the Nine Calamities, deploying a hundred-thousand-strong army within the Nine Diagrams and Eight Arrays, thus vanishing unseen.
This method is profound and difficult to grasp; even a master must demonstrate it face-to-face, lest one fail to execute it properly.
The Emperor received it, and indeed encountered fifty-nine battles, defeating Chiyou seven times.
The Emperor visualized the Original Master, Xuannü, and transformed the *Thunder Lord Taiyi’s Liu Ren* formations, shielding himself as he emerged—no army could perceive him.
When seen, the Emperor’s form rose above the Nine Heavens.
*Note: The Nine Heavens Above have their own formation scriptures, fully recorded hereafter.*
This wards off calamities.
Thus, even those who merely cultivate the Dao, though not leading armies, may wield Dao-power. Should Heaven’s favor descend, one might suddenly receive celestial talismans, forming a hundred-thousand-strong array to save a million souls—urgently responding to the command.
First, visualize the *Formation Master* clad in crimson robes, holding a scepter and formation, descending through the sky to guard the disciple, emerging above the Nine Heavens.
Pray for the master’s descent, leading generals and soldiers.
*Note: Among the generals—both Upper and Lower Elements—there are six generals. Within the formations, six generals command troops; visualize each leading fifty thousand soldiers, encircling the body three times, then circling again three times, vanishing above the Nine Heavens. Swiftly, as the law decrees.*
For a hundred thousand, a million, or ten million troops.
Let Li [your surname] and the disciple serve as the Grand General, with the master as the Deputy General.
Next, visualize the *Chief Halter Restraint Master*—*note: the master of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*—Li Hui, descending on clouds, riding a five-colored lion, clutching the Heavenly Formation in purple robes, stopping three steps ahead, then bow three times in reverence.
Then bow three times to the *Formation Master* who protects the Grand General.
Afterward, pinch the *Three Masters’ Formation Formula*.
*Note: The formula is on the right side of the left hand’s fifth finger’s first joint.*
Retrieve the formation talisman from the chest, don it on the head, then charge through enemy lines on horseback, entering and exiting battle unharmed.

**Five Talismans:**
1. *Talisman for Unharmed Entry into Battle*
2. *Talisman for the Enemy’s General Feeling Awe and Respect, Preventing Harm*
3. *Talisman for Overcoming Difficult Battles*
4. *Talisman for Commanding Strong Enemies*
5. *Talisman for Strengthening the Army’s Morale and Combat Power, Fulfilling All Desires*

**Heavenly Art: First Talisman for Unharmed Entry into Battle**
*Within this scroll, the talisman is inscribed in vermilion.*
*Usage:* Write the enemy general’s name beneath the talisman, then seal it with the *Great Void* and lunar stem-branch. The Heavenly Emperor’s seal shall be affixed.

**Heavenly Art: Second Talisman for the Enemy’s General Feeling Awe and Respect, Preventing Harm**
*Within this scroll, the talisman is inscribed in vermilion.*
*Usage:* Right Heavenly Art—enter battle to protect the general, causing his troops to feel awe and respect.

**Heavenly Art: Third Talisman for Overcoming Difficult Battles**
*Within this scroll, the talisman is inscribed in vermilion.*
*Usage:* Right Heavenly Art—enter battle to overcome difficult enemies.

**Heavenly Art: Fourth Talisman for Commanding Strong Enemies**
*Within this scroll, the talisman is inscribed in vermilion.*
*Usage:* Right Heavenly Art—deploy the general to command strong enemies.

**Heavenly Art: Fifth Talisman for Strengthening the Army’s Morale and Combat Power, Fulfilling All Desires**
*Within this scroll, the talisman is inscribed in vermilion.*
*Usage:* Right Heavenly Art—order all troops to have steadfast hearts and mighty strength.

The preceding five talismans are all inscribed by Master Li (師一一书).
They shall be transmitted on *Jiazi* days or the recipient’s birthdays to disciples.
After disciples use them in battle, they must remember their original master.
Then, each talisman shall naturally manifest its power.
When inscribed in vermilion, their effects are profound—like gods appearing and vanishing.
They must not be carelessly transmitted.

The Heavenly Master of West Shu (天師在西蜀) fought against demons and spirits in twenty-eight battles.
In every battle, he thought of the **Posterior Sage** (後聖君) leading the way.
When the demons and spirits saw the Posterior Sage, they fled in defeat, turned their weapons, and lay prostrate.
None dared resist the enemy.

The **Celestial Sovereign** (老君) instructed his attendants:
*"You who study the Dao must always remember and emulate your master’s methods and techniques.
Thus, you shall quickly attain enlightenment."*

The **Celestial Emperor** (上帝) rejoiced and granted him divine powers, enabling him to transcend the **Three Realms** (出離三界).
Earth, water, and fire—
On the sixth *Jiazi* day and his own birthday, he established the memory of his master,
As if seeing him in the void of space atop the five clouds, with winds and immortals accompanying him.

**Three Elements** (三元):
*Note:* The **Three Element Generals** (三元将军) consist of nine, each commanding officials, soldiers, and countless legions.

**Five Virtues** (五德):
*Note:* The **Five Virtue Generals**—Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, Dark Tortoise, and Yellow Court—each one leading soldiers in the tens of millions according to their respective directions.
All are summoned by the master.

Eastern direction: 810,000 soldiers;
Western direction: 360,000 soldiers;
Southern direction: 640,000 soldiers;
Northern direction: 250,000 soldiers;
Central direction: 120,000 soldiers.

This is the Heavenly Master’s instruction to **King True Person** (王真人).

**Six Records** (六纪):
*Note:* There are six records, each with soldiers numbering 120,000.

**Pillar-Heaven Generals** (柱天大将军) twelve in number:
*Note:* Each commands 36,000 soldiers.

**Twenty-Four Generals of the Six Jiazi and Central Branches** (六甲中干支将军):
*Note:* Each commands 60,000 soldiers, 1,800 officers, 36,000 talisman messengers, 1,400 Jade Boys, and 2,400 Jade Girls.
All follow the master and his disciples into battle—unfazed by enemies, unharmed by soldiers.
Divine officials guard and protect them; all who enter the ranks grow mighty.
**As the Celestial Sovereign of the Great Void, the Way’s Supreme Lord, commands: Urgent, urgent, like the heavens.**
The following generals and officials, numbering in the hundreds of millions and billions, follow Master Li, **Zhou Chong**, and **Su** (虚) in the void.
They deploy to rescue disciples, smashing enemy forces like collapsing mountains and splitting earth.
They cause the seas to surge and waves to crash—great winds rise, scattering foes.
All disciples and troops, hearts bold and strength unyielding, shall remain unbroken and mighty.
The enemy must be utterly defeated.
**Urgent, urgent, as the Supreme Lord commands: So be it.**

Then twist the **Grand Supervisor Talisman** (捻都监诀) and the **Three Master Talismans** (三师诀), and the **Roaming Master’s Three Talismans** (游师三诀).
*Note:* The Grand Supervisor is at the first joint of the left hand’s first finger.
The Roaming Master is at the second joint.
After twisting these three talismans, take the **Yugong Steps** (禹步) three times.
Then strike the drum to form the battle array.
Observe the enemy’s movements and engage accordingly—then protection is assured.
This is the ultimate method.

The **Celestial Sovereign** (老君) told the **True Persons of the Ten Directions** (十方真人):
*Note:* The **True Persons of the Ten Directions**—**Yunna**, **Zheng Ren**, **Shan Sheng**, **Jing Jia**, **Xu Lai Le**, and others—are the titles of ten True Persons.
In scriptures, they are called the **Ten Direction Heavenly Sovereigns** (十方天尊).

From the time of **Pangu** and the **Three Sovereigns** (三皇) until the present age,
Only these ten hold the positions of the **Ten Direction Heavenly Sovereigns** (十方天尊),
Unchanging, untransferable, stationed across the ten directions.

You are the masters of the ten directions,
Stationed in the ten-directional world,
Encouraging virtue and guiding people,
Upholding the true transmission of Daoist methods.
You must not transmit what is unworthy.
Do not praise false teachings,
Nor alter sacred scriptures and masterly doctrines.
Do not slander right and wrong—
Such people must not be taught or transmitted to.

If transmitted recklessly, both master and disciple shall be ruined.
If such offenders exist, I shall atone with you,
So that neither of us bears guilt.

Then the **True Person of the Southwest** (西南方真人), **Shan Sheng** (善胜), spoke:
*"Your disciple **Zhen Jingneng** (真净能) is a man of ancient refinement, skilled in speech,
And adept at flattering with his tongue.
Once, I saw him receive the **Highest Scripture and Highest Law** (上经上法) from **Lu Zi Zhen** (路子真),
A master of the **High Scripture and High Law** (上经上法).
Though he has not yet attained enlightenment, he practices the law rigorously.
I then transmitted to him the *Scripture of the Golden Talisman and Jade Talisman* (《金箓玉箓上经》),
*Note:* Also called *Scripture of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (《金锁流珠上经》),
The method of the **Three Element and Five Virtue** (三元五行) **Orthodox Unity** (正一).
In ancient times, it was called the *Scripture of the Golden Talisman and Jade Talisman* (《金箓玉箓》),
Where **Jin Zhen** (金真) performs the **Flying Steps** (飞步).
Along with it, I transmitted over forty volumes.*

*When he first received the scriptures, I commanded him to write them as he went.
Upon completion, I ordered him to immediately inscribe the master’s name and his own.
But **Zhen Jingneng** (净能) secretly conspired—
*Note:* Ancient people called secret plotting *yin’an* (阴暗), meaning mutual understanding.
He substituted for the master’s name and called me **‘Successor Grandfather, King Jing’** (父真王靖),
Claiming the scriptures were from me, not you.
Such a grave offense—how can it be atoned?*

*I humbly pray that the Heavenly Sovereign (天尊) grants me great compassion and mercy,
So that my transgression may be pardoned."*

The **Celestial Sovereign** (老君) replied:
*"Your offense may still be forgiven,
But **Jingneng’s** (净能) guilt is too great—it cannot be overlooked.
This is the crime of betraying one’s heart and turning from the Dao,
Of plotting against the master.
His offense surpasses even filial disobedience toward parents—
The heavens and earth themselves shall reproach him.
Soon, he shall meet ruin in both body and family.*
*Note:* Within ten years, his body and family were destroyed—was this not the heavens’ retribution?

The Celestial Sovereign spoke further:

*"My grace is vast—
To overlook minor slanders and instead bestow upon you the eternal scriptures of benevolence and teaching,
To perpetuate the sacred lineage of the Dao’s voice and doctrine—
This alone can redeem your transgression.

Moreover, the **Golden Talisman** and **Jade Talisman** rituals,
All unlock the Great Dao of liberation,
Sealing the heart’s inner secrets,
Treading the path of heaven and earth,
Subduing the stars and constellations,*
*Note: Also called "Clothing of the Celestial."*
*Reversing the heavens, turning the earth’s axis,
Binding the celestial gates—
This is the true and authentic Dao.

Yet your offense remains unforgiven by the cosmic laws.
You shall also be demoted one rank among the immortals,
And for fifty years, descend as a mortal teacher,
Healing three thousand souls to atone for your sins.
Later, this came to pass—
You were demoted and became **Master Bian Que**,
Skilled in healing, curing three thousand patients,
Before reclaiming your original rank.

For those who become teachers,
And for those who revere their teachers,
One must be ever vigilant and precise.

Thus, this oath is given—
The secret of honoring and remembering the teacher,
So that disciples may each guard their conduct,
Mindful of their duty to repay.

*Note: When a teacher instructs a disciple,
Not all inner secrets and profound teachings may be imparted at once.
One must first petition the Celestial Bureau,
And only if approved may the transmission proceed.
The Celestial Bureau replied:
‘If proven worthy, you may be entrusted with the recommendation.’

Yet even then, transmission must not be hasty.
Three or five trials must be conducted,
And only if all are passed may the teachings be given.
Otherwise, if one first grants the scriptures, talismans, and three ranks of initiation,
And yet the disciple’s devotion wavers—
If their body and mind remain impure, if they disrespect the Dao-teacher,
Then the secrets may not be fully revealed.
Only two or three volumes of essential Dao-teachings may be passed on gradually,
To delight the Celestial Heart.
The Supreme Sovereign, from afar, honors the unwavering devotion of teacher and disciple.

Later, the Holy Sovereign instructed **Yin Xi**:
‘To be a teacher is difficult,
To be a disciple is no easy task—
The balance of difficulty lies in both.
*Note: Human hearts vary; many betray and undermine the teacher’s path.
Again, if the transmission is false,
If talismans are falsified, if the secrets are severed—
If the teachings are incomplete, rendering them useless,
Both teacher and disciple shall bear the blame.
Thus, transmission must be tested three times.
Only if proven worthy may the scriptures, talismans, and three ranks be first granted.
Then, after three or five years of trial,
If their resolve does not falter,
The inner talismans may be bestowed,
Guiding them into the Dao’s gate,
Where they may inherit the lineage,
Honoring the teacher, preserving the path,
And their practices shall bear divine efficacy.

To cultivate the self, aid the nation, and save the people—
*Note: Those of Daoist resolve always act with compassion.
Each who reveres the teacher’s doctrine,
If they honor it as they should,
Shall see their lineage endure with sacred efficacy,
Their威灵通神 (mystic power and divine response) unbroken,
Their devotion ever alive.
But if they disregard their fate,
Defy the Dao-teacher,
And fail to act in emergencies,
Divine efficacy shall rarely manifest.
To subdue ghosts and govern spirits,
To uphold the virtues of the worthy and the Dao,
Follow this path and secret method,
So that teacher and disciple may attain immortality.

*Note: The Celestial Sovereign spoke of the teacher’s resolve
And the disciple’s resolve,
And only then may the true talisman secrets be transmitted,
Only then may disciples be properly initiated.
If the disciple’s resolve is sincere,
If they honor the teacher with filial devotion,
Then their practices shall swiftly bear fruit.

Later, the Holy Sovereign addressed the **Forty-Nine True Persons**—
*Note: The Forty-Nine True Persons—those who first practiced the True Way—
Included Xu Jia, Shi Cun, Kong Fangwai, Yang Zhen, Li Ziqī, Li Bāibǎi, Liu Gen, Zhang Jiànchéng, Lü Jīngjiān, Zhou Shànghé, Wang Dēng,
Wei Huaxun, and the two female True Ones, Fan Zhenying.
Also Li Shàojūn, Li Shàogāng, Wang Zinián, Han Yuánxìn, Zhang Shàozhēn, Shí Fān Gōng, Qin Jiāo, and Huang Tài—
Forty-nine in total, who successively inherited the teacher’s path.

He said:
‘For those who properly receive the sacred scriptures,
The talismans, and the true secrets of initiation—
It depends on their devotion to and remembrance of the teacher.

Whether they walk a hundred steps from home,
Or two hundred, three hundred—
No matter the distance,
Before taking their seat in any place,
They must first invoke the **Great Precept of the Celestial Master**,
As if the Cloud-Dragon and attendant warriors had arrived.
With three reverences, they pray:
*"May my teacher attain the rank of True Immortal King,
And ascend to the heavens, attaining the highest station."*

For me—
*Note: Now, immortals no longer address me thus—this is improper.
Henceforth, they shall address me as ‘Your Servant, [Name],’—this is the proper etiquette.

To open the **Five Paths**—
*Note: Later sages spoke of the Three Paths and Eight Difficulties,
But Master Zhang [of the Heavenly Masters] revised it to Five Paths and Eight Difficulties,
And this tradition has been followed, though not entirely adopted.
The Five Sorrows and Eight Difficulties—
Once named in the **Golden Talisman of Immortal Initiation**,
Shall forever grant the body of a True Person,
Bestowing the Dao’s grace and protection.
How dare I betray the teacher’s恩德 (virtue/power)?

Upon completion, they shall strike their teeth twenty-four times,
And recite the **Three-Teacher Secret**.

This method is wondrous—
After one year, a hundred ailments depart,
A thousand spirits guard them.
Within two years, their family and descendants shall live in eternal peace.
In three years, they shall command spirits with efficacy,
And heaven and earth shall respond to their heart and words.
In four years, they shall become immortals.
But if their heart remains upright,
Without favoritism or bias,
Within five years, they shall forever be immortals.
At twenty-one years, they may ascend if they wish,
Or remain if they choose—
Even to seek mortal office, they may do so.

**End of Volume Four of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Talisman.**

**Volume Five of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Talisman.**"

**Volume Five of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Talisman**

The **Grand Perfect Daoist Sovereign** of China, **Zhang Daoling** of the **Way of the Five Pecks**, **Zhao Sheng**, **Wang Chang**, **Li Zhongfu**, **Mao Ying**, **Xu Yufu**, and others, are successive compilers of this text. **Li Chunfeng**, the Daoist Immortal of China, annotated it. The **Great Mysterious** begins with **Primordial Qi**—here is the **Three Primordial** introduction.

**Annotation on the Great Mysterious:**
The **Great Mysterious** belongs to the **Upper Clarity** grade, marking the origin of **Upper Clarity** and the inception of **Primordial Qi**.

**Primordial Qi** generates the **Great Dao/Way**,
The **Great Dao/Way** generates **Taiyi**,
And **Taiyi** generates the **three colors of Qi**—
**Mysterious Yellow**, **Primordial White**, and **Initial Green**.

These three colors of **Qi** intermingle in a smoky haze,
Exchanging and returning in cycles—
**Yellow** produces **Red**,
**Green** produces **Qi**,
Thus forming the **five colors of Qi**.

**Qi** generates **color**, and **color** generates **Qi**,
The three and five in endless interplay—
**Qi** and **color** coalesce into **form**, and this is called **spirit**.

**Spirit** and **form** have names,
Marking their stations and clarifying their ranks—
They aid each other in transforming malevolence,
Guard the upright and preserve life,
Seeking immortality and renown.

With **incantations** and **seals**, they assist the realm and defend the family,
Dissolving guilt and bestowing blessings,
Protecting the virtuous and exterminating the wicked—
All may become generals, officers, or soldiers.

Different ages, different laws—
In times of simplicity, some may follow the **rituals of submission and humility**.
In eras of excess, others may prefer the **condensed essentials of practice**.

Thus, the **Dao/Way** adapts—
Restraining or expanding, concealing or revealing—
Later disciples who achieve perfection,
Assuming the **Mysterious Mandate** of their station,
Residing by name in their native villages,
Emerging in each generation—
Some may lack nothing, but today we record only what the **Master of the Way** transmitted as follows:

The **Later Sage** and **Divine Sovereign** instructed **Zhang Daoling**:
*"If you wish to cultivate and practice,
First know the **origin of life and death**.*

*The **origin of life and death** determines **calamity and blessing**,
Establishing clear distinctions—
Those who gain blessings flourish as **kings**,
Those who lose blessings decline.
And those who incur **calamity** perish,
While those who avoid **calamity** survive.
To eliminate **punishment and calamity**,
One must discern the **origin of life and death**.*

*For instance, a person born under the **Jiazi cycle** with a **Golden Command**—
Their **Primordial Qi** rests in **Chen**,
And **Chen** belongs to the **Xun direction**, encompassing all.
The **origin of life and death** is in **Si**,
Which matures into **Wu**, thrives in **Shen**,
And reaches its peak in **You**—
**You** is the **hour of the king and minister**,
**You** embodies **blessing and virtue**,
**Wei** is the **hour of rest**,
**Hai** is the **hour of decline**,
**Zi** is the **hour of punishment**,
And **fire** is the **hour of calamity**.
This is the **Wuyu Star**.*

*A person born under the **Wood Command**—
Their **origin of life and death** is in **Hai**,
Which matures into **Zi** and **Chou**,
Thrives in **Yin**,
And reaches its peak in **Mao**—
**Mao** is the **hour of the king and minister**,
**Mao** embodies **blessing and virtue**,
**Chen** is the **hour of rest**,
**Si** is the **hour of decline**,
**Wu** is the **hour of punishment**,
And **metal** is the **hour of calamity**.
This is the **Jinyuan Star**.*

*A person born under the **Shen Command** with a **Water Command**—
Their **origin of life and death** is in **Shen**,
Which matures into **You** and **Xu**,
Thrives in **Hai**,
And reaches its peak in **Zi**—
**Zi** embodies **blessing and virtue**,
**Chou** is the **hour of rest**,
**Yin** is the **hour of decline**,
**Mao** is the **hour of punishment**,
And **earth** is the **hour of calamity**.
This is the **Shuiyuan Star**—
And similarly, those born under the **Earth Command** share the **Water Command**’s pattern.*

*For those born under the **Fire Command**—
Their **origin of life and death** is in **Yin**,
Which matures into **Mao** and **Chen**,
Thrives in **Si**,
And reaches its peak in **Wu**—
**Wu** embodies **blessing and virtue**,
**Wei** is the **hour of rest**,
**Shen** is the **hour of decline**,
**You** is the **hour of punishment**,
And **water** is the **hour of calamity**.
This is the **Shuiyuan Star**.*

*For those born under the **Earth Command**—
Their **origin of life and death** is in **Xu**,
And **Xu** is the **hour of the king and minister**,
**Xu** embodies **blessing and virtue**,
**Wei** is the **hour of rest**,
**Shen** is the **hour of decline**,
**Mao** is the **hour of punishment**,
And **wood** is the **hour of calamity**.
This is the **Zhuyuan Star**.*

*Now, those who cultivate must first practice the **Yugong Steps**,
Then the **Northern Dipper**,
Then the **Central Dipper**—
The **Central Dipper** is called the **Heavenly Ruler**,
Thus one **leaps in flight**.
Next, the **Three Platforms**,
Then the **Five Stars**.

They then employ the **twelfth incantation** from the **upper volume of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Talisman**,
The **Flying Heavenly Ruler incantation**,
And petition the **Primordial Qi** of the **Yuan Star** (the **Lord of the Mysterious Body and Longevity**)—
To command the **Primordial Qi** of the **Zhen Star** (the **Lord of the Soil and the Subduing Qi**),
So that **punishment and calamity** may not be recklessly imposed.

If **punishment and calamity** are imposed upon the **Primordial Qi** of the **Yuan Star**,
The **Star Lord** and the **Qingtong Lord** will sever and restrain it—
Swiftly, as decreed by law.
