The rest follows this pattern.

Within the *Five Stars Sacred Scripture*,
There are already **Five Stars Talismans** to be used,
To restrain the **punishment and calamity** of the **Five Phases**,
And preserve **Primordial Qi**.

The **origin of life and death** refers to one’s **parents**—
**Annotation:** The **parents**’ **commands** are **golden wood**.
If their **commands** clash with one’s own,
Use a **talisman** to halt the **clash**—
For if one’s own **command** does not clash with theirs,
Then the **origin of life and death** (i.e., **Primordial Qi**) will be made clear.
*For example:* If a **mother’s command** is **gold** and a **child’s command** is **wood**,
The **mother’s command** restrains the **child’s command**—
The child will then not live long,
But with a **talisman** to halt the **clash**, both **mother and child** will be auspicious.

If a **mother’s command** is **earth** and a **child’s command** is **wood**,
The **child’s command** restrains the **mother’s command**—
Again, use the **Five Phases talisman** to halt the **clash**, and both **mother and child** will be auspicious.
**Annotation:** The rest follows this pattern.

This principle speaks of the **Primordial Qi** of the **origin of life and death**,
Not clashing or restraining—
For those who cultivate the **Dao/Way**, it brings great fortune,
And they may wear the **Five Phases talisman** to restrain and subdue **calamities**.

Upon completion,
Recite the **incantation of the parents’ origin of life and death**,
And employ the **talisman to restrain punishment and calamity** for oneself.
**Annotation:** For example, if one is born under the **Golden Command**,
**Fire** is the **punishment and calamity**—
The **talisman** is detailed in the **Five Phases Palm Talismans**.

The **invocation** goes thus:
*"I was born of my **parents**,
And grew long within the **mundane world**.
So it is."*

The **incantations** are found in the **upper volume of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Talisman**—
There are two of them.

After reciting the **incantation**,
Walk the **Yugong Steps of the origin of life and death**—
Twelve steps in total—
To restrain **calamities of the origin of life and death**,
And perform this each time one reaches their **native command day**.

After completing the **Yugong Steps**,
One again invokes:
*"I was born of my parents."*
And so forth—
This is the **later incantation**.
The incantation is also from the same source.

If practiced at birth,
In the first year, it wards off misfortune.
In the second year, **Metal and Wood** do not clash, **Water and Fire** do not harm.
In the third year, one departs death and enters life.
In the fourth year, one attains **Earthly Authenticity**, and others resolve one’s **origin-of-life calamities and misfortunes**.
At twenty years, one is named **Celestial Authenticity**, ranked among the **Celestial Hosts**, as the **origin-qi of the Three Five**.

Next, one is listed among the **Three Five’s born**.

**Annotation:** The Three refers to **Heaven, Earth, and Man**—the **Three Talents, Three Origins**.
Each Talent resides in one Origin, hence called the **Three Origins**.
**Annotation:** The **Upper Origin** governs Heaven, the **Middle Origin** governs Man, the **Lower Origin** governs Earth—
They are called the **Three Origin Generals**.
One general per Origin commands officers and soldiers; each Origin gathers **three million ten thousand troops**.
The **Ancient Highest Dao Lord** received this from **Yuan Shi**, who passed it to the **Dao Lord**.
**Annotation:** When the Dao Lord emerged, it was the **Age of the Heavenly Sovereign**, before laws existed among mortals.

The **Upper Origin Upper Division General**, one in number, surnamed **Tang**, named **Short**,
With divine strength and valor, his transformed body nine thousand million *zhang* long,
Leading soldiers, wielding sword and bow,
With nine thousand million troops,
Overseeing the **Supreme Great Luo** above the **Three Pure Ones of Heaven**.

**Annotation:** The **Jade Pure, Upper Pure, and Supreme Pure** are these.

The **Upper Origin Middle Division**
**Annotation:** The Middle Division is the **Upper Origin Middle General**, governing the **one within a person’s body**—
Also mirroring Heaven and Earth, aligning the body with Heaven and Earth, all aspects complete and identical.
One general, surnamed **Li**.
**Annotation:** Because **Laozi** bore the surname Li, he ordered it changed to Li.
Named **Jù**,
His body seven thousand million *zhang* long,
Leading soldiers, wielding sword and spear,
With seven thousand million troops.
Above the **Supreme Three Pure**, entering the human body,
He excels in dispelling **Celestial Net snares**, **Five Phase calamities**, and **Earthly misfortunes**.
Only **General Li** can greatly assist human strength,
Able to remove **Celestial origin-of-life calamities**.
**Annotation:** The ancients forged this [talisman] from gold, one *cun* long, worn in a crimson pouch on the head—
It excels in saving people during calamities.

The **Upper Origin Lower Division General**, one in number, surnamed **Eastern Sea Ancient Surname**.
Now, the **Holy One** changes it to **Xu**.
Named **Kang**,
His body five thousand million *zhang* long,
Leading soldiers, wielding sword and **Jade Yang Node**,
With five thousand million troops.
Above the **Upper Pure**, entering the human body,
He excels in healing diseases,
Dissipating **Celestial, Ten Directions, Nine Earths’ origin-of-life calamities, misfortunes, and Five Phase mutual destruction and assaults**—
Able to dispel these with Dao power.

There are also **Three Origin Three Functionaries**, three in total.
Under the **Upper Origin Upper Division General Tang**, the **Five Just Gods Functionary**, one, surnamed **Jiang**, named **Dú**,
His body nine hundred ninety *zhang* long,
Leading **hundreds of millions of layered troops**, in crimson robes and red headgear,
Holding a **golden talisman**, wielding a sword,
Stationed above **Great Luo**.

Under the **Upper Origin Middle Division General Li**, the **Five Just Gods Functionary**, one, surnamed **Zhang**, named **Jì**,
His body seven hundred seventy *zhang* long,
Leading **hundreds of millions of layered troops**, in red armor,
Right hand holding a spear, sword at the waist,
Stationed within the **Supreme Pole**.

Under the **Upper Origin Lower Division General Xu**, the **Five Just Gods Functionary**, one, surnamed **Wēn**, named **Shū**,
His body five hundred fifty *zhang* long,
Leading **hundreds of millions of layered troops**, in red headgear,
Right hand holding the **Jade Yang Node**, sword at the waist.
**Annotation:** Above the **Supreme Great Luo Heaven**, both above and below Heaven,
And entering the **right kidney** within a person.

The **Three Origin Functionaries**, entering and exiting,
Each pass through the **eyebrow’s Heavenly Gate**,
Greatly enabling one to attain **Law and Technique**,
To bark and command **ghosts, tigers, leopards, venomous snakes, malevolent men, poisonous dragons, spirits, demons, and specters**.
This recounts the names of the **Three Origin Upper Division Generals**.
**Annotation:** The **Upper Origin Upper Division General**, one, surnamed **Tang**, named **Short**.
The **Upper Origin Middle Division General**, one, surnamed **Li**, named **Jù**.
The **Upper Origin Lower Division General**, one, surnamed **Xu**, named **Kang**.
Together with the **Three Functionaries**, these are the **Upper Origin’s division**, governing Heaven.

The **Middle Origin’s Three Generals** emerged in the **Ancient Age of the Human Sovereign**,
When three ministers practiced the Dao alongside the Human Sovereign, achieving completion—
They obtained the **Middle Origin’s Three Generals**.
**Annotation:** Their names were **Fēng Ān, Luò Qiáng, and Tiān Shēng**.

Later, in the **Zhou Mu Wang era**, three ministers replaced the earlier **Fēng Ān** and others.
There were also three successors:
**Táng Hóng**,
**Annotation:** Serving as **Grand Counselor**, equivalent to today’s **Chancellor**.
Also holding the titles of **Grand Tutor and Grand Minister**.
**Gě Yōng**,
**Annotation:** Serving as **Attendant Lord and Chief of Rites**, equivalent to today’s **Grand Master of Rites**.
With the courtesy name **Wén Dù**.
**Zhōu Wǔ**,
**Annotation:** Serving as **Attendant Marshal**, equivalent to today’s **Right Marshal**, holding the same rank as the **Right Chancellor**.

The three studied the Dao, following **Mu Wang** in practicing the **Six Jia, Three Origin, Nine Palace Method**,
Then resigned their offices.
**Mu Wang** obtained the **Cave Palace Immortal**, hidden in **Wangwu Mountain**, feigning death and departing—
None could find him.
They then devoted themselves to refining **Embryonic Breath, Qi Cultivation, and Golden Elixir**,
Taking three doses but failing to ascend—
Only achieving immortality, living over five hundred years in **Emèi and Taibai Mountains**.

The three swore an oath, seeking the **Perfect Ones**,
Aspiring to the **Perfect Dao**, ascending to Heaven in broad daylight.
Now we know of the **Upper Realm’s new Highest Dao, Great Peace Golden Gate, Mysterious Origin Holy Emperor, Jade Dao Lord**—
We now pledge our sincerest hearts,
Wishing these three may serve as ministers beneath him.

With hearts most sincere, we vow to walk the Dao with the Jade Emperor,
Aspiring to serve and assist him below.
We receive the Dao’s chosen, amassing countless merits—
Yet dare not claim credit for our deeds.

Ever bearing a heart of salvation,
We beseech the Heavenly Emperor of the Golden Gate, Mysterious Origin, Great Peace, and Supreme Dao—
May he, in his boundless grace, perceive and bless those who pray.

After three years of practice,
We indeed encountered him upon Taibai Mountain.
In the second year of Qin’s *More Begins* (July 7th),
The Jade Emperor of the Golden Gate, Mysterious Origin, Great Peace, and Supreme Dao descended upon Taibai Mountain—
*(Anciently called Dayuan White Heaven Mountain).*

He conferred upon Tang Hong and the other two the *Fifteen-Juan Scripture of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl (Sanwu Jin Suo Liu Zhu Jing)*,
And the method of *Treading the Celestial Halter and Earthly Records*.

Each practiced for three years, attaining *Earthly Authenticity*.
*(Authenticity: the power to enforce prohibitions and heal many illnesses.)*

The Supreme Posterior Sage Lord rejoiced at their Dao,
Their true and sincere hearts—
And immediately granted them further instruction.
After ten years, he descended again,
Conferring upon them *Ten-Juan of the Induction Decisions*.

The three practiced day and night for two years,
And indeed ascended as immortals,
Gaining audience with the Posterior Sage Lord,
Appointed to fill the rank of *Three Great Generals of the Middle Element*,
Overseeing the *Three Heavenly Rectification Methods*,
Wearing the Dipper as clothing—
Clothing the Dipper, sandaling the Dipper, riding the Dipper,
Donning the Dipper, aligning with the Dipper, inverting the Dipper,
Reversing the Dipper, crossing the Dipper, lowering the Dipper,
Opposing the Dipper, raising the Dipper, sitting upon the Dipper,
Walking the Dipper, reclining upon the Dipper.
*(Reclining upon the Dipper: Before closing the outer eyes,
Visualize the Dipper covering your body like a quilt,
Conforming to the celestial Dipper’s position by lunar mansion.)*

Pointing the Dipper, summoning the Dipper, commanding the Dipper,
Leading the Dipper, firming the Dipper, yielding the Dipper,
Yin-Dipper, Yang-Dipper, Perverse-Dipper, Rectified-Dipper,
Seizing the Dipper, capturing the Dipper, executing the Dipper.
*(Steps of the Dipper to execute and behead ghosts.)*

Restraining the Dipper,
*(Visualizing the Seven Stars in step-form to suppress malevolence,
Forming the Dipper’s proper shape as a net,
Covering the prison of the Grand Duke to bind and restrain ghosts and spirits below.)*

Containing the Dipper,
*(Encompassing the Seven Stars within the heart and abdomen,
Illuminating the Five Viscera.)*

Expanding the Dipper,
*(Filling heaven and earth to dispel demons and evil.)*

And other such methods.
Together with the *Yugbu Steps*, they perfected the Rectification Methods,
Instantly stirring winds and rains as heaven and earth obeyed their will.

The Jade Emperor of the Golden Gate, Great Peace, and Supreme Dao
Granted them armies of thirty million soldiers,
Along with the *Rectification Talismans of the Three Generals* and the *Yugbu Steps*,
And the *Twenty-Four Stages of Step Prohibitions*—
Instantly capable of salvation techniques.
When merits were complete, they ascended to their celestial abode,
As if dwelling within the grottoes.

Those who received the talismans wielded them as thought answered hand,
Divine power manifesting instantly.
Thus, they could ascend to the heavens,
Serving beside the Sage Lord of the Golden Gate,
As middle-ranking Daoist generals,
Guarding the palaces,
Pursuing and subduing demon kings,
Recording the Three Officials’ affairs.

They could also protect those who practiced the talismans and step-prohibitions.
Humans who refined their hearts and thoughts to manifest these powers
Mastered the Three Diagrams.
*(The first two diagrams: one encompassing the body, the second deploying its use,
The third encompassing the shadow—
Their essence lies in visualization,
Entering and exiting the heart and kidneys.)*

When applied, the body lengthened by an inch,
Emerging from the heart and kidneys,
Gradually growing to eighty-one *zhang*,
Leading armies of thirty million soldiers,
Or capturing malevolent crowds,
Or entering through the brow to heal Five Viscera ailments—
The body lengthening by an inch within the heart and kidneys,
Calming the Five Viscera and hundred vessels.

Guarding steadied the Five Viscera.
*(The resolve: day and night, Tang General entered the left kidney,
Ge General entered the right kidney,
Zhou General entered the heart,
Pacifying the Five Viscera and hundred vessels,
Eradicating all demonic, malevolent *qi*, and disease roots.)*

This is the origin of the *Posterior Three Elements*.
*(At the time of the Posterior Sage Lord—Qin’s First Emperor—
In the second year of *More Begins*, July 7th,
Descending upon Taibai Mountain in Shu.)*

The Three Middle Element Generals were originally appointed by the Sage Lord of Great Peace.
They were granted the rank of *Daylight Ascension Generals*,
Capable of traversing heaven and earth, water and fire,
Encompassing the extremes of heaven and earth,
Or entering the human body,
Dispelling evil and protecting the rectified—
Like frost before the sun.
Thus, they could always exert influence over those of virtuous conduct.

When confronting malevolent ghosts and spirits,
They preserved the body and aided the state,
Their talismans fulfilling their merits,
Their resolve fixed upon ascension—
Within the heart, never lost—
Thus, they could firm their resolve,
And wisdom arose within them.

This must be done in the Middle Element,
With united strength to save others.
*(Humans, through talismans and orders, command the generals and soldiers,
Rescuing those in peril, curing diseases,
Mountains and seas as lips and teeth,
Poisons, fierce beasts, dragons, and water calamities—
All are delivered.)*

This is the function of *united strength*—
When humans and spirits alike gain merit through talismans,
It is called *salvation*.
Those who attain salvation rejoice,
Knowing the Dao’s transformation.
This is the benevolent function of the Three Middle Element Generals.

The Three Middle Element Generals first emerged in the age of the Human Sovereign,
And through the Dao, moved heaven to bestow upon them,
Protecting the Human Sovereign.

Later, when the Three Generals were first appointed as replacements,
It was the Posterior Sage Lord who petitioned the Supreme Dao Lord,
And conferred them upon Zhang Daoling—
Thus, it is said they were first appointed by the Posterior Sage Lord.
*(As recorded in the *Scripture of the Dao’s Mysterious Authenticity*:*
The Three Middle Element Generals, three in number,
Before the ancient Human Sovereign,
Were bestowed by the Supreme Dao Lord, the Primordial Sovereign of the Void,
Upon Taiyi,
Who became their commander,
Leading the Taiyi Palace.)*

This is the benevolent petition of the Posterior Sage Lord to the Jade Sovereign,
To summon from the lower realm those who have attained the Dao,
As replacements for the first three.

The previous three attained the Dao by descending from the **ascended-true** position
To the lower realm, thus replacing the Three Elements’ ranks.

The Posterior Sage Lord petitioned to enter the lower realm,
Establishing the **Orthodox One** (正一) for protection,
Assisting those who have received the Dao,
And binding all **structured hearts** (结心).
Using seals and finger gestures,
Following the **sacred talismans** (符箓) and their commands,
Those who receive the talismans today
Can make **structured laws** (结法) step in accordance,
And verify their efficacy immediately.

The sons of the Dao, after receiving the Way,
Gain the **gestures** (诀) and follow their teacher’s precepts in movement, dwelling, sitting, and repose,
Enduring like the **Forgetful Sitting** (坐忘),
Binding and twisting the **gestures** (捻诀).
Seals (印) are stored in thought as the diagram shows.
After one year, they are free from illness,
And can instantly dispel evil to aid others.
After two years, they repel soldiers,
And malevolent ghosts, fierce beasts, all submit.
After three years, they remove the **deadly records** (死籍),
And in the fourth year, they restore the **Orthodox One’s true essence** (正一地真).
By the fifth year, they achieve **divine penetration** (神通),
With godly power unsurpassed—
Their fingers alone can subdue the wicked, who all bow in submission.
Their hearts must not act rashly.
When moving, they must be those who harm themselves,
Or those they cannot avoid.
They must grasp the **root gesture** (本诀),
And in secret, visualize the **Battle Robe** (斗衣) upon their body,
The **Battle Fish** (斗魒) in their fingers’ motion,
As the Three Middle Element Generals
Command armies of three hundred million each,
And strike down water, fire, lions, and poisonous snakes one by one—
They must all be subdued by the heart,
And die without harming oneself.
If they do not submit,
Twist the **wicked talisman** (凶恶刀支),
And command it to cut and pierce again—
They will respond by vomiting blood and dying.
Recite in secret the **Five Phases Incantation** (五行咒):
Metal conquers wood, water extinguishes fire, and so forth.
This is the **Yin** method—
Caution must be taken, and it must not be recklessly employed.
The Daoist must resort to it only when necessary.
Again, the **gesture of command** (使诀) is taken
From the second joint of the left thumb, near the left side.
*(Near the left means the joint must be close to the left edge.)*
But it governs the Three Elements, Three Divisions, and Nine Generals,
Totally overseeing the second joint.
The **Upper Element** (上元) governs the **Rectified Heart** (正心),
And the **Lower Element** (下元) is on the left—
Always store and apply it as depicted in the diagram.
For men and women, the **gesture of command** (诀) is the left hand for men,
And the right hand for women.
Always store and apply it without confusion or recklessness,
*(Without letting illusions deceive the heart, without wrongly applying it to the virtuous.)*
Instantly attaining the **Heavenly True** (天真),
Evil and poison—
*(Evil: the malevolent kings and demonic qi. Poison: serpents, dragons, ghosts, and beasts.)*
—must stand in awe and respect,
And benevolence must be extended—
*(Those who follow the Dao, using talismanic arts,
Constantly relieve the poor, the sick, and those in distress,
Exerting compassionate power to rescue people from calamity,
Practicing benevolent virtue and teaching the worthy.)*
Divine penetration enables the eyes to endure and the body to firm.
The **Master Guangcheng** (广成子) instructed the Yellow Sovereign:
*"If you wish to seek the True,
Nothing surpasses firming the body.
If you wish to firm the body,
Nothing surpasses divine penetration.
After divine penetration,
*(To attain vision of the gods, there are six stages:
1. Receiving the talismanic method.
2. Cleansing the heart and guarding the secrets—
Do not divulge them to the unworthy.
3. Obtaining the True Scripture,
Transmitted by a True Teacher.
4. Grasping the essential principles fully.
5. Acquiring this **invitation** (引),
A dedicated practitioner who enters the gate to see the Dao.
6. Once seeing the gate and path,
Practicing the method,
Gaining the **gesture** (诀),
All applications will be without error.)*
These six stages of practice
All hinge on the **gesture** (诀)—
Without this **gesture**, the other five matters are useless.
In the present age, those who receive the talismanic method
Reach its peak in the **Upper Purity** (上清),
And combine **teachings of sound and doctrine** (声教) with fasting and reciting the Dao,
Their incense and flames never ceasing,
Their hearts kept pure without retreat,
Fulfilling all four prior matters,
And practicing the **Forgetful Sitting** (老一生) for a lifetime—
Yet none have attained it.
All must seek a **Clear Teacher** (明师),
Who transmits the **invitation gesture** (引诀) and **seal** (印),
Only then can divine penetration be achieved.
Once divine penetration is attained,
But the Dao is not yet realized,
Realizing the Dao requires the **Clear Teacher’s further gesture** (明师再诀),
To **degree the heart and spirit** (度心神).
The heart and spirit must not rise to idle thoughts,
*(Forgetting to add protective measures for oneself and others.)*
Only then can one **degree the Dao** (度道),
Attaining realization—
Many have ascended in broad daylight, their dwellings plucked up.
As for the **Heavenly Masters** (天师), **Xu Xun** (许逊), **Wang Chang** (王长), and the **Emperor’s younger brothers** (尹子兄弟),
And the disciples of the **Three Sovereigns of ancient times** (上古三皇之徒),
They all plucked up entire cities and departed—
None failed to do so
Because of the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Three Elements**, the **Nine Generals of the Five Virtues and Six Regulations** (五德六纪等将军),
And the **Seven Stars’ Essence and Five Battles’ Host of Stars** (七星精五斗众星),
As well as the **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water** (天地水三官),
And all the **divine ranks and true immortals** (众神众真仙灵) and **generals and soldiers** (将军吏兵)
Recorded in the *Scripture of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (《金锁流珠》) **fifteen volumes**—
Those who fully master these methods
Can ascend in broad daylight,
Or pluck up their dwellings and depart together.

In ancient times, during the **Zhou dynasty** (周时),
A **Hu deity** (西国胡神) from the Western lands attained the Dao—
This was when the **Supreme Sage Lord** (太上老君) instructed **Master Wu Cheng** (务成子),
And taught the **Hu King** (胡王).
Again entrusting the **body’s framework and essential gestures** (托身纲诀之法),
He became the **Rightmost True Person of the Mysterious** (右玄真人),
Serving the **Supreme Sage Lord of the Great Equality, Golden Threshold, and Mysterious Origin** (大平金阙玄元后圣玉皇帝上道君),
Also attaining **degree** (度) through this method.
With an **equal and balanced heart** (平等心),
He possessed the **virtue of neither wrong nor idle application** (不非不妄之德).
His name was **Earth Geography** (地理),
And his strength could match a thousand men.

The Three Sons of Earth Sovereign—Earth Monarchs—
and the Five Sons of Earth Kings,
three brothers of equal rank,
possessed mighty strength, courage, and relentless vigor,
with wisdom surpassing mortals.
Since they bore no name, they were ennobled as the **Three Great Daoist Marshals of the Lower Primordial**,
commanding armies to guard and protect those who attained **degree** and received **fa箓**.

*Note: The Later Sage now replaces these three, thus taking their surname as his own,
and their former titles as their given names.*

The present **Three Marshals of the Lower Primordial**—
surnamed **Li**, **Huang**, and **Wang**—
are the names of those three predecessors.

If mortals seek the Dao without knowing the origins of the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordial Three Great Marshals**,
not one in ten thousand can attain it.
Yet even now, those who glimpse the Dao
shall fulfill their eon’s measure.

*Note: When the three Marshals complete their term,
the Later Sage replaces them—
the Li, Huang, and Wang—
and the Later Sage’s Lord seals them as Marshals,
replacing their former ranks.*

When the former ascended as **Heavenly True Ones**,
those who followed assumed their roles,
leading and protecting those with resolve in cultivation,
and governing the **Lower Primordial** beings of earth and water,
as well as malevolent spirits, dragons, ghosts, and demons
who act without righteousness.

*Note: All things with qi crave life and fear death,
constantly seeking the Dao of life within them.
Wicked and cruel beings, who act in demonic ways,
using beasts, serpents, and dragons—
all must be exterminated and annihilated.
Whether human, spirit, dragon, or ghost,
all are judged and destroyed by law.
This is the command of the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordial Nine Great Marshals**.*

Their orders consist of six decrees:
1. **Subdue celestial demons.**
2. **Restrain evil men** who do not walk the righteous path,
   nor defy sovereigns and masters.
3. **Always protect the Dao and its laws,**
   rescuing those in suffering, poverty, and distress.
4. **Tame dragons, ghosts, and demons**,
   forbidding false sorcery—
   those who transgress shall be executed.
5. **Respond to the sincere hearts of those seeking the Dao,**
   regardless of noble or common birth, male or female.

*Note: The Great Dao does not discriminate between high and low.
If one has Daoic nature, a sincere heart, and receives the **fa箓** for cultivation,
their merit shall be acknowledged.
The Nine Marshals shall protect such individuals and their families
from all magical calamities.
They shall ensure no misfortune befall them,
and all suffering shall be transcended through **degree**.*

6. **Constantly guard the Perfected Ones**,
   whether in motion, rest, sitting, or lying,
   shielding them from external demons.
They shall swiftly report urgent matters,
submitting petitions and memorials to the Celestial Throne,
ensuring harmony with Heaven’s will,
rewarding virtue without failing in ritual propriety.
When their merit is complete, they shall uplift those of resolve in the Dao,
granting them **degree** and ascension in broad daylight,
with the power to depart their dwellings.
Those who attain Daoist transcendence
shall reside in the **Three Pure Ones**.

The **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordial Nine Marshals**
shall each ascend to the rank of **Supreme True Daoist of the Great Primordial and Great Extremes**,
following the succession of the **Three Sovereigns’ Three Primordial Marshals**.

*Note: "Ascend" means attaining the rank of Daoist True Ones.
"Replace" means each takes the rightful position of the three who preceded them.*

Thus, even within the **Release School**,
they are secretly called **Buddhas**.
The method of **sealing with the seal**—
this is the **heart-seal**.
This diagram speaks of **invoking, drawing, and manipulating the talismans**.

**Degree** is achieved through an **equal heart**.
*Note: The heart attains **degree** through equality,
not through receiving **degree** in the form of robes or garments—
such things are futile.*

**No haste, no harm.**
*Note: The True Heart is without deceit, without haste, without jealousy—
this is the nature of the True Person.*

**No desire.**
*Note: Those who love and cling to things,
when they obtain them, rejoice;
when they do not, they grow angry.
The True Person’s nature is free from such attachments—
gain and loss, possession and deprivation—
the heart’s thoughts are inherently without,
thus called the True Person.*

**Able to practice the Three Grades.**
*Note: Firming the body is the first,
communing with spirits the second,
and attaining **degree** of the heart is the third.
True Persons constantly practice these three grades.*

**The body itself contains the spirit.**
*Note: The body and spirit are inherently complete,
like an image contained within a mirror—
when invoked, it responds as a substitute.
Like the image within the diagram,
nothing remains unanswered.*

**All affairs are made manifest.**
*Note: When the True Person’s heart conceives a thought,
the object is immediately obtained,
and all malevolence vanishes.*

The **Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water**
all share the same heart.

*Note: Those who cultivate the Supreme Dao to become True Persons,
with hearts of compassion and boundless salvation,
harmonize with the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water,
generating and restraining all things,
fulfilling the transformations of ten thousand beings.*

The **Three Marshals of the Lower Primordial**
first emerged in the **Highest Antiquity**.
In the **Earth Sovereign’s era**,
the **Nine Princes**—
*Note: The Nine Princes, born of three mothers—*
learned the Dao alongside their parents.

In the time of the **Supreme Sage Lord**,
he was called the **Great Dao Lord of the Five Spirits**,
or the **Supreme Master of the Boundless**,
or the **Nameless Lord**.

*Note: According to the *Inner Transmission of the Supreme Sage Lord*,
the Supreme Sage Lord, born before Heaven and Earth,
surnamed Li, named Yuan, with the title **Wenchu Tianwang**.
Before the era of **Pangu**,
he was called the **Primordial Heavenly Venerable, the Void Sovereign, the Great Dao Lord**.
In the era of Pangu, he was called the **Supreme Dao Lord**.
In the **Heavenly Sovereign’s era**, he was called the **Highest Sage Lord**.
In the **Earth Sovereign’s era**, he was called the **Nameless Lord**.
In the **Human Sovereign’s era**, he was called the **Ever-Present Lord**.

It was then that the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordial Nine Great Marshals**
were first established—
all were those whom the Later Sage’s Lord, in past and present,
had **degreed** and ennobled as Marshals,
to guide later seekers of the Dao,
strengthening themselves while saving others from sickness,
and teaching those with Daoic nature.*

He expounded the *Earth Interior Classic* in fourteen chapters
*Note: This is precisely the *Golden Fa Book*,
discussing the methods of **swallowing the sun and expelling the moon**,
as well as the principles of **correctly stepping on the Big Dipper’s robes** and **consuming the stars’ qi**.*

The Earth Sovereign practiced it for fourteen years
and attained the Dao.
The Nine Princes also practiced it,
and were ennobled as Marshals.

After fourteen years of cultivation,
the Earth Sovereign ascended in broad daylight to the **Qingwei Heaven**,
and was titled **Xian Qing**.

「The Nine Princes followed their father-king in cultivation for fifteen years,
and likewise ascended in broad daylight to the **Celestial Palace**,
their ranks ennobled as **Marshal of the Long***.
*Note: The Marshal’s position is to guard and perpetually protect.*

The **Highest Venerable Sage-Lao** originally decreed:
*"The Great Dao produces One,
One produces Two,
Two produces Three.
This is its beginning—
the Upper Element* governs celestial phenomena*.
*Note: Celestial phenomena include the sun, moon, and starry hosts,
as well as the officials, palaces, gates, and celestial enclosures,
the sources of the rivers and clouds and mists,
and the patterns of rain, snow, frost, and **qi**.*

The Middle Element governs humans and spirits*.
*Note: Humans and spirits include divine dragons, ghostly essences,
ferocious beasts, and sacred birds of the kind.*

The Lower Element governs the earth and water realms*.
*Note: The earth and water realms include dragons and sea serpents,
fish and scaled creatures, and armored beings of the kind.*

Ten thousand spirits, a hundred thousand souls—
all are under the dominion of the Lower Element’s Three Marshals.

With the **Correct Dao** bestowed upon their armies,
each commands thirty million troops,
their bodies stretching nine *zhang* long—or three *zhang*,
wearing red headbands and towering caps,
or yellow headbands and towering caps,
clad in armor and wielding swords,
they oversee the **Earth Officials**,
reverse the records of calamity, sickness, and death*,
and register names for rebirth.

Then **Xuan Qing** commands them to recite the **Lower Element’s incantation***,
*Note: The Lower Element’s Three Marshals’ incantation,
also known as the "One on the Left Edge, One is Left" incantation.*
*and to wear the **Lower Element’s talisman diagram**,
as well as the **Ghostly Spear’s talisman diagram**,
and to tread the **Earth Measure**,
and the **Yujia Step—three steps, nine traces**—in its essentials,
and to chant the **Five Phases Mutual Annihilation Spells** in eighteen verses.
Each month, perform this three times.
Thus, they naturally avert disasters and repel calamities,
ward off death and invite life,
enter armies and waters,
enter fire and sickness,
enter mountains and distant travels.
In places where they pass through,
if there are malevolent men, evil spirits,
poisonous snakes, fierce beasts,
or demonic and malevolent essences,
all submit themselves without harboring harmful intent.

Their bodies attain longevity,
and their merits are fulfilled in truth*.
*Note: This refers to the previous statement:
one year averts non-combat disasters,
two years averts military disasters.*

The Sage-Lao said:
*"The Upper Element averts celestial demons,
controls the Heavenly Officials,
subdues the starry hosts,
and wields the **Flying Heavenly Rites**,
worn upon the head.
The Later Sage has revealed the **Upper Element Marshal’s Command Words**,
and the **Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper’s Nine Essences**—
the Command Words say:
‘Upper Element Marshal **Tang Qing**,
the lawmaster of the **Uppermost Clarity**,
the sun, moon, and starry hosts revolve without pause,
the Three Elements and Northern Dipper are formless by nature,
the Heavenly Officials banish demonic marshals,
the Dao’s **qi** is clear and bright,
the starry destinies align with **Xuan Qing**,
and the Marshal steps upon the stars,
his spirit and vital essence move together,
together they ride the dragon,
the **Supreme One** comes to greet,
reverently ascending to the **Celestial Palace**,
the Later Sage’s domain,
assisting and supporting the Later Sage,
together as **Marshal of the Long**,
fulfilling the **Flying Heavenly Rites**.
*Note: This is the talisman to be used before stepping forward.*

The Later Sage’s **Three Officials Command Words of the Northern Dipper** are also revealed,
found in the *Golden Lock Flowing Pearl—[□] Flying Heavenly Rites* chapter,
and in the *Great Possession Supreme Elixir Hidden Book*,
in two places. Again, there are the **Middle Element**,
which averts human demons,
controls the **Yang Officials** and military disasters,
and the **nets of gold, wood, water, fire, earth, and Heaven**,
as well as the calamities of speech and tongue,
and the malevolent and evil spirits and humans.
There are **seven vital essences and three souls’ Command Words and spells**,
*Note: The spells are found in the *Supreme Hidden Book*,
and in the upper scroll of *Golden Lock Flowing Pearl*.
The Five Phases Mutual Annihilation spells are as follows: gold subdues wood, wood extinguishes fire.*

The Later Sage’s **Nine Essences Command Words for Subduing the Body and Flying Steps**—
the **Earth Measure talisman with nine symbols**—
*Note: Found in the *Supreme Elixir Hidden Book*.*
are also revealed.

Again, the **Lower Element** averts earth demons,
controls the **Yin Officials** to keep them from disturbing my body,
and the cultivators’ **three souls and seven vital essences**,
following **Xuan Qing’s** body,
together they tread upon the **Heavenly and Earthly Measures and Rites**,
circling ten thousand times, turning a hundred thousand times,
transforming and manifesting in truth,
entering and exiting rivers and mountains,
divine spirits and souls reverently escort them.
All rely upon the **Lower Element’s Three Marshals**,
leading the Three Divisions of troops,
driving the **Thunder Official**,
commanding the winds and clouds with thunderous roars,
clearing the front and sweeping the rear,
successful in every endeavor,
thousandfold in their schemes,
all without fail.
Humans and spirits fear and respect them,
dragons and beasts obey their commands,
ever-present whether seated or reclining,
never without effect.
Keep this secret.*

The Later Sage instructed the **Heavenly Master**:
*"The Upper Element, Middle Element, and Lower Element,
each has Three Marshals.
Draw their true forms in miniature,
like talisman diagrams to be worn or carried.
*Note: The Upper Element is worn on the crown or headband,
the Middle Element is tied behind the left elbow,
and the Lower Element is tied behind the right elbow.
Retrieve them from the pouch when needed,
and wear them on the head or behind the elbows—left or right.
The diagrams for the Middle and Lower Elements are similar to those used in the two talisman diagrams,
and are deployed in battle accordingly.
If using the Upper Element diagram,
it is like the **Containing Prong** diagram—
deploy it as such.
If not in use, wear it as the **Containing Shadow** diagram.
To seek longevity, use the **Yujia Step**.
*Note: The Yujia Step is performed regardless of day or month;
do it at leisure.*

If someone in your household falls ill with speech-related afflictions,
perform it on their behalf.
Do not exceed three days,
and the illness will naturally dissipate.
The more repetitions, the quicker the effect—
especially urgent for water and fire calamities.
Keep this secret, do not pass it to unworthy individuals.

If there are disasters,
perform the **Yujia Step**,
which can dispel ten thousand calamities.
After completing the **Yujia Step**,
recite the spells.
*Note: There are two spells.
The first spell dispels disasters and seeks longevity,
found in the first volume of *Golden Lock Flowing Pearl*,
in eighteen verses—recite them all.
The second spell commands the Six Palaces of the **Yin Officials**,
found later in the text.
The spell commanding the Six Palaces of the **Yin Officials** is also revealed by the Later Sage.*

The spell says:
*"I am a disciple of the Highest Venerable Sage,
and subordinate to the Six Heavens.
The Six Heavens’ palaces are under my command.
Not only are they under my command,
but they are also under the Highest Venerable Sage’s dominion.
I know the names of the Six Heavens’ palace gates,
thus I attain longevity.
If anyone dares to violate this,
the Highest Venerable Sage will behead you.
This spell is not dependent on the **Yujia Step**,
but should be recited once or twice daily,
after cultivation is complete,
outside the quiet door.
It extraordinarily averts calamities and harm,
protects the body and household,
and benefits those who recite it with faith and respect—
their lives will not perish."*

The Highest Venerable Sage-Lao instructed the **Supreme Primordial Sage**.*」

The annotation states:
*"The Supreme Primordial Sage is the Sage of Summer, Yu."*

It is said:
*"You, my attendant, uphold the true teachings—
all the immortals below know the principles of origin and dissolution.
Even the celestial immortals of the highest and middle grades
have yet to master the passage through birth and death.
Now, listen well:
I shall instruct you one by one,
teaching those who seek immortality
how to transcend birth and death.

All beings of the lower realm—
regardless of noble or humble birth—
originate from the trigrams Three and Five.
*Annotation: Three refers to the Three Primordials; Five refers to the Five Phases.*
Mortals all arise from Three and Five,
and receive the sovereign *qi* of the Five Phases.
They also perish from Three and Five,
*Annotation: When one turns inward, they receive the Three Primordials’ *qi*;
when the Five Phases begin to manifest,
they belong to the categories of Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, and Earth.*
As the revolving years and seasonal stems shift,
the body experiences flourishing and decline.
The sovereign *qi* of the Three Primordials brings forth
auspicious stars and celestial guardians for protection.
If the Three *qi* wane,
calamity descends to subdue the self—
Metal and Wood clash,
Water and Fire counter one another—
and disaster strikes the body,
while blessings do not manifest.

To comprehend Three and Five
is the gateway to the *Yujia Step*.
Thus, one enters the Dao of eternal life and non-death.
This method is profound and secret—
it must not be transmitted to the unworthy.
If recklessly transmitted, the master descends from the immortal ranks,
and the disciple faces retribution.

The Three Primordials govern life,
circulating the *qi* of Heaven and Earth.
*Annotation: The Upper Primordial governs celestial phenomena;
the Lower Primordial governs earth and water.*
The enlightened one.
*Annotation: The enlightened one harmonizes Heaven and Earth.*
Humans also embody the Three Primordials.
*Annotation: Moreover, the Three Primordials command nine generals,
mirroring Heaven, originating from Earth, and harmonizing with humanity.
Humans possess nine orifices,
through which the Three Primordials’ *qi* is inhaled and exhaled.*
Humans are formed by the Five Phases
and are also subdued by them.
*Subdued* means *dissolution*.
To master the Five Phases—
*Annotation: Mastery refers to the *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū* (Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl)
First Scroll’s eighteenth spell,
as well as the *Yujia* earthly cycles.*
—is to master the calamities of the Three Primordials,
the Five Phases, and the mutual subjugation of Heaven, Earth, and humanity.

Next comes the *Liúzhū* (Flowing Pearl)
Middle Scroll’s *Feibù Tiāngāng* (Flying Step, Heavenly Halberd) spell:
*'Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth—
the Five Phases propel one another.
Seven stars radiant, the Heavenly Halberd’s might supreme.'*
When practiced for a year,
one attains non-death and stands in eternal life.
This is the Highest Sage’s instruction to the Sage-King.*

To the right: the *San Yuan Liúzhū Yǐn* (Three Primordials, Flowing Pearl Preface)
Five Phases Supplementary Transmission.

*End of the Fifth Scroll of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Preface.*
*Beginning of the Sixth Scroll of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Preface.*

Composed and annotated by the successive generations of:
The Grand Sovereign of the Total Perfection Dao—
Zhang Daoling, Zhao Sheng, Wang Chang, the Marshal of the Five Commands,
Li Zhongfu, Mao Ying, Xu Yufu, and others.
The Daoist immortal Li Chunfeng annotated and preserved
the laws of the Zhou General’s diagram."*

The Celestial Master said: *"Why is Zhou General placed last in the scrolls?*
The Most High Laozi spoke: *Because Zhou General is the master of the human heart, and thus the heart is the sovereign spirit of the body. Therefore, Zhou General was composed first as the foremost of the Three Mid-Autumn Generals in the *Flowing Pearl* scrolls. However, according to the *Zheng San Yuan Jing*, the Mid-Autumn Upper Division begins with Tang General, followed by Ge General, and then Zhou General. Now, though arranged first by the Most High’s decree, its application must follow the order prescribed in the *San Yuan Zheng Jing*.

The method’s purpose is to impart the Most High’s oral transmission—the essential formula of Mid-Autumn’s core technique. First, tread the *Ji* [纪] five times, then disperse into the *Yu Bu* [禹步], three steps with nine traces. Upon completion, adjust the clothing seven times, meditating as prescribed. Then, first visualize Tang General alone within the left kidney, emerging from there—initially only one inch tall, then expanding to eight *zhang*—commanding thirty million troops to a specific province, county, village, or household to address a matter. *Note: This may involve seizing malevolent spirits, a malefactor, or performing exorcisms to cure illness, or confronting malevolent spirits, officials, or those plotting against you. Visualize accordingly, and one image shall suffice for later use.*

The Later Sage-King instructed Master Zhang: *The Three Elements’ method—note: the Upper, Middle, and Lower Elements govern Heaven, Earth, and Humanity—is for cultivating the Dao, safeguarding one’s family, and subduing malevolence. *Note: ‘Malevolence’ refers to humans; ‘evil’ refers to spirits.* It must not be used for personal aggrandizement but also to rescue others from all calamities. One may then tread the *Ji* three times, disperse into the *Yu Bu*, and adjust the clothing. Upon completion, recite the incantation: ‘I was born of my parents, raised among the vulgar…’ *This incantation appears in the *Di Ji Jing* as the pre-incantation. The formula is on the second joint of the left hand’s first finger.*

Laozi said: *Zhou General is the human heart-spirit. If one practices the Dao to attain spiritual communion, the moment intention arises, action follows—no need for ritualized stepping or complete formalities. *Note: ‘Complete formalities’ means first treading the *Ji*, then the *Yu Bu*, adjusting the clothing, and finally pinching the formula while reciting to manifest. The first stage of cultivation requires these steps, for though beginners may receive scriptures and complete the rites—*note: receiving scriptures and rites is from the *Zhengyi* tradition’s Five Methods of Shangqing*—they must still practice stepping to attain spiritual efficacy. *Note: ‘Stepping’ refers to the Heavenly Halberd; ‘treading’ refers to the Earthly Measure.* Only then does one achieve communion with spirits. *Note: In ancient times, Liu Jiang’s wife, Lady Fan, secretly practiced the Heavenly Halberd and Earthly Measure for fourteen years without her husband’s knowledge. She would act only when he was absent, even during his official duties as county magistrate. One day, a divine being descended on five-colored clouds, accompanied by twenty-four attendants—four celestial boys and four celestial girls—and spoke to Lady Fan: ‘Your merit is complete, your power attained. Now you may act by thought alone—what do you desire?’ Lady Fan replied: ‘I wish to make water stand still and a riding tiger not harm.’ The divine being said: ‘A small matter.’*"*

The divine being then imparted to Lady Fan the method to **halt water** and the **talisman to subdue tigers**, saying:
*"Practice this, and you shall see results immediately. Continue your diligent cultivation for another fourteen years, and you may ascend to heaven when you will—or remain in the world, rich and noble."* Indeed, later, the couple ascended together as **Celestial Immortals**.

When one’s mind is focused, responses manifest instantly—**heaven and earth resonate in harmony**. If one has not yet attained communion with spirits, the practice must be performed with **ritual stepping and treading**, fully observing the diagrams and incantations, visualizing the spirit attuned to the **sacred robe**, and chanting as one acts. One must also **keep the General Zhou in mind**.

When the heart is fully devoted, communion is achieved. With a single thought, the spirit arises, and the mind aligns effortlessly—**all wishes are fulfilled without delay, in the blink of an eye**.

The **Celestial Master** received the diagrams and methods, which have five applications, all shared by the **Three Generals**:

1. **For personal cultivation outside**: To prolong life, one visualizes the General and retreats to mountain forests, sacred halls, or Daoist ritual grounds, dispatching malevolent humans and ghosts to guard and protect, ensuring no harm befalls one.

2. **When away from the grounds**: One visualizes the General returning to the ritual site to inspect and repel human and ghostly afflictions.

3. **To repel malevolent and rebellious forces**.

4. **For healing and emergency aid**: By focusing one’s intent, one treats illnesses, cuts off ghostly torment, and achieves immediate resolution—**fulfilling the will in an instant**.

5. **To assist the state and sovereign**: Capturing criminals, rescuing righteous Daoist friends wrongfully harmed.

These five methods must **not** be recklessly revealed to those without Daoist resolve. Do not speak of them lightly—**misuse brings calamity upon the Nine Ancestors**, not just oneself.

The **General Zhou’s Stepping Halberd Method** states:
*"Without stepping, none may act; all actions must follow the Stepping Halberd’s order."* With deep practice over years, one naturally attains communion with spirits and divine responsiveness—**no longer bound by ritual stepping and treading**; a single thought suffices. **Heaven and earth align as its framework; spirits move at its command.**

In ancient times, **Yu the Great’s sister, the Flying Immortal**,—*[Note: Some texts name her]*—
witnessed her brother practice the Stepping Halberd and learned it herself. **After one year, her minor ailments vanished.** *[Note: Some texts say all diseases were cured. This is the original text’s definitive account from the Great Immortal of the Cavern.]*
**After two years, her body grew light.**
**After three years, she entered the military to repel armies.**

The **Fourth Year**, she was enrolled in the **Celestial Register of Immortals**.
The **Fifth Year**, she attained **spirit communion**.
The **Sixth Year**, her **Dao/Way arts were perfected**.
The **Seventh Year**, she could **become invisible**.
The **Eighth Year**, she **walked upon water**.
The **Ninth Year**, she ascended to the **Pure Court of the Middle**, ennobled as **Lady Saint Immortal**, akin to the rank of **Immortal Official**.

All these follow this diagram—its method is most wondrous.
The **secret lies in binding the third knuckle of the left middle finger** with five-colored silk.
When done, **attach it to the garment**, and visualize **General Zhou** as per the diagram, to command **soldiers, officers, lions, and fierce flames** to burn the dwellings of malevolent ghosts and bandits.
**In all matters, visualize as per the diagram**—this ensures divine efficacy.

**Visualize General Ge’s method**:
The **Celestial Master** said: *"This General is the Right Division General—why is he ranked second?"*
**Laozi, the Venerable Celestial Sovereign**, spoke: *"Because General Zhou is the Forefront General, belonging to Yang, aligning with the Yang sequence—thus, he is first in the Yang order. If aligned with Yin sequence, he is second, fulfilling the principle of paired numbers."*

General **Tang** resides to the left, also belonging to Yang sequence—thus, he is third.
*[Note: According to the Master’s tradition, one first visualizes General Tang, then General Ge, then General Zhou. Now, ranking General Zhou first signifies the supremacy of the heart-mind. Hence, in the lane, he is first, corresponding to the image of the **Upper Primordial Spirit General**, the Human Spirit General. If used, General Tang must be placed foremost—this is the verified method of the Pine Invocation.]*

Again, referring to the *Three Primordial Elbow-Post Divine Book*, it states:
*"General Tang is first, belonging to the Upper Primordial.
Next is General Ge, second, belonging to Yin sequence and the Middle Primordial.
Then General Zhou, third, belonging to the Lower Primordial.*
Why do these two accounts differ?"*

The *Secret Record of the Highest Venerable Lord Lao* (*Gunzhongji*) states:

*"If one does not employ magical techniques, one relies instead upon the Three Primordial [Daoist] methods. General Tang is then placed above, as first, proceeding in accordance with the natural sequence of Heavenly Dao/Way and numbers. If one practices and utilizes all methods—rewarding the virtuous and punishing the wicked, acting throughout the world, and summoning ghosts and spirits—then General Zhou is first, residing within the heart and belonging to the Lower Primordial. This is for the sake of humanity, and it is also the Lower Primordial’s central method. Thus, General Zhou is placed foremost, acting contrary to Heaven’s Dao/Way, assaulting malevolent rebels, and conferring rewards upon the virtuous, enabling one to follow the *Liuzhu* [method] with certainty and efficacy.

If one adheres to the principles of Yin-Yang, the *Divine Physician’s Godly and Immortal Prescriptions of the Highest Unity* (*Taiyi Taiyi Shenxian Fang*) states: 'The left represents the **kidney** (*shèn*), the right represents the **Gate of Life** (*mìngmén*).' One may then follow this directive accordingly.

Moreover, General Tang governs the left kidney, while General Ge commands the male **Gate of Life** (*mìngmén*). Thus, when employing the *Bùgāng* [method] to invoke the generals, they are positioned as the second. Each leads three hundred million soldiers to guard the Gate of Life, with the **Western Guardians** (*Xīfāng Wèichén*) following behind to protect the **Mysterious Body** (*Xuànshēn*). When deploying from the right, one follows the *Bùgāng* [method] as illustrated [in the diagram]. When advancing with the diagram’s soldiers—*Bùgāng*—one invokes them as shown in the talismanic gestures. There is no failure in this.

**Bùgāng** [method].
*[Note: The **General Ge’s Step** (*Bùgāng*) is performed with the right foot first, symbolizing Yin. This is the standard procedure at the outset; do not deviate from it. This method differs from those of Generals Zhou and Tang.]*

Later, the **Sage Emperor** (*Hòushèng Jūn*) instructed **Zhang the Celestial Master** (*Tiānshī Zhāng*): 'Perform the **Bùgāng** [method], then swallow the talismans, and afterward practice the **Bùgāng** [method] again. There are three talismans—Upper, Middle, and Lower.'

The **Highest Venerable** (*Tàishàng*) commanded **Mìngwén Lìng**: 'First perform the **Three Primordial Bùgāng** [method], then invoke the talismans and dispatch them accordingly.'

In ancient times, there was a Daoist named **Liu Gen** (*Liú Gēn*), who habitually practiced the **Three Primordial Step** (*sān yuán bù*). Later, it was transformed into the **Nine Progression Step** (*jiǔ jì yǔbù*). After three years of such practice, all spirits and ghosts revered him and obeyed his commands, and his power could move mountains and rivers.

One day, he was pursued by an **Idiom: County Magistrate** (*Jùnzhǔ*—*Note: County Magistrate, an ancient title for a prefectural governor*), who sought to harm him. The magistrate ordered him to appear before a ghost by day, threatening that if he refused, he would become a ghost himself. Gen was enraged; he performed the **Bùgāng** [method] in the center of the hall, borrowing the magistrate’s official seal as a talismanic token. With the talisman in hand, he invoked the **Arcade Star** (*Yùxīng*) to mark the magistrate’s native county, villages, ancestral temples, and the graves of his deceased parents and grandparents. He first summoned and bound the magistrate’s departed father and mother, sending them through the southern gate to be hung on the wall. The magistrate saw them, descended from his bed, and knelt in welcome.

Gen cursed the magistrate: 'I was born from your body, yet you, as an official, do not honor your parents. You should bring blessings to your deceased ancestors, but instead you dare to provoke the Daoist officers, ordering them to pursue and capture me here? Your life is in peril—quickly kneel and beg the Daoist officers for mercy, and I shall release you. If you do not, you will die instantly.' The magistrate repeatedly knelt and apologized to Gen, who then said: 'Go.' In a moment, both the magistrate and Gen vanished. This is the efficacy of the **Three Primordial Step** (*sān yuán bù*) of the generals."

The talisman is also bound within the middle joint of the left hand’s middle finger, all these being tied with five-colored threads for one year by those who are beginners in the Dao.

**Gen** instructed **Tang General** (Fǎtú) to say: *"The Old Lord told **Luo** (Lüo) the Daoist Master: 'The scripture commands Gen to summon the Three Generals, with Tang General as the first, presiding over the Upper Primordial (*shàng yuán*). These are all used in ordinary Daoist cultivation, and one must follow the Upper Primordial as the priority.

If there are urgent difficulties or matters of the heart, then the talisman is used to strike and subdue them. First, one must arouse the mind, then **Zhou General** (*Zhōu Jiāngjūn*) is summoned to first awaken the Lower Primordial (*xià yuán*).

I have heard the Celestial Venerable (*Tiānzūn*) say: 'Cultivation of auspicious and benevolent Dao begins with the Upper Primordial;
Rescuing and healing the sick arises from the Middle Primordial;
Striking down the wicked and rebellious originates from the Lower Primordial.'

The *Golden Locks, Flowing Pearls* (*Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū*) scripture was originally established by the Celestial Venerable, the Most High, and others, all to obstruct **heavenly demons** (*Tiān mó*), **human spirits** (*rénshén*), and **dragon ghosts** (*lóngguǐ*) from hindering Daoists in their cultivation and attainment of the Dao. Thus, the *Flowing Pearls* scripture was set forth in one hundred fifty volumes, divided into the Three Primordials. Each Primordial has fifty volumes. The number five governs the Five Phases (*wǔxíng*).*

**Annotation:** *"In the past, the Celestial Venerable instructed the Most High Dao Lord: 'Each Primordial has fifty volumes, and each Primordial governs the Five Phases—the numbers of metal, wood, water, fire, and earth. Thus, those who study the Dao, when practicing with the Flowing Pearls scripture, can transcend the Five Phases, dispel a hundred evils, harmonize with spirits, benefit the realm above (the state), protect the body in the middle (oneself), and safeguard the family below. With sincere resolve, there is no attainment they cannot achieve.'*

I am the Most High Dao Lord (*Tàishàng Lǎojūn*)."

The text is condensed and refined into ninety-one volumes,
so that beginners may find it easy to practice and swiftly grasp its principles—
all who attain the Dao and become immortals shall employ its Five Transformations.

Now, when the Highest Primordial General Tang is commanded to strike the malevolent spirits of the Western Quarter,
he first advances with the *Yǔbù* step of the Southern Quarter,
for the Highest Primordial General’s origin lies in the left kidney of man—
the left kidney corresponds to Wood.
Advancing first through Wood, he enters Fire,
then Fire enters Metal,
thus subduing and conquering the calamities of that person’s spirit-dragon and malevolent ghosts.

**Annotation:** *Here, "malefactor" (贼) refers to humans, while "spirit" (祟) refers to ghosts.*
Thus, the steps align with intent and speech,
dissolving and eliminating calamities so they never arise.

If the Highest Primordial General Tang is instead commanded to strike the malevolent spirits of the Northern Quarter,
**Annotation:** *Here, "spirit" (鬼祟) refers to ghosts, while "malefactor" (贼) refers to humans acting as malefactors,*
he first advances through the Eastern Quarter,
entering the Central Palace of Earth,
and thus strikes the Northern Quarter’s malevolent and vicious calamities—
the calamities dissolve of their own accord when spoken.

If malevolent spirits from the Southern Fire Quarter attack,
one advances through the Eastern Quarter,
entering the Northern Water Quarter,
then turns back to strike the Southern Quarter—
all such actions will align with intent and speech,
dissolving and annihilating the malevolent forces without fail.
This applies equally to the Central Quarter and the Four Seasons.

**Annotation:** *The Four Seasons (四季) here refers to the Heavenly Stems (上), specifically the combinations of 辰戌丑未.*
Should malevolent spirits appear,
they will always come from the East.
Strike them directly, and they will be eliminated—
without fail, all will proceed as desired.

This method is not merely for deploying the General of Tang alone, nor for the joint assault of Generals Ge and Zhou. This teaching only discusses the sequential deployment of troops for striking and assaulting—it is not limited to a single army but encompasses all three armies.

When finished, the Five Virtue Generals further assist in striking down Heavenly Demons. The matter is not trivial; one must sincerely uphold righteousness in heart and practice the Great Dao without flaw, thus achieving harmony of speech and intent.

The **Step of the Halter** commands the Three Generals of Dao Officials and Soldiers to lead first. When facing a great battle against enemy spirits and demons, all nine generals must be deployed—not just the three of Zhongyuan. Both Shangyuan and Xiayuan must also send their aides, as in *Han Hongtu*.

Generally, the three Zhongyuan Generals lead the charge, striking and assaulting first. This is a formidable force, capable of rescuing urgent crises, suppressing false deities and spirits causing havoc, regulating the Five Viscera, and eliminating evil while promoting goodness—without favor or bias. They are the fierce and righteous divine generals of the Dao.

Later sages further refined *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl*, removing cumbersome passages and compiling it into fifteen volumes, along with thirty additional volumes of corrected prefaces, guiding disciples into the Daoist path of the Flowing Pearl and making the way easier for later seekers.

Granted to Zhang Daoling, it clearly explains the use of the Flowing Pearl’s methods, also treasured in later scriptures. It must not be recklessly transmitted by mortals. The Celestial Master instructed King Jun in the Zhongyuan Upper Halter Step, which also includes the **Ding Halter Step** and the **Yǔ Step**—sometimes as the **Proper Halter**, sometimes as the **Ding Step**.

*The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl Canon* states that the two aides take fifty-five steps in the Halter, always deploying the General of Tang first, commanding three hundred million soldiers. With the left hand holding the golden talisman and the right hand wielding the bow’s sinew-shaking force, he seizes the fierce and malevolent demons and bandits with overwhelming might. The soldiers and officials then demolish the lairs of the malevolent ghosts and demons.

Turning to face the Zhongyuan and Xiayuan Generals, he orders them to unite in purpose, swiftly converging upon the lair of the malevolent demon or bandit. Each exhales natural heavenly fire, burning the lair of the malevolent demon or bandit. There are also natural lions that devour the spirits and souls of the malevolent demons and bandits, preventing them from causing harm to humans or ourselves.

The General of Tang is then summoned, and immediately three hundred million officials and soldiers arrive, aligning their hearts with the two generals. Together, they encircle the distant encampments, temples, and dwellings of the malevolent demons and bandits.

The second-in-command to the General of Tang is General Ge, seventy-two *zhang* in height, wielding a spear in his right hand and a fist-shaking bow in his left. His sinew-shaking force is mighty and fierce, capable of shattering mountains. He arrives united in purpose with the General of Tang, attacking the malevolent demons and bandits in their dwellings and bodies. He also exhales natural heavenly fire, alongside lions, great serpents, and iron-clad soldiers marked with *seban* texts—fierce, poisonous, and savage. Wielding swords, they enter the lairs of the malevolent demons and bandits, exterminating each one without escape.

The lions and poisonous serpents also bite and devour the demons and bandits.

The third-in-command, General Zhou, governs the mind and spirit. Thus, *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* records him as the first in command, mastering the expansive Dao and commanding the spirits. *(Annotation: This is the Celestial Master’s proclamation to the Twenty-Four Great True Persons of Xuanzhou, instructing them in the practice of stepping along the celestial and terrestrial Halter, each attaining true immortality. Through the heart’s command of the generals and soldiers, their merit accumulates, reaching three thousandfold, and through deep cultivation, they attain the Dao—all governed by the mind, hence the emphasis on the first.)*

This is for exorcising demons. According to the later sages’ instructions to Zhang Tian Shi and King Jun, General Zhou should lead the vanguard or rearguard and must not be exclusively ranked first.

If one seeks the Dao for longevity, the General of Tang should lead as first. If one seeks to cure illnesses or capture malevolent forces, General Zhou should lead as first, and success will follow. If one masters the Great Dao, the General of Tang should lead as first.

General Zhou, with his left hand holding the scepter and his right hand wielding the sinew-shaking bow force, arrives to seize and drive away the malevolent demons and bandits, following behind. This clarifies that he is the third in the General of Tang’s formation, as explained in the scriptures and prefaces.

The current interpretation follows the *Flowing Pearl* text as primary, governed by the heart’s intent and used in sequence. *(Annotation: This addition is from Zhao’s commentary, not the Celestial Master’s original Golden-Mouthed teachings.)*

The Celestial Master told King Jun: The Three Elements govern the Four Seasons—*(Annotation: Spring, Summer, Autumn, and Winter are the Four Seasons, corresponding to the divine entry into Taiyi, Lei Gong, and Liu Ren’s methods.)*—the Four Seasons *(Annotation: The gods of Heaven)* govern the Five Phases, the Five Phases govern the Six Jia, the Six Jia govern the Seven Stars, the Seven Stars govern the Eight Directions—*(Annotation: The Eight Directions in Heaven, the Eight Trigrams on Earth—Qian, Kun, Xun, Zhen, Kan, Gen, Dui, and Xian—all centered in the Middle Palace, invoking the Nine Palaces.)*—the Eight Directions govern the Nine Palaces, and the Nine Palaces generate the Ten Celestial Stems—*(Annotation: The current Ten Stems.)*—the Ten Stems generate the Twelve Earthly Branches, all arising from the natural *qi* of the Great Dao. When called upon, they respond and assist.

With a single-minded and refined intent, one attains profound understanding, securing the protection of the Three Elements and Five Phases. Through persistent cultivation, one achieves the Dao of longevity and eternal youth.

I once transmitted this teaching to Shennong, who only understood the Three Elements but not the Six Jia. Though he lived over a hundred years without signs of aging, he later attained the method of *shīxiè* (corporeal ascension).

---

The Dao of the Six Jia is known to me; one who can guard the spirit and regulate the body attains communion with the Three Elements. The Three Elements, when harnessed, can guard and save humanity. Regulating the body leads to communion with the True, and seizing the True of the Seven Stars grants mastery over ghosts and communion with spirits, establishing control over malevolent *qi*.

Through prolonged cultivation—*(Note: "修" refers to the method of measured steps and attuned clothing; "求" denotes the ritual techniques of exorcism, invocation, and talismans.)*—the immortal method is secured. The Daoist adept, Madame Fan, would, on the day of her birth, often perform exorcism rituals. Ten years later, the Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper descended, teaching her the method of measured steps. Upon completion, she ascended in broad daylight. Only her old wedding garments remained, and the villagers buried them; to this day, people speak of the tomb of Fan and Liu’s ancient garments.

Thus, one attains longevity. All must first pass through the Three Elements and then the Seven Stars, relying upon them to begin practice. Knowing this, one becomes a Daoist adept.

Keep it secret; do not recklessly impart it to others.

Therefore, I begin with One, establish Two, command Three, harmonize Four, transform Five, don Five, command Six, point to Seven, and preserve Nine—the method of attaining immortality.

I teach the Dao of entering the True and communing with the spirit, all achieved through the Three Elements Generals. The initial method is One: the *yuanqi* (original *qi*), the elder spirit within the body, thus named *yuanqi*, as One. *(Note: The spirit within the body is the "神," residing in the *nìwán* (brain marrow). The "太一" is also this.)*

One has two categories: the first, external to the body, is Heaven—the spirit of the *Taiyi*. One can command the second, which is the Earth spirit. *(Note: The Earth spirit within the body is the spirit of the kidneys and spleen, also called the Dragon God’s commander, the *Dìzhuì*.)*

The second category, within the body, is the heart—the spirit of *Zhèngyī* (Upright One) can command the second, which is the spirit of the kidneys and spleen. Adding the left and right kidneys *(Note: Left kidney for men, right for women.)*—this is Three.

The method states: Two can command Three—namely, the Generals Tang, Ge, and Zhou. Three can subdue a hundred spirits, heal a hundred ailments, disperse a thousand calamities, and eliminate ten thousand poisons. *(Note: Poisons and malevolent afflictions of this kind.)*

All these methods are supreme; they are the workings of One *qi*.

The method of One begins with the principle of the first step, the "One" character, which governs the heart. *(Note: "One" refers to *yuanqi* (original *qi*), the brain spirit *Taiyi*, which enters the body and governs the heart.)*

The later sage-king said to Lord Wang: "One spirit enters the Five Phases—this is the way. When the heart generates a thought, it is the principle of the method’s discipline and order. Once discipline and order are established, the hundred spirits respond, and nothing fails to succeed.

But if one speaks from the heart, invoking blessings or curses, the consequences of fortune or misfortune, guilt or virtue, arise with a single thought. The ancients honored One, keeping it undisturbed. Sit upon Two, making it inactive. Invest in Three, so that ten thousand soldiers guard my longevity, and no evil may act.

The heart commands all spirits; the Three Elements are the leaders, and the Six Jia are the assistants. One can command them. *(Note: Commanding and using them means guiding them to follow the Dao, without harming people or things; this is to make them beneficial, ensuring good deeds take root. Using them to harm is the accumulation of evil karmic deeds, which must not be done recklessly.)*

One can command and establish communion with the spirits, thereby achieving longevity. Three circuits complete, and then the discipline of the steps begins.

Laozi said: "If one wishes to command the Three Elements Generals, first preserve the spirits of *Taiyi*, *Tiānyī* (Heavenly One), and *Xīnyī* (Heart One). Then step the discipline of *Taiyi* and *Xīnyī*, attune the clothing, and issue the command according to the method, as if commanding soldiers.

The later sage-king told Zhang Daoling: 'You wish to seek longevity; you must practice the steps of *Taiyi*.' *(Note: The discipline of *Taiyi*.)* 'To attain immortality, preserve and enter the steps of *Tiānyī*.' *(Note: *Tiānyī* refers to the Upright One’s Three-Five steps of discipline, the method of preserving the spirit and measured steps.)* 'To swiftly ascend as an immortal, the *Xīnyī* must first arise, surpassing all other methods.' *(Note: When *Xīnyī* is preserved, it is within the body, arising from the heart.)*

---

For those who cultivate the Supreme Dao, the heart must first generate a thought before all the Ones. The heart reigns over the body; once one knows the heart is the sovereign of cultivation, one practices the correct method before *Taiyi*, attaining the nature of *Zhèngyī*, and together with *Xīnyī*, they govern all immortals.

The heart must always be steadfast in the Three Ones, never losing the body, and thus attains the Dao of immortality.

Again, he told the Young Lord of the Eastern Sea: "On the day of your birth, practice the steps of *Xīnyī*; on the *jiǎzǐ* day of Upper Element, practice the steps of *Taiyi*; on the *jiǎzǐ* day of Middle Element, and on the *jiǎzǐ* day of Lower Element, practice the steps of *Zhèngyī*. Often do this, and in nine years, the Dao of immortality will be complete; the Three Ones will be fulfilled.

Again, he told the Old Woman of the Western Mountain: *(Note: Some say this is the Fragrant Maiden.)* "Practice the method of the Three Elements Generals: use General Tang as the leader during the *yín* hour, use General Ge as the leader during the *wǔ* hour and its aftermath, and use General Zhou as the leader during the *shēn* hour and beyond."

「This Old Woman performs this practice every five days, and after seven years, she reverses her aging, becoming a youthful maiden of about thirty. After ten years, the Dao is complete, and she appears as a woman of eighteen in form and visage.

The Celestial Master told the Yellow Emperor—*(Note: At this time, the Celestial Master was Broad Success Child, or else the Peerless Sage, or during the time of Yao and Shun, he was the Attendant of the Numinous.)*—"The Three Elements Generals' method: the Upper Element has its own three divisions—Upper, Middle, and Lower. The Upper Division is led by General Tang. The Middle Division is led by General Li. The Lower Division is led by General Zhou.

He said: 'The Three Elements Generals oversee the Five *Dé* and manifest the Five Phases. Knowing this Dao, one may learn longevity.' The Emperor thus studied it.

The Celestial Master taught the Emperor the method of the Upper Element's *Taiyi* steps, beginning with the *jiǎzǐ* day of Upper Element. Next, he took the *jiǎzǐ* day of Middle Element. Then, he took the *jiǎzǐ* day of Lower Element. The Upper Element steps of *Taiyi*, the Middle Element steps of *Zhèngyī*, and the Lower Element steps of *Xīnyī*.

The Upper Element's *Taiyi* General Tang leads the celestial officials and bureaucrats, all governed by this divine general, corresponding to the Upper Division's General Tang of Upper Element. Aspirants of the Dao earnestly seek to know this.

The Middle Element's *Taiyi* General—*(Note: *Taiyi* refers to the *Zhèngyī* Alliance's ritual steps, which must be practiced with due reverence to avoid harming the body. One begins by advancing the left foot first.)*—leads the earthly mandates, the Five Sacred Mountains and Four Seas, as well as the spirits of the Northern Du Capital, overseeing the netherworld's affairs. This corresponds to the Upper Element's Middle Division General Li. Those who practice the Dao but do not know this are recorded by the Northern Netherworld.

If one knows and practices it often, the Three Generals' assaults are invoked, all led by General Ge.

The Lower Element's *Xīnyī* General leads the Water Palaces, the Northern expanse of the Primordial Wastes, the Four Seas and Nine Rivers, the myriad streams and lakes, and all the spirits of their sources. He governs and invokes them to strike and subdue, all under General Zhou's command. This aligns with the Lower Division's General Xu of Upper Element.

To practice *Tiānyī*—*(Note: *Tiānyī*, these are the ritual steps of the *Zhèngyī* 威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威威

---

**Note:** *Xiaoziji* is a female immortal.

It is said: The **One Dipper** (*Yīdǒu*) completion is the **Kui Star**’s envoy. First, walk the **Earthly Measure** (*Dìjì*) and the **Celestial Dipper’s Ropes** (*Tiāngāng*), until the sequence reaches the **Three Generals’ Ropes**. When the **Three Ropes** are complete, then store the **Dipper’s Envoys** to strike and subdue. The scripture states: *"First walk, then summon the North Dipper’s Seven Stars to seize and kill"*—this is the **First Completion**.

Then turn the fingers to point at objects, but do not yet rely on the mouth. One must practice diligently and grow thoroughly familiar through prolonged study.

When the two methods yield results, the North Dipper follows, and whatever the mouth desires in intent, the fingers shall verify.

The **One Dipper** has its own diagram; store and visualize it for completion.

When visualization is complete, recite the invocation:

> *"One Dipper complete, Three Five united,*
> *Heaven reversed, Earth overturned,*
> *Follow my commands as envoys.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Two Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **One Dipper** completion, then proceed to the **Two Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are stored within the body, the practice succeeds and one attains communion with spirits. The body can then awe and subdue objects, safeguard life, rescue and gather the lost, and achieve anything desired—this is called the **Two Stars’ Envoys’ Awe**.

The **Two Dippers** also have their own diagram; store and visualize it for completion, and it shall manifest.

Recite the invocation:

> *"Two Dippers complete, Three Five enlightened,*
> *Gather and subdue malevolent spirits,*
> *Wickedness and evil shall submit in fear.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Three Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **Two Dippers** completion, then proceed to the **Three Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are stored within the body, its spiritual power gradually grows awe-inspiring. The **Three Manifestations** (*Sānyào*) radiate like light, and the form of the Dipper blazes upon the body. The **Three Dippers** also have their own diagram; store and visualize it for completion, and the envoys shall manifest in effect.

Recite the invocation:

> *"Three Dippers complete,*
> *Heaven and Earth purified,*
> *The Dipper follows my body,*
> *Those who see it shall flee in terror.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Four Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **Three Dippers** completion, then proceed to the **Four Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are summoned, the practitioner blazes with fire encircling the **Four Dippers**, assuming the Dipper’s form. Malevolent spirits and wickedness shall tremble, their hearts crushed and subjugated.

The **Four Dippers** also have their own diagram; store and visualize it for completion, and the envoys shall manifest in effect.

Recite the invocation:
