> *"Four Dippers complete,*
> *Three Five full,*
> *Traverse ten thousand miles,*
> *Wind and fire shall not cease,*
> *Slay and annihilate malevolent spirits,*
> *Wickedness and evil dare not act.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Five Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **Four Dippers** completion, then proceed to the **Five Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are summoned, the practitioner’s **refined light** (*Guāngqì*) ascends to Heaven, assuming the Dipper’s form, its radiance illuminating the four quarters. Malevolent spirits and wickedness retreat a hundred miles, a hundred ailments vanish, and demons and malevolent forces are crushed and extinguished.

The **Five Dippers** also have their own diagram; store and visualize it for completion, and the envoys shall manifest in the Dipper’s form. The true image shines a thousand miles distant, spirits and gods submit in awe.

Recite the invocation:

> *"Five Dippers complete,*
> *The Five Phases arrayed,*
> *The Five Metals rise like autumn clouds,*
> *The Wooden Spirits are extinguished.*
> **Note:** *Spirits* refers to the multitude of malevolent ghosts.
> *The Five Woods flourish in spring, subduing the Earth Star.*
> *The Five Waters flow and disperse, severing the Fire Phase.*
> *The Five Fires blaze fiercely, the Five Metals dare not howl.*
> *The Five Earths are purified and settled,*
> *I and all things are born together.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Six Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **Five Dippers** completion, then proceed to the **Six Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are summoned, the practitioner’s refined light illuminates Heaven and Earth, radiating in the eight directions. Malevolent spirits and wickedness hide and vanish, while the body attains communion with spiritual *qi* (*Língqì*), its nature merging with the True Immortals. A hundred ghosts shall fear and respect, a thousand spirits shall guard and protect.

The **Six Dippers** also have their own diagram; store and visualize it for completion, and the envoys shall manifest in effect.

Recite the invocation:

> *"Six Dippers complete,*
> *Three Five move in concert,*
> *Eliminate evil and wickedness,*
> *Purify ten thousand miles.*
> *I summon the Six Dippers and Six Hexagrams,*
> *All united to guard my body and home,*
> *Attaining eternal life.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

The **Seven Dippers** completion is the envoy of the **□ Star**. Also, store the **Six Dippers** completion, then proceed to the **Seven Dippers** completion.

When the envoys are summoned, the practitioner encircles the **Seven Stars**, bearing the **Seven Dippers** upon their body, their radiance illuminating the ten directions. The body aligns with the North Dipper, and malevolent spirits are struck with awe. Auspicious omens follow the practitioner, ten thousand miles are purified, and countless guards attend.

There is also its own diagram; thus, the **Seven Dippers** envoys are fully stored. Now, when the seven stars are established, the envoys manifest instantly, responding at the heart and mouth like lightning illuminating the body. Store the Dipper’s completion power, and the spirits shall endure thus forever. When the envoys are stored, the body ascends to the **Upper Pure** (*Shàngqīng*).

Recite the invocation:

> *"Seven Dippers complete the body,*
> *United with the Six Hexagrams,*
> *Drive and command the Three Elements,*
> *Reverse and turn the Five Phases,*
> *Enter the ranks of the immortals,*
> *Walk with the Supreme Unity,*
> *Dominate the Nine Heavens,*
> *Purify the Nine Earths,*
> *May my household all become immortals,*
> *Every dwelling share in eternal life.*
> *As it is, so it shall be done—just as the law decrees."*

**Laozi** says: *"The essence of the Six Hexagrams transforms into the Seven Stars."* The Seven Stars shift and move, overseeing and inspecting all spiritual beings.

**Note:** *Spiritual beings* refers to humans, gods, dragons, beasts, spirits, and ghosts, etc. Those within Heaven and Earth who are born with spiritual vitality and divine communion are called *spiritual beings*.

All spiritual beings fear the North Dipper’s Seven Stars. Thus, those who study the Dao all know of the North Dipper’s Seven Stars and habitually store and contemplate them, donning them like garments. Though garments differ in quality, length, and style, they uniformly cover the body without fail.

If one desires that all spiritual beings fear and respect, and to secure one’s own longevity, then with the **One Dipper** to **Six Dippers** according to merit, the depth and magnitude of their efficacy shall not falter by a single measure.

For those who are beginners, they must diligently cultivate day and night, memorizing this method and storing it in thought. Do not lose the names of the stars, and always keep them firmly in mind.

The Dao does not depart from the heart, nor does the heart need to depart from the Dao.
When the two are inseparable, divine efficacy is established, and immortality is attained.

**The Sixth and Seventh Scrolls of *Jin Suo Liu Zhu* (Golden Lock Flowing Pearl)**

Composed by the Great True Ones of Zhonghua:
Zai Wang Fang Ping, Zhang Daoling, Zhao Sheng, Wang Chang, Si Ming, Li Zhongfu, Mao Ying, Xu Yu Fu, and others of successive generations.
Commentary by the Daoist Immortal Li Chunfeng.

**Explanation of the Upper Section: *Zhuan Shen Cun Yong Tu* (Diagram of Transforming the Body and Storing Its Use)**

All Daoist practitioners who diligently cultivate with earnest devotion—reciting scriptures, chanting the True, offering morning and evening incense, whether three times a day, six times a day, or twice a day—
yet after ten years, twenty years, thirty years, or even their entire life, gain nothing, only to perish from old age or disease.

Some abandon food and dwell in mountains, burning elixirs and refining medicines for years without divine response—what then can they rely upon?
Such disciples perish in great numbers.

If one does not grasp the true path, what foundation can they have?
Those who rely solely on fasting, purity, and abandoning wife and child—whether Daoists or Buddhists—are even more numerous, yet none have prolonged life or extended their years, let alone ascended as dragons and phoenixes to become True Persons.

Now, the Buddhist scriptures say:
*"What one cultivates in this life will be received in the next"*—this is false.
**Note:** The Buddhist scriptures claim, *"What one cultivates in this life will be received in the next,"* but this is incorrect.

Our Great Dao does not even permit such thoughts. If kings and ministers seek to preserve their bodies eternally, why would they abandon the pride and wealth of this life to seek rewards in the next?
These words are utterly baseless and unworthy of trust.

One must seek the gate of the Supreme Dao and grasp its essential practice—realizing it in this life, becoming the Dao’s sovereign and minister. How could this not perfect body and heart?
The Dao is here, in this life. Body and heart must be cultivated together, attaining an indestructible form—how wondrous is this?

This is the explanation of cause and effect.
**Note:** The Buddhist scriptures often speak of cause and effect, yet ignorant people—especially foolish women—are deceived into believing in karmic retribution and induced to make empty offerings. This is wrong.

The enlightened follow the Dao naturally, as heaven nurtures and earth sustains.
Since heaven nurtures and earth sustains, water and fire first form the body, and when the body matures into humanity, it is again water and fire that bring about old age and death.
Thus, the origin of birth and death lies within the Three Realms, all governed by natural law, not by cultivation of seeds.
**Note:** The Buddhist scriptures emphasize the cultivation of seeds, ignoring the teaching of natural law.

Yet true alignment with body and heart lies within the Dao. The seed of the Dao and its blessings reside in body and heart itself.
All internal cultivation is complete—external seeds are irrelevant.
**Note:** True Persons cultivate body and heart, not earthen structures or temples.
True Persons refine body and heart, not metals and stones.
All is governed by the natural teaching of the Dao.

Thus, the Supreme True Ones employ methods and incantations that never leave the body, yet their influence permeates heaven and earth.
**Note:** This rejects the notion of grand diagrams.

Later, the Sage Emperor instructed the young daughter of Xi Wangmu:
*"Though you were young and read little, you will serve others well when grown."*
After several years, she saw someone reading the *Lao Jun Jing* and began learning the characters.
Once she recognized the script, she asked: *"Do you know the names of the gods within the body?"*
Hearing this, she was taught the method of *Zhuan Shen You Si Jie Xin Yin* (Transforming the Body, Silent Contemplation, and Sealing the Heart’s Seal).
**Note:** This is the inner method of the *Liu Zhu* (Flowing Pearl).

Later, with great spiritual power, she taught Xi Wangmu in return.
**Note:** Initially, Xi Wangmu could only prolong life, ride dragons across heaven and earth, and summon them at will—but she could not herself master dragons, cranes, lions, or tigers.
Now, by invoking clouds and dragons in thought, and summoning armies unseen, mother and daughter both attained it, and she is now called the Immortal King.

Again, she passed this down to the Heavenly Master, commanding him to refine his thoughts and combine the method of summoning.
When the method was perfected, he became the central teacher of the Orthodox Dao, a celestial official akin to a great prefect, his status unassailable.
He must meditate once every hundred days.
**Note:** To inspect and suppress malevolent spirits, ghosts, and evil *jing* (precise entities) that harm humanity.

He must store and apply the method once every ten days.
**Note:** *"Apply"* means to contemplate and store the method, observing the world for malevolent *jing*, evil spirits, dragons, and ghosts that might harm humanity—or for poisonous *qi* disrupting humanity and the cosmos.
He must also fear that the sun and moon may dim, stars may cease their courses, winds and rains may fail, and spirits may deceive people.
These are the first concerns.

The second concern is self-cultivation: keeping the Three Souls and Seven Spirits aligned, ensuring *qi* flows correctly, and distinguishing essence and spirit—thus attaining longevity.
Life is as depicted in the diagram: the sun and moon are clear, the stars shine within.
**Note:** Store the Seven Stars so they enter and govern the five viscera, guarding the body’s spirits.

One may also assume the form of the Dao Father as depicted in the diagram—
whether in battle, in the wilderness, or in a grand sealed retreat—
holding one’s breath, stepping in the Twelve Paces of Yu.
**Note:** The Twelve Paces of Yu, four steps in twelve paces, correspond to the Twelve Branches and the Twelve Months. The Supreme Lord Lao transmitted this to Yu, who passed it to the world, calling it the *Yu Bu* (Yu’s Steps).

With the left hand, hold the Dao Father.
**Note:** *"Father"* refers to the Yang. Men should use the left hand to grasp *Hu Qi* (Sudden Breath), and upon completion, contemplate it as a figure—
wearing a lotus-crowned headdress, clad in purple robes—
gradually rising until it stands before the heart, as if part of oneself.

Store its height as one’s own: nine *zhang* tall, in purple robes, surrounded by soldiers bearing spears and halberds—
the Azure Dragon to the left, the White Tiger to the right, the Black Tortoise and Vermilion Bird arrayed in the five clouds.

Then, with the right hand, trace:
the Ghost’s Eye,
the Spirit’s Eye,
the Tiger’s and Wolf’s Eyes,
and the Evil Man’s Knife-Supporting Eye,
marking them all in red.

「With both hands clasped before the heart, strike the teeth thirty-six times, then open the eyes and recite the invocation.

Store the self as the **Examiner-Invoker** (考召法师)—
**Note:** This is the modern term for the **Examiner-Invoker** when petitioned in official documents.
In ancient times, the Dao Father (太上老君) served as **Yu You Zi** (务犹子) during the reigns of Yao and Shun.
After two hundred and fifty years in the Western Realm (西国), he internally transformed the **Illuminated King** (明王) **Dali** (达利) into a Buddha (佛), and appointed **Wuji Zi** (无极子) as the **Examiner-Invoker** (考召法师).
That one was called **Guanyin** (观音), who attends to the sufferings and diseases of all beings,
so that none perish prematurely or are harmed by calamity (夭伤).
The soldiers and generals are arrayed on both sides as per the diagram.
**Note:** The diagram appears in the *Jin Suo Liu Zhu Jing* (金锁流珠经).

According to the method, traverse the world (世界), and from the mouth emit great winds and clouds (大风云),
filling all of heaven and earth—
this is the mandate of the Dao (行道之命).
Recite the incantation (捻诀咒) thus:

*"Heaven is luminous, Earth is responsive.
I am the Examiner-Invoker, born before Heaven and Earth.
I traverse as Heaven and Earth’s envoy, standing as their soldiers.
Misfortune and calamity meet their own destruction, virtue and power appear of their own accord.
Not only do I restrain the Tiger and Wolf (虎狼),
but I also command the Five Armies (五兵).
Divine Dragons dare not act divine, demons dare not act responsive.
I point to mountains, and mountains collapse;
I point to waters, and waters dry up.
I point to stones, and stones roll away;
I point to the sun, and it shines brightly.
My body guards me in both movement and rest,
with three hundred and sixty thousand soldiers following.
At my hand’s command,
winds, fires, thunder, and lightning arise immediately.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the **imperative decree** (如律令)."*

Upon finishing the incantation, trace the **secret formula** (捻诀).
**Note:** The secret formula is on the first joint of the left hand’s index finger,
covering the **Ghost’s Eye** (游鬼目) and the **Five Armies’ Commanding Eye** (都监).
The **Ghost’s Eye** is on the first joint of the fourth finger.

The Dao Father (太上老君) transmitted the **Twelve Manifestations of Yu’s Step** (十二迹禹步) to the Yellow Emperor (黄帝).
**Note:** This was when **Guang Cheng Zi** (广成子) instructed the Emperor.
During the reigns of Yao and Shun, he passed it to **Yu** (禹),
and **Yu** then transmitted it to the people of the world.

The Dao Father said:
*"To seek the Dao of longevity (求长生之道),
one must first align the **Step Framework** (步纲) and trace the **secret formula** (捻诀),
and also master the methods of saving others and subduing ghosts,
controlling divine Dragons, Tigers, and Leopards (神龙虎豹),
as well as averting plagues and epidemics (瘟毒疫疠).
Within the Five Armies (五兵),
one can emerge unscathed alone.
One can also restrain them,
or command them to withdraw from harm.
This method is profound and subtle (微妙),
and cannot be easily heard."*

Those who have seen and heard the **Manifestations of the Dao** attain communion with the divine, and the divine protect them as their guardians.

Those who attain this method must first receive instruction from a **Clear Teacher** (明师). Only after being transmitted the **Scriptures, Laws, and Talismans** (经法箓) may they, after three years or two years, then be granted this method’s **secret formula**. This formula is transmitted orally, strictly following prescribed rites and measures. It cannot be hastily passed in batches of three or five volumes at once. Instead, unrelated matters must be discussed, and the transmission day must be broken into three or two separate sessions of oral instruction.

Following the **precepts of past and future sages**, one cultivates the **Great Dao’s reverence for the Most Exalted Sovereign**. Knowing not to recklessly divulge the teachings, both master and disciple attain true immortality. How could this not be the master’s restraint in transmission and the disciple’s sincere resolve to receive it?

To seek the **Supreme Dao**, one must devote heart and soul, bowing in earnest and sincere petition—never casually requesting a teacher and expecting immediate instruction. In this world, ordinary teachers, yielding to human desires, recklessly transmit and lightly divulge the Dao’s methods.

**Note:** In ancient times, great immortals would transmit the Scriptures, Laws, and Talismans, then require three thousand days of cultivation before passing on the essential **secret formulas**. This was to prevent people from forgetting their cultivation, for life is fleeting. Thus, they would petition for instruction and warnings, testing the disciple through three or five matters. Only if their resolve was unshaken, their aspiration for longevity genuine, and their desire to benefit the world sincere—without leaking the teachings to the unworthy—would they grant oral transmission.

Originally, this method was not recorded in writing, for those who seek the Dao often suffer from forgetfulness, and written records would go unmastered. The **Celestial Tribunals** of the **Three Officials** (三官) and the **Divine Sovereigns of Heaven, Earth, and Water** (天曹上帝道君及后圣君) were informed, lest true immortals and holy masters be disgraced. If the transmission is not passed orally, the disciple will not attain immortality. The blame falls upon the **Three Officials**, who would then harm and kill them. This is not because the unworthy rejected the formula, but because they lacked the path to cultivation, hence failing to become immortals.

Thus, the **Ancient Sage Laozi** commanded the **True Person Light Resonance** (光妙音) to compile and practice the **secret formulas**, integrating them into the Dao’s gate. He then structured **Fifteen Volumes** and transmitted them to **Mu Tianzi** and the **Sages**, opening the path to cultivation. In the prosperous era, when the **Later Sage Sovereign** (后圣君) was known, he ordered **Wang Fangping** to compile **Thirty Volumes**, transmitting them to the **Heavenly Hosts** and **Cavernous Heavens**.

Among those who left the world and received transmission were:
**Zhang Tian Shi**, **Zhang Chongxu**, **Li Yanni**, **Li Shaojun**, **Li Babai**, **Li Jingyou**, **Li Fazhou**, **Li Changxian**, **Li Zhongfu**, the **three Teach brothers**, **Yuan Shaokang**, **True Yuanzi**, **Wei Zhongkuan**, **Zhu Shaoyang**, **Le Yi**, **Dongfang Shuo**, **Yin Xi**, **Xu Jia**, **Xu Cha**, **Xu Hui**, **Shi Jiazi**, **Jie Xiang**, **Li Buji**, and hundreds more—all who practiced this method and became **True Persons**, passing it down in succession. They compiled **Fifteen Volumes of Dao Lectures**.

From the ancient **Pan Gu era** to the present, this method has been compiled and transmitted through successive generations. **The crimes of neglecting this are grave.**

---

**Annotations:**
黄卢子葛越 (*Huáng Lú Zǐ Gé Yuè*)
少室山 (*Shàoshì Shān*)
幽思转身 (*yōusī zhuǎnshēn*)
告命万神 (*gàomìng wànshén*)
三魂七魄 (*sānhún qībò*)
五藏百脉 (*wǔzàng bǎimài*)
千筋万灵 (*qiānjīn wànlíng*)
行生布炁 (*xíngshēng bùqì*)
兴法动禁 (*xīngfǎ dòngjìn*)
甲子日 (*Jiǎzǐ Rì*)
六甲日 (*Liùjiǎ Rì*)
道灵使兵 (*Dàolíng shǐbīng*)
上清 (*Shàngqīng*)
玉女 (*Yùnǚ*)
考召法 (*kǎozhào fǎ*)
步纲 (*bùgāng*)
步蹑速频 (*bùniè sùpín*)
上界天真 (*Shàngjiè Tiānzhēn*)
金锁流珠引 (*Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Yǐn*)

---

**Translation:**

**Note:** In ancient times, **Huáng Lú Zǐ Gé Yuè** resided in **Mount Shàoshì**. Suddenly, a devoted seeker of the **Dao** appeared, but he did not meet a master. **Yuè** then suddenly communicated with him, agreeing to take him as a disciple. The seeker returned home, gathered gold and silk, and eagerly sought instruction. **Yuè** warned him, saying, *"Your haste is a grave offense. The **Dao** first transmits the **fa** of the **luóshu** (scrolls), then imparts the secrets of the **ling** scriptures. You press too urgently—your guilt extends even to me."* Thus, he refused to instruct him. The man departed.

Later, a divine being descended to inform **Yuè**, *"You have mastered the **Dao**-heart profoundly; never reveal it lightly."* **Lǎozǐ**, the **Tàishàng**, spoke to **Huángdì**, saying: *"When the mind is deeply focused and the body transformed, the **Dao**-command reaches all spirits."* **Note:** *To command all spirits means to follow the twelve steps of **yōusī zhuǎnshēn**—the pivoting of the body’s framework. This summons the spirits within the body: the **three souls and seven spirits**, the **five viscera and hundred vessels**, the **thousand tendons and myriad subtle essences**, ordering each to its proper station—**Zhèngdìng** and **Wáng**—to circulate **qi** and vitalize **fa**. When the **fa** is activated and prohibitions moved, it harmonizes with the spirits of **Heaven and Earth**, **Yin and Yang**, the **Sun, Moon, and stellar deities**, merging into one. Thus, on **Jiǎzǐ Days** or **Liùjiǎ Days**, in the first year, the **Dao**-spirits command armies. In the second year, they dispel a thousand poisons and subdue ten thousand soldiers. In the third year, the **Xian Dao** is fulfilled.

If you but focus your mind—whether walking, standing, sitting, or lying—constantly preserving the original master, you will naturally attain communion with the **Dao**. Merging with **Heaven and Earth**, you will spontaneously become **True**. Your **běnmìng** (natal destiny) shall be the first to transform. **Note:** *Always meditate on the **běnmìng** as depicted; in one year, you will commune with spirits, and spirits and ghosts will revere you in awe.* After one year, the spirits of **Heaven and Earth** will all respond to your will and speech, granting no wish unfulfilled. Each passing year, your merit grows.

Practice for one year and gain the **Five Spirits**. In two years, the **fa** is complete, and you become a **True Person**. In three or four years, the **Shàngqīng** will draw near, the **Yùnǚ** will descend in response, divine beings will appear, and all spirits will follow. Those who practice this **fa** will inevitably become **True**.

Later, the **Sage Monarch** instructed the **Shàngyuán True Person Lǐ Fāngqī**, saying: *"You wish to accumulate merit and receive divine summons."* **Note:** *The **kǎozhào fa**—healing one person’s illness counts as one merit. Three thousand people healed equal three thousand merits.* *"To attain communion with the **yōu** (mystic depths), you must cultivate stillness and transform the body."* **Note:** *The steps of **bùgāng** require bodily transformation. When the ancients spoke of **zhuǎnshēn**, they referred to the modern **bùgāng**.* *"To become **True**, quicken your steps and hasten your pace. If your **Dao**-practice is earnest and your body fails, yet your mind never ceases, you will still attain it. It is like practicing the **bù** steps—its efficacy is verified by its results."* **Note:** *The ancient **Xianren** all relied on mental cultivation.*

When a person’s practice is profound and enduring, the **Dao** naturally imprints upon the mind. A single thought suffices—no difficulty remains. If you persistently uphold this practice, your descendants will inherit it, and your merit will extend to your six relations.

---
**Volume Seven of *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Yǐn***
**Volume Eight of *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū Yǐn***

The **Zhōnghuá Zǒngzhēn Dàxiānrén Zǎiwáng**—**Fāng Píng, Zhāng Dàolíng, Zhào Shēng, Wáng Cháng, Shīmìng, Lǐ Zhòngfǔ, Máoyíng, Xǔ Yùfǔ**, and others—**of the lineage** composed and annotated the texts. The **Zhōnghuá Xiānrén** **Lǐ Chúnfēng** annotated them.

It depicts the **shàngyuán** **sānbù**—the **generals of the Three Departments** and the **sān gōngcáo**—**and their ranks**.

The text within is inscribed with **fú** and **zhūshū** (cinnabar script).

**Lǎojūn** says:

*"The **shàngyuán shàngbù** is the **Generals of the Upper Department**. There is one such general.
He oversees the **sānqīng**—**Upper Clarity, Supreme Clarity, and Middle Clarity**—above.
He resides within the **Dàluó**—**Note: Dàluó is a celestial name**—
**Luo** refers to the **Dàluó**, which encompasses the **sānshíliù tiān**—**thirty-six heavens**—
as the **capital canopy** of the **thirty-six heavens**, called **Dàluó**.
Within **Dàluó**, there are eight heavens arranged in the four directions—**east, west, south, and north**—
each direction hosting eight heavens, totaling **sānshí'èr tiān**.
From **Middle Clarity** to **Supreme Clarity**, there are **sān tiān**—**three heavens**—
and **sānshíwǔ tiān**—**thirty-five heavens**.
Including **Upper Clarity**, there is **yī tiān**—**one heaven**—
making a grand total of **sānshíliù tiān**—**thirty-six heavens**—
the entire realm of the heavens.

**Yuánshǐ Tiānzūn**, in the **Dùrén Jīng**—**Scripture of Leading People**—
declares: *"There are **sānshí'èr tiān**—**thirty-two heavens**—
and **sānshí'èr dì**—**thirty-two sovereigns**—
all referring to the four-directional heavens beneath **Middle Clarity**.
Additionally, it does not mention the **zuòzhě zhōngtiān**—**the Central Heaven of the Sitting Sovereign**—
For if one includes **Yuánshǐ’s** **zuòzhě tiān**—**the Heaven of the Sitting Sovereign**—
the total becomes **sānshǐsān tiān**—**thirty-three heavens**—
which counts all the heavens beneath the **lower realm**.
In the **heavenly world**, all realms—**earthly and celestial**—
have their **imperial sovereigns**.
He is the **xúnjiǎn**—**inspector**—
of **rénshén lóngguǐ**—**human deities, dragons, and ghosts**—
and his **attendants** are the **bǎi yì wàn zhòng**—**hundreds of billions of countless troops**—
the **armies of the heavens**.

The surname **Pán**, given name **Tǐ**.

*Note: The name of the ancient Upper Primordial General.*

In the age of the **Three Sovereigns**, the **Heavenly Sovereign**, the **Tàishàng Lǎojūn**—**Supreme Dao Lord**—as **Tàishàng Dàdàojūn**—**Supreme Lord of Ten Thousand Ways**—transferred the **Pán General** into the position of **Dàzhēnrén**—**Great True Person**.

Thus began the succession of the **Táng Duǎn**—**Tang Short**—as **Upper Primordial Upper Division Great General**, replacing the former.

*Use the method of the original teacher before oneself.*

*Note: If this method is transmitted, it may be preserved. If not transmitted, it must not be recklessly kept, lest it harm those who store it.*

In ancient times, the **Dìhuáng**—**Earthly Sovereign**—did not receive the reckless preservation of the Dao. Suddenly, the General appeared, his body nine hundred million *zhàng* in length. His voice like heavenly thunder, he called out to the Earthly Sovereign: *"Earthly Son, who is your teacher? Why do you summon me?"*

The Earthly Sovereign replied: *"My teacher is the Five Spirits Lord."*

The General said: *"Because you did not study under the Five Spirits Lord, if you had studied under the Lord, I would not have appeared. I now accuse you—what will you do? Bind yourself to him as your teacher! Bind yourself to receive the scriptures and methods. The Jade Registers are insufficient, the Golden Registers are entirely lacking. The oral transmission says: 'I received the Dao from the Eastern Xia Child. The Xia Child is your father. Though he lived, he transmitted the scriptures fully, never abridged. To claim you received the abbreviated Dao from Ling Mountain—what mountain is this? False words, false speech, will bring calamity upon your body. Give you three years to govern, then I will hold you accountable for your crimes."*

Thus, the Earthly Sovereign feared death day and night, ascending mountains and crossing waters to seek the Five Spirits Lord. When the Lord saw him, he knew he was being accused and said: *"Great Sovereign, your adherence to the Dao is not sincere, your reviling of the Dao is not divine. Now you are punished by the Heavenly Officials—who is to blame?"*

The Earthly Sovereign knelt twice before the Lord, declaring his guilt. *"I am of base nature, fond of the Dao but my practice is insincere. I am a foolish man, now encountering a foolish artisan. I have recklessly cultivated, and the Heavenly Officials punish me. How dare I hope to retain my human form? I beg the Great Dao’s great mercy, to accept and command me, lest beyond three years the Heavenly Officials punish my crimes, and I lose my human form. How dare I still receive the Sovereign’s position?"*

The Lord then transformed into a great divine method, closed his *qi*, and performed the *niǎnjué*—*muttered incantation*—which Westerners call *structuring the seal*. In an instant, the three generals—Táng, Lǐ, and Xú—descended together, acting as guarantors for the Earthly Sovereign. They transmitted the **Great Dao Golden Registers and Jade Talismans** in over eighty stages, the **Three Sovereigns’ Inner Texts**—*Heavenly, Earthly, and Human*—and forty-nine volumes of scriptures. After fourteen years of cultivation, he attained the Dao, governed the world for eighty-nine thousand years, and ascended to the **Xuánqiū Platform**.

In the presence of the original teacher, he performed the *niǎnjué* once more.

He then preserved the thought of the **Upper Primordial Upper Division Táng General**, surnamed **Táng**, named **Duǎn**.

*Note: Call him softly.*

This deity is the **Tàiyī**—**Supreme Unity**—Emperor’s general. Do not call him recklessly. His body is nine hundred million *zhàng* in length. Below him is the **Five Halters Divine Functionary**, surnamed **Jiāng**, named **Dú**. His body is also nine hundred *zhàng* long. He commands a hundred thousand million layers of red-clad attendants—red-clad, with crimson headbands, holding golden talismans and wielding the **Lóngzhōu Sword**—leading a hundred thousand soldiers. Above the **thirty-two heavens**, at the **extreme of Tàiqīng**—**Supreme Clarity**—he oversees all the **heavenly lodges and star clusters**.

*Note: The Supreme Lord told Pángǔ King: "The heavenly lodges are the Twenty-Eight Constellations. The star clusters are the Nine Stars of the Central Dipper and the Nine Spirits. All the stars and clusters of the nine celestial regions above belong to this deity’s jurisdiction."*

He is called the **Functionary**, like a prime minister in the realm. The Upper Primordial General is like the Emperor’s position. Hence, he is said to **inspect the extremes of the Three Pure Ones**.

Within the **Great Luo’s** four directions, all life and death stem from **registration and fall**—registered to be born, fallen to die.

O King, you must know this, then you will **long-live**. If you do not know, your lifespan will be short.

Pángǔ King knew that the **Eternal Essence** abides atop **Mèishān**, entering and exiting within the **left kidney**. Thus, for fourteen years, he cultivated and attained the **Way**, governing the realm for eighty-nine thousand years before ascending to the **Supreme Ultimate**. All the people of his realm ascended together with him.

From the heavens above, the **Eternal Essence** descended in a dense, cloudlike form—all converging in the **Níhuán** of mortals.
*Note: The Níhuán is the palace of the mind, named Upper Primordial, the abode of the Upper Primordial General.*

It resonates and communicates with the spirit of the left kidney. Mortals must cultivate and anchor the **Eternal Essence** in the Níhuán, where it stabilizes within the left kidney—women anchor it in the right kidney.

If one cannot discern this, they should gaze upon the *Containing Shadow Diagram* and then focus their thoughts, thereby harmonizing with the myriad heavenly deities and the body’s spirits, all converging within the self. Further, by mastering the **Thumbscrews of the Fate-Bearers**, one can immediately attain **long-life**—this is not empty doctrine.

This is what the **Later Sage-King** revealed to those who cultivated on the **Five Sacred Peaks of Ling Mountain**, including the Twenty-Eight Immortals—**Gěyuè, Péngshòu**, and others—recording their practices on Ling Mountain. These accounts were not passed down to the common world.

*Note: The* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl *states: The Later Sage-King revealed the Cloud Palace within the Níhuán, concealed within the left kidney.*
*Note: At night, one should cultivate and anchor the Eternal Essence in the left kidney; women anchor it in the right. By day, if engaged in affairs, it may surge forth, exiting through the left eyebrow and ascending to the heavens, enveloping the body. When needed, it surges from the left eyebrow, emerging through the **Heavenly Gate** in pairs.*
*Note: The* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl *omits the word "double," but the Later Sage-King’s revelation to Fúqiū Gōng included it. How do we know this?*

For mortals who cultivate the **Way**, their bodies attain it as well—mirroring Heaven and Earth, thus harmonizing in correspondence.

The **Supreme General of the Upper Primordial** is a celestial deity and great immortal official. Though he communicates with mortals, when humans, through sacred writs, register him within the left kidney, it is as though the human spirit and celestial deity resonate in harmony.

Thus, when the human spirit emerges, it ascends from the left kidney to the heavens above. The Supreme General of the Upper Primordial then descends through the **Heavenly Gate**, aligning with the human body. The human body likewise retains the brow as the form of the **Heavenly Gate**, like an inscribed petition with its diagram.

The **clustered clouds** revolve and descend, enveloping the body and household.

*Note: The* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl *omits these three characters. The Later Sage-King’s revelation to Fúqiū Gōng included them.*

As for those who cultivate the **Way**, after attaining it, they can benefit families, aid nations, and rescue people—how much more so if they can save the boundless worlds beyond their own body and household? If the body and household, or others, also attain it, in times of urgency, one may call upon the **Northern Dipper**, and it will descend immediately.

With the **coastal marshal**, *Note: The* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl *omits the three characters "元" (Primordial), which appear in the Later Sage-King’s revelation,* one may dispel calamities and disasters, subdue spirits, dragons, and ghosts.

*Note: These eight characters are also absent; they appear in the revelation.*

Then, one turns the **Heavenly Pivot**, forms the **seal of the finger** with the hand, *Note: This is the "twisting of the incantation." The incantation is hidden beneath the first fingernail of the left hand.* and with the right hand, twists it for a short while.

One takes **Yǔ’s Steps**—twelve strides, or nine. *Note: The Great Yǔ’s Step has nine strides; the Lesser Yǔ’s Step has twelve. This is the Later Sage-King’s distinction between the Great and Lesser Yǔ’s Steps. If the Most High Laozi speaks, the twelve-stride step is the Great Yǔ’s Step.*

One raises the **Heavenly Pivot**, pointing toward the direction of the malevolent force—*Note: This may be where soldiers or the sick reside, or where evil men and ghosts gather.*—and it vanishes instantly, faster than fire or water. *Note: This speaks to the swift response of the method, which can instantly manifest its efficacy. Calling without cause will bring ruin to oneself and one’s household.*

*Note: The* Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl *lacks the three characters "无事家" (without cause, household); these are from the revelation, as cited above.*

The Most High Laozi told the Yellow Emperor:
*"If one’s body, household, and nation are at peace, recklessly invoking them will bring annihilation to one’s clan. Do not call upon them lightly."*

The **Golden Writ** states:
*"Lightly invoking the Northern Dipper and the Supreme General of the Upper Primordial will bring ruin to one’s body and spirit."*

The Most High Laozi further told **Ānhé Zǐ**—*Note: Ānhé Zǐ was the younger brother of Shénnóng, who studied the Way at Hángshān and encountered the Most High Laozi, who descended to teach him the Upper Clarity Three-Five Flying Steps of Heavenly Restraint and Earthly Measure.*—that one should always retain the essential incantation of the Three-Five, thereby summoning the Three Primordial spirits to descend and instruct in cultivation. By day, one ascends to the **Southern Extreme Fire World** of the heavens, refining gold and stone as the foundation of the earth, and declares:

*"Among the Three Primordials, the Supreme General of the Upper Primordial is the most noble and exalted—like the position of a sovereign emperor in the world. It is greatly capable of helping one attain the Way. When using it, one must not act recklessly. Only on one’s natal day, **Jiazi days**, or **Upper Primordial days**—*Note: Jiazi is the Upper Primordial; one must not act recklessly on Jiazi days outside of these specified occasions.*—should one cultivate and employ it. If suddenly there is an urgent matter in one’s body or household—being plotted against, a grave illness on the verge of death, or bandits—one may call upon it, and it will vanish instantly. This is highly efficacious. Even if not on these days, it will still work.*

The Later Sage-King told the **Celestial Master Dàolíng**:
*"You wish to teach others to escape calamity and enter the path of longevity. Take the **Upper Primordial day**—*Note: From the Jiazi cycle, select the Upper, Middle, or Lower Primordial days.*—of that person’s natal hour, day or night, and beneath the Northern Dipper, burn incense while focusing on one’s original teacher. Upon completion, visualize the Supreme General of the Upper Primordial descending into the **Níhuán Palace**, then entering the left kidney. Next, the Middle Primordial, then the Lower Primordial—*Note: The Middle Primordial enters the right kidney; the Lower Primordial enters the heart.*—first stopping the spirit at the Níhuán, then entering the heart and kidneys to stabilize the five viscera.

Then, twist the incantation, take **Yǔ’s Steps**—four steps, twelve strides—and upon completion, visualize it emerging to envelop the body, like the **Encompassing Diagram**, fully encompassing the Three Primordials and Five Phases, the **Thunder Lord’s Five Thunders**, and the Eight Trigrams, sun, moon, and stars. When complete, recite the **Five Phases Eighteen Incantations** once to seek longevity. Within a year, one will enter the path of immortality. In two years, one will be named **Long-lived**, avoiding soldiers and escaping calamities, attaining spirit efficacy, moving heaven and earth by will, and achieving fulfillment of the heart. All will enter the Níhuán. Later, they will respectively enter the heart and kidneys. After a short while, when the body’s spirit is settled and still, one may summon it forth again, like the Encompassing Diagram. Upon completion, twist the incantation, close the **qi**, and take **Yǔ’s Steps**—twelve strides—to seek life and escape calamity. Within a year, the spiritual efficacy will manifest instantly, greatly aiding the **Heavenly Restraint and Earthly Measure**.

You must not recklessly transmit this to unworthy individuals. This method of the Three Primordials’ five techniques can directly lead one into the Great Way’s gate. Keep it secret for good fortune; reveal it for misfortune.*

The Most High Laozi told the **Three Primordial Deities of Antiquity**:
*"Cultivating the Three Primordials begins with the Upper Primordial’s natal day. Next is the Middle Primordial, then the Lower Primordial, completing the cycle. Within a year of cultivation, one may attain five degrees.* *Note: Within the sixty Jiazi days of the Upper Primordial, there is one natal degree. In the Jiazi days of the Middle Primordial, there are two natal degrees. In the Jiazi days of the Lower Primordial, there are three natal degrees. Following this cycle back to the Upper Primordial, one selects the natal day for practice. Within two years, ten days of cultivation will lead to the path of immortality.*

The Later Sage-King bestowed a **talisman of the Supreme General of the Upper Primordial** upon **Zhāng Dàolíng**, instructing him to swallow it. After swallowing, one should visualize its deployment—nothing will remain unfulfilled. He also commanded that it be passed down secretly among worthy disciples."

The Later Sage-King instructed those of **virtue/power** (志人): *Note: "Worthy disciples" (志人) are those who share his noble aspirations.* The **adepts of the Dao/Way** (志道之士), saying: "Thus, one may attain the **Way of the True Person** (真人之道)."

The Later Sage-King then bestowed the **talisman of the Supreme General of the Middle Primordial** (上元中部将军符) upon **Zhāng Dàolíng**, commanding him to swallow it. Upon swallowing, one should perform the rites of the Middle Primordial (行中部事), and he was also instructed to pass it down secretly among worthy disciples (志人), so that all may attain the **True Dao** (真道).

Next, the Later Sage-King bestowed the **talisman of the Supreme General of the Lower Primordial** (上元下部将军符) upon **Zhāng Dàolíng**, commanding him to swallow it. After swallowing, one should perform the rites of the Lower Primordial (行下部事), and he was instructed to transmit it to worthy disciples (志人) in succession through the generations, so that all may proclaim the **Way of Supreme Truth** (至真之道).

The Later Sage-King bestowed these three talismans (三符), each to be swallowed in turn, and declared to the **Supreme Generals of the Three Primordials** (命上元三部将军): "Let them aid and assist those who receive the **Three Five Primordial Rectification Laws** (太玄三五正法)." When practicing, one should meditate upon and visualize them—calling them forth, they will manifest according to one’s words and desires, and one’s intentions will be fulfilled. *Swiftly, swiftly, as the command is decreed!* (急急如律令) These three talismans are inscribed in **cinnabar** (朱书).

Again, he instructed **Shànxíngzǐ** (善行子): *Note: "Shànxíngzǐ" is the grandson of Lǐ Shàojūn, who attained the Dao/Way through his ancestral **virtue/power** (福德) and ascended to the **West Peak Cavern of the Primordial** (洞天) in the Western Mountains, where he took the name "Shànxíngzǐ."* Though you are devoted to the Dao/Way and your efforts are diligent, you have not grasped its principles. The principles derive from the **Three Primordials** (三元), yet cultivation begins through the **Five Phases** (五行). You may take **Zhāng Dàolíng** as your teacher.

Thus, **Shànxíngzǐ** entered **Shù** (蜀), seeking to receive the **Three Primordial Laws** (上三部之法) and the **essentials of the Five Phases** (五行之要). After fourteen years of cultivation, he ascended to the **West Peak Cavern of the Spirit-Master’s Palm** (西灵仙掌洞天). Thereafter, there were hundreds of disciples who followed this **Three-Five Law** (三五之法), all attaining the **Way of the True Person** (真人).

The **Supreme Elderly Lord** (太上老君) instructed **Rénhuáng** (人皇): "The king seeks the **Supreme Dao** (至道), desiring to attain the **True Nature** (真性). The **True Nature** lies within the **Three-Five Primordial Power** (三五三五之力), which is the **Dao Ancestor** (道祖). As water emerges from its spring, one attains its flowing source. As a person emerges from their cave, one attains their entrance and abode."

The **Supreme Elderly Lord** further expounds:

*"In ancient times, people dwelled in caves, hence the saying ‘emerging from the cave.’ The king received [the Dao], and his lifespan matched the extremes of Heaven and Earth. **Annotation:** The **Rénhuáng** received it. Indeed, he attained immortality, ruling for eighty-nine thousand years. Later, his entire palace ascended to the **Supreme Ultimate** (太极). He also left writings behind in the world; today, the *Rénhuáng Text* (《人皇文》) is transmitted.*

The **Supreme Elderly Lord** said: ‘The **Great Dao** has myriad gates and doors, yet its essentials are few. Earlier, I spoke of the **Three-Five** origin and the **Three Primordial Laws**, yet this has not yet exhausted its fundamental roots. Now, I shall enumerate them one by one in the following volumes.

The **principles, keys, incantations, and talismanic symbols**—though few in words—directly lead one into the **inner gates** to perceive the **Dao**. **Annotation:** This volume concludes the teachings on the **Three Generals**. It expounds the **Stepwise Principles, Rectified Keys, Talismanic Symbols, and Incantations**—these should be the matters of the **Upper Primordial Law’s** three divisions, all enumerated in their respective titles.

Next, consider the **Upper Primordial Law’s** middle division: **General Li** (李将军), surnamed **Li**, named **Jù** (拒). **Annotation:** He is invoked in a low, reverent tone—one of the **Supreme One’s** honored divine generals. His stature measures seven hundred million *zhang*. He commands—**Annotation:** The *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū* (《金锁流珠》) does not mention ‘commands,’ yet in the sacred texts received by the **Ancient Sovereign** (上圣君), both the upper, middle, and lower sections include the character ‘commands.’ This must be an omission in the transmission. The *Liúzhū*’s emergence in the world is ancient and distant; the records of its transmission have been lost over time. It must have existed originally—it was not absent. Now, I proceed according to the transmitted accounts."*

「Five [Divine] Generals of Rigidity
**Annotation:** According to the *Tóngtiān Zhōngbù* (《洞天中本》), the term *gāng* (纲) is used, while the *Ancient Sovereign* (前圣君) transmitted the term *jiāng* (将). The *Later Sovereign* (后圣君) instructed the *Sōngzǐ* (松子), naming them the **Five Generals of Rigidity** (五刚功曹), confirming the use of *jiāng* (将).

The *Liúzhū* (《流珠》) originally was the *Jīnluó* (《金箓》). The *Ancient Sovereign* and *Later Sovereign* did not grant permission to alter it, so I dare not change it. The **Functionary of Rigidity** (功曹), surnamed **Zhāng**, named **Lǐ**.
**Annotation:** Another account says his personal name is **Jì** (季).

His stature measures seven hundred *zhang*. **Annotation:** The *Liúzhū* (《流珠》) does not record his stature as seven hundred *zhang*, but the *Ancient Sovereign*’s transmission includes these five characters.

The **Hundred-Thousands-and-Tens-of-Thousands of Troops** (百千万重人), **Annotation:** According to the *Liúzhū* (《流珠》), the account is not detailed, and their affairs are not explicitly revealed. However, if we follow the *Later Sovereign*’s instruction to the *Dōnghǎi Xiǎotóng Jūn* (东海小童君), the **Upper Primordial Law’s** (上元) middle division has one general, surnamed **Lǐ**, named **Jù** (拒), with a stature of seven hundred million *zhang*, who commands one **Functionary of Rigidity** (五刚功曹), surnamed **Zhāng**, named **Jì** (季). The **Hundred-Thousands-and-Tens-of-Thousands of Troops** (百十万重人), their number unknown, are under his command. This refers to two individuals: the general and the functionary. The remaining hundred-thousands-and-tens-of-thousands of troops are the **divine officers and soldiers** (兵吏).

They wear **crimson headgear** (赤帻), and with their **right hand hold a spear** (右手持戟), their **waist sash bears the Sword of Subduing Demons** (腰带消魔之剑).
**Annotation:** The *Liúzhū* (《流珠》) states: The general of the upper division, **Táng Jiāngjūn** (唐将军), wears a waist sash with the **Dragon-Scented Sword** (龙浓之剑). The middle division general lacks a name in the text. The **Sword of Subduing Demons** (消魔之剑) is the name given by the **Supreme Venerable Lord Lǎojūn** (太上老君). The *Later Sovereign* instructed the *Dōnghǎi Xiǎotóng Jūn* (东海小童君) that the three generals of the three divisions wear the **Sword of Commanding Demons** (命魔之剑), which belongs to the upper division. The **Sword of Subduing Demons** (消魔之剑) is for the middle division. According to the Master’s words, there are many omissions, as it has been this way since ancient times—not a recent loss in transmission. They reside within the **Tàiqīng** (太清), beneath the **Shàngqīng** (上清).
**Annotation:** The **Supreme Venerable Lord Lǎojūn** (太上老君) told **Hán Yìzǐ** (韩义子), the **Tàihuáng** (太皇), saying: “The Heavenly Grandson (天之孙), *Tàiqīng* (太清) is the designation of *Tàijī* (太极). *Shàngqīng* (上清) is the designation of *Dàluó* (大罗), within the **Three Purities** (三清).” They are positioned above the **Middle Heaven** (中天).

They often descend into the **right middle chamber of the Mudan Palace** (泥丸宫右中) within a human body, as previously described. In youth, they enter the **right kidney** (右肾) to subdue and control affairs, then shortly emerge at the **right eyebrow** (右眉上), like a contained **Great Expansion** (含弘). When they exit through the **Upper Celestial Gate** (上应天门),
**Annotation:** The *Later Sovereign* instructed the Master: “When you summon the three divine generals from the *Upper Primordial Law* (上元), they originally reside above the **Three Purities** (上三清), descending into the **Nine Chambers of the Human Body** (人身泥九中). In youth, they again enter the **right kidney** (右肾中), subduing and concealing themselves within the body. Then, you think of them ascending from the kidney to the **right eyebrow** (右眉头), emerging as if from the **Celestial Gate** (天门).”

This is said to mean: “From Heaven descending into my body, receiving my command to patrol the heavens and inspect the earth, annihilating malevolent forces, ordering the **Three Officials** (三官) to manifest my form, and aligning with the **Great Dao of Heaven and Earth** (天地大道). When I chant to commune with the divine, then ten-thousands of gods and spirits, hundreds of spirits and thousands of malevolent forces, tens of thousands of **precise essences** (精) and human-shaped dragons (人龙) will revere me. Thus, with the **virtue of non-action** (无为之德), I attain the **Dao of longevity** (长生之道).

Their manifestation follows the diagram. **Annotation:** The diagram of **Great Expansion** (含弘) exists at the **right eyebrow** (右眉头), emerging gradually higher and longer, and the body grows accordingly, reaching a height of twelve hundred million *zhang*.

Upon completion, the hands are withdrawn, and the **Incantation of the Three Primordial Generals** (三元将军诀) is recited. Then, ascending the **upper division** (上部) and **middle division** (中部) of the *Primordial Law*, step by step, the teeth are struck thirty-six times.

The eyes are then opened, and the incantation is recited:
*“Ancient Sovereign and Later Sovereign, teach me—another account says to invoke by name for longevity—
to stride through the Three Primordial [Divisions],
commanding the Nine Generals and Ten-Thousands of Troops,
to govern the Six *Jia* (甲),
align with the Seven Stars,
and swallow the Six Officials and Seven [Entities].
Annotation: Six refers to the Six *Jia* talismans (六甲符). Seven refers to the Seven Stars (七星).
Malevolent forces are beheaded,
Metal and Wood harmonize,
Water and Fire balance,
Humans dare not offend me,
Ghosts dare not conjure malevolent forces.
If any dare offend me,
the **Celestial Barrier** (天关) will extinguish your life.”
Annotation: This refers to invoking the **Celestial Barrier** (天关), pointing to it to bring about annihilation.

The incantation concluded, the **Incantation of the Upper Primordial General’s Diagram** (上元将军纲) is recited three times. Next, the **Middle Primordial Law** (中元), then the **Lower Primordial Law** (下元). Each division has its own diagram and incantation, recited three times each.

For each recitation of the diagram incantation, the steps are accompanied by the words *“sè sè”* (摄摄).
**Annotation:** The youth’s words are also recited three times.
If malevolent humans or ghosts appear, the words *“chì chì”* (叱叱) are recited three times.
**Annotation:** If treating malevolent humans, the **Knife Support of the Malevolent** (恶人刀支) is pinched.
**Annotation:** The **Knife Support of the Malevolent** (人刀支) is located on the right side of the **third node of the fifth finger on the right hand** (右手第五指第三节). Left governs killing; right governs release. Both release and subjugation must be applied with proper reason and not recklessly.

In practice, it must strictly adhere to the Dao.

If treating malevolent ghosts, the **Knife Support of the Ghosts** (鬼刀支) is pinched.
**Annotation:** The **Knife Support of the Ghosts** (鬼刀支) is located on the upper side of the **third node of the fifth finger on the left hand** (左手五指第三节). It is the **Knife Support of the Ghosts** in total. When addressing a specific ghost, the appropriate pinch is applied as described.

The eighth volume of the *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū* (《金锁流珠》) transmission concludes. The ninth volume begins.

For treating malevolent humans and ghostly spirits alike, one must utter the command **"Chì-chì"** three times.

If addressing a malevolent person, pinch the **Knife Support of the Malevolent** (兽目).
**Annotation:** The **Knife Support of the Malevolent** (人刀支) is located on the right side of the **third node of the fifth finger on the right hand** (右手第五指第三节). Left governs killing; right governs release. Both release and subjugation must be applied with proper reason and not recklessly. In practice, it must strictly adhere to the Dao.

The **Knife Support of the Ghosts** (鬼刀支) is pinched when treating malevolent ghosts.
**Annotation:** The **Knife Support of the Ghosts** (鬼刀支) is located on the upper side of the **third node of the fifth finger on the left hand** (左手五指第三节). It is the **Knife Support of the Ghosts** in total. When addressing a specific ghost, the appropriate pinch is applied as described.

The transmission of the *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū* (《金锁流珠》) concludes its eighth volume.
The ninth volume begins.

---

The **Great True Master of the Central Plain** (中华总真大仙), **Lord of the Netherworld** (宰王) **Fāng Píng**, **Zhāng Dàolíng**, **Zhào Shēng**, **Lord of the Netherworld** (司命) **Wáng Cháng**, **Lǐ Zhòngfǔ**, **Máo Yíng**, **Xǔ Yùfǔ**, and others, are the successive authors of this text.
The **Daoist Sage** (仙人) **Lǐ Chúnfēng** provided the annotations.
The **General Step Diagram of the Upper Primordial** (上元上部将军步纲图) follows.

The **Pre-Eminent Sage** (前圣老君) instructed **Yǔ** (禹) with the **Step Diagram** (步纲).
**Annotation:** **Yǔ** received three grades of **Yǔ’s Step** (禹步): the first, three steps with nine traces; the second, twenty-two traces; the third, twenty-eight traces. Now, this **Great Daoist Method of the Three Five** (三五大法) is universal, and **Yǔ’s Step** is no longer transmitted, forever ceasing in the world.

The **Post-Eminent Sage** (后圣君) then instructed **Fāng Zhūtóng** (方诸童君), **Yǐn Xǐ** (尹喜), **True Person of the Netherworld Lord** (真人王君), and **Zhang Tiānshī** (张天师) and others. Those who recorded in **crimson script** (朱书) were all instructed by the **Post-Eminent Sage**.

With the **right foot stamping the ground** (右脚蹈地) and the **left foot turning once** (左转一转), one proceeds according to the matter at hand.

The **Pre-Eminent Sage** (老君) instructed **Huángdì** (黄帝) with seven **Daoist Secrets for Seeking Longevity** (求长生等法诀):

1. **Secret for Seeking Longevity and Honor** (求长生於世为荣贵法诀): Pinch the **Netherworld Lord’s Eye** (司命目) and recite the **Five Elements Incantation** (五行祝) once.
   The incantation reads: *"Gold, Wood, Water, Fire, Earth, blessings be upon you."*

2. **Secret for Summoning the Celestial Fox** (追召天狐法): Pinch the **Beast’s Eye** (兽目) and say, *"I request the Upper Primordial General* (上部功曹) *to summon and limit [the fox] to arrive by a certain day."*

3. **Secret for Summoning the Dragon** (召龙捻龙诀): Pinch the **Dragon Secret**.

4. **Secret for Summoning the Celestial Netherworld Lord** (召天神司命): To summon the **Netherworld Lord** (司命) and grant longevity, pinch the **Netherworld Lord’s Eye**.

5. **Secret for Summoning and Slaying Celestial Demons** (召杀天上妖魅): Pinch the **Knife Support of the Celestial Ghosts** (天鬼刀支).

6. **Secret for Summoning the Gods of the Sun, Moon, and Stars** (召请日月星辰神): Pinch the **Sun-Moon-Star Host Secret**.
   **Annotation:** This is located beneath the **left hand’s fingernail** (左手甲下).

7. **Secret for Ascending to Heaven** (欲升天): To ascend to heaven, or to think of one’s own spirit ascending to heaven, or to pursue celestial demons, ghosts, dragons, beasts, such as **Heavenly Dogs** (天狗) and **Heavenly Leopards** (天豹), or when the **spirits of the deceased** (祟人合死者) are summoned—before contemplating the original master, and after emerging from all departments, like **Hán Hóngbīng** (含弘兵) in joint pursuit and slaying—one pinches the **General Overseer Secret** (都监诀).

The **Post-Eminent Sage** (后圣君) said: *"After completing the steps, pinch the Upper Primordial General Secret"* (上元上部将军诀).
**Annotation:** The secret is located beneath the **left hand’s first finger’s nail** (左手第一指甲下) and also at two places on the **middle node** (中节).

To seek entry into the **Celestial Register** (仙籍) or to practice the Dao while avoiding calamities:
**Annotation:** If one encounters misfortune, decline, or malevolent illnesses, one must compose a petition in detail.

Or if one seeks **virtue and power** (福德) for another, or to dispel spirits and remove disasters and calamities, one must also compose a petition in detail. All such matters can be resolved.

The **Pre-Eminent Sage** (老君) said: *"The Upper Primordial’s original fate-day is for seeking longevity. Begin with the Upper Primordial General, then proceed to the Middle Primordial, and finally to the Lower Primordial."*

Within the **Upper Primordial**, the steps are the same.
**Annotation:** The **Middle Primordial** and **Lower Primordial** are also used in total, though their applications vary.

For the **Upper Primordial’s original fate-day**, recite the **Upper Primordial steps** three times and pinch the secret. Upon completion, **store the Upper Primordial General** (存上元上部唐将军).
**Annotation:** The **Upper Primordial General** (坎中元上部唐将军) is stored in the **Marrow Palace** (泥丸宫), entering through the **Upper Primordial General** (上元上部).

Afterward, it is directed to the **left kidney’s center** (臣则玄左肾中).
**Annotation:** When contemplating the stored image, as in **Hán Hóngbīng’s Diagram** (含影图), this is called the **True Spirit and Soul** (正魂魄).

After two years, the **verification of immortality** (神仙不死之验) is achieved, and the **Upper Primordial matters are concluded**.

---

The **General Step Diagram of the Middle Primordial** (上元中部将军步纲图) follows.
**Yǔ** (禹) received the **Step Diagram’s Dao** (步纲之道) from the **Pre-Eminent Sage** and applied it to the **Middle Primordial**.
**Annotation:** The **Middle Primordial** pertains to humanity (属人), the **Upper Primordial** to heaven (属天), and the **Lower Primordial** to earth (属地). Within the three departments, the **Middle Primordial** and **Lower Primordial** contain far more techniques than the **Upper Primordial**. The **Middle Primordial** handles human affairs, and the **Lower Primordial** handles earthly affairs. These methods are highly refined.

One may **dispatch tasks** (效功), **collect and bind those of virtue** (收捕有德), **conscript human and ghostly spirits** (驱役人鬼), **part the waters and open mountains** (决水开山), **control ghosts and aid humans** (制鬼助人), **command dragons and tigers** (使龙使虎), **manifest the nine traces** (分变九迹), **establish the myriad protections** (成卫万端), **accumulate virtue and goodness** (积德累仁), and **ascend to the Great Polarity** (飞身太极).

The **Middle Primordial** is retained to teach those with sincere intent.
**Annotation:** The **Upper Primordial General’s Step** (上部将军步) is transmitted in the world, known as the **Great Yǔ’s Step** (大禹步), also consisting of **fifteen steps** (一十五步). Its practice is intricate, hence slightly more difficult than the **Upper Primordial**. The **Lower Primordial** has similar techniques, but if one is proficient, it will not be difficult.

Those who **aspire to the Dao** (志道之人) can **conscript dragons, tigers, and leopards** (役使蛟龙虎豹), **save and assist the world’s people** (济助世人), and **simultaneously enable others to attain the Dao** (兼令得道), **riding dragons and taming tigers and leopards** (乘龙御虎豹).

With the **left foot stamping once** (左脚踏一转讫), one proceeds according to one’s heart’s wish.

This is the **prohibition of the Middle Primordial General** (中部李将军行禁), involving the **Five Elements** (五行), **Six Palaces** (六甲), **Seven Stars** (七星), **Nine Refined Essences** (九精), and **Five Battles** (五斗). When practiced, these steps are as **easy as wearing a garment** (依之如衣), and their power is as **obedient as a servant** (使之如仆), all in accordance with one’s heart and tongue.

The **Post-Eminent Sage** (后圣君) instructed the **Netherworld Lord** (命), and the incantation began with the **initial step** (初起纲), which also included:

*"The **Great Unity** (太一) is my body,
I am the **Celestial Ancestor** (天中仙祖).
My head is the **Great Unity Palace** (太一府),
My feet are the **Celestial Pillars** (天柱).
My five **viscera** (五藏) are the **Six Palaces** (六甲),
Guarding the **Celestial Pass** (天关),
Driving the **Big Dipper** (北斗).
With a single command,
Ten thousand gods and myriad spirits
All follow my words and move.
Swiftly, swiftly, as the **precepts decree** (如律令)."*

The **Venerable Master** (老君) instructed the **Yellow Emperor** (黄帝) and the **Young Lords of the Four Directions** (方诸童君), saying:

*"This method consists of sixteen precepts. It is the **Central Department General** (中部将军) who governs and commands the troops. When practicing, recite the **Step Framework** (步纲) three times, then pinch the **Central Department General’s Secret** (中部将军诀).
**Note:** The Secret is found in the middle joint of the left hand’s first finger.

The first precept: Though the Central Department is the **Lord of the Upper Primordial** (上元主人), humans belong to the Central Department, which itself contains **Three Generals**.
**Note:** These correspond to the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordials** (上中下三元).

This **Central Department General** can guide a person toward the **True Dao/Way of Immortality** (正仙道). On one’s **Middle Primordial natal day** (中元本命日), perform these sixteen precepts—these are the essential methods for all worldly applications, not merely the Step Framework.

**First Method:**
On one’s **Middle Primordial natal day**, recite the **Central Department Li General Framework** (中部李将军纲) three times to stabilize the **True Spirit** (正魂) and subdue the **Ephemeral Soul** (魄).

Recite:
*"Li General, enter my right kidney,
Ge General serves as your deputy.
May you grant me **Mysterious Longevity** (玄长生),
Long life in this world,
Fearless and without dread."
**Note:** The General is stored in the right kidney, preserved like an **Image Diagram** (含影图), seated and guarding the kidney.

After reciting, strike the teeth twelve times, then pinch the **Central Department Secret** (中部诀).
**Note:** The Secret is in the middle joint of the left hand’s first finger.

Practice this method for one year, and **Mysterious Longevity** and prolonged vision will manifest. All hundred methods will verify its efficacy.

**Second Method:**
When facing **calamity, misfortune, or illness**, return to one’s **Middle Primordial natal day**. Begin from the **Five Torments of the Body** (自身五苦地), recite the Framework once, and exit the **Royal Constellation** (出王相).
**Note:** The Royal Constellation is calculated in the **Five Phases divination** (上五行引中注).

Recite:
*"From death to life,
**Note:** In ritual texts and petitions, if the word *death* (死) appears in the upper line, the word *life* (生) must not align below it—this is taboo.
Endless regeneration,
Attaining the **Great Peace** (太平)."*

After completing the **Five Phases**, pinch the **Water-Fire-Earth Knife Supports** (水火土刀支) according to one’s **natal element**:
- **Metal-natal** (金命) individuals pinch **Fire Knife Support** (火刀支),
- **Wood-natal** (木命) individuals pinch **Metal Knife Support** (金刀支),
- **Water-natal** (水命) individuals pinch **Earth Knife Support** (土刀支),
- **Fire-natal** (火命) individuals pinch **Water Knife Support** (水刀支),
- **Earth-natal** (土命) individuals pinch **Wood Knife Support** (木刀支).

Each natal element has its own **Knife Supports** to break the **Five Torments, Eight Hardships, Nine Calamities, and Hundred Illnesses** (五苦八难九厄百病). Recite the Framework within the **Three-Five Methods** (三五法) to dissipate them. If misfortunes are not eliminated within a year, they will not prevail, and the practitioner will achieve **longevity**.

The **Five Knife Supports** are detailed in the **Palm Diagram** (掌图).

**Third Method:**
If one’s **residence or courtyard is restless**, select a **Middle Primordial day of the Jiazi cycle** (中元甲子日), recite the Framework while circling the dwelling three times, or take **long strides** (长禹步)—the number of steps is irrelevant; completion of the circuit is paramount.

After three circuits, recite:
*"The **Supreme Male** (乾尊) radiates with spirit,
The **Supreme Female** (坤) harmonizes within.
Thus it is." (云云).*

As recorded in *The Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl* (《金锁流珠》), within the **Upper Alley** (上巷), the dwelling will then stabilize.

**Fourth Method:**
If **family members suffer illness** or the household is restless, select a **Middle Primordial day of Jiawu, Jiaxu, Gengshen, or Renyin** (中元甲午日、甲申、庚申、壬寅日). In the courtyard, recite the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Department Generals’ Frameworks** (上中下三部将军纲), one circuit each, then pinch the **Bright Hall Secret** (明堂诀).
**Note:** The Secret is pinched on the second joint of the left hand’s second finger.

Spit **saliva in the four directions**, storing the **Three Generals**—each commanding **three million soldiers**—to encircle the residence three times. Drive out **fire, water, lion, and serpent soldiers**, banishing **ghostly and demonic qi**, purifying the clear and dispelling the turbid.

Afterward, inscribe a **Residence-Suppressing Talisman** (镇宅符) and affix it to the doors.
**Note:** The Residence-Suppressing Talisman is found in the **Miscellaneous Talismans of the Three Departments** (三部杂符文).

Recite:
*"The talisman subjugates a hundred ghosts,
The evil spirits are vanquished and suppressed.
The **Mysterious Tortoise** (玄武) ceases theft,
The **White Tiger**... (白虎云云)."

**Fifth Method:**
If **besieged by armies** or engaged in battle, mentally perform **fifteen strides of the Central Department’s Great Step** (中部禹步一十五迹), followed by **fifteen strides of the Lower Department** (下部十五迹), then **turn the Celestial Pass** (转天关), pointing as you go, while storing the **Three Departments**.
**Note:** The **Upper, Middle, and Lower Primordials** (上中下三元) command the **Nine Generals** (总都部九将军) to strike and disperse the enemy. The practitioner will then **break through and escape**; pinch the **Knife Support Secret** (刀支诀) immediately.
**Note:** The Secret is on the right side of the second joint of the left hand’s fifth finger. Pinch urgently until blood appears.

Use this to align with the **Five Battles Garment** (五斗衣), pointing five times. Where pointed, the enemy will break. Then lead the troops to charge, and the enemy will collapse and retreat. Release the Knife Support immediately—otherwise, they will die.

Recite:
*"From death to life,
Swiftly ascending to the **Celestial Court** (天庭).
The **Azure Dragon** (青龙) supports my escape,
The **White Tiger** (白虎) guards my path.
I am the **Celestial Envoy** (天使) of the **Celestial Pass** (天关),
Breaking through your five armies.
**Swiftly, swiftly break!** (急急急急急急破).
As the precepts decree." (急急如律令)."

**Notes:**
Raise the flag, charge with horses, strike the drums, and break through—then depart immediately.

**Sixth Method:** When traveling far and passing through mountains or grasslands, fearing bandits, wild beasts, or venomous creatures—whether malevolent humans or poisonous beasts—seize a treeless spot. Walk the **Three Generals’ *Yubu* Steps** (禹步) in the upper, middle, and lower sections, each three times. Then pinch the throat and eyes of a living person, the **Knife Support**, and the eyes of snakes and tigers. Upon completion, ascend to the **Nine Heavens above**—*i.e.*, the **Alone-Empty Void** (孤虚). Should you encounter malevolent or venomous beings, strike the Void alone; even one woman can defeat nine men without fear. You will never again meet such creatures. If encountered, they will flee in terror and never harm you again.

**Incantation:**
*"Lofty and pure, you wicked one—you die, I return.
I press the Three Elements, sealing water and mountain.
Bandits and beasts flee far—no need for paths between.
The earth’s axis binds you without effort.
If you refuse to leave, bind you swiftly, bind you swiftly, bind you swiftly.
As the precepts decree."*

**Note:** Before setting out, practice the **Heavenly Halter Steps** (天纲) at home. While walking, no bandits or beasts will dare approach you—those that do will die.

---

**Seventh Method:** If a relative or Daoist associate in another prefecture falls ill—or if there is no barrier separating you—*i.e.*, parents, uncles, brothers, cousins, or even non-blood kin like Daoist friends or disciples (but not outsiders without righteous intent)—begin with the **Middle Section**.

**Note:** The **Heavenly Halter** (天纲) is walked in the middle section first, then the Upper and Lower Sections, each three times. The **Celestial Sovereign** then instructs the **Heavenly Master**:
*"You must also tread the **Celestial Pass** (天关) and **Earthly Measure** (地纪), each once—or reverse and return three times. Then summon the **Middle Element’s Tang General** (唐将军), one figure, eighty-one *zhang* tall, with a red headband, a **Heaven-Piercing Crown**, a sword at his side, and a spear in hand, commanding a million troops. He proceeds to the sick person’s home, sets it ablaze to drive away ghosts, thrusts his sword into the door, and roars three to five times. Lions, dragons, and serpents enter the house—above the bed, below the bed, within the walls, before the door, behind the door, left and right—slaying all malevolent, poisonous, or afflicting spirits. Let the sand collapse and tiles shatter; let the deer flee a thousand *li*. Purge and exterminate all evil. When done, the illness will swiftly abate, and the enemy’s forces will be defeated. Report thus."*

**Note:** Compose the ritual words and pinch the **Upper Element Secret**. Next, summon the **Middle Element’s Ge General** (葛将军), seventy-two *zhang* tall, with a red headband, a **Heaven-Piercing Crown**, a sword at his side, and a scepter in hand, commanding thirty million troops to the sick person’s home in such-and-such prefecture, county, village, and household. *Note:* Adjust according to the illness—fearing harm from malevolent ghosts or spirits. Burn the house with fire and water, drive away ghostly bandits, thrust the sword into the door, and roar three to five times, as before.

Next, summon the **Middle Element’s Zhou General** (周将军), ninety-six *zhang* tall, with a red headband, a **Heaven-Piercing Crown**, a sword at his side, a scepter, and a talisman, commanding thirty million troops to the specified location. Proceed as before. Then pinch the **Secret**.

**Note:** The **Secret** is on the first joint of the left hand’s thumb. Pinch urgently, and the three generals’ formation will fly to the sky, obscuring the sun. Upon arrival, they will slaughter poisonous and disease-causing ghosts and bandits. Follow the **Three Elements, Three Generals’ Method** as illustrated in *The Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* (金锁流珠), using visualization.

---
**Eighth Method:** If you or your six relatives or Daoist associates are slandered, defamed, or plotted against, walk the **Heavenly Halter** and **Earthly Measure** once each. Then disperse your steps outward, leaving fifteen footprints in a wide arc. Walk the **Middle Element’s *Yubu* Steps** three times, then pinch the **Knife Support** of the offending person.

**Note:** Pinch the **Knife Support** briefly—it will not harm the previous target. If pinched for too long, the person will weaken and die within ten or five days. Observe the signs carefully; do not harm others recklessly. Within a month or half, the matter will resolve as before.

**Immediately declare:**
*"Because of a certain matter, I am slandered by a certain person, causing my body to be restless. Now I summon one **Middle Element General**, along with one each from the **Upper Element** and **Lower Element Generals**, and thirty million soldiers. As your servant, I command the **Dark Resolution** to remove the malevolent person’s wicked schemes, their slanderous plots, and suppress them so they dare not act. Urgently make that person hide in shame and suffer misfortune themselves. May all slanderous matters depart from my body and instead harm that person’s life. Swiftly, as the law commands."*

Then recite the *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* (**金锁流珠**) **Earthly Measure** spell eighteen times. The spell reads:
*"I receive the **Heavenly Qi**, and I act as the envoy of Heaven and Earth."* (Repeat as above.)

The eighteen spells are all contained within the **Earthly Measure Scripture**; recite each one in turn. Upon completion, pinch the **Slander Seal**.

**Note:** The **Slander Seal** is located on the left hand’s fifth finger, at the third joint’s **wen** (vein), moving upward to the right side. Pinch the **Slander Seal** at the first finger’s second joint and beneath the fingernail.

**Ninth Method:** Always expel the **Three Corpses Worms** from your body, ensuring no reckless daytime mistakes or internal illnesses arise, so you may attain eternal life. Do this by selecting **Middle Element** or **Gengshen** days, walking the **Middle Element General’s *Yubu* Steps** three times, then reciting the eighteen-spell incantation. Upon completion, ingest the **talisman**. (The talisman is found in the *One Hundred Fifty Generals’ Spirit Scripture*.)

**Tenth Method:** Each year, select **Middle Element** or **Jiazi** days, walk the **Middle Element General’s *Yubu* Steps** three times, then ingest **three Soul-Subduing Talismans**. **Note:** One for the **Upper Element**, one for the **Middle Element**, and one for the **Lower Element**. Then recite the **Five Phases Heavenly Halter Flying Steps Spell**—the five phases (metal, wood, water, fire, earth) in sequence, with the seven stars resplendent, for the **Heavenly Halter’s supreme might**. Also recite the **Five Phases Earthly Measure Spell**—the five phases in sequence, metal subduing wood, water extinguishing fire, the **copper-mouthed, iron-tongued** decree. Afterward, observe one day of abstinence.

**Eleventh Method:** Throughout the year, on **Middle Element** days, arrange seven mirrors in a row, spanning eighteen inches wide, to inspect your inner spirit. If one mirror lacks your reflection, it means your spirit is deficient—swallow the **Soul-Settling, Spirit-Subduing Talisman**. Then walk the **Middle Element General’s *Yubu* Steps** three times and recite the **Earthly Measure Blessing to Parents** once. **Note:** *"The five [senses] arise from parents, and I endure the mundane world."* (Two talismans: **Soul-Settling Talisman**, **Spirit-Subduing Talisman**.)

**Twelfth Method:** Select **Middle Element** or **Jiazi** days within the same decan, choosing your own **birthday**, and inscribe three talismans to wear, overcoming the **Nine Calamities and Eight Hardships**, along with the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Element Talismans**. (The **Upper Element Talisman**, **Middle Element Talisman**)

「Inspect whether there are seven **spirits** (*qìpò*). If one lacks the reflection of the **Middle Element Spirit** in a mirror, it is said that the spirit is insufficient—then swallow the **Soul-Settling, Spirit-Subduing Talisman**. Upon completion, walk the **Middle Element General’s *Yubu* Steps** three times and recite the **Earthly Measure Blessing to Parents** once.

**Note:** *"The five [senses] arise from parents, and I endure the mundane world."* (Two talismans: **Soul-Settling Talisman**, **Spirit-Subduing Talisman**.)

**Twelfth Method:** Select **Middle Element** or **Jiazi** days within the same decan, choosing your own **birthday**, and inscribe three talismans to wear, overcoming the **Nine Calamities and Eight Hardships**, along with the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Element Talismans**. (The **Upper Element Talisman**, **Middle Element Talisman**,)

**Thirteenth Method:** For those who constantly guard their bodies and protect their families, after morning practice, retain the three generals of the **Middle, Upper, and Lower Elements** within the heart and kidneys, constantly using them to shield and safeguard—this is called **guarding the body**. To aid others, at the appropriate time, retain [the talismans] for a certain state, county, village, or household, encircling and patrolling the premises of a certain family, driving away malevolent and wicked crowds, and warding over the body of a certain kinsman. This follows the **Thirteen Precepts of the Holy Sovereign to the Heavenly Master**, known as the **constant retention method**.

**Fourteenth Method:** For entering mountains, waters, or fires, or crossing rivers, before leaving home, over two or three days, walk the **Upper, Middle, and Lower Element *Yubu* Steps**, each three times. Then declare: *"The Heavenly One has nurtured me, and the Earthly One has formed me. Certain [name], wearing this talisman, now unites with it. Daoist immortals aid me, and the jade maidens guard my form. The five colors transform—yellow, white, red, black, and blue—twenty-eight constellations merge into the **Purple Court**. The talisman repels disaster, granting blessings and longevity."* **As it is decreed, so it shall be done.** **Note:** Talismans are worn on the left for men and right for women after use.

**Fifteenth Method:** For entering mountains, waters, or fires, or crossing rivers, before embarking, twist the **Mountain King Ghost’s *Ghost Swords*** or the **Beastly Eyes and Thieves’ *Sword Supports***. The Heavenly Master said: *"I follow the teachings of the Primordial Master and the Holy Sovereign. When entering mountains, twist the Mountain King Ghost’s *Ghost Swords* or the Beastly Eyes. When entering seas or rivers, twist the Sea God’s Eyes. When entering battlefields, twist the *Ghost Swords* of the multitude."* (Two talismans: **Crossing Rivers Talisman**, **Entering Waters and Fires Talisman**.)

Declare: *"Bow-bow, meet-meet, River Lord leads me forward, splitting the **snake-dragon** (*jiāolóng*). All evils perish by the Heavenly Emperor’s decree."* **As it is decreed, so it shall be done.**

(Three talismans: **Entering Water and Fire Talisman**, **Entering Mountains Talisman**, **Nighttime Mountain Entry Talisman**—to be worn.)

Declare: *"The shadow of **Hengshan**, the sunward face of **Taishan**. Spirits and demons do not arise; venomous serpents lie hidden. Tigers and wolves, seeing me, are all struck with terror. There is one surnamed Li, named Ear; fierce tigers, seeing him, break their fangs and snap their teeth; venomous serpents, seeing him, cannot coil."* **As it is decreed, so it shall be done.**

Twist the **Preceptor’s Sword Support** (*Dūjiàn Guānmiào*).

**Fifteenth [Method]:** To desire a single body and one household free from illness.
Constantly, on the proper days of the solar year, tread the **Three Elemental Generals’ Three-Grade Halters** (*Sān Yuán Jiāngjūn Sān Děng Gěng*), beginning with the **Central Elemental General** (*Zhōng Yuán*), then proceeding to the **Upper Elemental General** (*Shàng Yuán*), and finally the **Lower Elemental General** (*Xià Yuán*).
