**Note:** Since one is born under the Central Elemental General, the halter-treading begins with the Central Elemental General and ends upon completing the **Preceptor’s Sword Support** (*Dūjiàn Guānmiào*), the **Grand Ghost’s Eye** (*Dūguǐ Mù*), and the **Three Teachers’ Halters** (*Sān Shī Děng*), concluding with the recitation of the **Earth Chronicle Talisman** (*Dì Jì Zhòu*) eighteen times. After the incantation, recite the **Heavenly Halter Vow** (*Tiān Gěng Zhòu*) twelve times. Then complete the **Grand Halter** and **Grand Heart** incantations.
**Note:** The **Grand Halter** (*Dà Dūjiàn Guānmiào*) is inscribed on the left palm in a horizontal manner, resembling a clenched fist. The **Grand Heart** (*Dūxīn*) is inscribed beneath the first fingernail of the left hand. Twist them swiftly—these are the **inner incantations of myriad transformations** (*Qiān Biàn Wàn Huà Zhī Nèi Jué*). Swallow one talisman. For a year, one’s body and household—whether one or many—shall remain free from illness. Each person swallows one talisman and thus attains a year without affliction.

On the **First Day of the First Month**, ingest this talisman once.
Declare: *"The **Supreme Venerable Lord** (*Tàishàng Lǎojūn*), the One who begets and receives his ministers.
Swiftly binding and dispatching spirits, banishing them a thousand leagues away.
Those who confront me shall die; those who gaze upon me shall perish.
Swiftly, as the **Supreme Venerable Lord’s Female Green Dao/Way’s Heavenly Decree** (*Nǚ Qīng Xuán Dū Lǜ Lìng*)."*

**Sixteenth [Method]:** Constantly on the **Six Wu Days** (*Liù Wù Rì*—Wuzi, Wuchen, Wuyin, Wushen, Wuxu, and Wuwu), gather the **Six Wu Upper Soils** (*Liù Wù Shàng Tǔ*), shaping them into cakes.
Three inches and two *fēn* in length, three *fēn* in thickness, dried in the shade for several days.
Then tread the **Central, Upper, and Lower Three Elemental Generals’ Halters** (*Zhōng-Shàng-Xià Sān Yuán Jiāngjūn Gěng*), each three times.
Afterward, recite the **Earth Chronicle Talisman** (*Dì Jì Zhòu*) eighteen times.
Upon completion, attach these cakes to both soles of the feet.
Treading water becomes like walking on land; one forever crosses rivers and seas.
The **Avoiding Calamity Halter** (*Bì Nàn Dé Jué*) is inscribed beneath the left foot, along with the **Sea God’s Eye** (*Hǎishén Mù*) and **River God’s Eye** (*Héshén Mù*), etc., with vermilion ink. These soil cakes are tied to the **Earth Heart God’s Eye** (*Dìxīn Dìshén Mù*), thus prohibiting all manner of spirits from the rivers, seas, and lakes—treading water as if on land.

This method is most wondrous; keep it secret.
Within the **Upper Elemental General’s Central Division** (*Shàng Yuán Zhōng Bù*), only the **Central Division’s Dao/Way** (*Zhōng Bù Fǎ*) is accessible to mortals, allowing the gods to subdue demons and save the people in their pursuit of immortality. It is a **true and wondrous method** (*Rù Zhēn Miào Yī Fǎ*) found in the Central Division.

**Upper Elemental General’s Lower Division Halter Diagram**
Next, the **Upper Elemental General’s Lower Division** (*Shàng Yuán Xià Bù Jiāngjūn*), surnamed **Xu** (*Xú*), named **Kang** (*Kāng*).
His stature measures **five hundred million zhang** (*Wǔ Qiān Wàn Zhàng*). He leads...

---

**Annotations:**
*《金锁流珠》* (Jīn Suǒ Liú Zhū) – *"Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl"* (a Daoist scripture)

---

**Commentary:**
The *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* omits the character **领** (*lǐng*, "command").
The **Five Rigid Dao-Functionaries** (*Wǔ Gāng Shén Gōngcáo*)—one person, surname **Wēn**, given name **Shū**.
*Annotation:* According to *Liú Zhū*, only **"Dao-Functionary"** (*Gōng*) is mentioned, omitting **"person"** (*rén*). Thus, **"surname Wēn, given name Shū"** refers to this single individual alone.
The phrase **"hundred thousand million layers of men in red robes"** (*Bǎi Qiān Wàn Chéng Rén Zhī Chìyī*) should be interpreted as soldiers, not Dao-Functionaries.

According to the **Later Sage Emperor’s** (*Hòu Shèngjūn*) instruction to the **Celestial Master** (*Tiānshī*):
- **Upper Elemental General’s Upper Division** (*Shàng Yuán Shàng Bù*)—one general, **Five Rigid Dao-Functionaries** nine in number, **Administrative Dao-Functionaries** nine thousand.
- **Upper Elemental General’s Central Division** (*Shàng Yuán Zhōng Bù*)—one general, **Five Rigid Dao-Functionaries** seven in number, **Administrative Dao-Functionaries** seven thousand.
- **Upper Elemental General’s Lower Division** (*Shàng Yuán Xià Bù*)—one general, **Five Rigid Dao-Functionaries** five in number, **Administrative Dao-Functionaries** five thousand, with soldiers numbering **hundreds of thousands of layers** (*Bǎi Qiān Wàn Chéng*).

None know their exact multitude.
This is the **Later Sage Emperor’s** revelation—**true numbers**—where the **Five Rigid Dao-Functionaries** of the **Upper Elemental** are fixed at nine.
This applies to **Upper True Ones** (*Shàng Zhēn*), **Middle True Ones** (*Zhōng Zhēn*), **Lower True Ones** (*Xià Zhēn*), and **Upper Immortals** (*Shàng Xiān*).

The **"hundred thousand million layers"** refers to multitudes of **red-robed, red-headbanded** (*Chìyī Chìfù*) soldiers.

The **Grand General** holds in his right hand the **Jade Yang Scepter** (*Yù Yáng Zhī Jié*), and at his waist, the **Dragon Spring Mo-Ye Sword** (*Lóng Yuān Mòyé Zhī Jiàn*).
*Annotation:* According to *The Transmission of the Laozi*, it is the **"Sword that Beheads Evil"** (*Zhǎn Xié Zhī Jiàn*).

The **Great Luo Heaven’s** (*Dà Luò Tiān*) **Upper Inspection Ropes** (*Shàng Yóu Jiǎn*) descend into the **human heart-mind** (*rén xīnzhōng*), entering the **right kidney** (*yòu shèn*).
**Cultivation through contemplation** (*Cúnsī*) emerges from the **right eyebrow’s Heavenly Gate** (*Yántmén Zhōng*).
All methods follow those previously established for the **Upper and Central Division Generals**.

The **Later Sage Emperor** instructs the **Celestial Master** on the **Method of Extracting the Residence and Ascending to Heaven** (*Bá Zhái Shēng Tiān Jué*), stating:
These are the **Three Elemental Generals** (*Sān Yuán Dà Jiāngjūn*)—the **three divisions of the Upper Elemental** (*Shàng Yuán Sān Bù*).
They are also the **Celestial Sovereign’s** (*Tiān Huáng*) **decree**, appointed by the **Former Sage Dao-Lord** (*Xiān Shèng Dà Dàojūn*), to fill the **Upper Immortal General’s** (*Shàng Xiān Jiāngjūn*) position.
*Annotation:* *Liú Zhū* states: These are the **Three Sovereigns** (*Sān Huáng*) of antiquity, not the **Taiyi Era** (*Tàiyì Shídài*).

The **Three Divisions of the Middle Elemental** (*Zhōng Yuán Sān Bù*) were established by the **Later Sage Emperor**.
The **Lower Division Xu General’s** (*Xià Bù Xú Jiāngjūn*) methods of cultivation and practice follow those of the **Upper and Central Divisions**.
Generally, the **Lower Division** governs **earth-water-heart-mind** (*dìshuǐ xīn xíng*) affairs—all must be invoked through **awareness** (*qǐniàn*), which constitutes the method.
Each governs **earth-water spirits, dragons, and ghosts** (*dìshuǐ shénlóng guǐ*).

The **Later Sage Emperor** instructs the **Young Lords of the Four Directions** (*Fāng Zhǔ Tóngjūn*) and the **Great True Ones** (*Dà Zhēn Yán*):

The **Three Divisions of the Upper Elemental General’s** (*Shàng Yuán Sān Bù Jiāngjūn*) **Step Ropes** (*Bù Jiāng*) are used to **rectify and subdue the Three Souls** (*Sān Hún*), while the **North Dipper Step Ropes** (*Běi Dǒu Bù Jiāng*)—
*Annotation:* This is the **Flying Step of Heavenly Ropes** (*Fēibù Tiāngāng*).
—are used to **stabilize the Seven Spirits** (*Qī Pò*).
*Annotation:* Regardless of **Heavenly Steel** (*Tiāngāng*) or **Earthly Ropes** (*Dìjì*) methods, all conform to the **Seven Spirits’** regulation.

Those who study the **Dao of Immortality** (*Xiān Dào*) must first **rectify the Three Souls**, then **subdue the Seven Spirits**, establishing the foundation for the method and entering the **Gate of Immortality**. Upon completion, they ascend.

The **Yu-Step Ropes** (*Yǔ Bù Zhī Jiāng*) govern the **Ten Thousand Spirits** (*Wàn Shén*). When the **Ten Thousand Spirits** are rectified and stabilized, the **Five Viscera** (*Wǔ Zàng*) become firm and unassailable, and the **method is perfected, the body true**.

Thus it is said:
*"The True Person’s conduct—*
*When practicing the Lower Division Step Ropes,*
*All must be cultivated according to the **original name-day** (*Běn Míng Rì*) within the **Lower Elemental Jia-Zi Cycle** (*Xià Yuán Jiǎzǐ Zhōu*).*
*Walk three circuits*—
*Annotation:* **Three circuits** mean beginning from the **first step of leisurely movement**, ascending to the **second trace**, up to the **fifteenth trace**.
*—reciting the **Earthly Ropes’** (*Dìjì*) **Eighteen Chapters** (*Shíbā Piān*) and one **Invocation** (*Zhù*), and the **Heavenly Ropes’** (*Tiāngāng*) **Twelve Invocations** (*Shíèr Piān*), completing one circuit.
Upon completion, **twirl the Marshal’s Seal** (*Niǎn Dūjiān Jué*), and shortly thereafter, the practice is finished.
Other applications follow the previous methods.

**Beginning of Volume Ten of the *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* Introduction**

**The Complete Perfection of the Chinese Daoist Sovereign Masters**
**Zhai Wang Fangping (Zhang Daoling), Zhao Shengwang, Chang Sisheng, Li Zhongfu, Mao Ying, Xu Yufu, et al.**—*successive compilers*
**Li Chunfeng’s Daoist Immortal Annotation**
**Preserved: The Method Diagram for Reciting the Seven Stars of the Central Dipper**

**First Star:** *Tānláng* (Acronym: *Lùshénzǐ*)
**Second:** *Kuí*
**Third:** *Yángmíng*
**Fourth:** *Ruòwéi*
**Fifth:** *Shénwǔ*
**Sixth:** *Xuángǔ*
**Seventh:** *Tiānyīng*
**Eighth:** *Chǐfú*
**True Name:** *Pǒuliú*
**Inner Name:** *Quē*

*Superior to the Year-Star (Suìxīng), governing Xu Province.*

**The Celestial Censor-in-Chief (Tiānyùshǐ Zhōngchéng), of Xīhé lineage.**
*Annotation:* This star bears nine names, most being ancient star-official titles. The term *Celestial Censor-in-Chief* mirrors contemporary state offices. The *Northern Dipper’s Censor-in-Chief* holds celestial bureaucratic rank. Those born in the *Zǐ-Hài* branches are attributed to it.

**Second Star:** *Jùmén* (Acronym: *Zhēnzhī*)
**Second:** *□*
**Third:** *Yùjiàn*
**Fourth:** *Yīnjīng*
**Fifth:** *Gǎnwǔ*
**Sixth:** *Tiāngēn*
**Seventh:** *Fǎtí*
**Eighth:** *Yǐwú*
**Inner Name:** *□*

*Superior to the White Star (Tàibái), inferior to Yì Province.*

**The Celestial Grand Marshal (Tiāndà Sīmǎ), of Nánxiāng lineage.**
*Annotation:* Born in the southern lands of Yáng Province, beside Huò Mountain. Those born in the *Chǒu-Hài* branches are attributed to it.

**Third Star:** *Lùcún* (Acronym: *Zǐyí*)
*Annotation:* One manuscript omits *Yí*.
**Second:** *□*
**Third:** *Zhēnrén*
**Fourth:** *Lìjí*
**Fifth:** *Shénjiāng*
**Sixth:** *Tiānzhù*
**Seventh:** *Mìngjī*
**Eighth:** *Lǎoguǐ Yáng*
**Inner Name:** *□*
*Annotation:* The *Inner Name* is the true name. **Guān.**

**Superior to the Vermilion Star (Yínghuò), inferior to Ji Province.**
*Celestial Minor Treasurer (Tiān Shǎofǔ) of the Nine Ministers (Jiǔqīng), a native of Chángshā.*
*Ancient Chángshā County.*
Those born in the *Yín-Xū* branches are attributed to it.

**Fourth Star:** *Wénqū* (Acronym: *Shìhuìzǐ*)
**Second:** *□*
**Third:** *Xuánmíng*
**Fourth:** *Gēngyǔ*
**Fifth:** *Tiānshā*

**Seventh:** *Tiānchún*
**Eighth:** *Suǒnuò*
**Inner Name:** *□*

**Superior to the Star of the Hour (Chén), inferior to Jing Province.**
*In Heaven, the Grand Tutor (Sītú) and Grand Officer of Light and Honor (Guānglù Dàfū), a native of Kuàijī.*
*Some say from Wúzhōng.*
Those born in the *Mǎo-Yǒu* branches are attributed to it.

**Fifth Star:** *Liánzhēn* (Acronym: *Zǐhéng*)
**Second:** *□*
**Third:** *Dānyuán*
**Fourth:** *Zōushōu*
**Fifth:** *Sìwáng*

**Inner Name:** *□*

Those born in the *Chén-Shēn* branches are attributed to it.

**Second:** *□*

**Eighth:** *Chēn□*
**Inner Name:** *□*

**Superior to the Star of the Year (Suì), inferior to Yáng Province.**
*In Heaven, the Grand Officer of the Court of Judicial Review (Tíngwèiqīng), also of Yìyáng.*
*This county produces two Grand Officers—heavenly immortals.*
Those born in the *Yǐ-Wèi* branches are attributed to it.

**Seventh Star:** *Pòjūn* (Acronym: *Dàshíbīn*)
**Second:** *Zhuó*
*Annotation:* *Zhuó* governs the *qi* that subjugates and destroys all things. Thus, in heaven and on earth, humans, gods, dragons, and ghosts—all things are subjected to its influence. Seven degrees bring illness, fourteen degrees bring sickness, twenty-one degrees bring decline, twenty-eight degrees bring death. If one knows and preserves this, one naturally attains divine understanding. *Zhuó* points to malevolent ghosts and bandits, who conceal themselves at the appointed time—this is highly veracious.
**Third:** *Tiānguān*
**Fourth:** *Gǎnjiàn*
**Fifth:** *Jīnfāng*
**Sixth:** *Zhíguāng*
**Seventh:** *Tiānchōng*
**Eighth:** *Cìxīn*
**Inner Name:** *□*

**Superior to the White Star (Tàibái), inferior to Yu Province.**
*In Heaven, the Commander-in-Chief of the Foot Soldiers (Lǐngjūn Bùbīng)*
*Annotation:* An ancient title for a military officer.
*A native of Póyáng.*
Those born in the *Wǔ* branch are attributed to it.

**The Seven Stars, when visible, govern the affairs of birth, death, and ghosts among the people.**
They encompass all phenomena, patrolling the Nine Heavens, completing one circuit of the sky in a day and night. They oversee the Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water, regulating all things. In the lower realm, humans, gods, dragons, ghosts, and all malevolent forces—all fear and submit, daring not to resist.

The Emperor of the Golden Summit of Great Peace (Tàipíng Jīnquè Dìjūn) thus revealed the Nine Ranks to the Heavenly Master, entrusting them to the worthy Daoist children, lest they be misled.

The Venerable Lord said:
*The Seven Stars, when visible, govern the birth and death of all things.*
*Annotation:* All things between Heaven and Earth—those subject to life and death—are governed by the Seven Stars of the Big Dipper.
*All matters of birth and death are directed by these seven officials, not by other celestial departments.*
*There is nothing that does not belong to them.*

Only those with a Daoist heart, filial piety, and devotion to their master may orally transmit the Nine Names. If not a worthy person, one must not recklessly spread them. Misuse will bring calamity upon the seven ancestral generations—not just oneself.

The eighth star is named **Tàishàng Zhēnjūn** (Great Supreme True Lord), also called **Tóngyù** (Same as Jade), **Tiāngǔ** (Celestial Pivot), and **Jìyìng Tiānpéng** (Subduing Response, Heavenly Phoenix). It governs the **Kàn Palace** below, steadfastly presiding over **Jìzhōu** (Sufficiency State). In Heaven, it serves as the **Outer Department**, hidden in form and unseen, overseeing the affairs of the Water Official.

The ninth star is **Gāoshàng Yùhuángdì** (Highest Supreme Jade Emperor).
*Annotation:* The Highest Supreme Jade Emperor is the sovereign of the Nine Officials of the Northern Dipper. He is not the **Great Dao Supreme Jade Emperor**. Instead, he is a **Celestial Overseer**, inspecting the Seven Governments and Nine Palaces, along with all ministers and clerks, and the myriad soldiers. The Highest Supreme Jade Emperor judges all matters within the **Ten Thousand Symbols and Star Officials**, prohibiting unjust killings and warfare. He also oversees all beings, commanding their registration and classification. Externally, he foreknows the times of life and death, reporting them to the **Great Dao Supreme Jade Emperor** without error. Internally, he is named **□** (missing), **Tiānzhèng** (Celestial Rectification), **Shètí** (Concealing Submission), and **Yìyīn** (Augmenting Darkness). His affairs remain unseen in the human world, but if a mortal witnesses him, their lifespan extends by three hundred years.

The **Later Sage Emperor** instructed the **Twenty-Nine True Persons of Xuānzhōu**:
*"To know the inner Dao, one must first recite the Nine Names of the Central Dipper."*
*Annotation:* This refers to the Northern Dipper of today. At the time, people did not recognize it, calling it the Northern Dipper, but it is the Central Dipper. The **Supreme Venerable Lord** taught, also calling it the Central Dipper, commanding seekers of the Dao to know it themselves without instructing the ignorant masses. Thus, one may be removed from the **Death Register** and granted a **Heavenly Birth Name**. Keep it in mind and embody it:
*Annotation:* Keep the names of the two august stars in mind, internalizing them into the five viscera, reciting them day and night without ceasing.

The **clothing** is formed by the **One Dipper and Two Dippers**. After fourteen years, one attains longevity. The **method** was transmitted to the Twenty-Nine True Persons:
*"On your natal day, or on days of the **Jiǎzǐ** (Gengshen) cycle—at dawn or dusk—
*Annotation:* The best time is **midday** (upper), followed by **sì hour** (second), **yǒu hour** (mid), and **night hài hour** (upper), **zǐ hour** (middle), and **chǒu hour** (lower).
—recite the **One Dipper and Two Dippers** fully. Then, through the **Seven Dippers** (missing characters), each recitation must be completed. Afterward, recite the **Earthly Records and Heavenly Halter Charms** once more, and the practice is finished. Those who attain this will have no calamities for one year, no death for two years, become an **Earthly Immortal** in three years, enter **Non-Death** in four, and by five years, their power will be thoroughly attuned to Heaven and Earth, enabling them to rescue beings according to their will. By six years, their **spiritual penetration and longevity** will be self-sufficient—this is the verified power. Do not act recklessly; secrecy brings fortune, while disclosure brings misfortune.
*Annotation:* This is the **Supreme Later Sage’s True Speech instruction**; do not act rashly.

The **Supreme Venerable Lord** said:
*"When forming the **One Dipper and Two Dippers**, one must first grasp the original incantation of the seven stars, then internalize and embody them.
*Annotation:* **Embodying** means keeping the Dipper’s leader or, at the proper time, using the **left shoulder as □**, or **□**, the **mind as □**, or the **hand as □**—this is called **embodying and applying**. Only when the Dipper is formed does it have divine efficacy, allowing one to send forth [spiritual agents].

From the **One Dipper** to the **Seven Dippers**, all follow the original, correct incantation, which must be grasped and applied. The **first □ star’s incantation** is on the **second phalanx of the left second finger**. The **second □ star’s incantation** is on the **first phalanx of the left second finger**. The **third □ star’s incantation** is on the **first phalanx of the left third finger**. The **fourth □ star’s incantation** is on the **second phalanx of the left third finger**. The **fifth □ star’s incantation** is on the **second phalanx of the left fourth finger**. The **sixth □ star’s incantation** is on the **second phalanx of the left fifth finger**. The **seventh □ star’s incantation** is on the **first phalanx of the left fifth finger**.

The **Supreme Venerable Lord** said:
*"When forming the Dipper’s clothing, one must first know the seven stars’ original incantations. Only then can one internalize and embody them on the body, thus attaining spiritual communion. To make the Dipper’s power manifest, grasp this incantation, traversing all seven star-forms. Within the Dipper, the two august imperial stars, the three consorts, and the two ladies—along with the two beloved daughters and great officials—must be reverently honored. They register your **Heavenly Birth Name** above and remove you from the **Death Register** below.

Later scholars, if they practice filial piety, reverence for their master, and offer gold, jade, and silk to the **master’s sacred chamber**, may request this incantation beneath the **precious seat**. Only then should they follow the *Liúzhū* [scroll] to internalize and apply it, thus entering the **Immortal Register** and having their names inscribed on the **Jade Ledger**.

The officials of the Northern Dipper, along with the **Record-Keepers and Registrars**, oversee the **Green Tablets of Destiny** and the **Black Registers of Sentences**. These are all achieved through Daoist power, using the **scribed incantations**. Once applied, the body and mind commune with the **Heavenly and Earthly Spirits**, and their spiritual power becomes effective. If one does not know this incantation, even if they follow the scripture for a hundred years, their practice will yield no benefit.

When this method is obtained and applied, one understands its essence. In one year, they will attain spiritual communion; in two years, they will avoid death and warfare; in three years, they will become an **Immortal Official**. In fourteen years, if they wish to ascend, they ascend; if they wish to remain, they remain. The **Emperor of the Golden Summit of Great Peace** and the **Later Sage Emperor** will appoint them as **Worldly Immortal Officials**, commanding their departures and residences. This method must be kept secret—never transmit it to the unworthy. It is passed down only every seven hundred years, with each transmission limited to three persons. Beyond this, the master will face **Great Judgment**, descend from the **Immortal Rank**, and the disciple, if they steal and misuse it, will suffer **self-annihilation and clan destruction**. This is strictly forbidden.

The **Later Sage Emperor** instructed **Zhang the Heavenly Master**:
*"To practice the **Heavenly Halter and Dipper Clothing**, forming the sequence **One, Two, Three, Four, Five, Six, Seven**, and using it to benefit oneself, aid the nation, stabilize the family, and rescue those in urgent distress from **war, epidemics, fire, and water calamities**, one must first know the **hand incantations**. This is the true power of attaining the Dao."*

When encountering malevolent and wicked individuals approaching,

*Note: When they are still distant (heard but not seen), one may preserve [the power of] one or two *dou*—when they are near (seen), it is too late to preserve any more. Once the* dou *is formed, swiftly pinch the incantation and point at them, then flee to a wider space where an ancient immortal might dwell. There, preserve the* dou *again to halt their killing intent. Then pinch the patterns of one star, two stars, up to seven stars—this suffices.

With urgency, align with the *Clothing of the Dipper*, using the left hand to preserve the *Kui* and *Wei* to subdue [them]. Stand firm and they will submit on their own. Rest for a short while, then depart swiftly. Later, in a wider place with few people, pinch the incantation, preserve the *dou* again, and the malevolent and demonic will retreat in fear, unwilling to leave—if they refuse, they will die. This method is highly effective; do not practice it recklessly—be cautious.

Furthermore, the Sage instructed **Wang Jun**:
*"The incantation states: One* dou *preserves the soul, two* dou *preserve the spirit, three* dou *preserve the essence, four* dou *preserve the body.
*Note: For grave crimes, trust in the method to act accordingly.*
Five* dou *drink blood—
*Note: Drinking blood is another name for the prohibitive incantation.*
Six* dou *execute the spirit—
*Note: This is another name for the judgment of one’s soul and spirit.*
Seven* dou *halt the body.
*Note: If halting does not work, it means beheading—halt is another name for beheading.*

It is also said: Those who constantly practice and refine themselves—preserving one* dou *stabilizes the soul, two* dou *refines the spirit, three* dou *harmonizes the essence,
*Note: Essence is the refined substance of* qi*, the vital force of the form and meridians, moving through* qi*.*
Four* dou *heals illness, five* dou *repels bandits and strengthens the body, six* dou *invokes divine spirits to protect, seven* dou *completes the Dao and attains divine communion. Practicing this for seven years grants the title of *Tian Zhen* [Celestial Purity].
*Note: This means entering the rank of Tian Zhen, though one has not yet attained the method of ascending. After fourteen years, one ascends to heaven, receiving cloud dragons, phoenixes, cranes, music, and dancing. Immortal boys and girls, consorts, and guards—thousands and tens of thousands descend to welcome [them], or the entire family is lifted from their home to depart.*

**Laozi** said: *"Those who cultivate the Dao wish to have the North Dipper govern their lifespan and attain immortality. The incantation and method are found in the *Left Elbow Classic*.
*Note: The Classic is the sacred text of the Daoist scriptures, containing the essential seals and incantation patterns. The talismans are used internally, and the secret method is kept in a short silk pouch tied to the elbow.*

The method of the *Heavenly Halter* is detailed in the Classic diagram.
*Note: The Halter is the Heavenly Halter, the Memoir is the Earthly Memoir.*

**Laozi** said: *"Those who practice must always preserve the Dipper near their body. At night, meditate on the Dipper above the head, as if it envelops the body. By day, visualize it suspended over the forehead—a small, square *dou* of an inch.
*Note: By day, visualize it hanging over the forehead, shifting with each hour. It is one inch long, then cycles downward in the center of the heavens, beside the *Yintang* [third eye], so that malevolent spirits see it and are constantly in awe, subduing their poisonous hearts.*

Recite the invocation:
*'Forehead-suspended Seven Stars—malevolent ghosts flee in terror.
If any dare to harm, they will be beheaded upon turning back.
Swiftly, as the law commands.'*

**Explanation of the Four-Dou Diagram Method**
**Laozi** said: *"The Four-Dou Diagram is the formation of four* dou *across the body. Lift the left hand to the forehead in the shape of a* dou*, curving upward as in the diagram. The palm supports [the star] □, the left elbow [supports] □, the left shoulder to the chest [supports] □, the heart [supports] □, the left inner ankle [seen] from the left inner groin [supports] □, the left knee [supports] □, and the left inner ankle [supports] □. The right side mirrors the left, each forming a* dou *shape.*

Again, reverse the preservation—counting upward from the left inner ankle as *Kui* to the seven stars suffices. This is the method of the Four-Dou.
*Note: Laozi’s method calls the front* dou *the Yang Dipper, the back the Yin Dipper, with two Dipper formations on each side—thus, the Four-Dou. This Dipper dispels ten thousand calamities. The Four-Dou can eliminate the Four Killers, extinguishing malevolent disasters, warfare, ghosts, and demons, instantly dissolving them.
*Note: Dissolving warfare and ghosts means subduing their malevolent influence.*

The Classic states: Seven* dou *dispel celestial calamities and the five departments of malevolent ghosts. Four* dou *dispel earthly disasters and killings, including the Year Pillar, Earthly Officials, and the four departments of hellish ghosts. Five* dou *can dispel the five phases—calamities of metal, water, wood, fire, and earth.

All are preserved in two ranks, subduing malevolent and wicked beings—
*Note: Malevolent beings of the upper ranks.*
Five armies, plagues, poisons, snakes, insects, and beasts. The incantation lies in the Five Knife Supports.
*Note: The Five Knife Supports correspond to the metal, water, wood, fire, and earth phases, all contained within the palm incantation.*

**Explanation of the Dipper-Clothing Alignment Method**
**Laozi** said: *"The Clothing of the Dipper is like wearing the Dipper as garments, with left and right sides—men use the left.
*Note: Men begin with the left side, women with the right.*

For men practicing the Dipper-Clothing Alignment, first form the Four-Dou Diagram, then pinch the incantation,
*Note: The General Supervisory Incantation.*
After a short while, preserve [the star] □ on the left shoulder to the chest,
*Note: Referring to the diagram, the left shoulder to the chest, near the nape, is called the chest-below-head, or more accurately, the axillary chamber. This is named the left and right axillary chambers.*
□ resides in the heart, □ in the left foot’s *Fusu* [hidden mouse point], □ in the left wrist, □ in the left palm.
*Note: The five fingers of the hand are the great palm—grasp them firmly and apply accordingly."*

「□ star resides above the left knee, □ star resides to the right of the left ankle’s inner malleolus.
Women’s practice mirrors this, storing and invoking with the left side first.

This method is to be practiced by both men and women constantly, to avert calamity, disaster, and misfortune.
Those cultivating must first employ the Dipper-Clothing Alignment if they wish to repel malevolence.
Furthermore, cultivators entering deep mountains or valleys, fearing snakes and tigers, should first store [the stars] as a priority.

The Later Sage Emperor declared: This method originates from the Three Element Generals’ stored deployment, extending to the Seven Dou.
From Seven Dou to Four Dou.
From Four Dou to Dipper-Clothing Alignment, from Dipper-Clothing Alignment to Standing-Clothing Alignment—
*Note: This method is identical to Dipper-Clothing Alignment.*
Standing-Clothing Alignment: face south while standing; men turn to face east, women to face west.
The diagram names but does not depict [the stars], so it is omitted accordingly. This is absent in *The Flowing Pearl* [text].

Proceeding to Sleep-Clothing Alignment, then to Sitting-Clothing Alignment.
Once seated, store and deploy the incantation to strike away malevolent blades, and they will self-dissolve.
The Later Sage Emperor again admonished the Celestial Master: This method must not be recklessly transmitted, for reckless transmission invites misfortune and blame. Keep it secret—this is the way of the True Person.

Laozi imparted this method to aid Yellow Emperor in subduing Chi You, to help Yu control the floods, and to assist the Zhou in overthrowing Jie—all to vanquish evil and save the people, guiding them toward goodness.
Laozi often pondered the undiscriminating mix of good and evil, thus commanding rulers and subjects to subdue evil and embrace goodness, to pacify the common folk, to uphold the Dao of Heaven, and to aid the nation’s prosperity, ensuring personal safety and benefiting longevity.
*Note: Historical records show that successive generations inherited this as Heaven’s mandate. Heavenly messengers and divine men descended to impart martial arts, which were then deployed accordingly.*
Scripture states: Each generation’s figures were Laozi’s incarnations, though their names changed with the times, unknown to the populace as the same being adapting names to the era.

**Explanation of the Standing-Clothing Alignment Storage Method Diagram**
Laozi said: Standing-Clothing Alignment is to stand and immediately complete [the alignment].
Ancient True Persons practiced this text and diagram, mastering the incantations passed orally by their teachers. With refined cultivation, standing and thinking, speaking in unison with the heart—nothing is unattained.

**Explanation of the Sleep-Clothing Alignment Storage Method Diagram**
Laozi instructed the Western Mountain Hu King, Da Li: *"I have obtained Heaven’s method, teaching me to sleep in the Dipper [formation], summoning countless armies to encircle my teacher below, yet I endured their calamities unharmed while my teacher was seized for sustenance.
My teacher feared my Heavenly troops, so I saved him.
The Hu King, desperate, sought Laozi.
With a single thought, I lay in the Dipper formation for a short while, and countless armies encircled my teacher’s forces.
My teacher, sensing my intent, retreated and dispersed.
My teacher—
*Note: My teacher refers to Laozi’s disciple, who assumed a transformed guise to assist in subjugating the Hu, then descended from Heaven.*
—led Heaven’s armies to slaughter the Hu King’s forces.
The Hu King, terrified, turned to Laozi for salvation, seeking life with no hesitation.
Laozi immediately stretched out his feet on the bed, lying in the Four Dou formation to rescue him.
Thus, the Hu King’s great sovereign prostrated himself, begging for Daoist instruction, abandoning his throne to follow the Way, adopting the Sleep-Dipper method.
Laozi cursed the Hu King: ‘My multitude—hundreds of thousands—all wish to devour your kin to satiate themselves.
Now, a lofty Celestial True Immortal exists, teaching you the Sleep-Dipper method to repel my Heavenly troops.
Because I cannot yet consume you, I will return later to devour your people.’
Having spoken, he led his divine armies back to Heaven.
The Hu King then struck his head against the ground, beating himself with stones, beseeching the Celestial True Immortal to teach his subjects the Sleep-Dipper method.
Thus, Laozi composed *Two Hundred and Fifty Precepts*, instructing the Hu King.
The King adhered without deviation, and my teacher did not descend again.
After several months, the Hu King announced to his followers: ‘This old Daoist possesses the Sleep-Dipper method, capable of severing my teacher’s descent. My people must learn it together.’
Thus, the Hu King led his followers in three prostrations before Laozi, kneeling to ask: ‘My subjects, unprotected by Daoists, are all slain and devoured by the Heavenly Demon, my teacher.
I now kneel to receive this method to repel these malevolent spirits and ghosts who prey on us.’
At this, Laozi imparted the Sleep-Dipper method. The Hu King cultivated it with unwavering focus, further requesting advanced Daoist teachings, eventually attaining true Buddhahood—all through the Sleep-Dipper method, gaining the Obscure Immortal [status].
*Note: Obscure Immortal refers to Buddhahood.*

**Sleep-Dipper Method**
With the right hand, cover the head and grasp □.
□ resides at the left elbow, □ at the left chest—
the left side of the chest, specifically.
□ resides in the heart, □ in the navel, with the right hand pressed over the navel.
*Note: The navel must not receive the star’s qi directly, so the right hand covers it.*
Store the star on the back of the hand as prescribed; practice this nightly while lying down, and eternal life will endure.
□ resides at the left knee, □ at the left ankle’s inner malleolus.
Both sides are stored and invoked identically.
Additionally, the right side is used similarly: with the left hand’s □, store □ at the right shoulder, □ in the chest, □ in the heart, proceeding in the same manner.
For external coverage of the body, the left side begins with the Foot-Kua star, extending upward to the head.
Next, arrange □, □, □, □, □, □, □—the seven □ stars’ sequence.
The right side begins with the Head-Kua star, extending downward to the foot.
*Note: This follows the same principle as above.*

**Explanation of the Sitting-Clothing Alignment Storage Method Diagram**
Laozi said: Sitting-Clothing Alignment involves calculating and storing the Dipper stars on both sides.»

With hands joined in sitting posture, store □ at the left shoulder, □ in both hands, □ one inch below the left kidney.
This is the method of storing on the clothing.

□ at the left elbow, □ above the knee, □ three inches below the left knee, □ at the right outer ankle.
The right side’s storage follows the same principle.

**Explanation of the Diagram for the Heavenly Pillar Warrior Striking Malevolent Enemies**
The Most High Laozi says:
*"In the world, those who study the Dao may be among people, in the mountains and forests, or on the roads. Suddenly, malevolent bandits or officials may arise to harm them. Close the qi, grasp the incantation, and confront the evil foe. The scripture says: ‘From afar, strike their dwellings.’ The bandits will then cower and flee. This is also an avoidance.

*Note: Because of the Dao’s compassionate way, they are made to cower and retreat. If they do not cower, strike them until the bandits are defeated and dead—this is the proof of success. If they do not cower, strike them until the utmost defeat, until death is complete.*

*First, close the qi and grasp the incantation.
*Note: The incantation is the ‘Sword-Support Incantation,’ named the ‘Sword-Support Incantation for Malevolent Ghost-Bandits.’ Store the malevolent ghost-bandits as previously described in the upper robe.*

*For their dwellings, arrange the Four Dipper Stars to contain malevolent ghostly spirits, preventing them from moving east, west, south, north, or flying above and below. Oneself forms the Four Dipper Stars aligned with the clothing, sealing [them]—
*Note: The front is the mouth, the back is the posterior orifice, releasing the qi.*

Then, write the qi, crossing hands before the chest to form a bow-and-arrow.
*Note: For men, the left elbow is the crossbow, the right the bow—both are stored and verified in use.*

Draw and hold the arrow to shoot. Then, leap over the ground three times, shouting, ‘Shout! Shout!’ The malevolent bandits will immediately fall.
*Note: The scripture says: ‘If you spread the clothing and step.’*

*From the ‘Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl’ Scroll, Volume Ten*
*From the ‘Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl’ Scroll, Volume Eleven*"*

The **Grand Sovereign of the Dao** of the Central Realm, **Master Zaiwang Fangping**, **Zhang Daoling**, **Zhao Sheng**, **Wang Chang**, **Lord of the Command of Life**, **Li Zhongfu**, **Mao Ying**, **Xu Yufu**, and others—these are the successive compilers and authors.

The **Daoist Immortal Li Chunfeng** annotated and explained the **Hidden Names of the Celestial Lords**, where the **Most High Laozi** declared:

*"Those who bear the hidden true names of the Celestial Lords are all the ancestral names and ancestral titles of the Nine Heavenly Emperors. They must always be worn on the left elbow, following the Earthly Measures and the Celestial Ropes. As for the hidden names and hidden titles of the Nine Earthly [realms], they must all be carried in a single pouch.*

*Once the talismans for flight and earthly movement are worn, recite the eighteen chapters of incantations, manipulate the spells according to the method, and then perform the Great Dao.*

*The later Sage Emperor instructed the Celestial Master Zhang Daoling, saying:

*'If you wish to master the essential techniques of the Dao of Immortality, you must wear the true names and hidden titles of the Great Celestial Demons. The Three Elements, Five Stars, Seven Stars of the Northern Dipper, the Twenty-Eight Constellations, Thirty-Five Star Officials, Six Jia [Stems], Nine Provinces, Five Sacred Mountains, Four Great Rivers, the Eight Directions, Ten Thousand Nations, and the myriad mountains and waters—all their true names and hidden titles must be kept upon your person, unseen by others. Your entire life’s record of sins and transgressions shall be sealed by their reverence for you, and they shall all vouch for your name. They shall speak only of your hidden virtues, never of your manifest crimes. The same applies to the Lords of Life and the Lords of Records."*

The method of wearing the true hidden names has its own prescribed rites, found in the *Jīnsuǒ Liúzhū* ["Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl"] section.

Speaking of wearing the earthly hidden names, the Venerable Lord Lao said: On one’s natal day and on the Six Jia days, wearing them for cultivation is most efficacious. The celestial beings will proclaim one’s merits and vouch for one’s name, earning the reverence of the Highest Immortals—these are the true hidden names and true names.

In ancient times, the Yellow Emperor obtained the teachings of Guangchéng Jun, who instructed him to wear these nine earthly true hidden names. Wherever he passed, spirits and numinous beings would appear, bowing and escorting him, daring not to cause harm, and instead submitting to his command.

*Note: In days past, Gāoqīu Zi suddenly entered the mountains, where he encountered a Daoist who gave him the true hidden names of the Nine Provinces and the sacred names of the Five Sacred Mountains. Wearing them on his person, Gāoqīu Zi abstained from meat for one hundred days, then began to travel with them.

One day, as he reached Xiányáng and the sun was setting, he suddenly saw forty-nine men in crimson robes and black caps coming to greet him. Gāoqīu Zi asked why, and they replied: "Because you bear upon your person the true speech, hidden name, true name, surname, and lineage of [a certain] ancestor, we are compelled to serve you. We have come to pay our respects. We feared that the local earth deities and ancestral shrines might be unaware, so we now report this to them in advance, so that they may know the reason."

They then took their leave.*

「Thus, the Later Emperor [常行蹑纪] often practiced the secret steps of the Dao, attaining ascension to the Cloud Celestial [天]. He further spoke of the Western Mountain’s Zhao Rui [赵芮], who for seven generations carried the hidden names of Heaven and Earth [天地之讳] and their sacred names [名], each lineage thus empowered to command ghosts and spirits [驱使鬼神], heal maladies [救人疾病], and accumulate merit [累代着功]. In total, over thirty individuals attained the Dao [得道者计三十余人], achieving longevity [得长生], or the methods of corpse dissolution [尸解之道], or the immortals dwelling in cave palaces [洞府之仙]. Only Zhao Rui’s seventh-generation descendant [赵升] ascended as a Celestial Immortal [天仙], rising in broad daylight [白日] with his entire household [拔宅], all lifted together [俱随身举].

When it came to Sun Rui [孙芮], he was skilled in restraining *qi* [炁禁], but his excessive unlawful slaughter of ghosts and spirits [非法杀害鬼神太多] incurred the wrath of the condemned immortals [被谪仙], who decreed him to serve as a scribe in the Bureau of Examinations [考召书吏]. *注：today’s bureaucratic officials.*

Two thousand years later, he would finally attain the rank of Great Immortal [大仙]. *注：According to the *Nine Provinces Geographical Record* [九州地纪], the Western Mountain was once part of the ancient Jingzhou [古荆州], which is today’s Western Mountain, known as Hongzhou [洪州].*

**Ascension by Household Removal [拔宅] to the Celestial Palace [上升天宫]**
The Most High Venerable Lord [太上老君] declared: *"I received the primordial Dao’s true speech [元始真言] and orthodox teachings [正法], and the Most High Dao Lord [太上道君] vouched for my ascension. Through my mastery of subduing Heavenly Demons [天魔] and Earthly Spirits [地灵], I was able to achieve my body’s transformation and rise in daylight [白日上升]. Only by ascending alone [唯一身而上游] could I pay homage to the Celestial Lords [谒诸天] and worship the Most High Dao Lord [朝拜太上道君]. Afterward, I was permitted to worship the Primordial Heavenly Venerable One [元始天尊], yet I still could not attain ascension by household removal [不得拔宅上升]."*

Now, I have, with unwavering resolve [志心] and focused meditation [精思], compiled the sacred texts and secret keys [秘诀] of various Daoist teachings [众法经文], as well as the hidden scriptures and true speech of the Celestial Lords [诸天隐文真言]. Through this, I have grasped the essence of the Most High’s Golden Talisman [太上金箓之要], extracted from the myriad scriptures [众文中撰出], and achieved ascension by household removal [拔宅], whereby my entire family—men, women, and all—attained the Dao [得道], and even chickens and dogs ascended together [鸡犬一时俱升] to the Cloud Celestial [云天]. From that point onward, I began to manifest ascension by household removal.

*注：Before this, there were no recorded instances of ascension by household removal. Those who prepared and ingested the elixir [将作药成服] would rise to the Cloud Celestial, their entire household lifted, even chickens and dogs attaining the same fate.*

The practice of ascension by household removal [拔宅上升] originated with the Most High Venerable Lord [太上老君]. *注：Before this, there were no recorded instances of ascension by household removal. Those who now attain it [今时得者] are quite common [往往有之], all practicing this method, numbering tens of households [计数十家], already present in the Celestial Courts [见在上天].*

Families such as Li, Wang, Zhang, Xu, Peng, and Han [李王张许彭韩等数家] all ascended by household removal [俱以拔宅]. Li was the Later Sage Lord [后圣君], who in the Western Domain of Zhuqian [竺乾] country transformed the King of Hu into a Buddha [化胡王成佛]. Later, he established the Broad Benevolence Daoist Hall [拔广慈道场], where over a hundred rooms of his residence ascended together [宅院一百余间屋俱升]. Today, it is the Purple Micro Celestial Palace [紫微上宫], the former residence of the Later Sage Lord [后圣君旧宅].

The Later Sage Lord further bestowed upon his servants, chickens, and dogs [更添奴婢鸡犬], granting them ascension as well. *注：This is the Later Sage Lord’s vast compassion and profound mercy [大慈大悲]. His blessings extend to those who have accumulated great merit and achieved profound attainments [恩流赐言功，功大积着多者]. Thus, he permits even their wives, children, disciples, servants, chickens, and dogs [及妻子子弟子奴婢鸡犬] to ascend together [同得俱升].*

The orthodox method of ascension by household removal [拔宅正法] was revealed to the Five Emperors [告五帝]. *注：The Five Emperors [五帝] are the Five Great Celestial Lords of the directions [五方大帝君]. The Former Sage of the Upper Clarity [前圣上清] spoke of offering white jade talismans [素奏丹符], and the Later Sage Lord also revealed the true scriptures to the Five Emperors [真文中五帝亦是].*

If we follow the accounts given by the Former and Later Sage Lords [前后圣人所说], as well as the Celestial Venerable One’s teachings in the scriptures [天尊说经中言五帝], the Five Emperors are the five supreme Celestial Lords [一等五大帝], with no other ranks of Five Emperors [别无五帝位].

Since possessing true names and lineages [有真名姓], in the true scriptures [真文] and the Venerable Lord’s secret talismans [老君秘符], it is said:

*"You wish to ascend your entire household [全家拔宅] and become a Celestial Immortal [上升天仙], attaining the rank of one of the Five Emperors of the directions [为五方帝之位者]. First, you must transform the Five Stars [变五星], manifest the Five Phases [出五行], erect the Five Viscera [竖五藏], transcend the Five Spirits [超五灵], and then you can harness the Five Essences [力摄五精] and command the ten thousand soldiers [驱役万兵]. Your wives and children will become immortals [妻子俱仙], and your servants and livestock will dwell in palaces and courtyards [奴婢宫阙居舍]. Ascending by household removal [拔宅上升] to the Celestial Courts [天庭], you will be titled as one of the Five Emperors of the directions [位号一方之帝], and lead all spirits under the sun, moon, and stars [统领群灵日月星].*
*注：The sun rises and illuminates all directions and the central realm [日出皆照四方中央]. The Five Emperors’ domains [五帝之界] each have their own sun, moon, and stars [皆有日月星], with the three luminaries [三光] shining upon them. All are under the Five Emperors’ directional governance [俱照，皆是五帝随方统领者], and also belong to the Five Emperors by direction [亦随方属於五帝].*

*The Three Officials of Heaven, Earth, and Water [天地水三官], possess both soul and form [有魂魄，有形],*
*注：Those with soul and form [有魂魄，有形] are called *jing* [精].*

*and those with *qi* and without *qi*, with sound and without sound [有炁无炁，有声无声], all belong to the Five Emperors’ domain [皆属五帝之功], manifesting the Dao of nurturing and containing [生成含育之道].*
*This is the method you must practice [是卿所行]—the commandment [行令]."*

The **Dharma Key** [法诀]. The **Laozi** [老君] bestowed this key upon the Five Emperors [五帝], as well as the Three Sovereigns [三皇] and ten thousand **Daoist Immortals** [万仙人],*
*注：The **Laozi** was born before Heaven and Earth [老君先天地生], initially manifesting as the **Dao Master** [始生为道主], and through successive generations, the teachings were transmitted without interruption [代代传教不绝]. The number of those who passed on the teachings before and after him totals ten thousand **Daoist Immortals** [万仙人] and more [已上]. For brevity, we will refer to them collectively as ten thousand.*

—on the method of **ascending the body and extracting the dwelling** [举身拔宅之法], cultivating the **Way of soaring through the heavens** [修行飞蹑].*
*注：The **Way of soaring through the heavens** [飞天纲] and the **Way of treading upon the earth** [蹑地纪].*

In fourteen years, when the **virtue/power** [功] is complete [欲功满], one should begin on the **Spring Day of the Heavenly Stem-Earthly Branch (甲子)** [取春甲子日起], invoking the **Six Ten Kings** [甲子王文卿等六十人], the **Decan Commanders** [旬将], along with the **Twelve Divine Generals** [神将一十二人], the **Sixty Jade Maidens of the Six Heavenly Stems** [六甲玉女六十人], the **Sixty Jade Maidens of the Six Earthly Branches** [六丁玉女六十人], and the **Nine Hundred and More Attendant Officials** [从官九百余人],*
*注：The *Six Heavenly Stems Record* [《六甲录》] lists the exact number of Attendant Officials [从官直符正数], but these three texts differ, so the precise count is omitted here.*

—along with **a million soldiers of the Dao** [兵士一百万人], keeping the invocation both before and behind the body [存呼在身后身在前].

Commence from the **West-North (乾)** [西北乾] above the dwelling, facing **South** [面向南], proceeding with the **Yú Step** [步，作禹步行], circling the dwelling three times [绕宅三匝].*
*注：The three encirclements [三匝] are to be performed during the stillness of night, when no one can see [夜静无人知见].*

Then, **one attains it** [即　得], **but it must not be spoken of** [亦不得言之].

「Furthermore, invoke the **Eight Generals of the Three Primordial Elements and Five Celestial Virtues** [三元五德将军八人], each commanding their troops—*
*注：The **Three Primordial Generals** [三将军] are those of the Mid-Autumn (中元) recorded in the *Tang Ge Zhou’s Three Generals* [唐葛周三将军] text, with each commanding **thirty million soldiers** [兵士各三千万人]. The **Five Celestial Virtues** [五德] refer to the **Generals of the Azure Dragon, White Tiger, Vermilion Bird, Dark Tortoise, and Yellow Court** [青龙、白虎、朱雀、玄武、黄庭大将军等五人], invoked as though holding the *Grand Design* [含弘图].*

**Align the troops of the Three Primordial Elements with their respective generals** [三元随配兵士], as noted previously [具前注]. **Drive them in the four directions.***
*注：The **Five Celestial Virtues Generals** [五德将军] are as follows: the **Azure Dragon General** [青龙将军] of the East, commanding **eighty-one hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士八十一万人]; the **White Tiger General** [白虎将军] of the West, commanding **thirty-six hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士三十六万人]; the **Vermilion Bird General** [朱雀将军] of the South, commanding **sixty-four hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士六十四万人]; the **Dark Tortoise General** [玄武将军] of the North, commanding **twenty-five hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士二十五万人]; and the **Yellow Court General** [黄庭将军] of the Center, commanding **twelve hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士一十二万人]. Each follows their native domain [各随本属], with their officials leading the soldiers [官领兵士] and arriving accordingly.*

**Additionally, summon the Six Generals of the *Golden Lockets and Flowing Pearls*** [《金锁流珠》中六纪将军六人] from the text, each commanding **twelve hundred thousand soldiers** [兵士各一十二万人], and the **Pillar-Heaven Generals** [柱天将军] numbering **one thousand two hundred** [一千二百人]—*
*注：The **Pillar-Heaven Generals** [柱天将军] correspond to the **one thousand two hundred days** [一千二百日] of a sovereign’s reign, directly aligning with the celestial pillar [直柱天上也]. Each general leads **twelve hundred thousand soldiers** [人各兵士一十二万人].*

**Each holds a *Golden Lockets and Flowing Pearls*** [各金锁流珠], their radiance sharp and brilliant, with **three hundred sixty thousand soldiers and steeds** [兵马众三十六万人等], responding to the will and command of the invoker [随心应口]. Thus, they form a **mysterious bond** [玄结] with this humble servant, sealing this dwelling’s boundary—**
**circular and rectangular, measuring [方圆若干亩], ten zhang thick** [厚十丈], and **one hundred chi in height** [百尺], harmonizing with the house and land alike, all rising together [与地俱升].*

**Swiftly, swiftly, as the *Liturgical Commandments* decree** [急急如律令].
**Immediately, recite the *Flick of the Heavenly and Earthly Deities’ Talismans*** [即捻天神地神诀].

**Annotations:**
The *Heavenly Deity Talisman* is located at the third joint of the left hand’s third finger [左手第三指第三节], always bound with five-colored threads. Moreover, on each day of the moon’s waxing phase, it must be anointed with vermilion and ink before twisting.

The *Earthly Deity Talisman* lies beneath both feet. **Note:** Near the heart of the left foot is a mark resembling a fish—this is the *Earthly Deity Talisman*. Always, when approaching the *Step-Binding Rite* [步纲日], three days prior, anoint it with vermilion and ink before performing the rite.

Additionally, one must twist the *Dwelling Deity Talisman* and the *Water Deity-Kua Deity Talisman*, located at the second joint of the left hand’s fourth finger—this governs the entire dwelling. The *Superintendent of the Twelve Monthly Deities* must also be invoked through the *Supreme Deity’s Eye* and the *Descending Palace Talisman*, etc.

Upon completion, command the deities thus:

*"To the five celestial generals of the East—*Jia, Yi, Ying, Mao, Chen*—governed by the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches, leading eight hundred and ten thousand officers and soldiers, to forbid trespass and uproot this dwelling! The East marks the *Mysterious Dwelling’s* outer boundary, penetrating ten zhang into the earth, blending with the soil to uproot. May the decree ascend—along with the household’s living and dead, male and female, fowl and canine—all ascending to the Celestial Court. Swiftly, swiftly, as the *Liturgical Commandments* decree."*

*"To the five celestial generals of the South—*Bing, Ding, Ji, Wu, Wei*—governed by the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches, leading six hundred and forty thousand officers and soldiers, to forbid trespass and uproot this dwelling! The South marks the *Mysterious Dwelling’s* outer boundary, penetrating ten zhang into the earth, blending with the soil to uproot. May the decree ascend—along with the household’s great and small, male and female, slaves and maidservants, fowl and canine—all ascending to the Celestial Court. Swiftly, swiftly, as the *Liturgical Commandments* decree."*

*"To the five celestial generals of the West—*Geng, Xin, Shen, You, Xu*—governed by the Heavenly Stems and Earthly Branches, leading three hundred and sixty thousand officers and soldiers, to forbid trespass and uproot this dwelling! The West marks the *Mysterious Dwelling’s* outer boundary, penetrating ten zhang into the earth, blending with the soil to uproot. May the decree ascend—along with the household’s great and small, slaves and maidservants, fowl and canine—*
**Note:** *The ancient texts omit the term "slaves," but in *The Inner Transmission of the Later Sage-King*, it explicitly states that during dwelling-uprooting, disciples (male and female) and slaves and maidservants are included. Moreover, it is often recorded that disciples, male and female slaves, fowl, canines, oxen, and horses ascend together in great numbers. This is the work of the winds, hence the earlier omission in the Eastern invocation.*"

And from the South, beginning and concluding with the Four Directions, Four Cardinal Points, and Four Fixations—this is transmitted only to those who uphold the Dao/Way, not to the common folk. Together, ascend to the Celestial Court. **Swiftly, as the decree commands.**

Again, the Northern Five Deities of *Geng-Xin-Shen-You-Xu* and *Ren-Gui-Hai-Zi-Chou* branches, commanding twenty-five ten-thousand officers and soldiers, to forbid trespass and uproot this dwelling. The North marks the *Mysterious Dwelling’s* outer boundary, penetrating ten *zhang* into the earth, blending with the soil to uproot. May the decree ascend—along with the household’s great and small, wives and concubines, male and female alike.
**Note:** The ancient texts also omit the terms "wives and concubines, male and female," but in *The Later Sage-King’s Transmission to the Heavenly Master on Dwelling-Uprooting*, the decree to officers and soldiers explicitly includes "wives and concubines" and "male and female." Within the Northern invocation, it specifies three wives, four concubines, and one child. All are detailed in the Northern Dwelling-Uprooting Decree. This is transmitted to those who uphold the Dao/Way, for they know that through great merit in cultivation, wives and concubines may ascend together to the Celestial Palaces of the Immortals. Slaves, maidservants, fowl, and canines ascend to the Celestial Court. **Swiftly, as the decree commands.**

Again, the Four Directions—
**Note:** *Yin, Shen, Wei, Hai* are the Four Directional Deities.
Also called the Four Seasonal Deities.
And the Four Cardinal Points—
**Note:** *Zi, Wu, Mao, You* are the names of the Four Cardinal Points.
And the Four Fixations—
**Note:** *Chen, Xiu, Chou, Wei* are the Four Fixations.
Also, it is said: The Four Seasons are the earthly names for the Four Fixations, aligned with the master’s intent. The first Fixation is Southeast, the second Northwest, the third Northeast, the fourth Southwest—hence the name Four Fixations. The scripture states: Where the Fixation is set, great calamity shall arise. Aligned with the earthly branch, thus where Saturn’s influence lingers, great calamity shall befall. The Later Sage-King knew this, so he established the Dwelling-Uprooting Divine Method, naming it the Four Fixations, to repel misfortune and avert disaster. No calamity dares to encroach. The great Dao’s divine power, the rectified Fixation’s force, uproots the dwelling. The combined power of the twelve gods of the third and fourth ranks lifts the dwelling to ascend to the clouds, to the Seven-Treasured Mysterious Platform of the Golden Gate, the Jade Capital’s Upper Palace within the Luohean Great City, upon the vacant sacred land within ten *mu*, where the dwelling may reside. As a minister aiding the Later Sage-King’s Palace, one attains the rank of lesser official, eternal life and longevity, and may serve the Later Sage-King as desired. The decree commands the uprooting of this dwelling—**swiftly, as the decree commands.**

Again, the six *Wu-Ji* Generals and six *Liu-Ji* Generals, each commanding twelve ten-thousand soldiers, with the *Xuanbu* officers forbidding trespass, uprooting the dwelling to ascend. The Heavenly Immortals unite in heart and strength, alongside the twelve gods of the Four Directions, their beasts, soldiers, horses, and all—together forming the dwelling’s boundary, ascending to the Celestial Court within the Golden Gate and Jade Capital. **Swiftly, as the decree commands.** Recite and chant.

---

**Annotation:** *Note: When reading, one must roll the scroll; otherwise, it is not as effective as reciting. The Great Sage-Laozi says: If one wishes to uproot the dwelling and ascend to the Celestial Court—*

**Annotation:** *The Celestial Court refers to the Palace of the Jade Emperor, the Most High, and is thus called the Celestial Court.*

—*first invoke the deities of the human gate,*

**Annotation:** *The human gate (人门) refers to the gate of the mortal realm.*

—*from the southwest to the northwest of the dwelling, invoking the upper deities: the Monkey-headed, human-bodied one, clad in white robes, left hand grasping an arrow, right hand holding a crossbow, named **Jianbing** (监兵), who guards the southwest quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Rooster-headed, human-bodied one, clad in white robes, left hand grasping an arrow, right hand holding a crossbow, named **Zi’en** (子恩), guards the due west of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Dog-headed, human-bodied one, clad in white robes, left hand grasping an arrow, right hand holding a crossbow, named **Gonglong** (弓隆), guards the northwest quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers.*

—*from the northwest to the northeast of the dwelling, invoking the upper deities: the Boar-headed, human-bodied one, clad in black robes, left hand wielding a hooked spear, named **Bùlín** (不临), who guards the northwest quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Rat-headed, human-bodied one, clad in black robes, left hand wielding a hooked spear, named **Zhímíng** (执明), guards the due north of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Ox-headed, human-bodied one, clad in black robes, left hand wielding a hooked spear, named **Ājūn** (阿君), guards the northeast quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers.*

—*from the northeast to the southeast of the dwelling, invoking the upper deities: the Tiger-headed, human-bodied one, clad in green robes, left hand holding a spear, named **Mèngzhāng** (孟章), who guards the northeast quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Hare-headed, human-bodied one, clad in green robes, left hand holding a spear, named **Ménzhī** (门之), guards the due east of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Dragon-headed, human-bodied one, clad in green robes, left hand holding a spear, named **Tiānjīn** (天禽), guards the southeast quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers.*

—*from the southeast to the southwest of the dwelling, invoking the upper deities: the Serpent-headed, human-bodied one, clad in red robes, left hand holding a pike, named **Yìfáng** (寄房), who guards the southeast quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Horse-headed, human-bodied one, clad in red robes, left hand holding a pike, named **Língguāng** (陵光), guards the due south of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers. The Sheep-headed, human-bodied one, clad in red robes, left hand holding a pike, named **Chújūn** (除君), guards the southwest quadrant of Heaven and commands a hundred thousand soldiers.*

*The Left General emerges from the Southern Gate of the Big Dipper and flies to the left. The Central General emerges from the Southern Gate of the Big Dipper and flies ahead.*

The Right General emerges from the Southern Gate of the Big Dipper and flies to the right.

Summon the three generals by name in a low voice. When finished,
**Annotation:** Left General: surname Tang, given name Hong. Right General: surname Ge, given name Yong. Central General: surname Zhou, given name Wu.
The three generals’ names are recorded in their talismans (*fù*). When invoking, write only their names and append their talisman characters.

Whenever encountering multiple talismans without the three generals’ names, do not annotate them.

Next, invoke:
Left—**Qīnglóng** (青龙),
Right—**Báihǔ** (白虎),
Front—**Zhūquè** (朱雀),
Rear—**Xuānwǔ** (玄武),
Gate—**Shīzǐ** (师子),
Central courtyard—**Báiè** (白鹤),
and the **Zǐyún Gài** (紫云盖) over the dwelling.

Then enter through the **Earthly Gate**,
**Annotation:** The Earthly Gate is the southeast door.
Within the courtyard, tread the **Earthly Compass** (*Dìjì*) three times, then the **Celestial Ropes** (*Tiāngāng*) three times.

When finished, disperse into the **Great Yú’s Steps** (*Dàyǔ bù*) fifteen strides.

When finished, **align the robes** with seven *dǒu* of grain.
**Annotation:** In previous methods, alignment required one or two *dǒu* of grain. This **Dwelling-Extraction Method** demands seven *dǒu* for completion.

This is from *The Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* (《金锁流珠》), Volume Two, Upper Section—concerning the **Earthly Compass**—where the **qi of the Seven Mansions** first becomes sufficient, summoning ten thousand spirits and myriad sacred beings to guard and assist the body.

Then turn the **Celestial Ropes**, pointing to the four directions and the Central Palace, the four cardinals and four intercardinals—each as prescribed.

Within no more than three years, the dwelling, along with the practitioner’s family—men, women, and all household creatures—shall ascend as Heavenly Immortals.

**Facing east**, turn the **Celestial Ropes** and point to the **East Boundary** of the **Jia-Yǐ** region (Wood, the **Yin-Yǎo-Chén** three generals). Each commands a hundred thousand soldiers. Erect this dwelling’s eastern side with sturdy earth and wood above, and an iron-encircled steel foundation below. If the eastern side is properly aligned, the practitioner and household—noble or lowly, even chickens and dogs—shall all ascend as Heavenly Immortals in the Celestial Court.
*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

**Facing south**, turn the **Celestial Ropes** and point to the **South Boundary** of the **Bǐng-Dīng** region (Fire, the **Wǔ-Wǔ-Wèi** three generals). Each commands a hundred thousand soldiers. Erect this dwelling’s southern side with sturdy earth and wood above, and an iron-encircled steel foundation below. If the southern side is properly aligned, the practitioner and household—noble or lowly, even chickens and dogs—shall all ascend as Heavenly Immortals in the Celestial Court.
*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

**Facing west**, turn the **Celestial Ropes** and point to the **West Boundary** of the **Gēng-Xīn** region (Metal, the **Shēn-Yǒu-Xū** three generals). Each commands a hundred thousand soldiers. Erect this dwelling’s western side with sturdy earth and wood above, and an iron-encircled steel foundation below. If the western side is properly aligned, the practitioner and household—noble or lowly, even chickens and dogs—shall all ascend as Heavenly Immortals in the Celestial Court.
*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

**Facing north**, turn the **Celestial Ropes** and point to the **North Boundary** of the **Rén-Gǔi** region (Water, the **Hài-Zǐ-Chǒu** three generals). Each commands a hundred thousand soldiers. Erect this dwelling’s northern side with sturdy earth and wood above, and an iron-encircled steel foundation below. If the northern side is properly aligned, the practitioner and household—noble or lowly, even chickens and dogs—shall all ascend as Heavenly Immortals in the Celestial Court.
*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

**Standing before the Heavenly Gate**, face upward, surveying the Central Palace and its upper and lower realms. Turn the **Celestial Ropes** and point to the Central Palace and the four seasonal regions (Earth, the **Wù-Wèi-Chén-Xū-Zǐ-Wèi** six generals).
**Annotation:** The scripture speaks of the **Six Compass Generals**.
Each leads a hundred thousand soldiers, totaling six hundred thousand troops—all under the **Nine Earth Gods’** divine command, capable of moving mountains and damming seas, their dwelling-extraction power immense.

Together with the four cardinal and intercardinal officers and the **Great Generals of the Stellar Officials**, with united hearts and strength, they shall extract the dwelling and make it float in the sky—no greater difficulty than commonplace matters.

Each commands a hundred thousand soldiers. Erect this dwelling’s central palace with three inner chambers, east and west corridors, a hall, gate, and storehouse, four surrounding courtyards (east, west, south, north), a quiet chamber, granary, high-legged stove, central courtyard study, and slave quarters as needed.
**Annotation:** The Heavenly Master’s dwelling has one hundred twenty rooms. The Shu Zhang Heavenly Master’s dwelling, with one hundred twenty rooms, was also extracted and ascended to the **Golden Gate’s Inner City** in the **Yùjīng’s** southeast void, occupying sixty-four *mǔ* of land as his residence. There, he served as the **Left Celestial Prime Minister** under the **Posterior Sage of the Jade Capital**, his halls and structures fortified with iron foundations in the central palace.

The dwelling’s size—great or small—must have sturdy tiles and wood. Within: three inner chambers, east and west corridors, hall, gate, storehouse, four surrounding courtyards, quiet chamber, granary, high-legged stove, and all necessary slave quarters. The practitioner and household—noble or lowly, including residences, chicken coops, and horse stables—must all ascend together to the Celestial Court.
*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

Next, command the **Four Cardinals**,

The **Four Cardinals**—Mao, You, Zi, Wu—are fixed.
The **Four Defined**—Chen, Xū, Chǒu, Wèi—are established.
The **Eight Trigrams**: Qián, Kàn, Gèn, Zhèn, Xùn, Lí, Kūn, Duì.

The **Three Generals of the Residence**, the **Five Phases of Well and Hearth**, the **Six Jia and Six Ding**, and all divine soldiers—when summoned by the **Mystic Command**, they shall act as commanded. Lift the residence and its structures, fly alongside the body, and ascend to dwell above.

*As the command is given, so it shall be done.*

Then cease, and recite the **Grand Overseer’s Secret**, along with the **Heavenly Principles and Earthly Principles Secrets**, either inscribed in red or black ink. When finished, the task is complete.

Often thus, practiced for three years, the spirits will ever guard the residence and body, enabling the ascent of the dwelling together.

This method is most wondrous—do not recklessly transmit it to the unworthy.

The **Posterior Sage of the Jade Capital** instructed the **Twenty-Nine True Ones of the Mystic Realm** and **Master Zhang of Heaven** thus:

*"From this day forward, teach those with sincere Daoist intent and good will to first cultivate **yin virtue** in all things.
**Note:** *Yin virtue* is detailed in the preceding annotations.

Do not nurture malevolent creatures; instead, accumulate deeds of **yin virtue**.
**Note:** When *yin virtue* is complete, Daoist merit is established, and descendants flourish while the residence ascends with the body.

Avoid **yin schemes and envy**; always practice **yin benevolence and strength**.
**Note:** When virtue extends to all beings, such a path will naturally attract the worthy—it is not the worthy who seek the path.

In ancient times, the **Ascetic of Bitter Practice** relentlessly sought wealth to bestow upon others, amassing merit ten thousandfold. By day, a spirit descended, and together they ascended to the celestial realm.

Now, the **Mystic Command** of this method, infused with virtue, inspires you. Further refine this **central incantation**, summoning all great divine spirits to aid in lifting the residence and ascending to the heavens.

For mortals, use the **step-incantation** to invoke the great gods of Heaven and Earth, assisting you in lifting the residence and ascending to the Celestial Court.*

Again, the Sage instructed Master Zhang:

*"If you desire a residence, livestock, and all that ascends with you upon the Daoist chariot to the Heavenly Dao—when a new dwelling is fully constructed, its four gates sealed as in a prefectural or county home,
**Note:** The residence should resemble a temple, newly built with sturdy foundations. For newly constructed dwellings of solidity—

Follow the **step-treading central incantation** as before. When the merit reaches one thousand days, you shall naturally ascend with me.

The Heavenly Emperor selects auspicious land, erects the foundation, and plants the structure within the Jade Capital, ever commanding celestial spirits to guard this residence without ceasing.*

Again, the Sage instructed Master Zhang:

*"If a mortal’s residence is unstable, with loss of life or property, on the **Four Beginning Days**, inscribe on stones of five colors the characters **‘Dissipate Calamities and Repel Harm’**, each governing a cardinal direction.
**Note:** East—blue stone, South—red stone, West—white stone, North—black stone, Central Palace—yellow stone. For the Son of Heaven, one thousand *jin*; for nobles, six hundred *jin*; each weighing one hundred twenty *jin*.
According to the *Ritual for Pacifying the Residence*, for the fifth rank and below, one hundred twenty *jin*. Each stone bears four characters, buried one *chi* deep—this is the standard for lesser nobles. For commoners, one *chi*; for Daoists, three *chi*—these are the original measurements.

Later, if you wish to lift the residence and ascend, these stones need not be moved. This is the **Supreme Realm’s method for pacifying the residence**—keep it secret, and do not transmit it recklessly to the unworthy.*

**Laozi said:** *"When preparing to lift the residence and ascend through practice—
**Note:** This refers to those who practice the method of lifting the residence, reciting the step-incantation both day and night.

Before beginning, place the **Original Master** at the forefront, followed by the **Jade Boys and Jade Girls**, the **Three Sovereigns and Five Virtues**, the **Six Jia and Eight Trigrams**,
**Note:** The Eight Trigrams: Jia, Yi, Bing, Ding, Geng, Xin, Ren, Gui—these are the divine spirits of the trigrams.

the **Twelve Branches**, and the **Twenty-Four Qi Spirits**, riding the **Chariot of the Exalted**, driving the **Dragon Chariot**, arriving before you. The Original Master follows behind, and you stand as in the *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl* diagram.

Thus, for three years, the Master summons the Earth Spirits, ordering the **Earth Axis** to perpetually encircle the residence on either side, dispelling all malevolent and harmful *qi*, ensuring perpetual tranquility and security. The spirits are arrayed in ranks, awaiting the day the residence’s master ascends, following the Original Master’s commands.
**Note:** According to the *Canon of the Orthodox Dao*, when one attains the Dao, it is because the Original Master’s disciple naturally reveres the teacher. The Master, in the void, knows the disciple’s filial heart. On the day of attainment, the **Most High** dispatches an envoy to welcome them, leading them to pay respects to the officials, observing proper greetings and bows before announcing their ascent to a celestial abode.

The generals float above the residence, entering the **Five Clouds**, the Earth Axis and Earth Locks rolling with the land, ascending with the master without difficulty. In an instant, the **Dragon, Tiger, Phoenix, Warrior, Lion, and Crane** stand ready to lift them lightly into the air.

**Laozi’s Transmission of the Inner Central Incantation Diagram for Lifting the Residence**
This residence extends **560 paces** from west to east, north to south.
This residence extends **560 paces** from east to west, north to south.
If not adhering to this, it is the **Heavenly Master’s residential measurement**, as depicted in the diagram.
Now, mortals may adjust the length and breadth as needed.*

**Laozi said:** *"When the step-incantation is complete, invoke the **Central Marshal Spirit** from the earth—one thousand two hundred in number, each wielding a sword, six *zhang* five *chi* tall, with a single stride covering sixty *zhang*, possessing immense strength to aid in lifting the residence. When the incantation is recited and the secret is invoked, the spirit arrives to assist in lifting the residence—this is most efficacious, swift as the wind. The diagram is found in the *Canon of the Flowing Pearl*.
**Note:** Within the *Flowing Pearl*, in the **Central Element’s Three Generals** section.

*End of Volume Eleven of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl.*
*End of Volume Twelve of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl."*

Now, the **Zhenren** of the Central Kingdom, the Great Immortal Master, **Zaiwang Fangping**, **Zhang Daoling**, **Zhao Sheng**, **Wang Chang**, **Li Zhongfu**, **Mao Ying**, **Xu Yufu**, and others, are those who composed this in succession. The **Immortal Master Li Chunfeng** annotated it.

The **Five Phases** and **Six Seasons** give rise to the following:

The **Taishang Lao君 (Laozi)** said to the **Taiji Zhenren** (True Person of the Supreme Ultimate):

*"The Dao generates **One**,
**Note:** **One** refers to Heaven.
The **Taiyi** (Great Unity) Spirit, named the **Qi** of the **Taiyang** (Great Sun), emits the **Taiyang**’s radiant essence, condensing into the Sun.
The **Qi** of the Sun descends and unites with **Yin** below.
**One** generates **Two**,
**Note:** **Two** refers to Earth.
The **Qi** of **Yin**, ascending, forms the Moon. The **Qi** of the Moon merges below with **Yang**, thus the **Yin** and **Yang** **Qi** intermingle, condensing into sentient beings who dwell between Heaven and Earth—known as the **Three Talents** (San Cai).
**Two** generates **Three**,
**Note:** **Three** refers to Humanity.
Once there is Humanity, there arise the four seasons—**Cold, Heat, Spring, Autumn**—in cyclical rotation, endlessly recurring, giving birth to the **Four Heavenly Kings** (Sijian Sishen, Sifu).
This doctrine comes from the *Thunder King’s Rituals* (Leigong Shì), a record by the **Yellow Emperor** (Huangdi), applied to the four seasons, producing the **Four Pillars** (Sifu).
Each **Pillar** governs a direction, issuing commands—these are **Spring, Summer, Autumn, Winter**.
Called the **Four Heavenly Kings**, they harmonize with the **Four Rituals** (Sishi), overseeing the **Four Pillars** (Sifu).

**Three** generates the **Four Seasons**, as previously annotated.
The **Four Seasons** generate the **Five Phases**,
**Note:** The **Five Phases** are what follows.
The **Five Phases** generate the **Six Jia** (Lujia), the **Six Jia** generate the **Seven Stars** (Qixing), the **Seven Stars** generate the **Eight Trigrams** (Bagua), the **Eight Trigrams** generate the **Nine Essences** (Jiujing), the **Nine Essences** generate the **Ten Celestial Stems** (Shiganzhen), the **Ten Celestial Stems** generate the **Twelve Earthly Branches** (Shierzhixiang), the **Twelve Earthly Branches** generate the **Twenty-Eight Constellations** (Ershibaxiu), and the **Twenty-Eight Constellations** generate the **Five Luminaries and Thirty-Six Official Stars** (Wudou Sanshi Liu Guanxing). The **Five Luminaries** and **Thirty-Six Official Stars** generate the **Three Filths and Five Official Stars** (Sanwu Wuguanxing), which in turn produce the **Circulating Heavens of Ten Thousand Phenomena** (Zhoutian Wanshang), and the **Circulating Heavens** generate the **Boundless** (Wuqiong).

The **Five Phases** are thus generated. Named **Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, Earth**, they are the **Five Stars** (Wuxing).
When a mortal’s life begins, they are assigned the **Five Phases**, thus receiving their fate.
They also follow the **Five Phases**, determining their rise and decline.
**Note:** *For those who study the Dao, always observe that Metal and Wood oppose each other—I do not endure opposition. Metal generates Water—I follow accordingly. Water extinguishes Fire—I do not endure extinction. Fire generates Wood—I flourish and thrive. If the Five Phases do not harm me, I seek eternal life.*

The **Five** (Wu) are manifest in Heaven’s **Five Stars**, humanity’s **Five Viscera** (Wuzang), and Earth’s **Five Mountains** (Wuyue)—the **Three Fives** (Sanwu).

**One** is the sovereign of all **Dao**, the origin of all Spirits, encompassing the vast without exclusion, containing the minute without omission.
**Note:** **One** is said to permeate even the finest details, encompassing the greatest breadth—thus it is.

Hence, it can both generate and extinguish mortals.
**Note:** *When the Five Phases support each other, they generate. When they oppose each other, they extinguish.*
All that mortals generate are governed by the **Five Phases**.

For instance, a person born under the **Eastern Wood Phase** (Mingming) with **Hai** (亥) as their **Pillar** (Fufu), generates **Water**,
**Note:** *Water can float Wood, and Earth can nourish Wood. A Wood Phase fate receiving the Qi of these two stars is auspicious.*
and **Fire** can burn Wood, making them a **Great King** (Dawang).
**Metal** opposes Wood—Wood fears **Metal**.
They generate **Earth**,
**Note:** *Though Wood opposes Earth, Earth can also sustain Wood. Wood remains unharmed while generating the auspicious symbol of a king—thus, wearing an Earth Phase talisman is fortunate.*
and they generate **Fire**.
