**Note:** *Fire and Wood unite—though Wood is consumed by Fire, its Qi of transformation and assimilation remains unharmed, and it attains greatness as a king. It is fitting to wear a Fire Phase talisman to seek wealth.*
Yet they fear **Metal**.
**Note:** *Metal opposes Wood.*

In the **Jiazi** (甲子) cycle, there are sixty days when **Metal** opposes **Wood**—these are:
**Jiazi** (甲子), **Jiawu** (甲午), **Renyin** (壬寅), **Xinhao** (辛亥), **Renshen** (壬申), **Guiyou** (癸酉).
These six days are the ones in question.
If one practices as usual, on **Dingmao** (丁卯) Fire Days, inscribe the talisman of the **Yinghuo Star King** (Yinghuo Xingjun) and wear it. Replace the talisman every sixty days.

For those born under the **Fire Phase** (Mingming), using **Yin** (寅) as their **Pillar**, they generate **Wood**,
**Note:** *Wood nourishes Fire, and Earth sustains Fire. One might also say Water can extinguish Fire—Fire thus fears Water.*
and wear **Earth** talismans on long straps to subdue it, achieving longevity.
They generate **Metal**,
**Note:** *Though Fire melts Metal, it also refines and transmutes it into vessels—thus the way of mutual transformation.*
and their kingship lies in **Wood** and **Earth**.
**Note:** *Fire attains kingship through Wood and finds stability through Earth. Thus, wear Wood talismans for kingship and Earth talismans to stabilize the spirit.*

Yet they fear **Water**.
**Note:** *Water extinguishes Fire.*

Thus, those born under the **Fire Phase** are few, and their **Pillars** are often weak, with many afflictions, calamities, and encounters with ghosts and demons—this is because **Water** can extinguish **Fire**. Among the **Four Pillars**, only **Water** and **Fire** are said to mutually extinguish. One must invest in the Dao early in life.
Wear talismans of **Earth** and **Wood** to subdue the **Fire** within, thus attaining bodily peace and spiritual protection.
Additionally, chant the names of the **Earth** and **Wood** stars’ essences aloud—guard the body of this humble servant, repelling the calamitous **Water** star’s long essence. Command it to depart from this humble servant’s spirit and body, from the **Three Souls** (Sanhun) and **Seven Spirits** (Qipo), and remain two thousand *li* away, never to interfere again.

Inscribe **Wood** talismans on Fire Days and **Earth** talismans on Metal Days, and wear them perpetually—auspicious.

For those born under the **Metal Phase** (Mingming), using **Yi** (巳) as their **Pillar**, they generate **Earth**,
**Note:** *This is not the true Earth Phase; Yi borrows the position of Chen (辰), Chen being the true Earth.*
and **Yi** is the true Fire Phase.
Fire opposes Metal, which is not the Metal’s true origin.
In ancient times, the great immortals thus shifted their palaces to borrow positions, taking Chen twice—this is because the seasonal spirits do not properly receive their generated phases, and one must again push the true position to Yi.
Yi belongs to Fire, hence it is taken as the generated phase.
Yet always contemplate the **Earth** star—wear talismans of **Earth** and **Fire** together, never letting them oppose each other, but instead generating and transforming each other—thus achieving kingship.
They transform through **Wood** and **Fire**,
**Note:** *Though Fire opposes Metal, it also refines and transmutes it into vessels.*

The **Sage’s correct intent** states: *"A slight initial misfortune will be followed by lasting good fortune."*

Again, Metal can subdue Wood, and Wood can generate Fire. Fire cannot arise without Wood, so it is said that **Wood and Fire** generate each other and can thus subdue Metal.

**Metal-born individuals** must employ **Water and Earth** stars and planets, shifting and turning to subdue and harmonize. Therefore, each night when one sleeps, they should always preserve the **Earth star** and **Water spirit** to protect their body, with the **Wood spirit** before them and the **Fire spirit** behind them, constantly guarding them. They should also wear talismans of **Earth and Fire** upon themselves, so that they may always generate and transform each other, never opposing or harming one another.

Later, the **Sage of the Later Age** instructed **Chisongzi** (赤松子): *"You are a Metal-born individual. Your origin lies in **Yi** (已), which belongs to the Fire Phase, and within that Phase, you must always endure. This is because being of that Phase, it is naturally harmful to your body. You can take **Chen** (辰) as your borrowed palace, for the Earth Phase belongs to Metal, ensuring lasting good fortune. Also, wear talismans of **Wood and Water** to suppress any harmful **qi** (炁), for it will naturally dissipate and vanish. The **qi** that rules is **Water**,*
**Note:** *Water can generate Metal, hence it is taken as the ruling **qi**.*

*always wear talismans of the **Water star**, placing them upon your head, for lasting good fortune. The **qi** you fear is **Fire**.*
**Note:** *If Fire acts alone to subdue Metal, Metal will suffer harm. If Water comes before Fire, Fire cannot subdue Metal. Hence, for those seeking Metal’s salvation, Water is the answer.*

**Metal-born individuals** should always, at night, contemplate the **Water spirit**, visualizing it upon their body, beside them, and within the tent around them, keeping it ever-present as though seen. The **Fire star** and **Chen** essence will not dare to approach, ensuring that one will never be harmed throughout their life. With practice, they will achieve their desired outcome, and when their merit is complete, they will ascend during daylight.

Later, the **Sage of the Later Age** told the **Celestial Master** (天师): *"It is not only that Metal-born individuals fear Fire; all five types of individuals have mutual subduing and annihilation. They all depend on this Metal-born calculation to find their generating **qi**, teaching future generations. Though Metal fears Fire, it is refined and cast into form through Fire’s tempering, and supported by Water, it naturally attains firmness and integrity—such as the use of blackened Metal as vessels. This is the Metal of the five colors."*
**Note:** *Gold, silver, iron, copper, and tin are the five Metals.*

*All must follow the great principles to attain their true forms. For **Water-born** and **Earth-born** individuals, their generating palace is **Shen** (申), and they generate Metal.*
**Note:** *Metal, here, refers to the **Western Metal Phase** (西方金). The native Phase of Water and Earth.*

*Though Water and Earth generate the five Metals, it is not the five Metals that generate from Water and Earth. What is meant by "generating Metal" is that the **Western Metal Phase** (庚辛之地) belongs to the Metal Phase, and thus the **Water and Earth stars**, being of the **Greater Yin** (太阴) **qi**, form into the shapes of Water and Earth—this is their native Phase belonging to Metal. The **qi** that transforms is **Wood**.*
**Note:** *Though Wood floats upon Water, it can generate Water’s **virtue/power** (德).*

Again, it transforms into **Fire**.
**Note:** Fire finds stability in Earth, and Earth, with Fire, becomes firm and unyielding—thus, it is said that they mutually perfect each other in forming vessels.

It generates **Metal**.
**Note:** Metal is the child of Water; though unseen, it receives the **virtue/power** of the Sovereign, hence its alignment with the Sovereign’s symbols in the use of Water and Metal.

The methods of these two Phases are fundamentally the same as before.

Again, what they **Sovereign** is the same: Water **Sovereigns** over Metal, which is the **Sovereignty** of Earth.

The **qi** of the Five Phases each have what mutually perfects and what mutually restrains.
Thus, when a person receives mutual perfection, their lifespan is long; when they receive mutual restraint, their lifespan is short—this is not a matter of Heaven’s decree.
If one does not know this within oneself, they will inevitably meet death.
If one’s body and mind know this, their lifespan will be eternal without decay.
**Note:** This is Laozi speaking to Yin Xi.

The Sage is no different from Heaven and Earth, yet even they have their ailments.
**Note:** Their ailments are the winds and rains of sorrow—this is what is meant by "disease."
Disease is also the result of the **qi** of the Five Phases mutually restraining and defeating one another, hence it is called "Heaven’s disease."
I often ponder how to preserve firmness and unyieldingness in the body, thereby escaping disease.
The method to escape disease is rooted in the Five Phases.
**Note:** The Five Phases: Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, and Earth.

The divine method of longevity was passed down by the ancient Sages and practiced by the Yellow Emperor.

For **Wood-born** individuals, select **Dinghai** (丁亥, Fire Day) or **Guihai** (癸亥, Water Day), recite the **Water Star** incantation, and walk the Five Stars five times to receive the longevity incantation.
Often on **Yimao** (乙卯, Wood Day) or **Dingmao** (丁卯, Fire Day), establish **Mao** and walk the Five Stars to dispel calamities and diseases, ascending to the Palace of Life, Honor, and Sovereignty.
Recite the incantation to dispel calamities, walk the Five Stars nine times, and chant the Five Phase spells, eighteen verses each.
**Note:** The eighteen spells are found in *Liuzhu* (流珠), the second step of the fast section.
Recite the **Water-Earth** incantation, and **virtue/power** and blessings will assist—thus, the **Wood-born** body attains longevity.
If practiced often, within three years, one attains the **Way of Immortality**, a body of eternal life and enduring vision.

For **Fire-born** individuals, select **Gengyin** (庚寅, Metal Day) or **Wuyin** (戊寅, Earth Day), recite the **Wood-Earth** incantation, and walk the Five Stars five times to receive the longevity incantation.
Often on **Jiawu** (甲午, Metal Day) or **Renwu** (壬午, Wood Day), establish **Wu** and walk the Five Stars to dispel calamities and diseases, ascending to the Palace of Life, Honor, and Sovereignty.
Recite the incantation to dispel calamities, walk the Five Stars nine times, and chant the Five Phase blessings, eighteen verses each.
**Note:** As before.
Recite the **Metal-Wood** incantation, and **virtue/power** and blessings will assist—thus, the **Fire-born** body attains longevity.
If practiced often, within three years, one attains the **Way of Immortality**, a body of eternal life and enduring vision.

For **Metal-born** individuals, select **Guiwei** (癸巳, Water Day) or **Dingwei** (丁巳, Fire Day), recite the **Water-Earth** incantation, and walk the Five Stars five times to receive the longevity incantation.
Often on **Yiyou** (乙酉, Wood Day) or **Jiyou** (己酉, Earth Day), establish **You** and walk the Five Stars to dispel calamities, overcome hardships, and eliminate diseases, ascending to the Palace of Life, Honor, and Sovereignty.
Recite the incantation to dispel calamities, walk the Five Stars nine times, and chant the Five Phase blessings, eighteen verses each.
Recite the **Water-Earth** incantation, and **virtue/power** and blessings will assist—thus, the **Metal-born** body attains longevity.
If practiced often, within three years, one attains the **Way of Immortality**, a body of eternal life and enduring vision.

For **Earth-born** individuals, select **Bingshen** (丙申, Fire Day) or **Renshen** (壬申, Metal Day), recite the **Fire-Metal** incantation, and walk the Five Stars five times to receive the longevity incantation.
Often on **Jiazzi** (甲子, Metal Day) or **Bingzi** (丙子, Water Day), establish **Zi** and walk the Five Stars to dispel calamities, overcome hardships, and eliminate diseases, ascending to the Palace of Life, Honor, and Sovereignty.
Recite the incantation to dispel calamities, walk the Five Stars nine times, and chant the Five Phase blessings, eighteen verses each.
Recite the **Fire-Metal** incantation, and **virtue/power** and blessings will assist—thus, the **Earth-born** body attains longevity.
If practiced often, within three years, one attains the **Way of Immortality**, a body of eternal life and enduring vision.

For **Water-born** individuals, select **Gengshen** (庚申, Metal Day) or **Jashen** (甲申, Water Day), recite the **Wood-Water** incantation, and walk the Five Stars five times to receive the longevity incantation.
Often on **Renzi** (壬子, Wood Day) or **Jiazzi** (甲子, Metal Day), establish **Wu** and walk the Five Stars to dispel calamities, overcome hardships, and eliminate diseases, ascending to the Palace of Life, Honor, and Sovereignty.
Recite the incantation to dispel calamities, walk the Five Stars nine times, and chant the Five Phase blessings, eighteen verses each.
Recite the **Wood-Metal** incantation, and **virtue/power** and blessings will assist—thus, the **Water-born** body attains longevity.
If practiced often, within three years, one attains the **Way of Immortality**, a body of eternal life and enduring vision.

For those born under the Five Phases, each should follow their native Phase, calculating and selecting what harmonizes with their generation.
Practice for one year, and the body will be free of a hundred ailments.
**Note:** Also, one year repels misfortune, two years repels war, three years removes the register of death, and four years refines the essence of the **Way**, all aiding the body. The Five Stars of Heaven each transform into human form, descending to teach the true **Way** to mortals. When one attains the true essence of Earth and completes their cultivation, the Five Elders descend to welcome them, ascending to the Golden Gate, assisting the later Sage Sovereign as ministers of the Celestial Ruler.

Until the completion of forty-nine years, one may ascend if they wish.
**Note:** If one does not wish to ascend at forty-nine, they may instead remain in the mortal realm for leisure, requesting their original teacher to bestow an official title among the immortals. Thus, they may enjoy themselves without concern for marital or familial affairs, so long as their heart never strays from the **Way**, and the **Way** never strays from their heart.
They may also serve as officials in the world, with promotions unhindered.

In antiquity, the Immortal Ancestor Laozi served as a teacher to emperors across generations, also holding the positions of Prime Minister and Chancellor. He served sixty-four sovereigns during the Yin and Zhou dynasties, thrice as the **Zhushi** (柱史, a high official), and four times as Prime Minister. He nurtured eighty-two consorts and had three hundred sixty descendants. Seven hundred fifty-nine years later, he ascended to become the **True Person of Supreme Peace**, titled **Later Sovereign of the Golden Gate, the Celestial Jade Emperor of the Dao**.

The **Celestial Jade Emperor of the Dao**, the **Later Sovereign of the Golden Gate, the True Person of Supreme Peace**, addressed the **Supreme Master of the Way** Wang Zongzhen, **Celestial Master Zhang**, and **Master Shansheng**, saying:

*"You wish to become the **Way’s Teacher for All Beings**—a wondrous method to guide mortals. The **Supreme Master of the Way** can indeed teach humanity.*

*According to the **Record of the Later Sovereign of the Golden Gate’s Supreme Peace**, it was on the seventh day of the third month of the second year of Han An that the **Later Sovereign of the Golden Gate** instructed twenty-five **Supreme Masters of the Way**, bestowing upon them the **Divine Spirit of the Attendant Immortal**, with countless chariots and cavalry of **qi** and **Way**—their number unknown. They ascended in clouds of purple **qi**, adorned with five-hued floating silks, until the instruction concluded, and suddenly vanished from sight.*

*Thus, the **Supreme Masters of the Way** knelt and rose to speak: "Our humble minds are dim and unenlightened. We do not understand the **Dao’s** methods and laws, having often transgressed and erred. We fear incurring blame, so we dare not become teachers and transmit the **Great Dao’s True Law**.*

*Today, by Your grace, we receive blessings spanning a thousand ages. Fortunate indeed are we to encounter the **Dao’s** benevolence, to be mercifully granted the opening of instruction, and to awaken from our deafness to hear. After hearing, we will dare to follow the Law and transmit the **True Dao of the Immortals**."*

*The **Dao Emperor** replied: "Those who aspire to the **Way** with devoted hearts dwell in mountain forests or quiet chambers, burning incense and reading scriptures*—*the **Dao Books**, which the world calls **Jing**—*and observing pure abstinence with vegetarian meals. Some may even fast entirely, abstaining from grains for thirty, forty, fifty, or sixty years, until they perish from old age or illness. Others may dwell in the world, gathering many people, building grand towers and pavilions, expending their **virtue** in earthly labor—thousands or tens of thousands of rooms, towers a hundred feet high—yet they too will decline and die.*

*How many more such as these! Do they not wish to attain the **Way**? Yet their aspirations and efforts only further alienate them from the **Way**, drawing them farther away.*

*All beings rely on the false **qi** of **Yin** and **Yang**, forming their bodies and receiving life. When the gestation is complete, they are born, and their birth is calculated by the **Five Phases** of their destiny.*—*Why so? The year is one, the month is two, the day is three, the hour is four, and counting the month of conception as the mother’s **Phase**, this makes five.*

*After birth, as they grow, it is the **Five Phases** that rule their flourishing.*—*When a person reaches their prime, the **Five Phases** mutually support each other without opposition. But when decline and misfortune come, the calculated **Five Phases** indeed clash, as the **Later Sovereign of the Golden Gate** has spoken.*

*Some may even face the **Five Phases’** utter destruction*—***rest** meaning extreme decline and hardship, **extinction** meaning calamity striking to annihilate them in the pool of life. You must know this early if you seek the **True Dao**.*

*Even if you have a lifespan of three, five, or six hundred years, you are not yet the **True Person**. You must draw near to the **Three Celestial Platforms** and distance yourself from the **Five Phases**.*—*The **Five Phases** of the **Zhou** are the enemies that harm the body, while the **Three Celestial Platforms** are the divine protectors of the soul and spirit. To distance oneself from the **Five Phases** is to practice the **Dao’s** methods of isolation, while to draw near is to preserve the **Three Combinations** of life.*

*By storing the spirit to guard the body and severing the **Five Phases’** harm, you will avoid the peril of death. Even if you slightly align with the **True Person’s Dao**, you may transmit this method, instructing disciples to become **True Persons** of the future.*

*You must tread the **Seven Stars of the Earth’s Measure**—*the **Great Dipper** born from **Yu’s Step**—*and regulate the **Five Phases**.*—*The **Seven Stars of the Earth’s Measure** are the **Great Dipper**, and the **Five Phases** are the **Great Golden Talisman’s** robes, found in the **Upper Scroll of the Flowing Pearl’s** Step Halter.*

*You must ascend the **Three Celestial Platforms**.*—*Though treading the **Seven Stars of the Earth’s Measure** does not require the **Three Celestial Platforms’ Step**, you must perform the **Three Steps of the Three Celestial Platforms**—each step containing three traces, nine traces in total, known as **Yu’s Step**.*—*This is the **Way’s** teaching to **Xuanyu**, hence its name. It is the essence of **Yu’s Step**, with three steps and nine traces.*

*You must enter the **Heavenly Gate**.*—*For those who aspire to the **Way**, first they must align their hearts, sit in stillness within an empty chamber, and tread the **Seven Stars of the Earth’s Measure** seven times. Then, they step down to the **Three Celestial Platforms**, performing **Yu’s Step** nine times—three steps and nine traces—before storing themselves within the **Heavenly Gate**, thus ascending to the **Flying Step of the Heavenly Pass**.*

*Each has their own oil, and each day’s practice is detailed in their respective scriptures. When flying, they must do so three or five times.*—*Three refers to the **Three Primordial Generals**, and five refers to the **Five Phases**. The three must store the **Three Primordial Generals** to emerge, treading the **Seven Stars of the Earth’s Measure** together and capturing the malevolent and destructive forces among the **Three Phases** of heaven, earth, and humanity that seek to harm me.*

*Store them as in the **Flowing Pearl’s Diagram**. Again, as with the **Three Combinations** of **Containment, Expansion, and Unity**, use them to defend and protect the body. Among the five stars, there is the **Star of Calamity**, which constantly plots to harm my life and body. Whenever you tread the **Flying Step** or before sleeping each night, lie on your back and think of the **Five Virtue Generals** in their chariots.*

*The **Eastern Azure Dragon General**, eighty-one zhang in height, commanding eighty-one million soldiers, stands at my left to guard and ward off, bow drawn and arrows ready. The **Western White Tiger General**, thirty-six zhang in height, commanding thirty-six million soldiers, stands at my right, holding a bow and crossbow. The **Southern Vermilion Bird General**, sixty-four zhang in height, commanding sixty-four million soldiers, stands before me, horn blaring in advance, soldiers wielding blades. The **Northern Dark Tortoise General**, twenty-five zhang in height, commanding twenty-five million soldiers, stands behind me, striking drums and bearing gongs, soldiers holding staves to guard my rear. The **Central Yellow Court General**, twelve zhang or seventy-two zhang in height, commanding twelve million or seventy-two million soldiers, stands before or behind me, defending my body.*

*If malevolent stars, evil constellations, or the evil spirits and demons of heaven, earth, and water—along with wicked humans—plot in darkness or strike in light to harm me, the **Five Virtue Generals** and their soldiers, with the **Three Primordial Generals**, will unite in heart and strength, capturing and exterminating them utterly, so that they vanish as if by decree. Their destruction will be swift, like frost meeting the sun—exhausted and dissolved entirely."*

In the left hand’s first finger, at the middle joint, lies the **Upper Celestial Gate**[*].
*Note: The Celestial Gate’s Nine Stars of the Dipper (九星斗), known as the "Flying Step Heavenly Restraint" (飞步天纲) meridian.*

It governs **punishments and calamities**.
*Note: Employ the Three-Five Method—expel the malevolent stars and qi of punishments afflicting my own body, as well as the disasters of the Five Phases’ mutual assaults, and all celestial stars that oppress me. All must be countered by pacing the Nine Steps (禹步) nine times, invoking the talisman of a particular star, and summoning that star from Heaven to rescue my own fate (宿). Prevent it from violating my fate. For instance, if a certain star (e.g., 金) invades like a thief, fear the Fire Star (火星). When the Fire Star assaults the fate where I was born, I implore the Water Star (水星) to save my natal fate.*

The method for summoning the Water Star is as follows: On a **Child Day** at **midnight**, when the star and moon are visible, exit through the northern door of your dwelling, grasp tightly, hold your breath, and gaze upward at the **Vermilion Star** (辰星), bowing three times.

Then recite:
*"I, [Name], aged [X] years, born in the [Month] of [Year], my natal fate [Star] is now tormented and harmed by the Wandering Fire Star (荧惑火星). I now beseech the **Purple Enclosure Celestial Sovereign** (紫微天皇君) and the **Divine of the Northern Pole’s Vermilion Star** (北极辰星之神) to subdue and extinguish it, lest it violate or touch my natal fate (本命之星) or the fate governed by my birth hour (生日所管之宿). May they swiftly rescue and deliver me, driving the Fire Star’s essence to retreat in haste, scattering its malevolent qi, which shall then dissipate. I dare not betray the **Supreme Sage’s** favor.*

*I pray for Your grace to grant me longevity and enduring vision, a secure household, and I dare not betray the **Supreme Sage’s** favor, the **Purple Enclosure Celestial Sovereign’s** grace.*

Then perform the Nine Steps (禹步) once, and three times the **Earthly Restraint** (摄地纪). Adjust the clothing, rotate the **Celestial Gate** (天关), and point to the Wandering Fire Star (荧惑) nine times, invoking the Water Star’s talisman, while preserving the **Nine Abysses Great Sea** (存九泉大海) to sever and extinguish it.

Then pray:
*"The Five Phases push one another; Metal and Wood strike in opposition.
Water and Fire extinguish mutually—copper lips, iron tongues.
Those who resist me shall perish. So it is decreed."*

In the *Liu Zhu* (Flowing Pearl) Upper Scroll, it is recorded:

*"The **Supreme Sage** first instructed the **Purple Enclosure Celestial Sovereign** (紫微天帝), who then inscribed the **Supreme Sage’s** (後聖君) talismans in red—these are the prayers for blessings. The remaining four stars (余四星) mutually restrain one another; their explanations are detailed later.

**Prayers for Blessing and Auspiciousness** (修求福):
*The **Supreme Sage** (後聖君) taught the **Purple Enclosure Celestial Sovereign** (紫微天皇君), saying: "To cultivate the mind (修志心), always maintain thoughts of stillness and reflection (常思静念). Imagine your own divine light (自身神光) transforming into the **Northern Dipper** (北斗) Star, perpetually hovering above your forehead (常悬额上). When retiring at night, reflect on it once before sleeping (夜一度思便卧), and during the day, also preserve the **Northern Dipper** in mind (白日亦存北斗), applying its talismans to your body (為配衣於身上).*

*After three years of such practice, you shall attain communion with the **Divine** (通神), and the heavens and earth will bestow blessings (天地降福). The sun and moon will shine brightly in your honor (日月为之照明), the Five Stars will align to bring you fortune (五星为之修福), and the Six Jia (六甲) will guard you. Some say: Swallow the talisman of the Six Jia (吞六甲符), and the Seven Auspicious Stars (佳七星) will turn the **Celestial Gate** (转关) for you. Whatever you point at (随手所指), it shall grant life to those in childbirth (救人生产立生), and life to those poisoned or dying from evil (救毒恶死立生). All matters shall follow your will (万事随手所指).*

*Do not recklessly transmit these talismans to those unworthy of the **Dao** (非道之子), or you shall surely harm yourself (必反损身也).*

*May your body escape the Three Calamities (令身出三灾).*

The **Three Calamities** are thus defined:

**Celestial Calamities** (天灾) include sudden disasters, decline, misfortune, slanderous diseases, and afflictions from war and thunder.

**Earthly Calamities** (地灾) arise from the *qi* of construction in one’s dwelling—whether from the clash of the Five Phases, structural flaws (such as uneven terrain, improper dimensions, or ill-placed doors), or external influences like neighbors’ constructions disrupting the *qi*. They also stem from marital incompatibility, betrayal by friends, feuds, contagious illnesses, or malevolent *qi* from ghosts and humans clashing in lawsuits or violence.

Such calamities, when trodden upon in the **Astronomic Steps** (蹑纪) and **Celestial Gate** (天门), or when the **Earthly Portal** (地户) is stepped upon, shall all be self-destroyed. If fear remains, perform the **Agricultural Steps** (禹步) and align with the **Polar Axis** (配斗), turning the **Celestial Gate** (转天关) and pointing—each shall be self-annihilated.

The **Five Torments** (五苦) or **Five Evils** (五恶) are thus addressed. If one’s body follows the sequence of **Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, and Earth** to dispel them, stepping in the **Cosmic Ropes** (步纲), trodding the **Astronomic Steps** (蹑纪), turning the **Celestial Gate** (转天关), and pointing to the **Five Stars**—beginning with **Metal**—first encircle the **Agricultural Steps Diagram** (禹步图) thrice, then point to the **Metal Star** five times, reciting the **Metal Star Incantation** (捻金星诀). Next, step upon the **Metal Star**, point to the **Wood Star**, step upon it, point to the **Earth Star**, step upon it, point to the **Water Star**, step upon it, and point to the **Fire Star**, reciting the incantation for each.

Then recite the **Disaster-Dispelling Prayer**:
*"The Five Phases push one another—Metal subdues Wood,
Water extinguishes Fire—thus it is."*

—Excerpted from *The Flowing Pearl* (《流珠》).

Thus, day and night, one becomes a **Celestial Ancestor** (仙祖).
*Note: Ancient scholars of the Dao, like those who study diligently to forget labor and fulfill their ambitions, attain office and wealth. The Daoist path likewise demands such assiduous effort and perseverance to achieve transcendence. These are the words of the Later Sage-King instructing his disciples.*

**Laozi** says:
*"The methods for dispelling calamities through the Five Phases are numerous, but their subtleties follow an order. When the **Wood Star** is harmed by the **Metal Star** in one’s natal constellation and birth position—*
*Note: For those born under the Wood Star (East, *Jia-Yi*, *Yin-Mao* positions—*Jiao, Heng, Shi, Fang, Xin, Wei*), on a *Wu-Wu* Fire Day at nightfall, when the star is visible, stand in the courtyard or outside the door. Grip firmly, still the *qi*, gaze upward at the **Mars Star** (荧惑), and bow thrice. Speak thus:*
*'Subject [Name], aged [X], born on the [Month-Day], with natal star [X] and birth constellation [X], now suffers affliction from the **White Tiger Star** (太白金星), whose malevolent influence harms my natal star and birth constellation. I now petition the **Southern Pole’s DanTai Supreme Sovereign** (南极丹台太初君) and the **Southern Mars Star Deity** (南上荧惑星神) to subdue and annihilate this calamity, lest it assail my natal star or birth constellation. Swiftly rescue me, causing the **Metal Star’s essence** to retreat in haste and its malevolent *qi* to dissipate. I dare not betray the blessings of the Most Holy. May I be granted longevity, prosperity, and household peace, lest I betray the grace of the Supreme Sovereign DanTai.’*
*Then perform the **Agricultural Steps** once, tread the **Earthly Measures** thrice, align the **Celestial Garment** (配衣), turn the **Celestial Gate**, and point to the **White Tiger Star** nine times, reciting the **Metal Star Incantation** nine times while visualizing the **Nine Furnaces of Fierce Fire** (九炉猛火) to subdue it. Then recite:*
*'The Five Phases push one another—Metal subdues Wood,
Water extinguishes Fire—thus it is.'*

*When the **Water Star** is harmed by the **Earth Star** in one’s natal constellation and birth position—*
*Note: The Water Star (North, *Hai-Zi-Chou*, *Dou-Niu-Nu-Wei*), the two *Seasonal Stars* (季星), appears on a *Xin-Mao* Wood Day at nightfall. Stand on the eastern perimeter of the house, grip firmly, close the *qi*, gaze upward at the **Jupiter Star** (岁星), and bow thrice. Speak thus:*
*'Subject [Name], aged [X], born on the [Month-Day], with natal star [X] and birth constellation [X], now suffers affliction from the **Earth Star’s Suppression** (镇星土灾), whose malevolent influence harms me. I now petition the **Eastern Pole’s QingTai Primeval Sovereign** (东极青台太元君) and the **Eastern Jupiter Star Deity** (东上岁星之神) to subdue and annihilate this calamity, lest it assail my natal star or birth constellation. Swiftly rescue me, causing the **Earth’s essence** to retreat in haste and its malevolent *qi* to dissipate. I dare not betray the Most Holy’s blessings. May I be granted longevity, prosperity, and household peace, lest I betray the grace of the Supreme Sovereign QingTai.’*
*—Note: The original omits ‘Sovereign’ (君).*

Take one step in the **Yú-bù** stance, then stamp the **Dì-jì** three times. Adjust your clothing, then with the **Tiānguān finger**, press the **Earth Star** nine times. Nine times recite the **Earth talisman** while gathering soil from the Nine Ridges, breaking branches from the Nine Forests, and piercing them to block and suppress.

Then pray thus:
*"The Five Phases interact in their cycles—so it is.
The **Fire Star** is harmed by the **Water Star**, assailing my natal constellation and birth host.
*Note: Fire belongs to the South—**Sì, Wǔ, Wèi**—and the stars **Jǐng, Guǐ, Liǔ, Xīng, Zhāng, Yì, Zhěn** are its hosts.
Fire is the host of the Southern mansion.
At the beginning of a **Xīn-chǒu** Earth day, when the star host appears, face the **eastern-northern quadrant** of an empty, quiet space. Grip firmly, seal the *qi*, and gaze upward at the **Earth Star**, bowing three times.
*Note: The Earth Star has no fixed position—simply follow its location in the cardinal direction for the ritual; this is optimal.*

I, subject [Name], aged [X], born on the [Month-Day], with natal star [X] and birth constellation [X], now suffer affliction from the **Chen Star’s Water Calamity** (辰星水灾) assailing me. I now petition the **Central Pole’s Yellow Palace’s Upper Platform’s Supreme True Lord** (中极黄宫上台太真君) and the **Central Earth Star Deity** (中上镇星之神) to subdue and annihilate this obstruction, lest it overflow and assail my natal star or birth constellation. Swiftly rescue me, causing the **Water’s essence** to be sealed, severed, and retreat in haste, its malevolent *qi* to dissipate. I dare not betray the Most Holy’s blessings. May I be granted longevity, prosperity, and household peace, lest I betray the grace of the Supreme Sovereign Upper Platform’s Supreme True Lord."

Take one step in the **Yú-bù** stance, then stamp the **Dì-jì** three times. Adjust your clothing, then with the **Tiānguān finger**, press the **Chen Star** nine times. Nine times recite the **Water talisman**. Gather soil from the **Three Mountains and Nine Ridges** to press and seal it, and sever the **Nine Abysses’ waters**, lest they flow. Then pray thus:
*"The Five Phases interact in their cycles—metal conquers wood, water extinguishes fire.
*Note: An ancient Five Phases incantation.
Water flows, earth is severed.
*Note: From *Taiping Jinque Housheng Xuan Yuan Yuhuang Shangdao Jun*, reissued by Yín-jūn.
For those born under the Fire command, often harmed by the Water Star’s *qi* assaulting the body, within ten or five years, suddenly declining in a month or ten days, occasionally falling ill. Yín-jūn reported to the Jade Emperor, who transmitted this incantation, altering it from the previous version—now it is flawless.
Fire generates earth above, water dies from its own heat.
With a **copper mouth and iron tongue**, those who oppose me shall be slain, those who oppose Heaven shall perish.
Earth and water contend, yet self-destruct in return.
So it is."*

Complete the ritual as before.

「金锁流珠引卷之十二竟 金锁流珠弘卷之十三 中华总真大仙宰王方平张道陵赵升王长司命李仲甫茅盈许玉斧等系代撰述 中华仙人李淳风注 五行六纪所生引中
*Completion of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl [incantation] for the Twelve Volumes, expansion of the Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl [incantation] for the Thirteen Volumes. The Grand Sovereign of All-Perfect Daoist Masters of the Chinese Realm—including Fāng-píng, Zhāng Dàolíng, Zhào Shēng, Wáng Cháng, Sī-mìng, Lǐ Zhòngfǔ, Máoyíng, Xǔ Yùfǔ, and others—were commissioned to author this. The Daoist Master Lǐ Chúnfēng of the Chinese Realm annotated it. The Five Phases and Six Periods [of time] that generate [these stars] are detailed within.*

太上老君告太极真人 徐来勒是也。
*The Most High Lǎojūn instructs the Primordial Daoist Master [Tàijí Zhēnrén], and this is the method of Xú Lǎilè.*

曰：五命之中，唯火命帝王则吉，似衰则病。
*He says: Among the Five Celestial Mandates, only those born under the Fire Mandate as sovereigns are auspicious; if they appear to decline, then illness comes.*

注：按《五星论》云：火命入小年多忧病，及长大时，忽不称意亦病，长助王时即吉。
*Note: According to the Treatise on the Five Stars, those born under the Fire Mandate suffer anxiety and illness during their early years, and when they grow older, sudden discontent also brings illness. Only when they assist the sovereign in their prime do they flourish.*

上仙皆用此法，转令常王盛。
*The Celestial Masters all employ this method to transform their fate, ensuring the sovereign remains ever prosperous.*

吾今说此妙法授卿，令卿常王，不衰不病也。
*I now impart this wondrous method to you, so that you may always reign as sovereign, without decline or illness.*

卿可常用庚寅、辛卯木日，可作小坛子，
*You may frequently utilize days of the Gēngyín (Jupiter-Wood) and Xīnmào (Wood) commands, and construct a small altar,*

注：按《五行相成记》云：夫醮祭作坛，须向用日前，先结土为坛，三级，高一尺五寸，古仙为之也。
*Note: According to the Records of the Five Phases’ Mutual Generation, when conducting a ritual (jiào) to establish an altar, it must face the day’s cardinal direction. First, form the altar with earth in three tiers, standing one foot and five inches tall—this is how ancient Daoist Masters did it.*

今志人修求，以黄土布地为坛，佳也。
*Now, those who seek spiritual cultivation may spread yellow earth upon the ground as an altar, which is excellent.*

此是作一时之用。
*This is for temporary use.*

但於净室空院之中，用黄色土乾筛，过布地为坛，祭醮为上。
*However, within a pure chamber or empty courtyard, use yellow earth that has been sifted and dried, spread evenly upon the ground to form the altar. Rituals (jiào) conducted here are superior.*

如不要，却扫除之，不妨。
*If you do not wish to use it, simply sweep it away—it causes no hindrance.*

高一尺五寸。
*Note: The altar’s height should be visualized as one foot and five inches.*

注：令人心存坛高一尺五寸，用得。
*Note: Visualizing the altar’s height as one foot and five inches is effective.*

用酒五升，或五斗。
*Note: Use five sheng of wine for small rituals (jiào), or five dou for grand ones.*

注：夫大醮五斗，小醮只五升，或三斗。
*Note: For grand rituals (jiào), five dou of wine are used; for small ones, five sheng—or even three dou.*

醮脯 脯用鹿脯，鸿鹭脯也。
*Offerings of dried meat (fǔ) for the ritual (jiào): use dried venison or dried meat of the wild goose or egret.*

一斤，五盘饼果，
*One jin [of dried meat], five round cakes of grains or fruits,*

三果及时新物等。
*three fresh seasonal fruits, and other timely offerings.*

酒杯一十五，
*Fifteen wine cups,*

席六领。
*and six ritual mats (xí).*

五方五领一领按前。
*For the five directions, use one mat each, as previously described.*

菜二十五楪，
*Twenty-five dishes of vegetables (cài),*

酒蹲一坐，
*a single wine stand (jiǔdūn),*

褥铺设如法。
*and bedding arranged according to the ritual method.*

画岁星君，带之左肘后。
*Draw the image of the Star of the Year (Suìxīng), and wear it on your left elbow.*

祭醮岁星君，以王火之意也。
*The ritual (jiào) for the Star of the Year aims to reignite the Fire Mandate’s power.*

然五君总请，俱会於坛，
*Now, summon all five celestial lords—they will gather at the altar,*

此即请客迎宾，共作福力之意是也。
*which signifies inviting guests and benefactors to collaborate in generating auspicious power (fúlì).*

须作启请王相辞文，读所请五星。
*You must compose an invocation (qǐqǐng) and ritual address (xiàngcí) to the Five Stars, then recite them.*

从岁星起。
*Note: Begin with the Star of the Year.*

注：文在下醮祭引中具说讫。
*Note: The text is fully explained in the subsequent ritual (jiào) invocation.*

一画岁星君一人，与青童一人，及木符三道，同袋系之於肘后。
*Draw one image of the Star of the Year and one of the Green Boy (Qīngtóng), along with three Wood talismans (fú), and bind them together in a pouch on your elbow.*

一云：香木为之，长一二寸，戴安头，
*Some say: fashion these from fragrant wood, one to two inches long, and wear them on your head—*

此谓之戴王入相，盛之无穷。
*this is called "wearing the Sovereign’s talisman to enter the celestial phase," bringing boundless prosperity.*

注：香笺沈木堪，余木不可也。
*Note: Only fragrant wood like sandalwood (shēnmù) or aromatic paper (xiāngjiàn) is suitable; other woods are not.*

有人用金银为之戴头，且此即不入，
*Some use gold or silver to craft these talismans and wear them on their heads, but this method does not work—*

相成王盛，为火克金，
*for when the talismans align with the sovereign’s power, it is because Fire overcomes Metal (Jin),*

此入相克也。
*but this is the opposite of what we seek: the talisman’s power being overcome.*

异域香木及香不入中华，用者不堪，
*Fragrant woods and incense from foreign lands do not belong in the Chinese realm; those who use them are unworthy—*

犯道禁。
*for they violate Daoist prohibitions.*

注：夫大道中华正教，天地神仙之言，我中国神仙之乡人，
*Note: The Great Dao of the orthodox Chinese teaching is the discourse of Heaven and Earth, gods and immortals. We, the people of the Chinese realm, are the native land of divine immortals—*

不合夷戎蛮狄之宝，为神仙之器。
*we should not use treasures from barbarians, as they are not suitable for the tools of gods and immortals.*

不合烧异域熏臭秽毒烈辛之香。
*Nor should we burn incense from foreign lands that is pungent, foul, or poisonous.*

此香犯道禁，又非真人常修行之香也。
*Such incense violates Daoist prohibitions and is not the kind that true immortals (Zhēnrén) habitually use.*

真人爱紫微幽木之炁，笺沈之木，
*True immortals cherish the subtle *qi* of the Purple Enclosure (Zǐwēi) and fragrant woods like sandalwood (shēnmù) and aromatic paper (xiāngjiàn)—*

闻之皆喜。
*they take joy in their scent.*

胡狄之香，故皆恶。
*Incense from barbarian lands is therefore all evil.*

闻其炁，上真为之辛烈毒恶之炁也。
*When one inhales its *qi*, even the highest immortals find it harsh, poisonous, and malevolent.*

王桐栢谓王子登曰：苏上卿爱烧辛烈之炁，冲於中华天尊形象之前。
*Wáng Tóngbì said to Wáng Zǐdēng: "Sū Shàngqīng loves to burn pungent, harsh *qi*, which clashes with the divine image of the Chinese Celestial Sovereign (Tiānzūn) before him.*

地府奏上，太上大恶之，
*The Underworld reported this to the Most High, who greatly abhorred it,*

退仙一等，
*demoting the immortals one rank,*

减位阶。
*and reducing their celestial stations.*

又长令掌西国陀佛台，永不离胡身，
*Furthermore, he eternally commanded them to oversee the Ertao Platform (Tó Fó Tái) in the Western Realm, never to leave their barbarian forms,*

胡地仙人也。
*making them immortals of barbarian lands.*

卿可能依此之法，
*You can follow this very method,*

十年位为真人，
*and within ten years, attain the rank of true immortal (Zhēnrén),*

一生无衰病之时也。
*never to experience decline or illness in your lifetime.*

徐君依行。
*Xú Jūn followed this practice.*

以笺香沈香为岁星，
*Using aromatic paper (xiāngjiàn) and sandalwood (shēnmù) to fashion the Star of the Year, one inch long,*

及镇星君、青童君三身，
*along with the images of the Lord of the Constellation (Zhènxīng) and the Green Boy (Qīngtóng), three figures in total, each one inch long,*

各长一寸，
*each one inch long,*

以锦袋盛之，
*and stored in a brocade pouch,*

戴头上，
*to be worn upon the head,*

五年并思存如见。
*for five years, while also meditating upon them as if they were present.*

三君为之，
*The three lords (Zhènxīng, Suìxīng, and Qīngtóng) accomplished this,*

下化为老人，
*and transformed into an elderly man,*

告徐君曰：公以身坚体王，
*who told Xú Jūn: "Your body is now firm and your sovereign’s power is fortified,*

万邪不敢干也。
*so that no ten thousand malevolent forces dare to approach you."*

卿可能转乾坤於指足，
*You can thus manipulate the Heavenly Circulation (Qiánkūn) through your fingers and toes,*

转乾坤，是飞天纲，
*for manipulating the Heavenly Circulation is the celestial law of flying through the skies,*

蹑地纪是也。
*and the earthly law of walking upon the ground.*

指是掌诀，
*The fingers are the key to the palm techniques,*

皆在指节足，
*all of which reside in the joints of the fingers and toes,*

自身左右脚，
*and the natural alignment of your left and right feet,*

足步钢蹑纪是也。
*for the steps of your feet are the iron-clad earthly laws.*

纳三六於心胸，
*Internalize the Three and Six within your chest—*

注：三是三元将军，皆能纳入人身。
*Note: The "Three" refers to the Three Primordial Generals (Sānyuán Jiāngjūn), who can all be internalized into the body.*

六是老君六甲符，
*The "Six" are the Six Talismans of the Celestial Mandates (Liújiǎ Fú) of Lǎojūn.*

修行吞符，一十四年真人也。
*Through cultivation and swallowing these talismans, one becomes a true immortal (Zhēnrén) in fourteen years.*

如此十年，
*Thus, within ten years,*

白日升举为大仙真人也。
*you will ascend in broad daylight to become a great Daoist immortal (Dàxiān Zhēnrén).*

君初闻不识，
*When you first hear this, you may not understand,*

及其日久，
*but as time passes,*

渐有悟知。
*you will gradually gain insight and comprehension.*

为之八年，
*After practicing for eight years,*

白日上登太极，
*you will ascend in broad daylight to the Primordial Dao (Tàijí),*

仍传数弟子，
*and also impart this knowledge to several disciples,*

不转乾坤也。
*though they will not manipulate the Heavenly Circulation.*

犹数百岁，
*Yet even they will live for hundreds of years,*

后隐於山，
*and afterward, retreat into the mountains,*

而绝世也。
*and vanish from the world.*

土星被木星来害我本命生位宿者。
*If the Earth Star is harmed by the Wood Star, or if the Wood Star attacks your native celestial mandate and birth position,*

注：土虽居中位。
*Note: Though the Earth Star occupies the central position,*

为戊己而无正位，
*it lacks a fixed position for the days of Wù and Jǐ (Earth days),*

寄王在四季，
*and instead, its sovereignty is entrusted to the four seasons,*

辰戌丑未之地是。
*specifically residing in the hours of Chén, Xū, Chǒu, and Wèi.*

常以甲午金日，壬午木日，
*Frequently, on days of Jiǎwǔ (Metal-Earth) or Rénwǔ (Wood-Earth) commands,*

夜初星宿见时，
*when the Star of the Year (Suìxīng) appears at the beginning of the night,*

於中庭净扫地，握固，
*within the central courtyard, sweep the ground clean, then firmly grasp it,*

闭炁，
*and close your *qi*,*

仰观太白金星，拜三拜。
*gazing upward at the Bright White Metal Star (Tàibái Jinxīng) and bowing three times.*

注：太白星有不见之时，
*Note: The Bright White Metal Star sometimes does not appear,*

若不见，即存其位，
*so if it is not visible, simply visualize its position,*

即得，
*and you will still attain the effect,*

不秘须见。
*Note: There is no need to conceal it—it must be seen.*

启曰：臣某乙行年若干岁，某月某日生本宿某星，
*The invocation begins: "Your humble servant, born in the year of [Celestial Stem]-[Earthly Branch], at the age of [X] years, on the [Y]th month, [Z]th day, under the native star of [W], now offers this prayer—*

今被岁星木灾作祟祸害。」
*today, the Star of the Year’s Wood calamity harms me with malevolent *qi* and misfortune."*

Your humble servant now petitions the **Supreme Sovereign Lord of the Western Extremity’s Upper Platform (Tàisù Jūn)**, the divine spirit of the **Bright White Metal Star (Tàibái)**, to **subdue and utterly extinguish** the calamity, preventing it from ever arising again. May it not assail the star governing my life nor the constellation overseeing my birth.

**Urgent salvation must be granted**, causing the **Wooden *qi*** to dissipate naturally, its disasters to vanish, and its malevolent *qi* to disperse immediately. Dare I betray the **Supreme Sage’s grace**?

I beseech that I may **endure long life and clear vision**, my family and self in perpetual peace. Dare I betray the **Supreme Sage’s grace**, the **Supreme Sovereign Lord of the Upper Platform (Tàisù Jūn)**?

Then, with **one circuit of the *Yǔbù* (Turtle Step)**, **three recitations of the *Dìjì* (Earth’s Measure)**, adjusting my robes, I **rotate the *Tiānguān* (Celestial Pass) finger past the Year Star nine times**, **twist the Wood-Countering *jué* (decision) nine times**, and **visualize the Nine Cauldrons’ golden barrier** to sever and isolate it, ensuring it remains inert and motionless.

**The invocation proclaims:**
*"The Five Phases counter one another—Metal subdues Wood;
Water extinguishes Fire—so it is."*

Moreover, among the **Five Celestial Stems**, only the **Earth Star** completes a full cycle in **thirty-plus years**, moving contrary to the Sun and Moon’s regular orbits. When it opposes a person’s **native star or birth constellation**, it brings **no auspicious outcome**, only **decline and calamity**. Whether one’s nature aligns with Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, or Earth, one must **constantly invoke the name of the Wood Star Sovereign**, wear an **image of the Wood Star’s form** on the **left elbow**, and **ingest a talisman of the Wood Star**. By doing so repeatedly, others sharing the same star or constellation will bear the harm, while you **escape unscathed**.

**The Most High Lord Laozi instructed those seeking True Transformation:**
*Note: Those seeking True Transformation—such as Xú Lèi, Guāng Miàoyīn, Cháng Guīyī Kǒushān, Lǐ Yuānbù, Zhēndìng Guāng, and Miào Hán Yuántōng—received this technique before attaining immortality, transmitted from the Western *Qiánzhú* (Kashmir) and other lands.*

**"You must now practice the Five Stars’ method. Whether or not they conflict with your destiny, practice it if they do; if not, do not. It is impermissible to neglect it.**

I impart this method to you—**regardless of decline or vigor**—you must **follow the monthly lunar phase and daily hour**, practicing the **Morning Five Stars** (Cháohuáng). The Five Stars are the **sovereigns of the Five Phases**, also called the **Five Celestial Sovereigns**—thus, it is called *Cháohuáng* (Morning Sovereigns).

**Practicing for one year ensures the Five Virtues/Powers (*wǔdé*) reside within you; by two years, results will manifest.**
*Note: The Five Stars manifest as the Five Virtue Generals—**Qīnglóng (Azure Dragon), Báihǔ (White Tiger), Zhūquè (Vermilion Bird), Xuánwǔ (Dark Turtle), and Huángtíng (Yellow Court)**.*

**The schedule for the Morning Five Stars (Cháohuáng) is as follows:**
- **January 6th, at *wǔ* hour (noon)**
- **February 1st, at *shēn* hour (5–7 PM)**
- **March 7th, at *zǐ* hour (11 PM–1 AM)**
- **April 9th, at *chén* hour (7–9 AM)**
- **May 15th, at *zǐ* hour (11 PM–1 AM)**
- **June 3rd, at *wǔ* hour (noon)**
- **July 7th, at *zǐ* hour (11 PM–1 AM)**
- **August 4th, at *wǔ* hour (noon)**
- **September 2nd, at *yín* hour (3–5 AM)**
- **October 1st, at *yín* hour (3–5 AM)**
- **November 6th, at *zǐ* hour (11 PM–1 AM)**
- **December 12th, at *zǐ* hour (11 PM–1 AM)**

On these days, enter a **quiet, secluded chamber**, burn incense, face north, and **kneel and bow five times**. With focused mind, **invoke the names of the Five Celestial Sovereign Lords and their Consorts three times each**.
*Note: For each set of five bows, mentally intone once: **"[Name] True Sovereign Lord, [Name] True Sovereign Lady"**—beginning with the **Mars (Ming) Star**—then bow again, proceeding in the order of the current constellation.*

**The True Name of the Wood Year Star Sovereign Lord is:**
**Dènglán**, with the courtesy name **Qīngníng**.
His Consort’s name is:
**Bǎoróng**, with the courtesy name **Fēiyún**.

**The True Name of the Fire Mars Star Sovereign Lord is:**
**Wéitíng**, with the courtesy name **Sànróng**.
His Consort’s name is:

**The True Name of the Metal (Jin) Tai Bai Star Sovereign Lord is:**
**Liáolíng**, with the courtesy name **Zhènxún**.
His Consort’s name is:
**Biāoyīng**, with the courtesy name **Xū’ēn**.

**The True Name of the Water Chen Star Sovereign Lord is:**
**Qǐxuān**, with the courtesy name **Jīngyuán**.
His Consort’s name is:
**Xuánhuá**, with the courtesy name **Lóngé**.

**The True Name of the Earth Zhen Star Sovereign Lord is:**
**Zàngmù**, with the courtesy name **Dānyán**.
His Consort’s name is:
**Kōngyáo**, with the courtesy name **Fēixián**.

**Afterward, strike the teeth five times**, then rise and strike the teeth again. Loosen the headband and kneel in long obeisance, saying:

*Note: Loosen the headband and place it on the ground, then kneel in long obeisance while holding a ritual ladle, focusing the mind on the Dipper (Big Dipper) constellation, eyes gazing at the furnace, softly speaking.*

**I, [Name], of [State] [County] [Town] [Village],**
*Note: Officials should state their rank; others should state their residence.*

**a disciple of the Three Scenes of the Great Cavern of the Upper Pure Daoist Metropolis, the [Name] Master of [Name] Dynasty, the Little Talisman True Person, respectfully submit that I am [Name], born on the [Year] [Month] [Day], aged [Age].**

**I humbly petition the Five Celestial Sovereign Lords and Ladies of the Sun and Moon, the High True Daoist Sovereign Emperor, and the Holy Sovereign Emperor of the Upper Pure, the Supreme Pure, and the Jade Pure—several generations hence.**

**On the day of my birth in this mortal life, my seven generations of ancestors, along with my living parents, committed countless transgressions. After their passing, they were subjected to the scrutiny of the officials of the underworld. I pray for mercy and pardon, so that their restless spirits may ascend to present their case.**

**Again, I, [Name], though longing for immortality while in the world, was ignorant of the scriptures and teachings, and thus committed countless offenses beyond recall.**

**Moreover, since I entered the Dao and received the scriptures, I have violated my oaths, broken the precepts and prohibitions, and, as a mere ant-like remnant of life, have striven to uphold the sacred studies, hoping for blessings and felicitations. I now seek Your grace to purify my sins.**

**I pray to be granted deliverance and to record twice my transgressions before the Celestial Sovereign, so that my crimes may be erased and my name removed from the black ledger.**

**I pray to be blessed with a talisman, so that I may, along with the Five Stars’ True Ones, hasten to the Hua Chen, ascend to the Upper Pure, traverse the Jade Gate, and complete the rites.**
*Note: Prostrate oneself in tears, beseeching for a long time, then adjust the headband, extinguish the incense, perform five sets of double bows, and depart without letting others know.*

**If one steadfastly practices the Hidden Method of the Eternal Highest, invoking the Five Celestial Sovereign Lords, within five years, their forms will appear as if in a dream. In seven years, they will manifest fully and accompany one in all travels. By the fourteenth year, the Five Sovereign Lords will gather and descend together, riding in the carriage of the Jade Pure (Xuánhuá), with three layers of purple clouds, leading the Five Emperors and following the myriad True Ones. The Five Stars will escort them, ascending the White Day to the Chen, entering the court of the Jade Pure, and receiving the scriptures to become an Upper Pure True Person.**

**The Five Phases (Wu Xing) generate and transform all things, each in its own way.**

*Note: All things are born from the Five Phases, and they also return to the Five Phases—this is the forward and backward cycle.*

**Those who enter the Communion of Spirits (Tong Ling) can also maintain their essence, govern and stabilize the human body, hence the transmission of their names.**

*Note: The later sages passed down to Master Yin, who composed the *Five Phases Talisman Record* and left it in writing. The following is the text of that work.*

**The *Five Phases Talisman Record* of Master Yin states:**
**The Metal (Jin) Phase begins first,**
*Note: The classics originally placed the Wood Phase first, but the later sages, following the Celestial Master’s *Flying Heaven Regulations*, established the order as Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, Earth—hence the order is not altered here.*

**though in reality, the Wood Phase precedes it. Metal is the Tai Bai Star, which disperses downward to form the Metal Phase. The Metal Phase, capable of transforming essence and spirit, condenses the Yang Qi of the Tai Bai to generate the human form.**

*Note: Yang Qi of the Tai Bai congeals to form humans.*

**The Yin Qi of the Metal Phase generates the human form. This is the meaning of "Shang" (商). Shang refers to humans. Once humans are born, they naturally take the surname Shang. Having this surname, they then marry with descendants of the Yu (羽) surname and produce six sons. The eldest son resumes the ancestral surname Jin. Jin’s descendants cross the Eastern Sea to become the ruling class of a nation. The second son takes the surname Yin, a branch of the Jin surname. The third son takes the surname Xia, not the ancestor of today’s Xia clan, but the original character for "upper and lower." The fourth son takes the surname Jiang, which is the Jiang of today. The fifth son takes the surname Zhang, the ancestor of today’s Zhang clan. The sixth son takes the surname Lang, the ancestor of today’s Hu and Kang clans. Over time, as the years pass, none have truly received this transmission.**

**Even in the Han Dynasty, when Jing Fang expounded the Five Phases’ laws, he redefined the Five Surnames, yet it is unclear whether his arrangement was accurate.**

**If one takes the original *Qi* (炁), the differences are certain. If one’s black *Qi* aligns with the surname, and they ingest Metal in accordance with its prescribed regimen, they will gain the benefits of prolonged youth and longevity.**

**The *Record of Master Ma* states:**
**Though the Metal Elixir Method involves refining Metal into liquid, it is not as effective as consuming its powder. The powder, when combined with water, is even more potent.**

**These three methods have distinct scriptures, which are found in the *Upper Pure Sacred Scriptures*.**

**Those who consume White Metal, Silver, or Lead will all align with their original surnames, and the methods will bring benefits. If they do not align, the methods will be ineffective.**

**The Silver Powder Method, which involves consuming silver as Silver Ointment, is all based on silver. The methods are detailed in the *Upper Pure Sacred Scriptures*.**

**Moreover, the method of subduing Lead as the *Purple River Cart* (紫河车法) is divine and mysterious, and is recorded in the *Inner Secrets of the Great Alchemy Talisman Scripture*—it is not further detailed here.**

**The method of subduing Copper as the *Purple Powder, Purple Flower, Light Snow Elixir* is found in the *Sacred Scriptures of the Great Dragon-Tiger Talisman*.**

**The method of subduing the Five Metals—Silver, Copper, Iron, Lead, etc.—as the *Return to Ancestry Method*, which returns to the original Metal (Jin), uses the method of refining Copper and Iron into gold, as recorded in the *Sacred Scriptures of the Great Dragon-Tiger Talisman*—this is not further detailed here.**

**The method of refining Iron into *Divine Treasure Instruments*—swords, mirrors, tripods, and cauldrons—is found in the *Sacred Scriptures of the Treasure Sword Record*.**

**Shang (商) refers to humans, as explained earlier. Humans are the Yang Qi of the Tai Bai dispersing and the Yin Qi congealing to form. This is analogous to the relationship between husband and wife.**

**Metals and stones are the Yin Qi congealing in the Earth, forming substances. Thus, teaching those of the Shang surname to align with beneficial metals and stones enhances the refining of elixirs and aids in cultivation, bringing great benefit.**

**Annotation:** *The following is a record from the Daoist Canon (正统道藏), detailing the teachings of Gongsun Huai-chang during the reign of the Yellow Emperor.*

---

**Record:**
In ancient times, during the reign of the Yellow Emperor, Gongsun Huai-chang refined gold into powder or elixir. Upon ingesting it, he attained an age of three hundred years without death, his appearance resembling that of a man in his forties. The Emperor then inquired why he had not yet ascended to become an immortal of the heavens.

Huai-chang replied: *"Though I was young and sought guidance, I had no master to follow. I searched all the famous mountains, even reaching the southern Flaming Continent, where the mountains of Bao-cang and Tian-tai—once called Bao-cang—lie. There, I encountered Hua-gai Zi, who taught me the arts of prolonging life. Yet, I have not yet attained the ultimate method of ascending to the heavens.*

*However, among the five metals, I can transform and refine them into various elixir and medicinal methods, all of which grant longevity—thousands or even tens of thousands of years. Yet, none allow one to ascend as a true celestial immortal."*

The Emperor pressed further on the reason.

Huai-chang answered: *"Gold, by its heavy nature, cannot ascend to the heavens."*

The Emperor then asked for the methods.

Huai-chang responded:
*"My methods include:
- Refining gold into powder,
- Refining gold into flower powder,
- Refining gold into liquid,
- Refining gold into *Su* [a refined elixir form],
- Refining the five metals into liquid,
- Transmuting the five metals into elixir,
- Transforming the five metals into elixir liquid,
- Refining the five metals’ elixir liquid into *Su*,
- Refining honeyed five metals,
- Refining the five metals into essence,
- Refining into *Jin Tong Shen* [Golden Elixir of Divine Penetration],
- Refining essence into *Yu Tong Shen* [Jade Elixir of Divine Penetration],
- Refining *Qian-shi* [precious stones] into divine methods.*

*All these methods grant only the arts of prolonging life, preserving youth, avoiding death, and wandering the Five Sacred Peaks. One’s descendants may live to eighty or seventy years, and their dwellings remain unharmed. Yet, if one exceeds these limits, they must relocate and change their name. Should they fail to do so, the Most High will not permit it."*

「The Emperor bowed twice and said, *"Please grant me this divine method."**
Huaixu received it.
The Emperor rejoiced greatly and appointed Huaixu as his left and right Master.

All these methods are contained within the *Shangqing Ling Shu* [Scriptures of High Clarity]. Therefore, they are not detailed here.

The Most High Laozi spoke:
*"I often pondered the lower-grade earthly immortals who refine the five metals in flight, seeking the auspices of water and fire.
**Note:** The five metals and water-fire are all refined through the method of *Taofei* [soaring in the Dao].

Yet, after years of effort, success or failure is decided.
**Note:** Of those who refine in flight, only one in ten may achieve success, while many more fail.

The labor is arduous.
**Note:** Those who refine gold, stones, and such under a master’s guidance, with proper technique, may attain the Great Elixir of the Upper Alchemy in nine years—this is called *Jiuxuan* [nine transformations].
But if they lack a master’s guidance, laboring blindly without regard to time, none shall succeed. Their toil reaches its utmost, their years and months wasted in vain. Thus, their suffering is extreme.

It is better to serve the *Five Star Ancestors* [of the five metals].
The Most High commands you to practice according to the sun, traverse the Five Stars, and ingest the *qi* of Taibai* [Great White Star] and the Five Stars. Then, advance further to ascend the Dipper, follow the *Tian Gang* [Heavenly Ropes] and *Di Ji* [Earthly Measures] methods, and you shall rise in broad daylight.
This surpasses those who merely burn and refine gold, stones, and mercury.

Now, regarding the methods of the Upper Immortals for refining elixirs:
They depend solely on numerical precision.
**Note:** The Five Stars (referring to the five celestial stars).

The *Dengzhen Yinjue* [Secrets of Ascending the True] fully explains the method of *Benxing Yixiang* [racing the stars and embracing the *qi*].

To *fei* [soar] through the Seven Dipper Stars, one must avoid calamity.
**Note:** The Seven Dipper Stars—this is the method of *Di Ji* [Earthly Measures].
With the furnace fully activated, the steps and incantations complete, and the ritual attire prepared, this is called the *Seven-Dipper Earthly Measures* method.

To traverse the Nine Stars, one must stabilize the soul and spirit.
**Note:** The Nine Stars—this refers to the Central Dipper’s nine stars, which are the *Yangming Yinjing* [Sunlight and Yin Essence] stars.
One must firmly grasp and guard the inner *qi*,
**Note:** *Woguo* [holding firm], *Bihu* [closing the *qi*], *Fu Xin* [massaging the heart], and *Die Li* [stepping measures] are the ways.
and ingest the vast and profound elixir.
**Note:** The great immortals possess their own *Jin Jing* [golden essence] and *Yu Ye* [jade fluid]; this refers only to their practice of swallowing.

Often, those who practice these methods—of the Five Stars, the Seven Dipper Stars, the Nine Stars, and the Three Primordials—
**Note:** Practicing the methods of the Five Stars, the Seven Dipper Stars, the Nine Stars, and the Three Primordials, in fourteen years, their merit is fulfilled and they ascend. Many have already departed in broad daylight, leaving their homes behind.
—find such joy.
**Note:** *Zhī lè* [this joy] refers to the delight of those who pursue these refined methods.»

The nature of Heaven is such that it does not demand harsh trials or exhaust the spirit and body through labor. **Note:** This is taken from the words of *Laozi’s Inner Transmission*, addressed to the True Person of the Primordial Command.

When the *Wood Star* [木行] first emerges, it scatters as *Sui Xing* [the Grand Cycle Star, 歲星], and this is the origin of *Wood* [木]. The *Wood Star*, once it can transform into *Jing* [essence], borrows the *Sui Xing*’s *Yang Qi* [yang qi], and thus gives birth to *Jiao* [the Horn Branch]. **Note:** *Jiao* [角] is the *Sui Xing*’s *Yang Qi* [yang qi] scattered, condensed into *Yin Jing* [yin essence], and thus becomes *Wood* [木].

The *Horn Branch* [角] born from the *Yang Qi* of *Water* [水], is the surname of humanity. Once there are people with this surname, they take it and intermarry with the children of *Zheng* [征], producing nine sons. The eldest son bore the surname *Zu* [祖], later changed to *Da* [大] and then to *Da Chao* [大巢氏]; the third son bore the surname *Dong* [东], the fourth *Ji* [姬], the fifth *Si* [姒], now collectively called *Zhou* [周]. The sixth bore the surname *Zhang* [长], the seventh *Chun* [春], the eighth *Ruo* [弱], now collectively changed—though not all can be listed individually. The ninth son bore the surname *Lu* [卢], now the *Jianqiu* [間丘家] clan.

All those who now bear the surname *Jiao* [角] are those who ingest the *Wood Star’s* elixir—*Muzhi* [木芝]—and align their nature with the *Wood Qi* [木炁], thereby attaining longevity and eternal life. The *Inner Transmission of Muzhong* [木公内传] states:

*"In the east, the Wood Star bears the surname Jiao* [角]. *It can give birth to all things, not just humanity. Its inherent nature opposes* *Jin* [金], *so it constantly fears* *Jin* [金] *and does not wish to undergo refining and smelting. The Five Metals* [五金], *when reversed, become the Six Bandits* [六贼], *and within the Five Viscera* [内五藏], *they cause emptiness, failing to guard the soul and spirit, as the bandits dwell within. One may ingest* *Yue Jing* [月精, moon essence] *and* *Tu Ying* [土之英, earth’s refined essence], *which are the* *Yingzhi* [英芝, elixir herbs]. *This comes from the wisdom of the immortals who drink water. Later, one may apply this to nurturing life."*

The *Nine Star System* [九星] begins with the *Wood Star* of the *Heavenly Court* [天庭], and those who practice early and diligently achieve success. The father of the nine sons was named *Xian* [先], with the surname *Jiao* [角]. *Jiao Xian* [角先] had two wives. The first wife bore nine sons, each taking their own surnames as noted before. The second wife also bore nine sons, but they did not separate and collectively retained the surname *Jiao* [角]. Today, according to the ninefold divisions of the eastern realm, they are known as the *Jiu Jiu* [九九, ninety-nine] lineage. The nine sons from each wife, scattered across the eastern seas or within them, are all descendants of the *Sui Xing*’s dispersion.

Those who practice the *Dao* [Way] must understand the great efficacy of the *Wood Star*’s transformations. They should know that the realm where the *Jiu Jiu* [二九子] descendants reside is ruled by *Wood*’s *Huang* [皇, sovereign] *Fire* [火]. The *Wood Star* benefits those with the *Four Commands* [四命], especially the *Fire Command* [火命]—those who align with it achieve the highest success. Thus, *Fire* and *Wood* mutually reign: *Fire* is born from *Wood*, and *Wood*’s nature thrives in growth, finding harmony with *Fire*, so it naturally follows *Jin* [金] in strength. **Note:** *Jin* [金] overcomes *Wood* [木], so if one seeks *Wood* below, it will be attained. Next, those with the *Fire Command* [火命] receive blessings. Among the *Five Commands* [五命], only *Tu* [土] slightly fears *Wood* [木]. If one aligns with humanity’s expansive nature, then fear arises. However, within the *Five Star Palaces* [五星宫], they do not oppose each other—how much less so their star sovereigns! **Note:** The Five Stars often gather in the mortal realm to drink wine, yet they do not harm humanity, as the world knows. Their opposition lies only in the essence of their stars. Due to the inherent natures of *Jin* [金], *Wood* [木], *Water* [水], *Fire* [火], and *Earth* [土], and humanity’s ability to craft ritual methods and utilize them, there is no longer opposition between *Water* and *Fire*. Roughly, *Wood*’s nature is kind in seeking and receiving, so those who practice know this.

Thus, after the *Winter Solstice* [冬至] and before the *Establishment of Spring* [立春], one selects an auspicious day to sacrifice to the *Wood Star Sovereign* [木星君] first, then inviting the remaining five sovereigns in total. If practiced for five years, the star sovereign descends, receiving the *Wood Star’s* elixir herb—*Muzhi Yingzhi* [木英之芝]—growing in the courtyard. By eight years, the five sovereigns collectively descend with divine omens into the son’s dwelling. By fourteen years, the five sovereigns descend to welcome the son at the *Five Capitals* [五都], where he ascends the *Five-Colored Cloud Platforms* [五色霄台]. **Note:** The *Eastern Platform* [东青玉之台] of the *Jade Clouds*, the *Western Platform* [西向玉之台], the *Southern Platform* [南丹陵玉之台], the *Northern Platform* [北黑霄玉之台], and the *Central Platform* [中黄金玉之台]—each platform corresponds to its direction, with the *Eastern Platform* having nine days of observation, and the others following similarly. The *Jade Clouds*’ *Platforms of the Five Colors* [五色霄台] are where the immortals’ music is heard. Sacrificing to the *Wood Star Sovereign* [木君], if one attains success, it is due to the alignment with this method. The primary day is the *native day of the command* [本命日]. If that is not available, then *Gengyin* [庚寅] or *Renmao* [辛卯] days will suffice. For those with the *Earth Command* [土命], these days are not used; instead, *Jia-yin* [甲寅], *Yi-mao* [乙卯], *Wu-yin* [戊寅], *Geng-zi* [庚子], or *Ren-chou* [辛丑] days are chosen, as auspicious. One must use fifteen *leads* [席] of the *Sacrificial Array* [领], along with incense, flowers, lamps, and candles of seasonal fruits, or offerings of food and drink—all must be solemn and pure to invite the true descent of divine omens. **Note:** The *Fifteen Leads* [三五一十五] correspond to the *Fifteen Star Sovereigns* [十五君官精], collectively inviting them in one session, forming a *Fifteen-Array Platform* [十五盘]. Alternatively, there may be thirty-five platforms. **Note:** If one adds three platforms for the *Three Primordial Generals* [三元将军], six platforms for the *Six Celestial Stems* [六甲], three platforms for the *Six Memorial Generals* [六纪将军], one platform for the *Pillar of Heaven Great General* [柱天大将军], seven platforms for the *Nineteen Star Sovereigns* [十九星大众] and *Twenty-Eight Constellations* [二十八宿], and three platforms for the *Three Platform Star Sovereigns* [三台众星], *Nine Wilds* [九野], and all star officials, generals, officers, soldiers—then the total is eighty-one platforms. The *Sacrificial Array* [菜楪] must be set accordingly, as in a *fasting ritual* [斋楪].

Eighty-one cups of wine, fifteen cushioned incense burners with incense, and five *liang* of blended fragrance.
**Note:** Exclude stinkwood, Buddhist incense, frankincense, and *jia-long nao* (elephant brain resin)—these emit noxious *qi*, and the Five Stars abhor them.

Use paper to steep *Reduced-True* *Suhexiang* (agarwood), sandalwood, and cloves in wine jars, along with five fragrant censers and five tables with six sides. Forty-nine floral lanterns, or thirty-five, or twenty-eight, as one’s capacity allows.
**Note:** The ancient emperors and feudal lords used thousands or hundreds—today’s forty-nine is already a reduced offering for those practicing asceticism. Even so, it remains modest.

One thousand *wen* in coins, or one hundred twenty *wen* for those of meager means. Alternatively, two thousand four hundred *wen*.
Emperors and feudal lords would use ten thousand or twenty thousand, or thirty thousand forty thousand—this is the *settling-seated* coinage.

One bolt of plain silk; emperors and feudal lords would use one hundred bolts, or one thousand bolts.

Two *fen* of refined gold—emperors would use one *jin*, feudal lords one *liang*.

Twelve boxes of rare fruits, precious woods, and ornate flowers. Emperors and feudal lords would use eighty-one boxes.

On a clear night of star and moon, construct an altar of yellow earth.

When the altar is complete, the furnace is ignited, and the incantations are recited—*wenyi* texts are read separately as prescribed. Three recitations and nine libations are performed. The three recitations are the texts, and the nine libations are the offerings of wine.

After the rites conclude, the Five Talismans are swallowed to seek the five virtues for bodily protection. The talismans are then dispersed, for failure to do so invites dark retribution.

The **Later Sage Emperor** proclaims the talismans of the Four Seasons and Five Phases, the Nine Heavens’ Spring, Summer, Autumn, and Winter Command Talismans, the Talismans of the Wood Phase’s Year Star Sovereign, the Fire Phase’s Mars Star Sovereign, the Metal Phase’s Venus Star Sovereign, the Water Phase’s Jupiter Star Sovereign, and the Earth Phase’s Stabilizing Star Talisman. These six talismans are entrusted to the **Bundle-Sea Child Sovereign** by the Later Sage Emperor.

The Child Sovereign is a Wood Commanded being, and thus the talismans are passed down to him, commanding him to refine them with the other Commanded beings.

All the above talismans are inscribed in cinnabar.

The **Most High Venerable Lord Lao** instructs the **Benevolent and Virtuous True Person**—
*Note: The Benevolent and Virtuous True Person is a Western barbarian, now serving as the Later Sage’s Left Celestial True Person*—

*"The Wood Phase star’s qi thrives in generation. On days and hours ruled by the Wood Star, first align with the Wood Star, traversing all five stars. Twist the talismans of Metal, Water, Fire, and Earth.*

*The Later Sage Emperor grants the Heavenly Master the Five Phase talismans of the Five Stars. The Wood talisman is on the left hand’s second finger, beneath the second joint, ascending to the second knuckle’s apex to command the Wood talisman. The Fire talisman is on the left hand’s third finger, at the third joint’s left edge, commanding the talisman at the joint’s center. The Earth talisman is on the fourth finger’s third joint. The Metal talisman is on the fourth finger’s third joint, commanding the talisman at the midpoint below the joint. The Water talisman is on the third finger’s first joint, commanding the talisman at the third division.*

*This is the first Five Phase talisman. When performing rituals, use five-colored brushes to mark them repeatedly until the talismans are fully activated. Practice consistently. After three years, the Five Star Sovereigns descend to teach their children Dao refinement, granting all desires naturally.*

*Those who attain the Dao need not act further—merely cherish the Dao, and the Dao will bestow its essence upon you.*

*Perform the Five Stars’ Yu Step three times, then recite the Five Phase Incantations eighteen times in full. After nine days, you ascend to the Celestial Register, attain the Immortal Rank, and are named among the True Ones. You escape the Nine Calamities and Hundred Illnesses, the Three Corpses and Nine Vermin, malevolent ghosts, and slanderous schemes, entering the Immortal Realm forever.*

*After nine years—*
*Note: Each spring’s third month, practice for nine days monthly. This method spans from the Celestial Ropes to the Three Enclosures and Five Stars.*

*—perform the Yu Step and strike the fingers. If malevolent ghosts appear, they will be crushed under a fifteen-*jin* fist. If they dare speak, the Northern Dipper will strike them down—do not misuse this power.*

*The Year Star is subject to the Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper, the True Consorts, and the Lovely Daughters. The Year Star Sovereign, the Five Direction Star Sovereigns, the Northern Dipper’s Nine True Sovereigns, their True Consorts, and the Five Star Sovereigns’ Ladies—*
*Note: True Consorts are the Northern Dipper’s True Consorts; Ladies are the Five Star Sovereigns’ wives.*

*—along with the assembled multitudes, supplement the ranks of the Upper Clarity True Persons.*

*After fourteen years, the residence is elevated, and wife and children ascend with you.*

*[End of] Volume Thirteen of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Scroll*
*[End of] Volume Fourteen of the Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Scroll*

「Its weight totals **150 catties** [1]. If one practices the **Constant Fist** [2], it subdues and kills malevolent ghosts—if they dare speak, the Northern Dipper will strike them down, but one must not misuse this power. The **Year Star** [3] is subject to the Nine Stars of the Northern Dipper, the **True Consorts**, and the **Lovely Daughters** [4], and so forth.

The **Year Star Sovereign** [5], along with the Five Direction Star Sovereigns, the Northern Dipper’s Nine **True Sovereigns** and their **True Consorts**, and the Five Star Sovereigns’ **Ladies** [6],—
*Note: True Consorts are the Northern Dipper’s True Consorts; Ladies are the Five Star Sovereigns’ wives.*

—together with the assembled multitudes, supplement the ranks of the **Upper Clarity True Persons** [7]. After fourteen years, the residence is elevated, and wife and children ascend with you.

The **Grand Sage of the Unified Dao**, **Master Sovereign** Zhang Fangping, **Daoist Lord** Zhang Daoling, **Master** Zhao Sheng, **Commander** Wang Chang, **Master** Li Zhongfu, **Master** Mao Ying, **Master** Xu Yuzhu and others [8] are those who have compiled this text in succession. **Daoist Master** Li Chunfeng annotated it. The **Five Phases** [9] and **Six Periods** [10] produce the **Way’s Essence** below. The **Later Sage Emperor** [11] instructed the **Twenty-Nine True Persons of Mysterious Isles** [12], saying: *"You wish to be the Teacher of Heavenly and Human Beings; you must transmit the **Dao’s Key** and cultivate the **Inner Secrets of True Personhood**, bestowing them upon the **Aspirants** [13]. One must not recklessly transmit this to others, lest it invite calamity upon oneself.*

For indeed, the **True Essence**—when humans transmit these **Five-Phase True Secrets** and the **Way of Talismans, Rituals, and Offerings** [14], it is also the **True Essence**. Moreover, all the **Key Secrets of True Personhood** [15] and their **High Dao**, their most guarded mysteries lie in the **twisting of the fingers**, the **attunement of the ritual robes**, the **rotation of the Dipper**, and the **pointing to Heaven** [16]. Those who can **fly through clouds and traverse rain**, who can **uproot and snap trees**—these are **Dragons** [17]. Aspirants who obtain these **wondrous Dao Secrets**—if they merely perform the **Stepping Flight** [18],—
*Note: Stepping Flight refers to the **A-yu Step** [19].*

—the **A-yu Step** [20], **twelve years** of practice, **attunement of the ritual robes**, the **twisting of the Dragon Secrets**, and the **rotation of the Heavenly Lock** [21]—will cause the target to fall dead at their touch. Though they can strike down, they must not act recklessly. Reckless action will forfeit one’s **Sage position**. Knowing this, one should not act.

If one were to act recklessly against another person, merely to play with one’s power for a moment, one would not realize that the **Dragon** [22] bears no guilt while the target dies, and the blame would instead fall upon oneself and even implicate one’s **Teacher** [23]. One must **carefully examine** and **not act** without necessity. If an enemy comes to harm you and you cannot evade them, then you may use this method, but **quickly resolve the matter** afterward.
