*Note: The Later Sage Emperor bestows this secret only to those who aspire to the Dao, to safeguard their lives and families. This method of **Left Suppression, Right Release**—*
*Note: Suppression refers to twisting the fingers of the left hand; Release refers to twisting the fingers of the right hand. The Later Sage Emperor taught the Celestial Master [24] the method of Left Suppression and Right Release, which can be used endlessly.*

—is the **Refining of the River Vehicle** [25]. **Master Zhang Shaozhen** obtained the teachings of **Laozi, the Celestial Lord** [26], and was able to **delay his lifespan for a thousand years**, serving as a **pillar of stability for the mortal realm** and warding off calamities. Later, he did not ascend to Heaven, fearing the **Five Viscera** [27] might decay and disperse. He then employed **200 catties of green lead** [28].
*Note: Excessive mercury is called **cup lead**; impure cinnabar is called **grind lead**, and both are unfit for use. Only the **I-yang** [29] and **Persian** [30] varieties are acceptable, with **purple cinnabar** being superior. This is highly potent.*

He placed **one inverted moon iron cauldron** [31] to the right, measuring the lead according to the cauldron’s size, and roasted it with **fierce fire**. When the lead had fully melted, he **stirred it thoroughly to the bottom**. In a short while, it would naturally turn into **green sand** [32]. Initially, when the fire was lit, the lead would sometimes form **green sand**, and sometimes fail to change. One must **stir continuously without pause**, and stop only when all has transformed. If the fire cools, the lead will revert to its original state.

If one wishes to **forcefully transform the lead into yellow flowers** [33], after the lead becomes **green sand**, one must **not extinguish the fierce fire**, but stir it continuously, and it will immediately turn into **yellow flowers of lead** [34]. Then, placing the **green sand** in a basin, one **gradually adds bitter wine** [35] and **refines it with a pestle**, using **sugar and vinegar**. If one does not use **strong, concentrated wine**, the **green sand** will become **fine, clear powder**. When finished, one **dries it on tiles** under the sun. After a short while, one **gently warms it with a low flame**, takes **imperial river sediment powder** [36], and **mixes it with the left flavor** [37]. Without this method, the **pill** cannot be formed. The lead, once dried, is placed into a **cast-iron pot**, covered above and below, and **roasted with fierce fire**. Using a **leather bag to pound the lead**, it flows through the **cast-iron channel**, and the **green sand** will immediately transform. One places a **cast-iron vessel** below to collect it, taking all until it is exhausted.

Its color is **bright white**, named **Lead Grandson** [38]. After **eight reversals and nine rotations**, it turns **purple**. For every **catty of lead**, after **nine rotations**, it consumes **15 catties and 1 ounce**, yielding **1 ounce**. This is called **Jin Gong Dan** [39]—**Strong Lead Elixir** [40]. It is also known as **Purple River Vehicle**, **Golden Dog**, **Nine-Rotation Treasure**, and **Nine-One-Rotation Lead Essence**. Its uses are manifold.

Other accounts are found in the *Upper Clarity Spirit Book* and the *Dragon-Tiger Rectified Talismans*.

The **Eastern Wood Star Sovereign** instructed **True Person of the Supreme Ultimate**, **Master Jie Ziliang** [41], saying: *"When the apricot kernels are ripe, mix them with their skins and flesh, leaving them in a dry place. If the place is damp, use a **wooden tray** to contain them. Wait until the skins and flesh naturally dry up, until early autumn. Then, **cut two sharp, pointed holes** into them. When the **kernel is exposed**, roast it with **gentle fire**—when it makes a **hissing sound**, the **gold** emerges. Use a **bamboo knife** to collect it. A **round, one-inch piece** yields **one catty**, and it is used to make **A-yu Golden Elixir** [42].*
*Note: The elixir is recorded in the *Upper Clarity Spirit Book*, which states that **yellow flower gold** is the true substance. The remaining gold is **mountain and river gold**, not the superior medicine.*

Those who have not yet obtained the *Golden Lock, Flowing Pearl Upper Scripture* and this book cannot yet attain **True Personhood** and ascend to Heaven. Moreover, they can **delay their lifespan for two hundred years**, seeking the **Perfect Ones** [43]. This is the **most wondrous method of cultivation** above.

The **Refining** is fully explained in the *Upper Clarity Spirit Book*; no further annotation is needed.

---

The **Later Sage Emperor** instructed **Yellow Stone Master** [44], saying: *"You are a teacher for mortals; you know that the **Year Star’s Wood Essence** descends into the **Paulownia tree** [45]. At the moment when the **thunder’s initial strike** [46] echoes, **cut the eastern branch** as a **talisman-symbol** [47], and bestow it upon **Zifang** [48], to aid **Conqueror Liu Bang** [49] as his master. Would this not save the lives of **tens of thousands of people**? You are not one who performs **hidden virtuous deeds** without merit."*
*Note: The *Flowing Pearl Outer Chapter* uses the **Paulownia talisman**, which is derived from this instruction. Zifang is **Zhang Liang**, the Han general and chancellor. He used **Yellow Stone Master’s strategies** to defeat **Strong Item** [50].*

**Strong Item** [51] and the **Han House** [52] contested the **Mandate of Heaven**, killing **one hundred thousand soldiers** in their struggle. **Strong Item** was finally defeated. **Zifang** used his military prowess, **calculating the battles before and after**—**seventy more**—and **killing 560,000 soldiers**, while **subduing Strong Item’s remaining 400,000 soldiers**. He **did not repay the debt of death** [53], but later, **each one received their due**. Afterward, **Zifang** knew that the **Han House’s soldiers** were the **ones who had been killed first**, and that the **soldiers of Strong Item** were the **ones who had died in the dark** [54]. Thus, he praised **Zifang and Yellow Stone Master’s virtue** in safeguarding the lives of the multitudes.

With me and the **forty thousand multitudes**, we emerged without the **bloodshed penalty**, each able to die in peace and become **pure ghosts**. Reflecting upon this, the **weight of thought** and the **greatness of the deed** are profound.

When the **multitudes** were fully revealed to **Taishan Jun**, the **Lord of Taishan** knew of the matter. After reporting to **Heavenly Oracle** and the **Most Holy Primordial Jade Emperor**, the **Supreme Dao Lord**, the decree was issued to **transcend Zifang and Yellow Stone Master**, granting them **immortality as celestial officials**. Though they did not ascend to the **bright daytime heavens**, they attained **embodied dissolution**—**wooden dissolution**, departing as corpses.

They were **restored as the Celestial Consorts of Qingcheng Mountain’s Immortal Realm**, a feat of **Mars’ qi-transformation**.

**Warned against**, the **perfected sage** who practices the Dao should only perform **subtle deeds**—rescuing the sick, aiding the desperate, relieving poverty, and mediating conflicts between warring factions. They should **dissolve and disperse** those entangled in strife, and **protect the world** from harm by **divine dragons, ghosts, and malevolent spirits**, as well as **calamities of flood and drought, epidemics, and curses**—such as **nightmares, tongue-twitching, and hexes**. Such deeds carry **vast and wondrous virtue**.

The **Most Holy Lord** declared to the **Celestial True Persons**: *"Those who cultivate to perfection, with single-hearted devotion to the Dao, attaining **True Dao and True Qi**, dissolving **unrighteous qi**, accumulate **infinite and wondrous merit**."*

**Laozi** instructed **Yu** (注: *At Yu’s time, Laozi was Ji Kezi’s descendant, teaching the Dao to Shun and Yu.*):
*"The essence of **Mars** manifests as a **boat**, drifting across the **Stygian wilderness**, seeking the **Central Water’s source**.*

*Again, the **soul of Mars** shapes the **pattern of Heaven and Earth**.* (注: *Pattern of Heaven—maplewood. Pattern of Earth—jujube wood.*)

*When these two woods unite, they are **engraved** into the **stars and deities of the cosmos**, encompassing **all of Heaven and Earth**. Their revolving wheels interweave, restraining **wicked men and malevolent ghosts**, as **hand obeys mind**. They can **command all things**, **subdue gods and spirits**, **reverse Heaven and turn Earth**, and **assist me in ascending the Dao of Earthly Foundations and Heavenly Principles**.*

*They can **tame tigers and leopards**, **command ten thousand soldiers**, **overpower the wicked**, **halt winds and rains**, **subdue serpents and dragons**, and **reverse malevolent speech**—all verified by their effects.*

*To craft this **Pattern** brings **pure fortune** to the virtuous. The **filthy and unfilial** must never use it.*

*If one touches it before death, they will die afterward. Such wood is **unfit for crafting the Pattern**, nor should it be used for **deceased patterns**. One must never gaze upon them.*

*How much worse for the **common and foolish** to take and reuse them—this is **great impurity**! Those who practice the Dao improperly are thus condemned.*

*The **Pattern** must not be seen by **monks or nuns**; to do so is **impure and taboo**.*

*If a **Daoist** must use it, they must first **don heavy ritual robes** and remain outside for **twenty-five days** before approaching. If using it urgently, they must **purify impurity** by swallowing the **Purification Impurity Talisman**, then wear **auspicious robes** before use.*

*If **unfilial, monks, nuns, or pregnant women** see or handle it, they must **never touch or employ it**.*

*If a **woman** receives the **Pattern**, she must **measure her own use carefully**—if she falls ill afterward, she must **not touch it again** until the illness subsides.*

**Zhenren Wang Ziqiao**, the **True Person of the Paulownia Tree**, instructed his **second daughter**:
*'The **Pattern** is for **emergency use**. When sickness arises, swallow the **Purification Impurity Talisman**, drink **Purification Impurity Water**, and **recite the incantation**—thus it is effective.*

*It can **assist those who walk the Dao**, mastering **prohibition and restraint**, rendering them **omnipotent**. Its **divine power is verifiable**.*

*There are **separate scriptures and diagrams**—I shall now transmit to you the **Taiyi** [Supreme One]."*

「**Note:** The **Patterns** of the Thunder Lord for the Four Seasons, the *Liu-Ren* and *Liu-Jia* [Six Ren and Six Jia], the Eight *Man* and Six *Rong* [Mystical Protective Spirits and Martial Deities], were transmitted to **Yu** [Great Flood Controller].

**Yu** refined them into a **ten-scroll scripture**, expanding it to **forty-nine scrolls**, which he titled *The Yellow Emperor’s Gathering of Spirits*.

**Note:** This is the *Gathering of Spirits* in its Upper, Middle, and Lower sections, as well as the *Yellow Emperor’s Pattern Scripture*.

Later **sages and rulers** conferred upon the **Celestial Master** [天師] the *Ten-Scroll Pattern Scripture* and the *Three-Scroll Liu-Ren Talismans*, instructing:

*"When the **Wood Star’s essence** scatters below, upon the **maple tree’s branches**, the **Pattern** that does not grow taller than people is the **Ling Pattern** [灵式], while the one that towers above is the **Xiong Pattern** [凶式].
Though the **Xiong Pattern** is harmful, it does not **assist in spiritual response**—if it does not align with the **Pattern’s true nature**, it is not a **Pattern**.

**Obtaining it**, one must follow the **scripture’s instructions**, perform **sacrificial rites** [祭醮], and **employ it to aid the Dao** and benefit others—**as the divine responds with certainty**, none shall fail to succeed.

Its **power matches that of Heaven and Earth**, and its **control is swift as a breath**.

**Note:** The **Pattern**’s upper section corresponds to **Heaven**, its lower to **Earth**; the **divine stars and celestial spirits** of Heaven and Earth are all inscribed and deployed within it, just as the **functions and transformations** of Heaven and Earth themselves.

**Common folk** who practice it may **attain the Dao and become immortals**, and **ascendants** have observed them.

Further, it is said: *"When the **Wood Star’s essence** first scatters, it transforms into a **jujube tree** [枣树].
The **jujube tree** is the **mother of all trees**, and the **maple tree** is the **father of all trees**.

**Note:** The *Pattern Scripture* states: *"The **maple tree** is the **longest of all trees**, and the **jujube tree** is the **mother of all trees**."*

Only **maple or jujube trees** that have aged for many years are **suitable for the Pattern**—**how much more** so for those who **cultivate the Pattern** or **refine the Pattern’s essence**, whose **spiritual response** extends to the **Nine Heavens**!

**Note:** The **Pattern’s essence** grows swiftly beneath the **maple tree**, not towering above people—this is the **Ling** [灵]. It can **emerge at night**, ascending to **leap upon the tree**, surpassing the **mother tree** in height. Those who have **tested it** often find **cotton** [绵] on the tree’s branches—**this confirms its nocturnal ascent**, surpassing the **mother tree’s stature**, and thus its **Ling** nature.

This **tree’s essence** is the **true qi of the Wood Star**—**taking it harms others**. **Never recklessly cut or damage it**, for this is **murderous**.

**Take it** with the **Dao/Way’s qi** and **prohibitionary techniques**—
**Note:** The **technique** is applied to the **left hand’s fourth finger**, at the **second joint**, binding it with **five-colored silk**.

—then **inscribe the Pattern’s talisman** and **wear it as a belt**. **Swallow the talisman**, and **cut the tree accordingly**. **Affix the talisman** with **summons**.

**Note:** The **summons** are **conjured with the Earthly Deities** together—this is called **taking Yang from Yin**. The **Yin field is felled**, **connecting Heaven and Earth**, stirring **divine immortals**, capturing **spirits, dragons, and ghosts**, and **expanding the human realm**. It enables one to **move mountains, block seas, uproot trees**, and **enter armies, waters, or fires**—none shall harm them.

This is the **power of human wisdom and insight**—**embracing Heaven and Earth’s Yin and Yang**, one naturally **communicates with spirits**, known as **wondrous application**.

When the **Pattern’s essence** is **controlled and refined**, it must be done on **auspicious days**. The **master** must be **upright and pure**, with the **upper section narrow as Heaven** and the **lower section broad as Earth**, adjusting proportions to match **cosmic harmony**. The **large Pattern** must not exceed **four inches**, nor the **small Pattern** fall below **two inches**. The **length and breadth** must align **equally** in all **four cardinal directions**.

Within it lies the **Heavenly Pillar** [天柱], named **Flowing Pearl’s Complement** [配流珠], arranged in sequence—
**Note:** The **Flowing Pearl** contains the **General of the Heavenly Pillar** [柱天将军], also **conjured and named** in this manner.

The **sage’s intent** in crafting the **Pattern’s form** was to **harmonize with Heaven and Earth**, **directing Yin and Yang**—all through **wisdom**. Wisdom **encompasses all things as Patterns**, and **nature aligns with this unity**.

Thus, **all undertakings** shall succeed if **applied rightly**—but **if misused**, none shall prosper, and it shall **bring harm**. You can **craft and refine** the **Pattern**, obtaining a **twelve-faced Pattern**, whose **power aligns with the Dao** and **walks the Path of Rectification** [正一], the **True Teaching’s prohibitionary techniques**, serving as the **Dao’s martial aspect**.

The **Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl** constitute the **Dao’s literary aspect**, the **True Teaching’s prohibitionary techniques**. When **both aspects are complete**, Heaven and Earth **rest within your grasp**, and Yin and Yang **lie within your heart and speech**—
**Note:** One **scroll** states *"within the hands."*

—**standing, one may seize the Dao**. **This requires a loyal heart and upright nature**—
**Note:** Loyalty is **filial devotion to the Master**, uprightness is **compassion for others**, without **deceit or crookedness**.

—**virtue** shall **benefit all beings**, rooted in **compassion**. **First aid the region and state**, then **secure your own household**. If you **practice with sincerity**—
**Note:** The **technique** is the **Flowing Pearl’s method**, which includes **conjuring garments, footwear, and talismans** [衣履斗蹑纪].

—**employing the Pattern**, its **effects shall be vast**. You may **lift your household and ascend**, becoming **the teacher of Heavenly beings**.

**Note:** Later, it was indeed as the **Celestial Master** [太上] spoke. Today, those who **practice and employ** it do not follow **Yu’s fixed scriptures**. They **invoke the Yellow Emperor’s words**, all **matters of ancient and modern application**.

In **current use**, it is **not as effective** as **Yu’s composed scriptures**, which **verify spiritual response** and **align with the Wood Star’s qi**. **Always select auspicious days** between **the start of Spring** and **before the Spring Equinox**, performing **two sacrificial rites** [醮] each year to the **Pattern’s spirit**. After the **rites conclude**, **seal it away** if no further use is needed.

**Note:** The *Liu-Ren* [六壬] originally lacked the **sealing of the Pattern’s text**. The **Pattern’s upper and lower sections** must **face Heaven and Earth**—**never let them lose alignment**. The **Pattern’s upper section** must also **face the Celestial Master of Earth**, and the **Thunder Pattern** must **include the Food Spirit** [食神], which is the **Ghost Gate** [鬼门].

The **Liu-Ren** and **Taiyi** [太一] must all **face Heaven and Earth**—**never let them lose alignment**, or it shall **harm others**. **Never let the alignment** [纲] **include one’s own natal life-force** [本命].

The **Four-Season Patterns** must be **aligned seasonally**: **Spring** with **Summer**, **Summer** with **Autumn**, and so forth. **Winter** aligned with **Spring** shall **face Summer**, and **Summer** shall **face Autumn**—this is their **application**.

The **rites and sacrificial procedures** are **detailed in the Yellow Emperor’s Gathering of Spirits** above. **Always bind it with five-colored silk**, ensuring **no shifting or alteration**, and **inscribe the master’s life-force and year of application**—
**Note:** The **year of application** is recorded in the **Yuan-Chen Diagram and Ritual Procedures**.

—**calculating the *Jia-Zi* cycle** [甲子] as the **great year of application**, the **three celestial cycles** [三元] as the **small year of application**, and the **eight trigrams** [八卦] as the **wandering year of application**. The **three cycles** govern the **three celestial applications**—the rest are **not true calculations**, lacking **verifiable basis**.

「Moreover, the **Jia-Zi cycle** [甲子] as **application year** is the composition of the **Ancestral Sage, Elder Lord of the Void** [前聖老君虚皇], serving as the **inner talismans for the Six Jia** [六甲內符行年]. The **Later Sage, Jade Emperor** [後聖了玉皇] and **Lord of the Dao** [上道君] bestowed the title **Master of the Heavenly Arts** [天師], calling it the **Six Jia Talismans’ Application Year** [六甲箓行年].

When calculating, one must take the **location of the Five Ghosts of Yuan-Chen** [元辰五鬼] and their **overlapping configurations** [相重], then **invoke the Yuan-Chen talismans** [上元辰章解] to **pass through this calamity** [過度此厄]. Such a person **should always be treated as a royal relative** [長宜王相]—then **no worries or calamities** [無憂厄] shall befall them. If **sudden disasters or calamities** [忽有災厄] befall them, and their **body escapes but their essence does not** [身出厄不出], then according to the **Sages** [聖人], this is **not the true Application Year** [別說行年], and **not the Great Application Year** [非大行年] either. Thus, there shall be **some loss** [則有所損].

**Those who study talismans** [夫人學轉式] should **always consider others’ fortunes** [常謀他人], not calculating their own. If one **recklessly applies talismans near the Four Gateway Gods** [近於四門之神],—**Heaven’s Gate** [天門], **Human’s Gate** [人門], **Earth’s Portal** [地戶], and **Ghost’s Portal** [鬼戶]—**they shall never bind such talismans to the Four Gateway Years** [切不得纲加四門].

If the **Application Year falls within the Four Minor Years** [四孟], such as **Yin** [寅], **Shen** [申], **Wei** [巳], and **Hai** [亥], then **one must not bind talismans to these Four Minor Years** [纲即不加四孟行年]. If it falls within the **Four Central Years** [四仲], such as **Zi** [子], **Wu** [午], **Mao** [卯], and **You** [酉], then **one must not bind talismans to these Four Central Years** [纲不加四仲行年]. If it falls within the **Four Seasonal Years** [四季], such as **Chen** [辰], **Xu** [戌], **Chou** [丑], and **Wei** [未], then **one must not bind talismans to these Four Seasonal Years** [纲不加四季行年].

**Note:** If there are **urgent matters** [有急事], then **twist the Talisman Supervisor’s Incantation** [捻都監誥], **digging the time** [堑時] on the **10th or 5th day** [十日五曰]. If there are **no pressing affairs** [事無], then **quickly resolve it** [即急解之], and **success shall follow** [即得]. If there are **sudden and dire emergencies** [更有急卒], and **one has not yet obtained resolution** [未得解者], then take the **Heavenly Talisman’s position of the Application Year** [天式上行年神位], place a **single layer of the Long-Life Talisman** [長生符] upon it, and **subdue and suppress** [鎮克] the calamity. Thus, **one shall forever not fear being harmed by others** [永不畏加臨人害].

The **Long-Life Talisman** [長生符] is **woven with inner talismans** [卷內符] and **inscribed in vermilion** [朱書], with **this single layer** [此符一道] placed **upon the Heavenly Talisman’s original life-force and Application Year position** [安天式上本命行年神位]. It **subdues and repels calamities** [鎮卻災厄]. If **worn on the left arm behind the elbow** [一道帶之於左肘之後], it **shall not protect other talismans** [用加諸式不畏], but rather **harm one’s own body** [反損己身].

The **Five Agents** [五行] begin with **Worldly Water** [世水], which is the **Chen Star’s scattered *qi*** [辰星散炁]. Water can **transform into refined *qi*** [精炁] and **become a Dragon** [從龍], and the Dragon **borrows the Chen Star’s yin *qi*** [假辰星陰炁] to **generate feathers** [而生羽]. Feathers are the **Chen Star’s yang *qi* dispersing** [羽是辰星之陽炁散], **congealing into yin** [凝陰], and **returning to water** [而為水]. **The yang *qi* of water** [水陽炁] is what **produces feathers** [所生羽], and **feathers represent humanity** [羽是人].

The surname **Feather** [羽姓] is taken from this, and **one who bears this surname** [既有其人] should **marry with descendants of the Shang surname** [而取商姓之子], producing **five sons** [生五子]. The **eldest son** [長子] shall take the **original surname of Water** [初姓水], the **second son** [二子] shall bear the surname **Feather** [羽姓], the **third and fourth sons** [三子、四子] shall **collectively be surnamed Feather** [總成羽姓], and the **fifth son** [五子] shall bear the surname **Red** [赤], which is the **modern Red Clan** [今之赤氏]. Many have **altered their surnames** [亦多改姓], such as the **Jufu Wu Clan** [朱浮吳氏].

Additionally, the **third and second sons’ branches** [三子、二子支中] often **change or alter surnames** [後代多改易姓], such as the **Pan, Luo, Gan, Wang, and Shi surnames** [潘、羅、甘、王、石之姓].

Now, **those who gather these talismans** [今據合是羽姓之人] should **refine Mercury** [合煉水銀]. Mercury **belongs to Water** [水銀屬水], while **Metal belongs to Shang** [金屬商], and **Metal and Water are harmoniously combined** [金水合宜]. These two substances **form a medicine** [為藥], and **taking it shall benefit longevity** [服而有益壽之理].

The **Floating Mound Master’s Inner Teachings** [《浮丘公內傳》] states: **"The Northern realm’s Water surname Feather** [北方水姓羽] has the nature of **nourishing and prolonging all things** [羽性潤長萬物]. It can also **extinguish all things** [亦能滅萬物], adapting to the **Four Seasons** [以隨四季], and **executing the command to generate or perish** [而行令生滅]. All these are **utilized by humanity** [皆用人弘之], to **nourish and benefit** [令潤益亦得], or to **follow its nature and harm figures and things** [令從性損人物亦得]. It **has no inherent moral principle** [本無正心], but **its *qi* is upright** [而有正炁]. **The intentions of mortals lie in warmth and cold** [志人行溫冷在人], which **depend on humanity** [岂在乎水].

**Floating Mound Master** [浮丘先生] **often ate Water Kei** [常以采水芝而食], thereby **living to over two hundred years** [生長二百 ‘乎年]. When he **encountered the Most High Ancestral Sage, Elder Lord** [遇太上前聖老君], the **Elder Lord taught him the method of recording the Middle Dipper’s position** [教中斗地紀之法]. After **four years** [四年], his **body grew light like a Dragon’s** [驾龍體輕], and **he could fly by himself** [自能飛身]. In the **fifth year** [五年], the **Chen Star Lord** [辰星君] descended to **test his talents** [下觀試才], finding **nine faults** [有九過], and **bestowed upon him a secondary Dragon** [便以別驾一龍與公]. The Master **feared falling from its back and dying** [公畏落身死], so he **prostrated himself twice more** [再拜求], **begging for his body to grow feathers** [乞自身生毛羽], so that **he could ride the Dragon without falling** [即乘龍無或堕落], and **his body would become fine dust** [身粉為微塵], **unable to be immediately removed** [不可即去].

The **Chen Star Lord, the Most True One** [辰星太真君], then asked: **"You are surnamed Floating Mound** [卿姓浮丘], but **your original surname is Feather** [本姓羽]. I shall **grant you the method of transforming the Middle Dipper’s position into the clothing of Yu, the Great Dipper’s configuration** [與卿變履斗為禹配衣之法], and **when practiced for five years** [行之五年], your **body shall naturally grow feathers** [體自生毛羽], allowing you to **soar through the Celestial Abyss** [飛遊洞天]. **Such a Daoist official** [此之仙官] is **most noble and grand** [至貴至大], **why must you necessarily ascend to Heaven** [何必要升天]? Even if you **ascend to Heaven**, you shall **arrive at the Celestial Bureau** [到天曹], **where the Lord of the Court is summoned** [引朝太平君], **and later return to the Celestial Abyss** [後即還配於洞天].

**"If you are capable** [子若能], then **you may also teach it** [即可便教]. The Master **prostrated himself twice more in request** [公再拜請受], **begging to receive the instruction.**」

The Lord said: *"I have not heard that there is the Step of the Great Yu, the one who tamed the floods. When he regulated the waters, the Most High descended and personally observed him as he took three steps with nine strides.*

The Most High, Laozi, instructed Yu: *'Do you not see the spirit of the Douyi bird, which takes flight? Even birds follow the principle of three steps and nine strides, turning stones and wood to seize serpents. A note: If birds, which have such intent, can do this, how much more so can humans?'*

Yu received the teaching and sought the method, and thus mastered the **Five Dipper Transformation** [翻五斗], ascending to the **Supreme Polarity** [太极], assuming a **water-essence corpse** [水精为尸], and being buried in the **Southern Yue** [南越].

Upon this, the Master awoke and learned it. After five years, his body truly grew feathers and hair. In one year, he could fly ten *li*, five *li*—people at the time called this feathered man who could fly the **Guest of the Plumed Body** [毛羽之客]. Thus, he earned his name.

Later, after seven years, he could fly a thousand *li*, entering the **Celestial Abyss** [洞天], coming and going between the mortal realm for hundreds of years. Suddenly, one day, he rode a dragon and departed, never returning.

His five descendants each changed their surnames, though even after changing them, they could not depart from the North. Thus, they became the **Five Qi** [五炁].
*A note: All regions follow the Five Surnames, corresponding to metal, water, wood, fire, and earth as qi. Each color governs a direction; hence, people today are called "born on a certain *yin* day, the son of green," and so on.*

The virtue of accumulated water and the spread of Yu’s achievements—this is the transformation of the **Minister of the Hour Star** [辰星]. Though slightly fearful of earth, earth, though subduing water, cannot utterly extinguish it when water is abundant.

The use of the Five Surnames lies in water’s ability to both nourish and harm things. It leans toward supporting wood while embracing metal’s mutual generation and assistance.

Practitioners of the Dao, when walking upon the **Water Star** [水星], must also manipulate the **Wood Key** [木诀] and the **Metal Key** [金诀], aligning with water. Water will then nourish the **True Qi** [真炁] and sustain it within the body.

Later, the **Saintly Sovereign** [后圣君] told the **Great King** [大王君]:
*"Your disciple, Master Mao Ying and Master Mao Gu, are water-destined individuals. When practicing the Step, first manipulate the **Wood Star Key** [木星诀]. Then, with the fingers of your next hand, point to the Wood Star, supporting the body and solidifying the spirit. Only then can one attain the **Lower True** [下真] and become the **Earthly Master of the Celestial Rank** [地上主仙位]. For though aged and spiritually exhausted, they can no longer ascend and fly. Only after a hundred or a thousand years, if they do not encounter a great Daoist, can they await the **Upper True** [上真]."*

The Most High, Laozi, told **Yuanji Zi** [元极子]:
*A note: This is Mr. Wuji, a Qin native, surnamed Zheng, named Jichu.*
*"You too follow the principle of the Five Surnames, leaning toward the Water Surname. You have merit, and you revere water well—thus, the water dragon appeared and bestowed a book upon you. Those who revere the Water Surname and honor water deeply are often those of the Water Surname, who habitually walk the Dipper and manipulate the Water Star Key, their hearts ever respectful.*

If one practices the Dao, and again manipulates the **Earth Key** [土诀] for five years, the gods of the rivers and seas will appear before them, teaching you the method of **taming dragons**, making rain and clear skies respond to your will as if by hand, accomplished in an instant. Is this not the result of preserving the merit of water in practice, thus enabling you to **race dragons and command rain**, swift as thought?

Wuji followed this teaching, and indeed, as foretold, he later rode a dragon and ascended to the **Mysterious Isle** [玄洲]."*

In the time of **Emperor Yao and Shun**, there was **Mountain-Dwelling Child Xu Xun**, a water-destined individual. He often revered water, creating a pond, and always instructed his household to treat it with utmost respect. He also habitually drank a *he* of water daily.

After six years, suddenly, a mirror appeared at the pond’s center, six *cun* wide, round and beautiful like the moon. Xu Xun carried it, and sixteen mirror spirits followed him. There were also fourteen jade maidens, fourteen jade boys, and one general.

Xu Xun asked, and they replied: *"We are great gods. The Great Minister of the Hour Star returned the **Northern Sky Water Mother’s Mirror** [北霄水母之镜] to us, fearing you might lose it and suffer harm. We tested you. If you truly revered water, believed in the Five Phases, habitually walked the stars and Dipper, and used the method without deceit, then if you passed the test, we would grant you the **Celestial True Rank** [天真之位]. Later, though you failed, you ascended to the **Supreme Polarity** [太极] and did not attain the **Upper Pure** [上清]."*

The **Saintly Sovereign** then instructed **Mao Xi** [茅喜]:
*A note: Xi was the great-grandfather of Ying, serving as the teacher of Le Ba.*
*"At the end of the Qin Dynasty, he attained immortality and could transform water into rain. The method of transforming water into rain:*

On **homologous *bingzi* days** [丙子日] and **homologous *jiazi* days** [甲子日], take a basin of water, holding it in your left hand, and walk the **Earthly Circuit** [地纪] three times.
*A note: If skilled, simply walk while mentally visualizing the shape of the Northern Dipper’s Earthly Circuit—do not form the Central Dipper shape. The Central Dipper belongs to earth, causing rain to fail. Always form the Northern Dipper shape. If your visualization and intent are profound and effective, even without walking the circuit, it will work. Merely walk while focusing your mind—it will surely take effect.*

After three circuits, perform the **Yu Step** [禹步] three times, then spread to the **Three Wilds** [三野] six times, and to the **Six Wilds** [六野] nine times. The **Nine Wilds** [九野] will fill the sky with rain. Obtain the nine circuits.

After completing the steps, manipulate the **Rain-Invoking Key** [行雨诀], holding nine mouthfuls of water, and spit them toward the sky. In an instant, the heavens and earth darken, and rain falls.

This method is divine and verifiable—do not use it recklessly. If there is no drought, do not employ it. For drought is a prohibition by the **Celestial Emperor** [天帝], and using it invites the crime of **rebelling against Heaven** [反天之罪]. The **Saintly Sovereign’s decree** will surely demote you in the **Daoist ranks** [仙品]. This method was granted only to those of sincere intent.

If there is a fire disaster, you may use it to save people’s homes and those in peril from fire. Spread open, perform the **Yu Step** three times, expand to the **Three Wilds** six times, and to the **Six Wilds** nine times. Walking the circuit will cause rain to fall across the **Nine Heavens**, even a thousand *li* away.

The **Four Directions’ Dragon Gods** will race through the clouds, bringing rain to save a certain household or family from fire disaster."
*A note: This refers to Emperor Wu’s subject Le Ba, who, after serving wine to the emperor, bowed and, facing southwest, spat and summoned rain to save his own home and relatives from fire.*

「When the **Saintly Sovereign** [后帝] first perceives the **Way’s** [道] **spiritual protection** [仙品], its efficacy is undeniable—it must be a **Daoist adept** [神仙] who guards the **Way** [道]. Such a one should be revered in the annals of history.

The incantation reads:
*"The essence of the **Morning Star** [辰星], condensed into watery form.*
*When flames erupt suddenly, invoke the **water’s spirit** [水之灵].*
*Dissipate its shape and unleash its spirit—rain will fill the heavens.*
*The spirit ascends into the **Dark and Mysterious** [冥晦], and the **Dragon** [龙] exhales it to act.*

*Fivefold torrents [霶霪] in all seasons shall quench that calamity.*
*Swiftly, as the **Law of the Dao** [律令] decrees."*

*A note: Master Wang [王真人] stated: "This method must not be recklessly practiced. It should only be employed to save one’s family or aid others."*

---

**The Four Seas and Five Phases [五行] Incantation** [六纪]
Beneath the **Five Phases** [五行], the **Six Divisions** [六纪] arise.

The **Venerable Lord Lao** [老君] instructed **Great Yu** [大禹]:
*"You govern the waters—on the days of **Jiazi** [甲子], write the names of the **Four Seas’ Gods** [四海之神名] in vermilion on thin paper."*

*A note: The names of the Four Seas’ Gods are as follows:
The **East Sea God** [东海神] is **Preli Ni** [颇利尼],
the **South Sea God** [南海神] is **Dazhe Jia** [大遮迦],
the **West Sea God** [西海神] is **Huo Luo Wen** [和罗问],
and the **North Sea God** [北海神] is **Wen Ji Jian** [文季间].
These names were newly inscribed by the winds [各风新注], not previously recorded.*

After dawn rituals and practice, swallow the paper. When three years’ merit is fulfilled, the waters will obey as if by earth’s command—unblocking rivers and opening seas. The **Sea Gods** [海之神水官], the **Four Seas’ Great Gods** [四海大神], will appear at your summons.

To command them to unblock rivers and open seas, recite the **Four Seas’ Incantation** [四海诀], and their **Three Steps and Nine Marks** [三步九迹] will manifest. Call their names, and they will arrive instantly—dispatch them swiftly. Their dominion extends beyond the Four Seas, encompassing both land and sea.

If you request rain, it will come in moments.

After five years, follow the same method to invoke the **Ghost King Incantation** [鬼王诀].*
*A note: The incantation is inscribed on the second joint of the left hand’s second finger [左手第二指第二节中].*

*The **Great Ghost Marshal** [大鬼帅] of the North, **Pishamen** [毗沙门神], will appear. Command him to aid the nation in its affairs."*

This is used when subduing rebellions in certain lands or against bandits, or against the **Tibetan and Western barbarians** [吐蕃西戎]. All such cases employ this method.

Additionally, one may inscribe the **Ghost King Incantation** [鬼王诀] with vermilion or black ink, empowering it to traverse **Heaven and Earth**, enter **fire, water, or armies**—all as desired. The **Ghost Kings** of the **Four Directions** [四方] are governed by this **Incantation’s Master** [管主], who submits to the **Morning Star’s Sovereign Lord** [辰星太皇君].

Practitioners need only walk the **Five Stars** [五星].*
*A note: The **true Five Stars Diagram** [真五星图] is found in the *Scripture of the Flying Step* [《飞步经》]. Use the Five Stars Diagram for practice.*

*The **Five Phases** [五行].*
*A note: This refers to transforming the **Five Stars Diagram** [五星图] into the **Five Phases** [五行], following the sequence: **Metal** [金], **Water** [水], **Wood** [木], **Fire** [火], **Earth** [土].*

Begin with **Metal** [金], moving leftward. Upon completion, you reach **Water** [水].*
*A note: From **Metal** [金], enter **Fire** [火], then **Earth** [土], then **Wood** [木], and finally **Water** [水].*

For the **Five Phases** [五行], begin with **Wood** [木], moving rightward. Upon completion, you reach **Water** [水] again.*
*A note: From **Wood** [木], enter **Fire** [火], then **Metal** [金], then **Earth** [土], and finally **Water** [水].*

Each step must be **tread upon** [蹑],*
*A note: Tread upon the **Five Stars** [五星], then walk the **Five Phases** [五行].*

four times. Upon finishing, step outside the diagram’s bounds and perform the **Yu Step** [禹步] four more times.

Thus, the **Four Gate Gods** [四门神] will aid the nation in its campaigns.

When armies march across **rivers, lakes, mountains, and valleys**, all trees will bloom with **thunderous winds and rain**, and obstacles will be removed, transformed, or altered.*
*A note: **Transformation** [变改] refers to rivers and lakes being blocked or cleared, mountains and valleys being opened like rivers and streams, and trees being uprooted or snapped.*

This method can also grant one the **essentials of longevity and eternal life** [长生久视].

When flames first ignite, the **worldly fire** [世火] is the **Mangon Star** [荧惑星], dispersing **vital essence** [炁], a **portent** [征].

**Portent** [征] is the **Celestial Sovereign** [天皇], surnamed **Zheng** [姓征].
The remaining **vital essence** [炁] becomes **copper-red stone** [铜赤石].

The **Celestial Sovereign** [天皇] strikes the stone to ignite fire, while **Suiren** [燧人] drills wood to kindle it—thus fire is born.

Fire originates from the **Celestial Sovereign** [天皇] and **Suiren** [燧人], and from this point, **fire and water** [火水] transform **raw into cooked** [生为熟], fulfilling fire’s function—another **portent** [征].*
*A note: **Portent** [征] here refers to humanity [人]. It is the child of the **Mangon Star** [荧惑星], bearing the surname **Zheng** [姓征].*

This **Celestial Sovereign** [天皇] intermarried with the **Earthly Sovereign’s descendants** [宫姓之土子], producing three sons.

The eldest son changed his surname to **Li** [理], and later, the **Saintly Sovereign of the Later Han** [后圣李君] adopted the surname **Li** [李].
The second son bore the surname **Ji** [纪], branching into the surnames **Dai** [戴] and **Zheng** [郑], among others, totaling **thirty-nine surnames** [三十九姓].
Among the **Five Correct Surnames** [正五姓], only those of **Fire** [火] and **Metal** [金] lineages are suitable for refining **elixirs** [丹药].

When their **virtue/power** [德] is cultivated, they will surely achieve **longevity** [延驻].
With **longevity**, the **Great Elixir** [大丹药] will be perfected.

The **Venerable Lord Lao’s** [太上老君] **Inner Transmission Master** [内传], **Guangchengzi** [广成子], was surnamed **Li** [理].
The scripture states: *"Guangchengzi is the **Venerable Lord Lao’s** [老君] incarnate form. If one follows the surname **Li** [理], it is one body, continuously manifesting as rulers or ministers in each generation."*

To refine the **Golden Elixir** [金丹], one may take **golden liquid** [金液] and undergo **ninefold refining** [九炼].
Alternatively, refine **golden stone** [金石], **mercury** [水银], **lead** [铅], **cinnabar** [朱砂], or **malachite** [曾青], among others, into the **Great Dragon-Tiger Elixir** [龙虎大丹], which will be completed in nine years.

When the emperor consumes it, his **vital essence** [气] will gradually stabilize, his strength will grow, and he will tirelessly march a hundred *li* daily.

Later, he will **follow the Celestial Pattern and Earthly Divisions** [履蹑天纲地纪], forming the **heart seal** [心印] beneath the nail of the left thumb [左手大指甲下], and storing it with the right hand [右手就之存之].

All such practices should be conducted on the **third, thirteenth, and twenty-third days of the eighth month** [八月三日、十三日、二十三日], seated as per the diagram.

Alternatively, one may stand while holding the **diagram of the Encompassing Whole** [含弘图].
The diagram should be hung with both hands lowered—this is **concealment** [隐].
Simply retain it in mind as the **Encompassing Whole** [含弘], whether standing or seated, as one’s intention dictates.

The **Venerable Lord Lao** [太上老君], the **Empty Celestial Sovereign** [虚皇上帝], instructed **Yuanming Shangzhenren** [元明上真人] to teach the **heart seal’s seated and standing methods** [结心印坐立总行].

The **Yellow Emperor** [黄帝] originally drew the **Encompassing Whole** [弘一] for seated and standing practice, but later generations need only cultivate **one diagram** [一图].

The three sons each had three descendants, hence the **ninefold lineage** [三三九人].

They married within the **Jue Palace** [角宫], and their descendants flourished. Among them arose those of the **Five Phases** [五行], and at their deaths, they all ascended to the heavens **riding clouds and dragons** [乘云驾龙].

The **lineage perpetually transmits the Dao’s teachings**, with the **Cloud-Fire clan** [云火姓]—
*Note: "Clan" here denotes lineage affiliation; Cloud-Fire is the lineage of Fire.*

—**aligned with Fire’s mandate** [与火命].
*Note: Human life is inherently linked to Fire, hence also aligned with Fire’s mandate.*

They **greatly fear Water** [甚畏水].
*Note: Why does Fire fear Water? Because Water extinguishes Fire.*

All other clans are said to **mutually subdue** [相克], but Water and Fire **mutually extinguish** [相灭], hence their profound fear.

They **preserve the *Jiji* Diagram** [存蹑纪图] on the **four seasonal days** [四季日]—
**Chen, Xū, Chǒu, Wèi** [辰戌丑未]—

in accordance with **inversion, reversal, and the three transformations** [顺倒反三等].

Upon completion, they **walk three circuits** [散步三匝].

Then, they **stand before the *Diji* Seven Stars Diagram** [存地纪七星图处前], adopt the **Yǔ Step** [变作禹步], and **point to the Water Star** [指水星]—
*Note: The stars are preserved as well; just as the Five Stars Diagram represents five stars, this is the same.*

—**twisting the Water Talisman** [捻水诀].

Upon completion, they **point to the Earth Star** [次指土星] and **twist the Earth Talisman** [捻土诀].

Then, they **recite the incantation**:

*"The Five Phases mutually propel,
Metal and Wood mutually subdue,
Water and Fire mutually extinguish,
And so forth."*

*Note: This incantation is found in the *Liúzhū* [《流珠》].*

If one performs this **three times within a month** [三度为之],
and since a month has **three decans** [三旬], each decan contains the **four seasonal days** [四季],
then practicing it daily throughout the year **ensures a life free from calamity, misfortune, or illness** [一生无灾厄疾患].

The *Liúzhū* and *Fēibù Tiāngāi Jīng* [《飞步天纲经》] state:
*"A year free from calamity—this is precisely it."*

**In truth, those who adhere to this talisman shall never fail to attain immortality** [实但依此言，无有不得仙之者].
If one follows the *Shǒuwén Jīng*’s teachings [手文经说修行] instead, **not one in ten thousand shall succeed** [万无一成].

Thus, this talisman is **recorded for those whose will and resolve are upright and sincere** [志修志信直心之人].
It is to be **passed down only to such individuals** [可一一传付].

The talisman is **transmitted orally** [诀以口传], with each generation **faithfully receiving and reciting it** [继代相付勑祝].

**Only the worthy may pass it on**; for the unworthy, **not even a billion ounces of gold and jade could justify transmission** [非人者万亿金玉不传].

If no worthy disciple arises to transmit it, it is **sealed on the Sacred Mountain** [封於灵山].
If even that fails, **burn the talisman and let the water flow to the Heavenly Treasure** [火烧水流天宝].

**After two years**, one is **free from military strife** [辟兵].
*Note: Practicing for two years allows the Five Phases to manifest, thus warding off the Five Armies of calamity.*

The **Sage Emperor** [后圣君] told the **Celestial Master** [天师]:
*"You may become an Immortal King.
When the Five Phases converge, you shall be able to **strengthen one through all five** [强一].
The **Upper Elemental Lord** [上元主天], who governs the **Heavenly Step Talisman** [飞步天纲],
the **Middle Elemental Lord** [中元主人], who governs the **Yǔ Step** [演禹步],
and the **Lower Elemental Lord** [下元主水地], who governs **Treading the Earth** [蹑地],

are all **aligned with the Northern Dipper** [北斗星], hence the name **Earth-Water** [地水].
Together, they **subdue the Water Regions** [俱镇水乡].

**For those who cultivate immortality with sincere resolve** [志心学仙],
to **abandon the immortality-treading talisman** [去仙履地水] is to **practice the Lower Elemental method** [即今蹑地纪图顺倒反],

which is the **Yǔ Step** [即为禹步], **three steps and nine traces** [三步九迹], known as the **Middle Water Elemental** [谓中水元].

To **master the Heavenly Step Talisman** [履天纲] and **fly with nine traces** [飞行九迹] is called the **Upper Elemental** [谓之上元].

This doctrine of the **three methods** [此说三者] is to **record the Three Souls** [以录三魂] and **restrain the Three Officials** [制止三官].
The Five refers to the **Five Phases** [五行], as explained above.

**After three years**, one attains **divine communication** [通神] and the **path of non-death** [不死之道], whether standing or seated.

**After nine years**, one may **enter Water, enter Fire, enter Stone, enter Wood, enter the Sun and Moon without obstruction** [入水入火，入石入木，入日月，无碍也].

The **Venerable Lord Lao** [太上老君] bestowed the **Fire Phase Talisman** [火行符], which the **Three Celestial Mandate Lords** [三天司命君] wear to **ward off Water’s harm to life** [辟水害命水官].
It is **worn on the head** [戴安头上],
*Note: Some say it should be worn long-term; others say it should be inscribed on the day of one’s birth or the Water Day, ensuring lasting protection from calamities.*

—**to dispel Water’s harm to *qi*** [去水害炁].

The **Fire Phase Talisman** [火行符]—
*Note: The first talisman of the Fire Phase, carried by Fire-Mandate individuals to ward off Water calamities.*

—**the Sage Emperor** [后圣君] said:
*"The talismans of the earlier sages to subdue the Water Mandate Officials were all in written form* [告命水官符，皆是文字].
I now **explain the Fire Phase Talisman** [解火行一符],
*Note: Some say "now reveal."*
and the **four subsequent talismans follow the same principle** [后四符同].
The **Venerable Lord Lao’s talisman** [太上符] is used to **steam the Earth and block Water’s calamities** [火行蒸土，塞水害灾是也]."

The **Wood Phase Talisman** [木行符]—
*Note: The second Fire Phase talisman, worn by Wood-Mandate individuals to ward off Metal’s harm to *qi*.*

The **Metal Phase Talisman** [金行符]—
*Note: The third Fire Phase talisman, worn by Metal-Mandate individuals to ward off Fire’s harm to *qi*.*

The **Water Phase Talisman** [水行符]—
*Note: The fourth Fire Phase talisman, worn by Water-Mandate individuals to ward off Earth’s harm to *qi*.*

The **Earth Phase Talisman** [土行符]—
*Note: The fifth Fire Phase talisman, worn by Earth-Mandate individuals to ward off Wood’s harm to *qi*.*

The **Venerable Lord Lao instructed the Mandate Lord Hàn** [老君告司命韩君]—
*Note: Named "Xìn Xiàngshàng," Hàn Xìn was the Mandate Lord during the Yellow Emperor’s era, not the Han Dynasty’s Hàn Xìn.*

—**Hàn Xìn of old**, who was **faithful to the Celestial** [上古信上], and served as the **Three Celestial Mandate Lords** [三天司命].
In the **Han Dynasty**, he was the **Mandate Lord overseeing the regions of Qi, Chu, Yan, and Qin** [信汉将].
*Note: After the death of later heroes, Hàn Xìn became the Mandate Lord for the Han general.*

*"Within the Five Phases**, two phases favor life and completion** [二行好人生成].
The **Eastern Nine *Qi*** [东方九炁] **govern life’s flourishing** [主好生].
The **Southern Three *Qi*** [南方三炁] **govern completion’s success** [主好成].

Now, the **Great Dao’s teachings** [大道之教] **emphasize life and completion** [以重生成].
The **teachings of the Netherworld** [阴鬼之教] **prioritize repose and decay** [以重休废].
*Note: The Netherworld is also called the Earth Teachings.*

**Repose and decay belong to Yin** [休废属阴].
*Note: Yin is anciently termed the Earth Teachings.*

In the **recent Zhou Dynasty**, the **Western lands produced the Hu deities** [西国出胡神], with the surname **Shì** [姓释], titled **Fó** [号佛], and called the **World-Honored One** [称世尊].
They **prospered the Yin teachings**, instructing people in **dragon ghosts** [教人龙鬼].
Chinese **scholars named this the Yin Teachings** [中国名儒以号阴教].

Those who **master the teachings of dragon ghosts** [通人龙鬼之教] **are skilled at encouraging virtuous conduct and sincere resolve** [甚能劝善行心],
and their talismans **share the same efficacy as the Dao’s** [诀与道同].
Yet, they **do not advocate early transcendence and early birth** [不合令劝人早化早生],
for such views **prioritize repose and decay without merit** [如此之见，以重休废不虚].
Thus, they **do not surpass the Great Dao’s emphasis on life and completion** [即不似重生成之义而为大].

The **teachings of the Yang Deities** [阳神之教] **prioritize life and completion** [以重生成], which belong to **Yang** [生成属阳].
*Note: Yang is anciently termed the Heaven Teachings, with no distinct name.*

In the **era of the Three Sovereigns** [三皇之世], the **multitude of deities had no names** [众尊无名], and their teachings were **equal and strong** [平等之教].
However, the **Yellow Emperor’s time**, the **Emperor valued the Great Strength** [帝重大强], and its name **seemed inconsistent with the Great Dao’s laws** [其名似不合大道之教律],
so it was **renamed the Heavenly Dao** [改名曰天道].

In the **era of Yǔ’s succession** [近禹代之时], the **proper name was restored** [而取正名],
and it became the **Supreme Great Dao** [曰太上大道也].

**Yin is likened to the moon** [阴与月为喻],
*Note: The moon symbolizes thirty days, with fifteen days representing fullness and fifteen days representing gradual waning,*
to signify **that life’s mandate is not long-lasting** [喻命不用久长].

**Yang is likened to the sun** [阳以日为言],
to signify **long life and enduring vision** [言长生久视].
Thus, **Yin and Yang in their seasons** [阴阳二时],
**practice Wood and Fire for life and completion** [行木火好生成].
This is the **first and second principle** [是一二义].

**Practice Metal and Water for repose and decay** [行金水好休废].
This is the **first principle** [是一义].

**Another principle is to follow auspicious and inauspicious patterns** [又一行顺吉凶].

「**Note:** Thus, Earth follows auspiciousness, yet also follows inauspiciousness.
Hence it is said that the Sage-King follows both auspicious and inauspicious patterns—or follows inauspiciousness.

My teaching, though likened to the origin of Yin and Yang,
returns to the **qi of Yin and Yang**,
abandoning the paths of auspiciousness and inauspiciousness,
treading the **Lunar Steps** and **Starry Paths**,
ascending to the **Celestial Immortal Gate**.

Later, the **Sage-Sovereign** instructed **Yinxi the True Person**:
*"The **Supreme Void Emperor** transmitted the **Five-Phase Talisman** to the one of Fire.
Fire belongs to the summer’s heat,
able to nurture and complete all things,
and also to refine through fire, dispelling calamities and dust.
**Note:** Gold and silver refine away the taint of dust to reveal their luster;
fire refines away misfortune and affliction to reveal vitality—
thus, fire’s hundred virtues are recorded, and the **Fire Phase** is inscribed.

What was transmitted was the **Fire Phase**.

The **Supreme Dao-Sovereign** told **Laozi**:
*"What Phase did you command?"*
Laozi replied:
*"I commanded the Phase of Wood."*
The Dao-Sovereign said:
*"I commanded the Phase of Fire."*
We both have emerged from Water and Fire,
and thus have no worries.
**Note:** These two Most High True Ones, with their bodies transcending the Five Phases,
have no term of decay or ruin—hence the saying.

Yet the lower True Ones of the Immortal Way struggle to depart from Water and Fire.
Though their bodies may linger, they do not exceed a thousand years.
Water and Fire cycle endlessly, with decay and suffering ever in attendance—
self-destruction and slaughter are inevitable unless the Dao intervenes.
Thus, the two Most High Teachers discussed Water and Fire.

Later, the **Sage-Sovereign** told the **Celestial Master**:
*"I have heard that the two Most High True Ones of Ultimate Reality discussed Water and Fire—why?"*
Because among the Five Phases,
Water and Fire **clash destructively**,
bringing countless illnesses, afflictions, and failures,
and even shatter Heaven and Earth.
How much more so for the human body,
which lacks an unbreakable form!

Moreover, the **Fire Star** and the **wandering Mars**,
suddenly dispersing into **Yang qi**,
become **Fire’s destructive poison**.
The great wind blows the Water,
and the **Water’s Star of Chen** suddenly disperses into **Yin qi**,
becoming **thunder and rain**—
both move in assault, striking and conquering each other,
thus creating **Heaven’s affliction**.
Suffering this **howling wind and violent storm**,
Heaven is struck by falling stars and shattered rocks,
Earth by snapped trees and crumbling mountains,
and humanity by ruined dwellings and lost lives.
This afflicts the **Three Realms**—
hence the Most High True Ones’ intent in their discourse,
desiring that the lower True Ones of the Immortal Way
receive these words within their hearts.
The heart must not suffer Water and Fire’s calamities and ruin,
nor must the body and mind fail to attain **transcendence**—
to transcend the Five Phases’ paths,
seeking the **Three Pure Ones’ essence**.
The nature of Water and Fire, when natural, is without worry,
unaffected by Water and Fire’s disasters and misfortunes.

Thus, the three Most High Saints of old
used the analogy of Water and Fire
to admonish the lower True Ones of the Immortal Way,
so that they might transcend Water and Fire’s calamities,
enter the **effortless nature**,
and naturally attain True Reality.
Their **Dao-bodies** become firm and pure,
cleansing Heaven and Earth.

As for the body,
refer to the previous notes.»

「This also brings worry to mortals.
*(Also, refer to the previous notes.)*
You are the teacher of humanity and Heaven—
thus, you may transmit the **Water and Fire talismans**,
to guide the lower True Ones into the ranks of the Immortals,
and help them escape the **Water and Fire afflictions**.

**Note:** Those who cultivate the Way with sincere resolve,
all lack the Water and Fire **Dao-nature**,
dwelling in mountains and forests,
devoting their utmost sincerity and resolve,
burning incense and reciting scriptures without cease.
Some refine gold and stones, ingesting their elixirs,
others practice **shell-breaking** and **breath-work** (*xūqì* 服炁).
These ranks of practitioners,
through years of earnest Dao-cultivation,
remain trapped in Water and Fire’s afflictions,
succumbing to decay, aging, and death,
yet gain nothing—at most.

The **Most High Dao Lord** (*Tàishàng Dàojūn*) commands **Laozi**,
who teaches those of steadfast resolve
to escape the Water and Fire afflictions within the body,
and the Water and Fire calamities of the Five Phases,
thus bestowing the **Five Star Talismans** from the *Líu Zhū* (*Flowing Pearl*) scripture,
and issuing this book,
along with the **Later Saints’** talismans passed down by the **Celestial Master** (*Tiānshī*),
the **Three Five** (*Sānwǔ*) *Líu Zhū* scriptures,
and the **Most High Three Five Orthodoxy Talismans** (*Tàishàng Sānwǔ Zhèngyī Fúluò*),
the **Eighty-One Stages**,
to safeguard body and home,
and avert Water and Fire disasters.

**First Water Talisman.**
**Note:** The talisman is within the *Língbǎo Wǔ Fú* (*Soul Treasures Five Talismans*).
The great one declares:
*"This is the talisman of the Northern Emperor,
written in black ink,
to be worn upon the back."*
The Five Phases’ **master talisman**,
which **Laozi** bestowed upon **Yellow Emperor** (*Huángdì*),
is the true original.
**Yǔ**’s version from **Jīngshān** (*荆山*) and his later cultivation
is a lesser copy—
not personally inscribed by **Laozi**.
It is somewhat similar,
yet not as efficacious as the great original.

**Second Fire Talisman.**
**Note:** These two talismans appear together in the *Five Talismans*—
this one is not further detailed here.
**Laozi** instructed **True Lord of the Southern Pole** (*Nánjí Zhēngōng*):
*"How old are you?"*
The True Lord replied:
*"I am one hundred and seventeen years old.
When I must walk, I walk;
when I must run, I run.
My **qi-force** does not wane,
and my hair, once white, will never darken again."*
**Laozi** said:
*"White hair is trivial—
your body has yet to escape Water and Fire’s afflictions."*
The True Lord pondered this for a long time,
then realized its meaning.
He prostrated himself twice,
begging:
*"I humbly implore the Most High’s boundless compassion
to save my withered bones,
granting me the path of eternal life.
Moreover, I have always heeded your teachings,
yet you say my body has not escaped Water and Fire’s calamities—
how then can I attain the rank of the Immortals?
I do not know how to escape Water and Fire’s afflictions.
These Water and Fire afflictions are called **‘years of ruin’** (*huài jié* 坏劫),
and yet, what specific year will they arrive?"*

**Laozi** laughed for a long time,
then spoke:
*"The Water and Fire ruin—
that is your body.
If your body does not escape Water and Fire,
then all will be destroyed and ruined—
thus, it is called **‘ruin of the years’** (*huài jié*).
The heavens and earth have no set time for collapse.
Now, I reveal the **meaning and talismanic key** of Water and Fire.
This scroll contains them.
After nine years of practice,
the Dao will be perfected,
and you shall become the **True Lord of the Southern Pole**—
**Zhèng Rén’ān** (*郑仁安*), whose given name is **Zǐ Zāi** (*郑子崎*).
The *Běnxíng Jīng* (*Scripture of Original Conduct*) states:
*"The **Red Emperor of the South** (*Chìdì* 赤帝) is **Zhèng Rén’ān**."*
Even now, he still wears these two talismans,
along with the *Five Talismans* belt.

**Third Talismans of Metal, Wood, and Earth.**
**Note:** These three talismans
are worn by those of earnest resolve
according to the seasons,
and used in morning rituals.
They are also observed on **natal days**, **Gēngshēn days** (*庚申*), and **Jiǎzǐ days** (*甲子*).
On other days, they are not worn—
these are called the **Five Phases Talismans**.
For those practicing Water and Fire,
these talismans are always worn on the head,
never removed,
and changed every two years.
All are inscribed by the **original teacher**,
each bearing a specific date.
The **Later Saints’** talismans instructed **Yīn Xiānsheng** (*尹先生*):
*"The Five Talismans of the *Soul Treasures* are inscribed on different days.
The **eastern green talisman** (*Qīngfú* 青符) is written on **Spring Begins** (*Lìchūn* 立春),
requested from the original teacher,
and worn on the back of the left elbow.
The **southern red talisman** (*Chìfú* 赤符) is written on **Summer Begins** (*Lìxià* 立夏).
The **western white talisman** (*Báifú* 白符) is written on **Autumn Begins** (*Lìqiū* 立秋).
The **northern black talisman** (*Hēifú* 黑符) is written on **Winter Begins** (*Lìdōng* 立冬).
The **central yellow talisman** (*Huángfú* 黄符) is written on **Winter Solstice** (*Dōngzhì* 冬至).
And on **Pure Brightness Day** (*Qīngmíng* 清明) in spring,
and **Duanwu Day** (*Duānwǔ* 端午) in summer,
each is written on the day corresponding to the seasonal **pure qi** (*zhèngqì* 正气).
If one cannot adhere to the seasonal **rectification of qi** (*zhèngqì* 正气) days,
then on the **fifth of the fifth month** (*Wǔyuè wǔ* 五月五),
**ninth of the ninth month** (*Jiǔyuè jiǔ* 九月九),
or **tenth of the tenth month** (*Shíyuè shí* 十月十).
These three months’ days are also acceptable.
When writing these talismans,
the **original teacher** must inscribe them
in a state of purity,
after fasting and abstaining,
and at **midday** (*shízhōng* 日中),
before bestowing them upon the disciple,
who should then wear them.
The **wood talisman** is worn on the back of the left elbow,
the **fire talisman** on the head,
the **metal talisman** on the back of the right elbow,
the **water talisman** around the waist,
and the **earth talisman** upon the back.
For the **Five Talismans** above,
each must be stored in a **silken pouch** (*jǐnchuāi* 锦袋).
One inscription lasts five years.
If there is no original teacher,
or if the teacher is elderly and unable to inscribe,
then a **worthy disciple** (*bǎojǔ shī* 保举师) should write them.
If none is found,
then a **high-ranking adept** (*fǎluò gāozǔ* 法箓高三五足) from the assembly may inscribe.
When obtaining such a person’s name,
the **Five Phases’ keys** are revealed.
Do not recklessly practice—
let not one who cannot receive **efficacious qi** (*língqì* 灵炁) inscribe them,
nor one who knows not their meaning.
The **Five Stars and Five Emperors** will not submit to such.
Each must be inscribed by the original teacher,
on the days of the **Five Laws and Five Talismans**,
as with the **talismanic scriptures** (*luò* 箓),
and each must be transmitted to disciples who chant and recite,
teaching them the **method of enlightenment** (*míngdù fǎ* 明度法).
If the teacher does not know the **Five Laws** as the **keys to escaping the Five Phases**,
nor the **efficacious texts** (*língwén* 灵文) that avert great and small calamities,
then they should not separately inscribe the talismans along with the transmission.
Instead, from **Spring Begins** onward,
*(as noted previously)*
request a **clear teacher** (*míngshī* 明师) to inscribe them,
and wear them according to the seasons.
If fearing that the Five Phases’ calamities may approach,
then inscribe them on a **auspicious day** (*jí rì* 吉日),
or on **Duanwu Day** (*Wǔyuè wǔ* 五月五) or **Chóngyáng Day** (*Jiǔyuè jiǔ* 九月九)—
these two days are **‘days of extending life and dispelling calamities’** (*xùmìng xiāozāi* 续命消灾),
and thus are acceptable.

**Guāngchéng Jūn** inscribed the Water and Fire talismans
on **Duanwu Day** (*Wǔyuè wǔ* 五月五),
and at midday bestowed them upon **Yellow Emperor** (*Huángdì*).
**Yellow Emperor** then prostrated himself twice and asked:
*"First, you dispelled Water and Fire—
then, how do you escape the Five Phases?"*
**Note:** Though the **true Immortals of the Most High Way** possess
**spiritual mobility and freedom** (*shén tōng zìrán* 神通自在),
their bodies have yet to escape Water and Fire.
Though their hearts have escaped Water and Fire’s afflictions,
their bodies remain trapped within them.

The body and mind both transcend Heaven and Earth, yet Water and Fire remain unvanquished.

When speaking of the calamities of Water and Fire, those whose body and mind both transcend Heaven and Earth—meaning they have escaped Water and Fire, departed the Three Realms—are called **Middle True Great Immortals**. The Three Realms are Metal, Wood, and Earth.

Metal: The vulgar scholars, following the Buddha’s teachings, liken Metal to precious gems, jade, and treasures that do not attract women or music—unaffected by them.

Earth: The vulgar scholars liken Earth to official rank, honor, wealth, and the arrogance of territorial rule—unaffected by them.

Wood: The vulgar scholars interpret Wood as not sitting in pavilions, halls, or lofty structures, with no attachments of the heart—this is called the mind transcending the Three Realms. This, according to Daoist classification, is called the mind transcending, yet the body has not yet transcended.

When the body fails, the next life’s body will again suffer the afflictions of honor and nobility—still within the Three Realms, governed by the Five Phases—this is called the body not transcending the Five Phases.

I have grasped the essence of the **Middle True**, dispelling Water and Fire calamities, transcending the Five Phases, surpassing the Three Realms, and dwelling with body and mind intact, traversing Heaven, Earth, Water, and Fire without harm.

Wearing the talisman for one year dispels the Five Sorrows and Nine Calamities.
For two years, one can repel all poisons and subdue the Five Armies.
For three years, one avoids death and rebirth.
For four years, one receives a worldly appointment—named **Book of the Jade Capital**.
For five years, one escapes Water and Fire.
**Note:** To depart from their afflictions is to no longer consume the *qi* of Water and Fire; their *qi* cannot harm those who wear the talisman.

**Laozi, the Most High Venerable, told Mr. Yin:**
*"Wearing the Water and Fire talismans for five years renders Water and Fire powerless to harm.
Wearing the Metal, Wood, and Earth talismans renders Metal unable to conquer, Wood unable to harm, and Earth unable to injure. The Five Phases depart from the body, making it firm and enduring—long-lived, yet not attaining the rank of the lower-grade Immortals."*

In six and seven years, one gradually attains wondrous powers.
At forty-nine years, one ascends in broad daylight.
**Note:** The Five Phases’ ultimate subtlety lies in Water and Fire, which govern life, growth, sickness, and decay.

**Laozi told the Great True Ones:**
*"The characters Water and Fire are not merely feared by beings of the lower realms for their power over success and failure.
**Note:** Because humans have fate and rely on water for sustenance, escaping creation and avoiding decay is difficult—that is why they are feared.

Even the highest True Immortals, in their constant practice, still employ talismanic steps to avoid their original fate.
**Note:** *Fate* refers to one’s destiny.
The Dao Lord was born in the *yin* hour of the Fire Phase, always using the *bing* hour of the Water Phase to manipulate Water talismans, then the Fire talismans, to seek longevity. How much more so for worldly folk, who do not seek immortality, yet must observe their natal day’s talismans.

The natal day’s Earth Phase rises first; the worldly Earth corresponds to the *Zhen* star, dispersing *qi* from the Earthly Palace.
**Note:** *Palace* refers to **Di Huang** (地皇).
Surname: Palace; given name: Wind.
Di Huang ruled with Earth’s virtue, piling earth to form platforms, erecting stone pillars, and digging earthen chambers.
**Note:** High earthen mounds were built, over a hundred *zhang* tall, with four-directional cavities as palatial dwellings. These cavities were called the Palace surname.

Why is the character *Palace* (宮) written with a doubled mouth radical?
Because palaces were built of earth, with layered towers, and chambers dug to shelter people—*Palace* (宮) carries the meaning of layered accumulation, hence the doubled mouth radical. Over time, the upper layers collapsed, damaging the lower ones.

The **Human Sovereign** observed this, knowing that the upper collapse and lower damage of the Palace chambers were written as *harm* (害), resembling *Palace* (宮), thus depicting the destructive force of collapse. The lower mouth radical signifies the upper overcoming the lower.

Thus, the character *harm* (害) spread in the world, corresponding to the Earth star, bringing destructive *qi* that injures and kills people.

A large chamber is called a *Palace*, and Palace became a surname.
Today, those with the Palace surname are honored, reflecting Di Huang’s intention to elevate humanity—thus, the Earth surname is revered as the first of the Five Phases.

They intermarried with the Zheng surname, producing six sons.
The eldest changed his surname to Wind, the second to Gong, the third to Worker, the fourth, fifth, and sixth retained the Palace surname.

When the Zheng wife died, he again intermarried with a Shang surname descendant, producing another six sons.
The eldest changed his surname to Gongsun, the second to Li, the third to Fei,
**Note:** Today’s surnames Zhan and Ren are derived from this.
the fourth, fifth, and sixth retained the Palace surname.

Moreover, Di Huang had twelve sons, taking the abundant *qi* of Earth.
He intermarried with the five surnames, and their descendants became kings, mirroring the Earth star’s retrograde cycle through the four seasons.
Thus, Earth’s sovereign rule over the four seasons was established.
The Earth’s harmful *qi* constantly circulates through the seasons, and those whose fate aligns with it suffer illness within ten days.
Those who know this manipulate Wood talismans, step the Wood Array,
**Note:** The Eastern Host of Seven Stars is the Wood Array.
to disperse it and halt the affliction.
Thus, Earth fears Wood, for Wood can conquer Earth.
Earth constantly supports Wood, yet Wood fears it in return.

Practitioners with an Earth destiny should manipulate Metal talismans to stop Wood calamities.
Those with a Wood destiny should manipulate Fire talismans to stop Metal.
Those with a Metal destiny should manipulate Water talismans to stop Fire.
Those with a Fire destiny should manipulate Earth talismans to stop Water.
Those with a Water destiny should manipulate Wood talismans to stop Earth.

Thus, within the Five Phases, the Earth Phase harbors the most destructive *qi*.
All Five Phases’ mutual generation and conquest are subsumed within Earth’s influence.
Moreover, the Earth star completes a cycle every thirty-five years, governing the Nine Regions and the Five Phases.

Among the Five Tones, *Gong* (宮) is primary.
If following the *Fei* Step Talisman’s teachings, then Metal is primary.
The two accounts differ.
**Note:** According to the *San Cai Lun* (三才论), Heaven, Earth, and Human are called the Three Powers.

From the moment Heaven arises, Earth immediately follows.
Earth is established, and then **Earth Phase** is born from Earth.
The Earth that comes before is **Metal**, and Earth produces Metal—so Metal is primary.

According to *Master Yin’s Record* (《尹先生记》), the *Divine Record of All Spirits* (《神灵具录》) states:
The **Venerable Laozi’s** mother was of **Metal destiny**, and from her arose the **Venerable Laozi**.
The **Venerable Laozi** then ascended and took the position of **Posterior Sage Celestial Sovereign** (后圣天尊).
Thus, when he proclaimed the talisman to the **Three Officials of the Northern Dipper** (命三官北斗咒),
he said: *"Metal, Water, Fire, Wood, Earth—
the Way’s principles never stray from their natural connections.*
All Five Phases are means of generation,
yet they dwell upon Earth.
The **Posterior Sage Sovereign** takes Metal as primary."

For Earth is the **longest of the Three Realms** (三界).
The **Venerable Laozi** declared to all **Imperial Sovereigns** (帝君):
*"I often ponder the **Lower Truth** and **Upper Immortals** (下真上仙),
those who seek the Dao without departing the Three Realms.
How can they attain imperishability and non-extinction?
You have mastered the Three Realms—
why not awaken and guide those who remain unenlightened,
so they may forever transcend and escape the Three Realms,
unobstructed by **demonic thieves** (魔贼).
Beyond the Three Realms lies the **Three Pure Ones** (三清),
where the **Supreme Truth** (至真) resides.
Is this not the **palace of compassionate efficacy** (慈力济度之功),
the **peerless virtue** (无上之德) of the body?"*

Fire is the **male of the Three Realms** (三界之男人).
Without Fire, one’s destiny is incomplete.
Thus, one must borrow **qi** to refine it,
nurturing the **vital roots** (身根) for longevity’s pulse.

Water is the **consort of the Three Realms** (三界之妻).
Without Water, humans perish;
with Water, humans live.
Life and death both depend on Water,
which nourishes all things—
how much more so the human body alone?

The **Posterior Sage Sovereign**’s talisman commands the **Three Realms’ Destructive King** (命三界魔王):
*"Your domain encompasses the Three Realms—
all beings and figures return to you.
Without the Three Realms, nothing is born;
without the Three Realms, nothing is nurtured;
without the Three Realms, nothing grows.
From birth to death, they cycle endlessly,
yet none know how to return.
Water and Fire never cease—
life and death return to Earth.
No high nor low, no old nor young—
all come and go, lost in delusion.
They do not know where their minds originate,
yet they seek escape from the Three Realms.
The **demonic kings** all kneel and bow twice,
begging to transcend the Three Realms,
but their minds cling—
they do not know to abandon Water and Fire,
and thus their bodies starve and die.
Without Water and Fire, food cannot be refined;
without Earth, Water and Fire cannot dwell and interact.
Thus, I know that such beings
cannot step away from suffering—
how can they escape the Three Realms?"*

The **Posterior Sage Sovereign** replied:
*"There are six methods to escape the Three Realms.
If one follows them, the body and mind naturally transcend the Three Realms.
Why restrict oneself from Water and Fire?"*

For Water and Fire are the **true qi of Yin and Yang** (阴阳之真炁),
and Earth is the **master of the Five Phases** (五行之主).
Why would one remove them?

Moreover, the **Supreme Celestial Immortals** (上圣天仙)
each employ distinct methods.
I shall now reveal them to you—
listen and receive them.

**First Method:** The body and mind receive instruction,
abandoning Water and excluding Fire.
**Note:** Water and Fire are two **natures** (二性).
The **nature of Water and Fire** benefits humans—
this is called **virtue/power** (德).
If Water and Fire inflict harm upon humans,
this is called **theft** (贼).
Thus, this is the **second method**.

Heaven cannot bring calamity,
Earth cannot cause disaster.
**Note:** When the mind excludes the **nature of Water and Fire**,
Heaven cannot harm, Earth cannot ruin—
the body is at peace.

**Second Method:** The body and mind are **Earth-locked**, **sealing the essence** (土镇锁津).
**Note:** This metaphorically refers to **ascending immortals** (身上仙者) preserving their **vital essence** (精).
Those who practice **chambered cultivation** (行房帷之事),
must **seal their essence** (闭精不泄).
If it leaks, the **spirit is diminished** (损神),
and **vital essence exhaustion ruins the body** (少津败身).
If one can **store and return it to the spirit** (存归神),
and **excess essence moistens the body** (溢津润身),
then **longevity’s pulse flows abundantly** (通多).
Moreover, **practice must not be stagnant** (行不陈),
and there are **precepts within the Dao** (自有经旨),
thus attaining **Celestial Truth** (天真).

**Third Method:** **Conquer Metal and regulate Fire** (制金理火).
**Note:** The **root destiny day** (本命日) begins with one **step of the Yu’s tread** (地纪一遍),
then transforms into **Yu’s tread** (禹步),
and the **Metal talisman** (捻金诀) is performed.
On the **left hand’s fingernail**, the **Fire talisman** (甲为火) is manipulated,
and the **five fingers point to the Metal star** (指金星) three times.
Upon completion, one recites the **Metal-Wood talisman** (金木咒),
invoking the **conquest of Metal and Wood** (金木相克), saying thus:
*"The seven stars shine resplendent,
the **Metal talisman** is most formidable."*

**Fourth Method:** **Conquer Wood and regulate Metal** (制木理金).
**Note:** The **root destiny day** (本命日) begins with one **step of the Heavenly Tread** (天纲一遍),
then transforms into **Yu’s tread** (禹步),
and the **Wood talisman** (捻木诀) is performed.
On the **left hand**, one forms the **Metal Axe** (金斧),
and points to the **Wood star** (指木星) three times.
Upon completion, one **treads three times** (蹑三度),
and recites the **Five Phases invocation** (五行祝),
saying: *"The **Heavenly Tread talisman** (天纲中咒),
Metal, Water, Wood, Fire, Earth—
Metal and Wood mutually push aside,
the seven stars shine resplendent,
the **Heavenly Tread talisman** is most formidable."*

The **four methods above** are means to **dispel the Three Realms’ calamities** (消三界之灾害)
and **harmonize the Five Phases’ mutual conquest** (五行之相人於难克).
If one follows these methods,
within a year, the **five torments** (五苦), **eight hardships** (八难),
**nine adversities** (九厄), and **hundred diseases** (百病) in the body
shall naturally be eliminated.
This is called **alignment** (顺).
The original **teacher treads the Earthly Tread** (履地纪),
**steps on the Dipper** (蹑斗),
and upon **receiving transmission and guidance** (传度时受讫),
now practices the **root destiny day** (本命日) for **cultivation of the truth** (修真),
the methods to escape the Three Realms and Five Phases.

**Note:** According to *The Secret Precepts of Inner Perfection from the Great Peace Scripture* (《太平经□内品修真秘诀》),
the **Uppermost Pure Immortal** (上清大真人) before ascending to Heaven
each took their **root destiny day** (本命),
and practiced the **four talismanic methods** (四等法诀).
Later, they **trod the Dipper star** (步履斗星),
**grasped the Earthly Tread** (镊地纪),
and ascended through the **Heavenly Gate** (升登天门).
They then entered the **Golden Threshold and Jade Terrace** (金阙玉台),
becoming the **Posterior Sage Sovereign** (后圣君).

**Fifth Method:** **Comprehensively conquer the Five Phases** (总制五行),
**transcending them from the body’s exterior** (於身之外).
**Note:** The **Posterior Sage Sovereign** said:
*"The **talisman given to the Heavenly Master** (授天师诀),
the method to **comprehensively conquer the Five Phases from the body’s exterior** (制五行於身之外法)."*

The **Six Celestial Stems** (六甲) encompass **six periods** (六旬),
and within each **six periods** (旬),
there is a **root destiny day** (本命日).
First, one **treads the Earthly Tread** (蹑地纪),
then **treads the Three Platforms** (蹑三台),
which is **treading the Five Stars** (履五星),
each requiring **five repetitions** (各须五遍).
One recites the **Five Phases talismans** (五行咒) **eighteen times** (十八篇),
and *The Rolling Pearl* (《流珠》) **upper scroll** (上卷) contains the precepts.

Then, one **treads the Fire Tread** (步火纲) three times,
and performs **three repetitions of forward, backward, and inverted steps** (顺、倒、反三遍).
One also recites the **three talismans of forward, backward, and inverted** (顺倒、反三等咒).

Upon completion, one stands at the **eastern-southern earthly gate** (东南地户上立),
facing the **western-northern** direction,
**storing thoughts of generals and soldiers** (存思将军吏兵).
First, one **stores the Three Generals of Middle Element** (先存中元三将军),
leading **soldiers and officials** (领吏兵) as per the diagram.
**Middle Element** oversees the **host** (主人).
Next, one **stores the Three Generals of Lower Element** (次下元三将军),
leading **soldiers and officials** (领吏兵),
**overseeing Earth** (主地).
**The Palace** (宫) **declares the body’s merit** (奏身有功),
and **cultivation is never incomplete** (修行不阙).
Then, one **stores the Three Generals of Upper Element** (次上元三将军),
leading **historians and soldiers** (领史兵) to descend and welcome.

「Next, one **stores the Five Virtue Generals** (次五德将军),
then the **Heavenly Sovereign and Thunder General** (天公雷公等将军),
each leading **myriad armies of soldiers and horses** (兵马百千万众),
as **five clouds soar through the void** (五云飞空),
while the **Golden Just Strength-Soldiers** (金刚力士) **guide the body** (引身),
ascending to pay homage to the **Emperor of the Great Peace Golden Threshold** (太平金阙帝) **and the Holy Sovereign of the Morning Court** (晨后圣君).

**Store them as per the diagram of the Three Element Generals** (存之如三元将军图),
