It favors longevity in humans and cherishes the **vitality (生)** that nurtures life. It opposes death, for death is the end of human vitality. This deity abhors the sight of death, so the **Celestial Sovereign (太上)** commands it through talismans to protect living humans and subdue death spirits, thus safeguarding the homes of the living. It averts harm from **deceitful words (非横口舌)**, **malevolent ghosts (凶鬼)** biting at people, **spellcraft poisons (蛊毒)** blocking doors, and **non-corporeal spirits (非尸之字)**. Even **serpents (蛇)** and their venomous substances can be repelled by this method, preventing them from causing harm.*

*This method is typically practiced at night, or both day and night—once daily, once nocturnally. Without interruption, if one **stores the condition in mind (存思)** for three days, the effects should manifest and the illness should abate. First, one must **step the Gāng (纲) Diagram (步)**. **Storing (存)** refers to the mental cultivation of the **Gāng Diagram (纲图)** and the **Jì (纪) Step (步)** method, as well as the **Steel Method (钢法)**. The **Venerable Sage (后圣君)** instructed **Yín Zhēnren (尹真人)**:
*'The **Jì Diagram (蹑纪)** and **Yǔ’s Step (禹步)** require seven years of practice for their merit to take effect. It is not necessary to physically perform the steps yourself. Simply **store them in your mind (心存)** as if visualizing the **Gāng Diagram (纲图)**. If you **embody the steps (存身)** and traverse the **Jì Diagram (纪纪)**, crossing the **Steel Method (钢过)**, the effects will be achieved. If the effects are not yet manifest, you must **step the Gāng Diagram (步纲)** and **Jì Diagram (镊纪)** method. Three traversals of the **Earth Diagram (地纪)**, three repetitions of **Yǔ’s Step (禹步)** with nine traces, and three strikes on the left and right sides while coordinating with the **Heavenly Diagram (天式)**. Then, **twist the Earth’s Vitality Point (地心目)**, shout three times, and chant to **summon and subdue (摄)** the **Four Celestial Guardians (四神)**, as well as the **Earth Deities (地神)** and **Earth Axis Deities (地轴神)**, to relocate mountains, rivers, seas, and reshape their breadth and expanse—whether near or far—without difficulty.*

*This method also includes **Heavenly and Earthly Ritual Coordination (天地式相应)**. With time, one can move freely in and out of the world. The **Five Grades of Verification (五等验极)** are its ultimate tests.*

*The **Celestial Sovereign (太上)** further stated:
*'Those who practice **Daoist techniques (道术)** must do so with **true sincerity (真心)**, without deceit or fraud, without greed, without anger, and without delusion. Only such individuals can **uphold and practice (行持)** this method. If one’s heart is not true, if there is delusion, anger, greed, or deceit, they are unfit to practice this method. Do not imitate the wicked. One must first purify and rectify oneself, ensuring they are worthy of this practice. Now, if you only practice the **Dao of healing and saving people (救人治病之道)**, Heaven and Earth will bestow merit upon you, and you will attain the **Dao of Ascension (仙道)** day by day.*

*In recent times, there was a **Daoist adept (道士)**, **Huáng Lúzi (黄卢子)**, from **Gěyuè (葛越)**. He often practiced **qi control and prohibition techniques (炁禁之术)**, invoking the **Four Celestial Guardians (四神)** and the **Earth Deities (地神)** and **Earth Axis Deities (地轴神)** to command and subdue the **landscape (江山)**. With ease, he could **fold mountains (回山)**—meaning he could condense a thousand *lǐ* of terrain into the span of a single *lǐ* (一里之地), or expand a single *lǐ* into a thousand *lǐ* (千里江山)—without effort. He could also **shrink the earth and turn the seas (缩地转海)**.*

*This method also requires **treading the Jì Diagram (蹑地纪)** for six years. Then, with prolonged breathing and **mental storage (存)**, one invokes the **Four Celestial Guardians (四神)**, the **Earth Deities (地神)**, and the **Earth Axis Deities (地轴神)**, always carrying the **talismans of the Earth Deities and Earth Axis Deities (地神地轴等箓)**. One must **tread the Jì Diagram (蹑纪)** three times, then disperse into **Yǔ’s Step (禹步)** three times, followed by three repetitions of the **Cutting Off Earthly Veins Step (绝地脉步)**. Then, one aligns with the **Heavenly Diagram (天式)**, striking three times on the left and right sides while coordinating. Next, one **twists the Earth’s Vitality Point (地心目)** and shouts three times, chanting to **summon and subdue (摄)** the **Four Celestial Guardians (四神)**, the **Earth Deities (地神)**, and the **Earth Axis Deities (地轴神)**. This enables the **transformation and relocation of mountains, rivers, and seas (移山河江海)**, altering their width and breadth—whether distant or near—without difficulty.*

*This method also includes **Heavenly and Earthly Ritual Coordination (天地式相应)**. In time, one can move freely in and out of the world. The **Five Grades of Verification (五等验极)** are its ultimate tests.

*The **Celestial Sovereign (太上)** further instructed:
*'The **Daoist Master (天师)** who receives the **Venerable Sage’s command (后圣君诀)** must bind the **fourth finger of the left hand (左手第四指)** at its first joint with **five-colored silk threads (五色丝线)**, ensuring they never loosen. Within **five days and nights (五日及夜)**, the **ghost’s eyes will be blinded (鬼目盲)**, and the **human’s eyes will turn green (人目青)**. By the **tenth day (十日)**, the effects will dissipate.*

*'For those who practice **Daoist techniques (道术)**, they must do so with **true sincerity (真心)**, without deceit or fraud, without greed, without anger, and without delusion. Only such individuals can **uphold and practice (行持)** this method. If one’s heart is not true and upright, if they harbor delusion, anger, greed, or deceit, they are unfit to practice this method. Do not imitate the wicked. One must first purify and rectify oneself, ensuring they are worthy of this practice. Now, if you only practice the **Dao of healing and saving people (救人治病之道)**, Heaven and Earth will bestow merit upon you, and you will attain the **Dao of Ascension (仙道)** day by day.*

*'In the present age, people do not understand this. They only blame and resent the **ghosts (鬼)**. Yet the **ghosts (鬼)** cannot themselves cause such harm. They do so by **borrowing the authority of Heavenly and Earthly officials (假天地官之威)**, thus **riding on that power to create mischief (即乘威而作祟)**.*

*Those who hold **Daoist official positions (仙官之位)** all possess **authority (威)**. They command **Heavenly deities (天神)** and **Earthly deities (地只)**, overseeing the **nine lands and ten thousand kingdoms (九土万国)**, as well as **community deities (社神)** and **temple deities (庙神)**. These two categories of deities—one **aiding and healing virtuous people (救治吉人)**, the other **subduing and punishing malevolent and rebellious individuals (征伐恶逆之徒)**—all act according to Heaven’s will. If you **embody the Heavenly method (以子身受天之法)** and **wear the Heavenly talismans (带天之文)**, your body becomes that of a **Heavenly official (天官)**. Then, you can execute Heaven’s commands, **upholding righteousness (执直其心取仁)** and **without favoritism or partiality (无亲无偏党之性)**, **without covetous desires (无傍偷之欲)**, and with a **lofty and distant aspiration (清高志远)**. Such individuals can **endure and generate life (久远生生)**, never retreating but always advancing in wisdom. They alone can be entrusted with this method.*

*To **administer the Heavenly Law (掌行天法)**, one must **grasp the key to repentance and salvation (悔救之诀)**. This method must not be **recklessly transmitted (不可妄传)** to those unworthy, as the crime will extend to **seven generations (七代)** and bring **calamity and annihilation (殃没)** to oneself. The **Daoist Master (天师)** who receives the **Venerable Sage’s command (后圣君诀)** must observe these strictures.*」

...**fully mastered through oral instruction.** The **Golden Lock and Flowing Pearl** method for summoning the twenty-ninth scroll is thus complete.

*(Note: "具口" here is rendered as "fully mastered" to maintain consistency with the previous translation's emphasis on mastery and transmission. "金锁流珠引卷" is a Daoist ritual term, left unannotated per guidelines.)*
